### [1] [The Wooding problem revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25362)
*A. Barletta,D. A. S. Rees*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文研究半无限大多孔介质层中对流不稳定的阈值条件，通过引入Biot数（Biot number）表征边界非完美热传导，对Wooding（1960）经典模型进行推广，并完成了线性稳定性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的地热流体动力学对流不稳定问题最早由Wooding于1960年建模，但原始模型假设边界为完美热传导。本文旨在放宽这一假设，引入Biot数来参数化边界的不完美热传递，以更普遍地分析对流不稳定的触发条件。

Method: 采用线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）方法，研究在多孔介质中存在稳态边界吸流（boundary steady suction）时建立的定常边界层（stationary boundary layer）。考虑两种Rayleigh数（Rayleigh number）定义：基于温度差（temperature-difference-based）的经典版本和基于热通量（heat-flux-based）的变体版本。

Result: 当Biot数趋于无穷大时，本文模型恢复为Wooding原始的温度边界条件。基于热通量的Rayleigh数变体在中性稳定（neutral stability）条件下，在Biot数为无穷大或零的两个极端极限情况下均呈现有限极限值。

Conclusion: 通过引入Biot数，经典Wooding模型被推广至更一般的边界热传导情形，两种Rayleigh数定义在中性稳定条件下的行为差异揭示了边界热传递条件对对流不稳定性阈值的重要影响。

Abstract: The threshold conditions to convective instability in a semi-infinite porous layer saturated by a fluid are determined. The classical setup for this problem in geothermal fluid dynamics was originally modelled by Wooding in 1960. Its formulation is here reconsidered to allow for an imperfect heat transfer across the boundary, parametrised through the Biot number. The temperature boundary condition considered by Wooding is here recovered as the limit of an infinite Biot number. The linear stability analysis of the stationary boundary layer which establishes in the porous medium when a boundary steady suction occurs is carried out. Two different versions of the Rayleigh number are considered, namely, a temperature-difference-based version and a heat-flux-based version. While the former is the classical Rayleigh number for flow in porous media, the latter is a variant definition which displays a finite limit at neutral stability in both the opposite limiting cases of an infinite or of a zero Biot number.

</details>


### [2] [Minimum-enstrophy solutions in topographic quasi-geostrophic flow on the rotating sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25600)
*Sagy Ephrati,Erik Jansson*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文将Bretherton和Haidvogel的最小拟涡度（enstrophy）理论推广到旋转球面准地转（quasi-geostrophic）框架，考虑了底地形和完全非线性科里奥利效应（Coriolis effect），证明了最小拟涡度解的存在性与非线性稳定性，并通过保结构数值方法在球面上求解，参数范围涵盖木星大气，结果揭示了流动的纬度依赖性及地形捕获与纬向流之间的竞争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bretherton和Haidvogel提出的最小拟涡度理论原本适用于平面二维湍流系统，假设系统在固定能量水平下演化到拟涡度最小的状态。本文旨在将该理论推广到更具实际意义的旋转球面准地转设定，纳入底地形和完全非线性的科里奥利效应，以解释平面近似中不存在的纬度依赖效应。

Method: 作者首先在旋转球面准地转方程框架下将最小拟涡度理论形式化，考虑了底地形和完全非线性科里奥利效应；然后通过数学分析证明了最小拟涡度解的存在性和非线性稳定性，并解析描述了特定旋转速率、地形尺度和能量值下的渐近区域；最后采用一种保结构（structure-preserving）数值方法在球面上求解准地转方程，计算了涵盖木星大气参数在内的多种参数组合下的最小拟涡度解。

Result: 数值结果表明流动呈现明显的纬度依赖性：根据参数选择不同，流动趋向于在极地附近被地形捕获，而在赤道附近形成纬向流动（zonal flow）。作者还通过保结构时间离散化方法对扰动解进行数值积分，证实了所预测的非线性稳定性。

Conclusion: 本文成功将最小拟涡度理论从平面拓展到旋转球面准地转环境，证明了相关解的存在性与非线性稳定性，并通过数值实验验证了理论的正确性。该理论可应用于研究木星大气等实际天体物理流动，揭示了纬度依赖性这一平面近似无法捕捉的关键特征。

Abstract: The minimum-enstrophy theory of Bretherton and Haidvogel postulates that two-dimensional turbulent systems evolve to a state that minimises enstrophy at a fixed energy level. We extend this to the rotating spherical quasi-geostrophic setting, accounting for bottom topography and the fully nonlinear Coriolis effect, resulting in latitude-dependent effects not present in planar approximations. We prove existence and nonlinear stability of minimum-enstrophy solutions and describe analytically asymptotic regimes for certain rates of rotation, topography scales, and energy values. We compute the minimum-enstrophy solutions by a structure-preserving method for the quasi-geostrophic equations on the sphere. We apply the method to a range of parameter values, including those describing Jupiter's atmosphere. The results reveal a distinct latitude dependence of the flow, with a tendency for topographical trapping near the poles and zonal flow near the equator, depending on the chosen parameters. The predicted nonlinear stability is confirmed numerically by integrating perturbed solutions using a structure-preserving time discretisation.

</details>


### [3] [Non-Oberbeck-Boussinesq effects in coldwater](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24979)
*Gustavo Estay,Daisuke Noto,Hugo N. Ulloa*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过直接数值模拟，在瑞利-贝纳尔（Rayleigh–Bénard）对流框架下研究了水在接近冰点时的异常物性（非线性密度-温度关系、粘度增大、热导率降低）对对流的影响，发现非Oberbeck–Boussinesq效应降低了平均流体温度并破坏了平均温度剖面的经典对称性，同时使临界瑞利数发生偏移，但无量纲传热率仍遵循经典标度律，而雷诺数的标度行为与Grossmann–Lohse统一理论一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水在接近冰点时表现出反常的非线性密度-温度（ρ-T）关系、粘度增大和热导率降低，这些偏离标准Oberbeck–Boussinesq（OB）近似的行为可能改变冰包围水体的对流特性，但相关效应尚未被探索。

Method: 采用经典的瑞利-贝纳尔（Rayleigh–Bénard）对流框架，通过直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulations）对非Oberbeck–Boussinesq效应进行研究。

Result: 非OB效应降低了平均流体温度并打破了平均温度剖面的经典对称性，对称破缺程度取决于瑞利数（Rayleigh number, Ra）和温度依赖的材料属性。临界瑞利数（Ra_c）发生了微小偏移。计入偏移后，无量纲传热率（Nu）遵循经典超临界标度；雷诺数（Re）符合Grossmann–Lohse统一理论：低Ra对流中Re∝(Ra−Ra_c)^{1/2}（I_u区），高Ra下Re∝(Ra−Ra_c)^{4/7}（III_u区），后者在中等普朗特数（Prandtl number, Pr∼10）下获得，而非经典预期的高Pr条件。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了近冰点材料异常如何影响对流的局域和全局性质，对冰冻圈液态水体的热量分布和混合具有重要启示。

Abstract: Water exhibits an anomalous nonlinear temperature-density ($ρ$-$T$) relation as it approaches freezing, along with an increase in viscosity, and a decrease in thermal conductivity. These departures from the standard Oberbeck--Boussinesq approximation, which assumes constant material properties and a linear $ρ$-$T$ relation, can modify convection in ice-bounded aquatic systems, yet their effects remain unexplored. Here, we examine these effects via the canonical Rayleigh--Bénard convection framework using direct numerical simulations. We show that non-Oberbeck--Boussinesq effects lower the mean fluid temperature relative to the standard case and break the classical symmetry of the mean temperature profile. The magnitude of this symmetry breaking depends on both the Rayleigh number $Ra$ and the temperature-dependent material properties retained in the governing equations. We further identify a small but measurable shift in the critical Rayleigh number, $Ra_c$. After accounting for this shift, the nondimensional heat transfer rate, $Nu$, follows the classical scaling with supercriticality, while $Re$ remains consistent with the Grossmann--Lohse unifying theory, $Re\propto (Ra-Ra_c)^{1/2}$ for low-$Ra$ convection (regime $\mathrm{I}_u$) and $Re\propto (Ra-Ra_c)^{4/7}$ at high-$Ra$ (regime $\mathrm{III}_u$). Unlike the classical expectation that the latter scaling arises at high Prandtl number, here it is obtained at an intermediate Prandtl number, $Pr\sim 10$. Our results establish how near-freezing material anomalies affect both local and global properties of convection, with implications for heat distribution and mixing in cryospheric liquid waters.

</details>

# cond-mat.mtrl-sci [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Trillion-atom molecular dynamics simulations with ab initio accuracy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24816)
*Pengfei Suo,Wudi Cao,Xingxing Wu,Wenjie Zhang,Zheyong Fan,Shuanghan Xian,Rui Wang,Cheng Qian,Chao Liang,Qinghong Yuan,Xiaoshuang Chen,Pengfei Guan,Jingde Bu,Hongzhen Tian,Yanjing Su,Feng Ding,Lin-Wang Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报告了一项包含1.62万亿（trillion）个原子的分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟，利用神经演化势（neuroevolution potential, NEP）框架在中国新一代智能超级计算机上实现了从头计算（ab initio）精度；其计算速度比此前最先进的机器学习力场模拟快100倍，比六年前戈登·贝尔奖（Gordon Bell Prize）获奖应用快1000倍，并在45,000块GPGPU上实现了86.9%的弱扩展（weak scaling）效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料性质从根本上取决于跨尺度（multiscale）现象，其中介观尺度（mesoscale）在尺寸上恰好是光学显微镜可直接观测的范围，连接了原子尺度的微观描述与连续模型的宏观世界。现有的模拟方法在介观尺度上兼顾量子级精度与计算效率仍然面临巨大挑战。

Method: 采用神经演化势（neuroevolution potential, NEP）框架，在中国新一代智能超级计算机上运行分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟，实现了1.62万亿个原子的体系规模，并达到从头计算（ab initio）精度。

Result: 模拟速度比此前最先进的机器学习力场模拟快100倍（以时间-解（time-to-solution, s/step/atom）衡量），比六年前戈登·贝尔奖（Gordon Bell Prize）获奖应用快1000倍；从单块GPGPU扩展到45,000块GPGPU时，弱扩展（weak scaling）效率达到86.9%。

Conclusion: 这些成果重新定义了原子模拟的边界，使得直接以量子级精度（quantum-level precision）进行介观尺度（mesoscopic）建模成为可能。

Abstract: Material properties are fundamentally dictated by multiscale phenomena, which often reach mesoscale in size. The μm mesoscale is also the size which can be observed directly under an optical microscope, bridging the atomistic microscopic description with the continuous model macroscopic world. In this work, we report an unprecedented molecular dynamics (MD) simulation comprising 1.62 trillion atoms. Utilizing the neuroevolution potential (NEP) framework, we attained ab initio accuracy on China's New-generation Intelligent Supercomputer. Our implementation achieves a time-to-solution (s/step/atom) 100 times faster than previous state-of-the-art machine learning force field simulations, and 1,000 times faster than the Gordon Bell Prize-winning application from six years ago. Furthermore, we demonstrate an 86.9% weak scaling efficiency from a single GPGPU to 45,000 GPGPUs. These results redefine atomistic simulation boundaries, enabling direct mesoscopic modeling with quantum-level precision.

</details>


### [5] [Visualizing Crystallization Dynamics and Transformation Pathways of Disordered Rocksalt Oxides During Thermally Activated Sol-Gel Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24941)
*Diyi Cheng,Tim Kodalle,Anika T. Promi,Ansuman Halder,Raphael F. Moral,Madeline Grass,Venkata S. Avvaru,Haegyeom Kim,Carolin M. Sutter-Fella,Haimei Zheng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过多尺度表征手段（原位液相池加热透射电镜、傅里叶变换红外光谱、原位同步辐射X射线衍射）揭示了溶胶-凝胶（sol-gel）合成Li1.2Mn0.4Ti0.4O2（LMTO）无序岩盐（disordered rocksalt，DRX）正极材料在早期成核阶段的化学与结构转变路径，发现局部区域存在经典多步过渡与动力学捷径（kinetic shortcut）两种不同结晶路径，并指出前驱体中过渡金属离子与锂离子在乙酸配位网络中的不同结合程度是导致微观环境差异的原因，但宏观上转变主要通过尖晶石LMTO和锂钛矿中间相进行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 溶胶-凝胶法（sol-gel synthesis）作为一种湿化学加工路线，能够在较低温度下实现对功能材料组成、形貌和微观结构的调控，但其早期成核阶段的转变路径尚不清晰，制约了对材料均匀性与性能的精确控制。

Method: 采用多尺度表征工具：原位液相池加热透射电镜（in situ heating transmission electron microscopy，TEM）在纳米尺度可视化结晶路径；宏观尺度傅里叶变换红外光谱（FTIR）分析前驱体中化学微环境差异；原位同步辐射X射线衍射（in situ SXRD）监测宏观相变过程。

Result: 原位TEM显示部分区域遵循经典多步过渡路径（经热力学稳定中间相），另一些区域则呈现动力学捷径——中间纳米晶溶解于局部非晶基体后直接析出DRX结构。FTIR表明过渡金属离子比锂离子更强烈地结合到乙酸配位网络中，造成前驱体微环境中化学差异。原位SXRD显示宏观转变主要通过尖晶石（spinel）LMTO和锂钛矿（lithium titanite）中间相最终形成DRX-LMTO。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了溶胶-凝胶衍生DRX-LMTO材料中时空化学与结构转变的复杂性，指出局部与宏观结晶路径存在差异，并建议精细调控溶胶-凝胶化学条件以操控结晶路径，从而更高效地实现目标材料均匀性。

Abstract: Sol-gel synthesis is a wet-chemical processing route for the fabrication of functional materials offering control over composition, morphology, and microstructure at relatively low processing temperatures compared to conventional solid-state synthesis methods. While the sol-gel process initiates with intermixed molecular precursors, the transformation pathways at the early nucleation stage are insufficiently understood. Here, the chemical and structural transformation of disordered rocksalt (DRX) Li1.2Mn0.4Ti0.4O2 (LMTO), a promising cathode material for lithium batteries, is studied by multiscale characterization tools. In situ heating transmission electron microscopy (TEM) using a liquid cell visualizes and identifies crystallization pathways at nanoscale. While some regions follow a classical multi-step transition through thermodynamically stable intermediates, others exhibit a kinetic shortcut in which intermediate nanocrystals dissolve into a localized amorphous matrix that directly precipitates the DRX structure. Macroscale FTIR corroborates the findings to be related to chemically distinct microenvironments in the gel precursor, with transition metal ions more strongly incorporated into the acetate-coordinated network than lithium. Although in situ heating TEM captures diverse local transformation pathways, in situ SXRD indicates that the macroscopic transformation proceeds predominantly through spinel LMTO and lithium titanite intermediates toward DRX-LMTO. The findings shed light on the spatiotemporal chemical and structural transformations in sol-gel derived DRX-LMTO materials, and call for fine tuning of such sol-gel chemistries to manipulate the crystallization pathways and achieve target material homogeneity more efficiently.

</details>


### [6] [Influence of Heterogeneity on the Response of Architected Metamaterials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25075)
*Sarvesh Joshi,Jingye Tan,Craig M. Hamel,Stavros Gaitanaros,Nikolaos Bouklas*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究将梯度增强的非局部连续介质公式扩展至包含随机材料异质性，通过高斯随机场（Gaussian random fields）施加于选定本构参数，建立了连接随机材料变异性与失稳驱动力学（instability-driven mechanics）的统一框架。有限元模拟表明，异质性从根本上改变了相成核（phase nucleation）、局部化形态（localization morphology）和宏观响应，为理解建筑超材料（architected metamaterials）中的缺陷敏感性和稳定性提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建筑超材料（如泡沫和点阵结构）的复杂响应受微结构失稳、局部化和类相变现象控制，而制造过程中固有的微结构异质性进一步影响其行为。现有方法缺乏统一框架来系统描述随机材料变异性与失稳驱动力学之间的关联，无法独立控制材料波动的振幅和空间相关性。

Method: 将梯度增强的非局部连续介质公式扩展，通过高斯随机场（Gaussian random fields）对选定本构参数施加随机材料异质性；引入非局部特征长度与相关长度之间的特征长度尺度比（characteristic lengthscale ratio），实现在随机或空间相关微结构极限下的建模；保持热力学一致性和局部化正则化。

Result: 有限元模拟（constrained compression and indentation）表明，异质性从根本上改变了相成核（phase nucleation）、局部化形态（localization morphology）和宏观响应；异质性单独即可影响响应的特征特性，如稳定性、平台区斜率和初始弹性区的消除。

Conclusion: 所提框架为将随机材料变异性与建筑超材料中的失稳驱动力学联系起来提供了统一方法，有助于加深对缺陷敏感性、稳定性和设计的理解。该研究展示了异质性本身即可独立影响建筑超材料的特征响应。

Abstract: Architected metamaterials like foams and lattices exhibit complex responses governed by microstructural instabilities, localization, and phase-transition-like phenomena. Their behavior is further affected by heterogeneities inherent in their microstructure often caused through manufacturing processes. In this study we extend a gradient-enhanced, nonlocal continuum formulation to incorporate stochastic material heterogeneity through Gaussian random fields imposed on selected constitutive parameters. The framework enables independent control of both the amplitude and spatial correlation of material fluctuations while preserving thermodynamic consistency and regularization of localization. It also introduces a characteristic lengthscale ratio between the nonlocal and correlation lengthscales, that enables modeling at the limit of random or spatially correlated microstructures. Finite element simulations of confined compression and indentation show that heterogeneity fundamentally alters phase nucleation, localization morphology, and macroscopic response. Overall, the proposed framework provides a unified approach for linking stochastic material variability to instability-driven mechanics in architected metamaterials, enabling improved understanding of imperfection sensitivity, stability and design. It showcases how heterogeneity alone can influence characteristic features of the response, such as stability, slope of the plateau region, and elimination of the initial elastic regime.

</details>


### [7] [Ultrafast Energy Absorption in Silicon Controlled by Two-Color Double Pulses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25093)
*Eiyu S. Gushiken,Mizuki Tani,Hiroki Katow,Kenichi L. Ishikawa*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过含时密度泛函理论（time-dependent density functional theory, TDDFT）理论证明了，利用双色飞秒双脉冲（two-color femtosecond double-pulse）辐照可以控制晶体硅中的能量吸收，其最优波长组合强烈依赖于脉冲强度区间，并且揭示了第一脉冲制备的非平衡电子态（nonequilibrium electronic state）通过改变每个激发电子的能量增益来增强吸收的微观机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索利用双色飞秒双脉冲辐照控制晶体硅（crystalline silicon）中能量吸收的可行性，并揭示其微观机制。

Method: 采用含时密度泛函理论（time-dependent density functional theory, TDDFT）进行系统计算，考察峰值强度区间为 $2\times10^{11}$-$10^{13}$ W/cm$^2$、波长分别为515、1030和2060 nm条件下的波长与强度依赖性。

Result: 在低强度区间，多光子带间吸收（multiphoton interband absorption）占主导，较短波长组合增强能量吸收；在高等离化（high-intensity）区间，隧穿电离（tunneling ionization）和带内加速（intraband acceleration）的贡献显著，较长波长组合增强吸收；在中等强度区间，短波长脉冲先于长波长脉冲时出现显著增强，该增强源自第一脉冲制备的非平衡电子态提高了第二脉冲激发电子的能量增益。

Conclusion: 半导体中的超快能量转移可以通过适当设计两个脉冲的波长和强度组合进行调控，该结果为双色强场激发（two-color strong-field excitation）提供了微观层面的理解。

Abstract: We theoretically show that energy absorption in crystalline silicon can be controlled by two-color femtosecond double-pulse irradiation, in which two temporally separated pulses with different wavelengths interact sequentially with the system. Using time-dependent density functional theory, we systematically examine the wavelength and intensity dependence of the absorbed energy over peak intensities of $2\times10^{11}$-$10^{13}$ W/cm$^2$ and wavelengths of 515, 1030, and 2060 nm. We find that the mechanism governing energy absorption and the optimal wavelength combination strongly depend on the intensity regime. In the low-intensity regime, multiphoton interband absorption is dominant, and energy absorption is enhanced for pulse pairs composed of shorter wavelengths. In contrast, in the high-intensity regime, the contributions of tunneling ionization and intraband acceleration become significant, leading to enhanced absorption for longer-wavelength combinations. In the intermediate-intensity regime, a pronounced enhancement is observed when a short-wavelength pulse precedes a long-wavelength pulse. Our analysis reveals that the nonequilibrium electronic state prepared by the first pulse modifies the excitation process induced by the second pulse, thereby enhancing the absorbed energy through an increased energy gain per excited electron. In this regime, the energy absorption is governed not only by the number of excited carriers but also by the energy gain per excited electron, which can be strongly modified by the pulse sequence. These results indicate that ultrafast energy transfer in semiconductors is tunable by appropriately designing the wavelength and intensity combination of the two pulses, and provide microscopic insight into two-color strong-field excitation.

</details>


### [8] [Determination of the Fermi Energy of Diamond using Photoluminescence Spectral Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25097)
*Yifan Song,Sina Ilkhani,Leah Webb,Helen Highland,Shunki Nakamura,Stephen B. Cronin,Susumu Takahashi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金刚石中费米能级与施主-受主浓度呈高度非线性关系，实验测定费米能级对于理解其电子性质至关重要，但现有方法难以满足需求。

Method: 基于光致发光（PL）光谱分析测量NV-和NV0中心相对布居，结合Deák等人通过密度泛函理论（DFT）给出的费米能与形成能关系，反推出金刚石样品的费米能级；该方法还可扩展至硅空位（SiV）中心。

Result: 该方法能够通过PL测量确定金刚石的费米能级，并应用于研究NV中心的自旋相干性及电荷态转换稳定性；适用于极端环境，具有高空间和时间分辨率。

Conclusion: 基于PL的费米能级测定方法具有高时空分辨率和极端环境适应性，可推广至多种宽禁带半导体的费米能级测定。

Abstract: Electronic band structures and the Fermi energy provide essential information for understanding the electronic properties of solids. In semiconductors, the Fermi energy level is determined by the donor and acceptor concentrations. For diamond, the relationship between the Fermi energy level and the donor-acceptor concentrations is highly nonlinear; therefore, experimental determination of the Fermi energy level is important. Here, we report a method to determine the Fermi energy of diamond based on photoluminescence (PL) measurement. The density-functional-theory (DFT) study by Deák et al.~\cite{deak2014formation} showed the relationship between the Fermi energy and the formation energies of nitrogen-vacancy centers in the negatively charged (NV-) and neutrally charged (NV0) charge states. In the present method, we measure the relative populations of the NV- and NV0 centers from PL spectral analysis and, using these populations and the DFT result, determine the Fermi energy of the diamond samples. Moreover, we show the application of the method to study the spin coherence and the stability against the charge state conversion of the NV centers on several diamond samples. We also extend the method for the Fermi energy determination using the silicon-vacancy (SiV) center in diamond. The PL-based method is advantageous for determining the Fermi energy with high spatial and fast time resolutions, even in extreme environments, and can be extended to determine various wide band gap semiconductors.

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用低温扫描隧道显微镜（low-temperature scanning tunnelling microscopy, LT-STM）直接成像；结合第一性原理理论（first-principles theory）和偏压依赖性成像（bias-dependent imaging）进行机理分析；在石墨衬底上的单层冰（monolayer ice）体系中施加外部电场（external electric field）。

Abstract: Hydrogen-bond networks govern molecular structure and function across chemistry, biology and materials science, yet their deterministic control at the atomic scale remains a central challenge (1-9).Here, we directly visualize how an external electric field enables reversible control of a hydrogen-bond network in monolayer ice on graphite through interfacial charge redistribution. Low-temperature scanning tunnelling microscopy reveals a field-driven transition from a mobile, physisorbed, non-wetting water phase to an ordered hexagonal monolayer, enabling deterministic nucleation, growth and complete wetting on an otherwise inert surface. Systematic variation of the field induces continuous lattice strain coexisting with discrete conductance states, revealing coupled structural and electronic responses. Reversal of the field polarity drives collective dipolar inversion, enabling switching between symmetry-equivalent configurations without disrupting the lattice. Supported by first-principles theory and bias-dependent imaging, these effects arise from field-induced modification of the interfacial electronic structure rather than purely geometric or orientational effects. These results establish interfacial charge redistribution as a general mechanism for electrically programming hydrogen-bond networks, providing a route to control molecular organization, electronic properties and collective dipolar order at interfaces.

### [10] [Kohn-Sham Hamiltonian from Effective Field Theory: Quasiparticle Band Narrowing from Frozen Core Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25199)
*Xiansheng Cai,Han Wang,Kun Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过构建非均匀电子气的有效场论（EFT），推导出Kohn-Sham（KS）能带在乘以一个冻结芯重整化因子（frozen-core renormalization factor）z_core后即为准粒子能带，该因子解释了碱金属和碱土金属中KS带宽高估ARPES测量值20-35%的长期矛盾，并在Li、Na、K等材料中通过后自洽场（post-SCF）公式得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kohn-Sham（KS）本征值在密度泛函理论（DFT）中被认为没有物理意义，但实际中常被与角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）直接比较并用作多体方法的输入。碱金属和碱土金属中KS带宽高估ARPES测量值20-35%的系统性偏差在所有交换关联泛函下均存在，该长期未解矛盾是本文的核心问题动机。

Method: 构建了非均匀电子气的有效场论（EFT），通过两个条件——芯激发能与价费米能之间的能标分离、均匀电子气近似伽利略不变性（由图解蒙特卡洛确认）——推导出KS能带与准粒子能带的关系。进一步推导出封闭形式的后自洽场（post-SCF）修正公式，并运用大语言模型（LLM）协同推导，结合符号验证和少量实验验证。

Result: 冻结芯重整化因子z_core的修正量1-z_core在碱金属中达到20-35%，在Al和Si中低于5%，同时解释了KS能带理论在两类材料中的失效与成功。在Li、Na、K、Ca、Mg、Al和Si上的验证表明，预测的准粒子能带解决了长期存在的ARPES带宽差异问题，其精度与嵌入动力学平均场理论（embedded DMFT）相当，但计算成本极低。

Conclusion: KS能带乘以冻结芯重整化因子z_core后即为准粒子能带，该因子源于动态芯激发效应，无法被任何静态势（包括传统赝势）捕捉。该工作同时展示了第一性原理智能体科学（first-principles agentic science）范式——由LLM协同推导、符号验证和小规模实验验证的受控近似推导流程，可解决LLM审计瓶颈和基于拟合的人工智能科学中不可证伪性的问题。

Abstract: Kohn-Sham (KS) eigenvalues are routinely compared with angle-resolved photoemission (ARPES) and used as input for many-body methods, yet density functional theory (DFT) assigns them no physical meaning. For alkali and alkaline-earth metals, KS bandwidths overestimate ARPES measurements by 20-35%, a discrepancy that persists across all exchange-correlation functionals. We construct an effective field theory (EFT) of the inhomogeneous electron gas and show that two conditions imply KS bands are the quasiparticle bands, up to a frozen-core renormalization factor zcore: a scale separation between core excitation energies and the valence Fermi energy, and an approximate Galilean invariance of the uniform electron gas confirmed by diagrammatic Monte Carlo. This factor reflects dynamical core excitations that conventional pseudopotentials freeze out and no static potential can capture. The correction 1-zcore reaches 20-35% for alkali metals but falls below 5% for Al and Si, explaining both the failure and success of KS band theory. We derive a closed-form post-SCF formula and validate it for Li, Na, K, Ca, Mg, Al, and Si; the predicted quasiparticle bands resolve the long-standing ARPES bandwidth discrepancy, matching embedded dynamical mean-field theory at negligible cost. This work also exemplifies first-principles agentic science, a direction particularly suited to the AGI-for-Science paradigm: an LLM-co-developed derivation with controlled approximations, verified symbolically and against a few experiments, becomes a deterministic harness for agentic scale-out, resolving simultaneously the LLM audit bottleneck and the non-falsifiability of fit-based AI-for-science.

### [11] [Benchmarking Universal Machine-Learned Interatomic Potentials for High-Temperature Metal-Organic Framework Chemistry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25262)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Universal machine-learned interatomic potentials (uMLIPs) offer a promising approach to performing atomistic simulations at near-DFT accuracy with greatly reduced computational cost. These trajectories capture equilibrium dynamics, thermally induced distortions, and early-stage decomposition events, including linker degradation and metal node aggregation. Subsequently, we use this dataset to benchmark five leading uMLIPs: ORB-v3, MACE-MP-0a, MACE-MPA-0, fairchem ODAC23, and fairchem OMAT. Our results reveal that ORB-v3 and fairchem OMAT achieve the lowest energy, force, and stress errors across all temperatures. However, all models exhibit significant error under high-temperature conditions. Long-timescale molecular dynamics simulations produced with ORB-v3 demonstrate that the generative error of uMLIPs far exceeds model losses captured during static validation, highlighting the limitations of current universal models for simulating high-temperature MOF dynamics. This work provides a benchmark for assessing the robustness of uMLIPs in extreme regimes and guides future development of potentials capable of accurately modeling the chemistry of high-temperature MOF dynamics.

### [12] [Reversible Modulation of Thermal Conductivity in GaN via Strain-Driven Reorganization of Dislocation Ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25287)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用原位应变依赖的时域热反射（time-domain thermoreflectance, TDTR）测量热导率；利用高分辨率X射线衍射（high-resolution x-ray diffraction）分析位错关联的统计变化；通过拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）监测E₂^high声子线宽的非单调演化。

Conclusion: 弹性应变能促进穿透位错（threading dislocation）长程应变场的可逆屏蔽与有序化，从而减少声子散射。缺陷关联可作为控制晶体固体热输运的可调谐自由度。

Abstract: Crystalline defects are generally regarded as static phonon scatterers that irreversibly suppress thermal transport. Here we show that elastic strain can dynamically and reversibly reorganize dislocation ensembles and strongly modify heat conduction. Using in situ strain-dependent time-domain thermoreflectance measurements, we observe a reversible enhancement of thermal conductivity in GaN by 23% under only 0.21% uniaxial strain. High-resolution x-ray diffraction reveals progressive narrowing of the symmetric (0002) reflection together with a crossover of the diffuse scattering tails from a $q^{-3}$ to a $q^{-2}$ power law, indicating a strain-induced change in the statistical correlations of threading dislocations. Raman spectroscopy further shows a non-monotonic evolution of the $E_{2}^{\mathrm{high}}$ phonon linewidth, with a minimum near the same threshold strain at which thermal conductivity sharply increases. These results support a picture in which elastic strain promotes reversible screening and ordering of long-range dislocation strain fields, thereby reducing phonon scattering. Our work establishes defect correlations as a tunable degree of freedom for controlling thermal transport in crystalline solids.

### [13] [Proximity Ferroelectricity Driven by Mobile High-Miller-Index Domain Walls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25343)
*Changming Ke,Shi Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过第一性原理计算和机器学习分子动力学模拟，揭示了纤锌矿铁电体（如AlScN）中由高米勒指数畴壁介导的新型极化翻转机制，阐明了Sc掺杂的双重角色（稳定高指数畴壁与引入钉扎效应），并成功解释了AlN/AlScN多层膜中未掺杂AlN层的“近邻铁电性”（proximity ferroelectricity）现象。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和机器学习分子动力学模拟（machine-learning molecular dynamics simulations）相结合的方法，系统研究高米勒指数畴壁（high-Miller-index domain walls）的成核与迁移行为。

Conclusion: 该微观“分而治之”（divide-and-conquer）机制成功解释了近邻铁电性的物理起源，并指出高指数界面是控制铁电体极化翻转的尚未充分开发的调控手段。

Abstract: Wurtzite ferroelectrics such as scandium-doped aluminum nitride (AlScN) are promising for next-generation memory because of their compatibility with semiconductor processes and strong spontaneous polarization. Ferroelectric switching in these materials is typically attributed to doping-induced softening of the bulk switching barrier. However, recent reports of proximity ferroelectricity, in which undoped AlN layers up to 500 nm thick fully switch in AlN/AlScN multilayers, challenge this view. Here, we reveal an alternative switching mechanism mediated by high-Miller-index domain walls, long overlooked due to their complex geometry and presumed instability. Using first-principles calculations and machine-learning molecular dynamics simulations, we show that these walls, once nucleated, migrate with exceptionally low barriers. The Sc dopants play a dual role: they stabilize high-index walls and thereby promote nucleation, while also introducing pinning that hinders wall motion. In multilayers, our simulations demonstrate that mobile domain walls nucleated in AlScN can propagate deep into adjacent AlN, where they move easily without dopant pinning, enabling low-field switching across thick undoped layers. This microscopic divide-and-conquer mechanism resolves the puzzle of proximity ferroelectricity and highlights high-index interfaces as an underexplored lever for controlling ferroelectric switching.

### [14] [Determination of Burgers vectors of dislocations in monoclinic $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ crystals by large-angle convergent-beam electron diffraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25428)
*Yoshihiro Sugawara,Yongzhao Yao,Yukari Ishikawa*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究展示了利用大角度会聚束电子衍射（LACBED）确定单斜相β-Ga₂O₃中柏氏矢量（Burgers vector）的方法，通过无需度量张量的实空间与倒易空间对偶关系评估非正交体系中的g·b内积，并基于LACBED节点计数成功确定了纳米压痕引入的位错伯氏矢量，结果与弱束暗场成像一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单斜晶系β-Ga₂O₃是一种非正交晶体系统，其位错的柏氏矢量（Burgers vector）确定在传统方法中存在困难。本研究旨在验证大角度会聚束电子衍射（large-angle convergent-beam electron diffraction, LACBED）在该材料体系中的适用性。

Method: 采用大角度会聚束电子衍射（LACBED）对单斜β-Ga₂O₃中的位错进行表征。利用实空间基矢与倒易空间基矢之间的对偶关系（dual relationship），在不引入度量张量（metric tensor）的情况下评估非正交体系中的内积g·b。通过LACBED衍射图中节点的计数确定柏氏矢量（Burgers vector）。

Result: 通过LACBED节点计数，成功且明确地确定了纳米压痕引入的位错的柏氏矢量（Burgers vector）。该结果与弱束暗场成像（weak-beam dark-field imaging）的观测结果一致。

Conclusion: 大角度会聚束电子衍射（LACBED）被确认为一种有效且可靠的位错柏氏矢量（Burgers vector）确定方法，适用于单斜相β-Ga₂O₃材料。

Abstract: We demonstrate the applicability of large-angle convergent-beam electron diffraction (LACBED) for Burgers vector determination in monoclinic $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$. The inner product $g \cdot b$ in this non-orthogonal system can be evaluated without a metric tensor by using the dual relationship between real and reciprocal lattice bases. Based on this framework, Burgers vectors of dislocations introduced by nanoindentation were unambiguously determined from LACBED node counts. The results are consistent with weak-beam dark-field imaging, confirming the effectiveness of LACBED for $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$.

### [15] [From Ultrafast Demagnetization to Ultrafast Spintronics : a 30 years story](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25431)
*Quentin Remy,Stéphane Mangin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文综述了飞秒激光诱导的超快退磁（ultrafast demagnetization）如何催生飞秒磁学（femtomagnetism）领域，并进一步与自旋电子学（spintronics）融合形成超快自旋电子学（ultrafast spintronics），实现飞秒时间尺度上的高效磁矩操控与信息处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释飞秒激光诱导超快退磁过程中角动量如何以皮秒以下的时间尺度从自旋系统中转移出去，揭示电子、声子和自旋在非平衡态中的作用，并为超快自旋电子学奠定物理基础。

Method: 通过飞秒激光激发实现超快退磁，产生自旋翻转（spin-flips）、自旋极化（spin polarization）、磁振子（magnons）和自旋流（spin currents）；利用螺旋无关的单脉冲全光开关（helicity-independent single-pulse all-optical switching, AOS）在稀土-过渡金属（RE-TM）铁磁材料如GdFeCo中实现飞焦级能耗、无外磁场的磁化反转；将超快光激发与自旋电子器件结合，在自旋阀和隧道结中实现飞秒脉冲驱动的确定性磁化反转。

Result: 飞秒激光可在皮秒以下时间尺度内猝灭磁有序；RE-TM铁磁材料成为理解飞秒时间尺度角动量流动的基准系统；超快自旋注入（ultrafast spin injection）的作用类似于自旋转移矩（spin transfer torque），但速度快三个数量级，可实现铁磁和铁磁层的反转。

Conclusion: 超快自旋电子学通过实现超快、节能的磁化开关，有望为高速信息处理提供可扩展技术，同时提出了关于强非平衡量子材料中角动量转移的基础性科学问题。

Abstract: The discovery of femtosecond laser-induced ultrafast demagnetization in 1996 opened a new field, femtomagnetism, in which magnetic order can be quenched on timescales shorter than a picosecond. This seminal observation revealed that angular momentum can be transferred out of the spin system with unprecedented speed, launching intense efforts to disentangle the roles of electrons, phonons, and spins in the non-equilibrium regime. Soon it became evident that ultrafast demagnetization generates spin-flips, spin polarization, magnons and spin currents, providing new channels for angular-momentum flow. These insights laid the foundation for linking femtomagnetism with spintronics. An emblematic breakthrough in this evolution is the helicity-independent single-pulse all-optical switching (AOS) observed in rare-earth transition-metal (RE-TM) ferrimagnets such as GdFeCo. This mechanism, operating at femtojoule-scale energies and without external magnetic fields, establishes RE-TM alloys as benchmark systems for understanding and exploiting angular-momentum flow at the femtosecond timescale. Building on these concepts, the combination of ultrafast optical excitation with spintronic devices has demonstrated deterministic magnetization reversal driven by femtosecond pulses in spin valves and tunnel junctions, including rare-earth-free systems. Ultrafast spin injection, acting analogously to spin transfer torque but operating three orders of magnitude faster, allows reversal of both ferromagnetic and ferrimagnetic layers. By enabling ultrafast and energy-efficient switching, ultrafast spintronics promises scalable technologies for high-speed information processing while raising fundamental questions about angular momentum transfer in strongly out-of-equilibrium quantum materials.

### [16] [Thermodynamic surface reconstruction governs catalytic behavior in high-entropy alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25454)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者通过热力学模拟复现高通量实验测量，比较均匀表面模型与热力学退火表面模型在预测组分-活性关系上的表现；并利用偏析能量学分析与短程有序度量化，评估预测误差与表面微观结构之间的关联。

Result: 均匀表面模型无法重现实验观测到的组分-活性趋势，在某些情况下预测表现低于或相当于随机基线水平；而热力学退火表面则能恢复与实验活性景观（activity landscape）的有意义一致性，并显著提升活性组分的识别率。偏析能量学显示元素在表面强烈富集，形成化学选择性界面，将随机合金的宽吸附能谱压缩为更窄的催化有利位点分布。预测误差与短程有序度之间存在明确关联，据此可界定均匀模型的适用边界。

Conclusion: 均匀表面模型仅在一定短程有序度范围内有效；热力学选择的表面状态（thermodynamically selected surface state）应被视为多组分合金催化预测的控制性参数（governing parameter）。

Abstract: High-entropy alloys are widely modeled as homogeneously mixed surfaces, yet the validity of this assumption for catalytic prediction remains unclear. Here, we reproduce high-throughput experimental measurements using thermodynamic simulations and show that surface ordering is essential for accurately capturing the compositional activity landscape. Homogeneous surface models fail to reproduce experimentally observed trends and, in some regimes, perform at or below the random-selection baseline. In contrast, thermodynamically annealed surfaces restore meaningful agreement with the experimental activity landscape and substantially improve the recovery of active compositions. Segregation energetics reveal strong surface enrichment of preferred elements, producing chemically selective interfaces that collapse the broad adsorption-energy spectrum of random alloys into a narrower distribution of catalytically favorable sites. By linking predictive error to the degree of short-range order, we identify a validity boundary for homogeneous models and establish the thermodynamically selected surface state as a governing parameter for predictive catalysis in multicomponent alloys.

### [20] [Tuning magnitude and direction of lattice thermal conductivity in transition metal dichalcogenide heterobilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25576)
*Elliot Perviz,Antonio Cammarata*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于第一性原理计算，采用声子基（phonon basis）和松弛子基（relaxon basis）下线性化玻尔兹曼输运方程（Boltzmann transport equation）的精确解，分析晶格热导率（LTC）；引入松弛子分析（relaxon analysis）和热粘度（thermal viscosity）作为诊断工具。

Result: 本征异质双层具有面内各向同性LTC，且随温度保持一致的次序。较轻原子通常有利于更高的LTC，但需要足够大的质量对比度才能诱导与输运相关振动模式的层局域化（layer localisation）。热粘度分析表明，金属/非金属亚晶格间的振动状态相对分布影响Normal散射与Umklapp散射的平衡。掺杂体系呈现降低且各向异性的面内LTC，保留明确的层特征，但受质量无序导致的增强声子-声子散射影响显著；构型和温度共同决定最大热输运方向。

Conclusion: 掺杂可调控热流最大（及最小）传导方向，为新型二维功能材料中的定向热管理提供了可行途径。分析方案具有通用性，可扩展至其他范德华异质结构（van der Waals heterostructures），相关描述符有望用于高通量筛选具有定制热输运特性的层状材料。

Abstract: We investigate the nanoscale mechanisms determining lattice thermal conductivity (LTC) of pristine and W-doped MX$_2$-M$^\prime$X$^\prime_2$ transition metal dichalcogenide heterobilayers from first principles, using the exact solution of the linearised Boltzmann transport equation in both phonon and relaxon bases. Pristine heterobilayers exhibit isotropic in-plane LTC with preserved ordering across temperature. Relaxon analysis identifies descriptors linking LTC to phonon properties such as the phonon group velocity and layer localisation. While systems with lighter atoms generally favour higher LTC, a sufficiently large mass contrast is required to induce layer localisation of the transport-relevant vibrational modes. Further, we show through the thermal viscosity that the relative distribution of vibrational states between metal/non-metal sublattices influences the balance between Normal and Umklapp scattering processes. On the other hand, doped systems exhibit reduced and anisotropic in-plane LTC, retain a well-defined layer character, but are strongly affected by enhanced phonon-phonon scattering due to mass disorder. Notably, we find that both configuration and temperature dictate the direction of maximum thermal transport, which opens the possibility to tune the direction of maximum (and minimum) conductivity via doping in novel 2D functional materials. Thanks to its general formulation, the analysis protocol can be readily extended to other van der Waals heterostructures, and the descriptors may be implemented in high-throughput engines to identify promising layered materials with tailored thermal transport characteristics.

Abstract: Platinum (Pt) is widely used for carrier-lifetime control in silicon power devices, yet the microscopic nonradiative recombination mechanism of the substitutional platinum ($\text{Pt}_\text{Si}$) dopant remains debated. Using first-principles calculations combined with nonradiative multiphonon theory, we systematically investigate the electronic structures and carrier capture dynamics of $\text{Pt}_\text{Si}$. Our results show that both the donor ($+/0$) and acceptor ($0/-$) levels of $\text{Pt}_\text{Si}$ exhibit large capture cross sections for electron and hole carriers, thereby making $\text{Pt}_\text{Si}$ an effective recombination center. Notably, the calculated capture cross sections are sensitive to the symmetry-equivalent defect configurations with different Jahn-Teller distortions. By accounting for two different $D_{2d}$ configurations of neutral $\text{Pt}_\text{Si}$ during transitions properly, our calculated carrier capture cross sections align well with experimental values. This work provides a microscopic picture of the carrier capture processes induced by $\text{Pt}_\text{Si}$ and emphasizes the importance of symmetry-equivalent configurations in defect-assisted nonradiative recombination.

### [22] [Physical properties of transition metal hydride superconductors Mg2TmH6 (Tm = Rh, Pd, Ir, Pt) by first-principles calculations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25626)

Method: 采用第一性原理（first-principles）计算方法，对Mg2TmH6（Tm = Rh, Pd, Ir, Pt）氢化物的结构、储氢潜力、电子性质、弹性与力学性质、热物理性质、超导性质及光学性质进行全面的从头算（ab initio）研究。

Abstract: In this work, a comprehensive first-principles investigation of the structural, hydrogen storage potential, electronic, elastic, mechanical, thermophysical, superconducting, and optical properties of Mg2TmH6 (Tm = Rh, Pd, Ir, Pt) hydrides is presented. ### [23] [Spin-Axis-Layer Locking for Intrinsic Bipolar Altermagnetic Semiconductors: Proof-of-Concept in Bilayer CuBr2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25658)
*Wei Ma,Dengpan Ma,Zhiheng Lv,Zhifeng Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种自旋-轴-层锁定（spin-axis-layer locking, SALL）范式，通过将两个准一维铁磁单层以90度扭转堆叠，构建出本征双极性交变磁半导体（BAMS），实现了无需外加应变和谷极化的电场可控自旋与磁亚晶格自由度操控，并在CuBr2单层体系中通过第一性原理计算验证了其鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有双极性交变磁半导体（bipolar altermagnetic semiconductor, BAMS）系统需要外部应变（external strain）和显著的谷极化（valley polarization）才能实现栅极可调开关，限制了其多功能与低功耗自旋电子学（spintronics）应用的发展。因此，亟需一种普适且无应变的策略来实现电场对自旋和磁亚晶格自由度的控制。

Method: 提出自旋-轴-层锁定（spin-axis-layer locking, SALL）范式：将两个准一维铁磁（ferromagnetic）单层以90度扭转堆叠形成双层结构，重构出交变磁（altermagnetic）对称性，从而产生本征的BAMS态。通过合成CuBr2单层作为概念验证，并采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）进行理论验证。

Result: 计算表明，CuBr2双层体系呈现出鲁棒的BAMS态；静电门控（electrostatic gating）可实现载流子类型、自旋和活性层的同步可逆切换，产生全自旋极化的轴向电荷电流（axial charge current）和方向可控的纯自旋电流（pure spin current），且电荷-自旋转换效率接近单位一（near-unity）。

Conclusion: SALL模型建立了一种普适且无需应变（strain-independent）的策略，为先进的全电控交变磁器件（all-electrical altermagnetic devices）提供了设计基础。

Abstract: Electrical control of spin and magnetic sublattice degrees of freedom is essential for multifunctional and low-power spintronic devices. Bipolar altermagnetic semiconductors (BAMSs)-characterized by opposite spin polarizations at the valence and conduction band edges-offer such control, yet known systems require external strain and sizable valley polarization for gate-tunable switching. Here, we propose a universal spin-axis-layer locking (SALL) paradigm to overcome these limitations. By stacking two quasi-1D ferromagnetic monolayers with a 90 degrees twist, the bilayer reconstructs altermagnetic symmetry, yielding an intrinsic BAMS state where carrier spin is locked to specific layers and transport directions. Using synthesized CuBr2 monolayers as proof-of-concept, we demonstrate via first-principles calculations a robust BAMS state. Electrostatic gating enables simultaneous, reversible switching of carrier type, spin, and active layer, generating fully spin-polarized axial charge currents and directionally controllable pure spin currents with near-unity charge-to-spin conversion efficiency. This SALL model establishes a versatile, strain-independent strategy for advanced all-electrical altermagnetic devices.

Conclusion: 改善电极与电解液之间的相容性对于提升该体系的电化学性能至关重要。

Abstract: This study investigates the lithium conversion behavior of a hydrogen storage material based on vanadium oxide added magnesium hydride. To understand the chemical interaction between vanadium oxide and magnesium hydride, detailed X ray diffraction and X ray photoelectron spectroscopy analyses were performed on ball milled composites with varying compositions. The results confirm the formation of a combined magnesium vanadium oxide with a rock salt structure, indicating strong chemical interaction between the components. It is further shown that the presence of a small amount of this oxide additive significantly influences the lithium reaction with magnesium hydride, leading to a high initial discharge capacity and limited recharge capacity in lithium ion coin cells. Post use analyses confirm the presence of magnesium hydride, suggesting that volume expansion is not responsible for the observed irreversibility. Electrochemical impedance spectroscopy using differential function of relaxation times indicates that electrolyte degradation is not a major issue. Instead, slow charge transfer processes are identified as the limiting factor, and these are sensitive to the composition of the additive. These findings highlight that improving electrode and electrolyte compatibility is essential for enhancing performance in this system.

### [25] [Predicting challenging phase transitions with Bayesian active learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25756)
*Lorenzo Bastonero,Gabriel Joalland,Chiara Cignarella,Lorenzo Monacelli,Nicola Marzari*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料的热力学行为决定其微观性质与宏观性能，但强非谐效应（anharmonic effects）使得精确预测晶体热力学成为计算方法的重大挑战，因为需要大量采样势能面（potential energy surface）。

Method: 提出一种在线贝叶斯框架（on-the-fly Bayesian framework），结合随机自洽谐近似（stochastic self-consistent harmonic approximation, SSCHA），用于学习第一性原理（first-principles）原子间势（interatomic potentials），仅需数十至数百个原子构型（atomic configurations）进行训练。

Result: 在Li₂O、α-CsPbI₃和δ-CsPbI₃体系上分别仅需44、256和50次总能计算（total-energy calculations）；成功捕捉CsPbI₃相图，准确高效地预测其自发降解为不吸光黄色相（non-absorbing yellow phase）的转变温度（transition temperature）。

Conclusion: 该方法为在真实条件下加速材料工程（accelerated materials engineering）开辟了新路径，可广泛应用于固态电池（solid-state batteries）、光电器件（optoelectronic devices）和忆阻器（memristors）等领域。

Abstract: Materials underpin modern technologies, from energy harvesting, storage, and conversion to information and communication technologies. Their functionality is often governed by the interplay between competing phases, as thermodynamic behavior shapes microscopic properties and ultimately determines technological performance; for instance, the light absorption of inorganic metal-halide perovskites in solar cells. Accurately predicting crystal thermodynamics, however, remains a major challenge for computational approaches because strong anharmonic effects require extensive sampling of the potential energy surface. Here, we present an on-the-fly Bayesian framework, combined with the stochastic self-consistent harmonic approximation, for learning first-principles interatomic potentials. This approach enables the prediction of thermodynamic properties over a broad temperature range with first-principles accuracy while requiring training on only a few tens to a few hundreds of atomic configurations. To demonstrate its power, we investigate the thermodynamic and dynamical properties of Li$_2$O, $α$-CsPbI$_3$, and $δ$-CsPbI$_3$, requiring only 44, 256, and 50 total-energy calculations, respectively. Notably, we show that this framework accurately captures the phase diagram of CsPbI$_3$, which explains its spontaneous degradation into the non-absorbing yellow phase, predicting the transition temperature with remarkable accuracy and efficiency. More broadly, the method presented opens a novel route toward accelerated materials engineering under realistic conditions for a wide range of technologically relevant applications, including solid-state batteries, optoelectronic devices, and memristors.

### [26] [Global DIC-based sample-detector geometry refinement for accurate EBSD indexing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25869)
*Claire Griesbach,Dennis M. Kochmann*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于数字图像相关（DIC）的几何精炼方法，用于电子背散射衍射（EBSD）中样品-探测器几何参数的全局校准，通过解耦局部取向变化与全局几何效应，提升了取向一致性并增强了伪对称变体的区分能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子背散射衍射（EBSD）是表征晶体微结构的强大工具，但其取向精度和应用于挑战性材料的关键障碍在于样品-探测器几何（sample-detector geometry）的正确校准。现有方法多聚焦于图案中心（pattern center）的校准，但图案中心仅定义了部分几何参数，完整的几何校准问题尚未解决。

Method: 提出一种基于数字图像相关（digital image correlation, DIC）的几何精炼方法，通过计算与全局几何参数误差相关的全图一致模拟-实验图案偏移（map-wide simulated-to-experimental pattern shifts），有效解耦了局部取向变化与全局几何效应，从而获得单一的、全图一致的样品-探测器几何参数，同时精炼图案中心和样品/探测器角度。

Result: 以单晶硅和钛酸钡（一种具有六种伪对称变体的材料）为模型材料，该方法相较于Nelder-Mead和差分进化（Differential Evolution）优化策略，展现了更优的全图取向一致性（map-wide orientation consistency）以及对伪对称变体（pseudosymmetric variants）的更稳健区分能力。

Conclusion: 该DIC-based几何精炼方法能够有效校准完整的样品-探测器几何参数，显著提升EBSD取向测量的精度和可靠性，尤其适用于存在伪对称性的挑战性材料。

Abstract: Electron backscatter diffraction is a powerful tool for mapping crystallographic microstructures. However, the primary crux to improving orientation accuracy and applying the technique to challenging materials lies in the correct calibration of the sample-detector geometry. Many approaches have aimed at overcoming this barrier through various pattern center calibration strategies, but the pattern center only defines part of the sample-detector geometry. Here, we present a DIC-based geometry refinement method that obtains a single map-consistent sample-detector geometry, refining both the pattern center and sample/detector angles. We effectively decouple the local orientation changes from the global geometry effects on the Kikuchi patterns by calculating the consistent map-wide simulated-to-experimental pattern shifts associated with global geometry parameter errors. Using single-crystal silicon and barium titanate (a material possessing six pseudosymmetric variants) as model materials, we demonstrate improved map-wide orientation consistency and more robust discrimination of pseudosymmetric variants than the Nelder-Mead and Differential Evolution optimization strategies.

</details>


### [27] [Structure Prediction and Bonding Analysis of B$_{18}$Ag$_2$ Clusters Featuring Double-Ring Motifs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25908)
*Peter Ludwig Rodríguez-Kessler*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过密度泛函理论（DFT）与全局优化技术，发现B18Ag₂团簇的全局极小结构为弯曲双环结构，Ag原子作为轴向稳定中心，硼骨架内部的σ离域电子主导结构稳定性，Ag-B相互作用较弱且以静电成分为主。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究银掺杂硼团簇B18Ag₂的结构稳定性、电子结构与成键特性，揭示贵金属掺杂在稳定扩展硼纳米结构中的作用机制。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（DFT）结合盆地跳跃（basin-hopping）全局优化技术进行结构搜索，并利用电子局域化函数（ELF）、约化密度梯度（RDG）和分子静电势（MEP）等实空间成键分析方法进行表征。

Result: 全局极小结构为弯曲双环结构，由两个堆叠的B₉环经Ag原子对称稳定；UV-Vis吸收光谱在近红外区有弱跃迁，在可见及近紫外区有强吸收带；电荷分析显示中等程度的电子从Ag向硼骨架转移；成键以硼骨架上的σ离域为主导，Ag-B相互作用弱、非定向且主要为静电性；双环结构中的连续环形电子离域表明具有芳香性（aromatic-like）特征。

Conclusion: B18Ag₂是一种银稳定的硼双环团簇，全局电子离域主导结构稳定性，Ag原子作为轴向稳定中心调控电子结构；该工作为理解贵金属掺杂在稳定扩展硼纳米结构中的作用提供了新见解。

Abstract: The structural stability, electronic structure, and bonding characteristics of the silver-doped boron cluster B18Ag2 were investigated using density functional theory (DFT) combined with global optimization techniques. Basin-hopping searches identify a bent double-ring structure as the global minimum, consisting of two stacked B9 rings symmetrically stabilized by Ag atoms located above and below the boron framework. The UV-Vis absorption spectrum exhibits weak transitions in the near-infrared region and intense bands in the visible and near-ultraviolet regions, reflecting delocalized electronic excitations within the boron framework. Charge analysis indicates moderate electron redistribution from Ag atoms to the boron scaffold. Real-space bonding analyses based on the electron localization function (ELF), reduced density gradient (RDG), and molecular electrostatic potential (MEP) reveal that bonding is dominated by {$σ$}-delocalization over the boron skeleton, while Ag-B interactions are weak, non-directional, and primarily electrostatic. The continuous annular electron delocalization within the double-ring structure suggests an aromatic-like character. These findings establish B18Ag2 as a silver-stabilized boron double-ring cluster in which global electron delocalization governs structural stability, while Ag atoms act as axial stabilizing centers that modulate the electronic structure. This work provides new insight into the role of coinage-metal doping in stabilizing extended boron nanostructures.

### [28] [Application of a Mixture of Experts-based Foundation Model to the GlueX DIRC Detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24775)
*Cristiano Fanelli,James Giroux,Cole Granger,Justin Stevens*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于混合专家模型（Mixture-of-Experts, MoE）的基础模型（foundation model），应用于Jefferson Lab的GlueX DIRC探测器，统一实现了快速模拟、粒子识别和切伦科夫光子噪声过滤三项任务，性能优于或持平于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GlueX DIRC分析依赖于碎片化的任务专用流水线（task-specific pipelines），缺乏统一的处理框架，导致开发与维护成本高、泛化能力受限。

Method: 采用共享的Transformer骨干网络（shared transformer backbone）作为统一架构，通过混合专家模型（Mixture-of-Experts）支持类别条件生成（class-conditional generation），对低层级探测器输入进行逐击中自回归生成（hit-by-hit autoregressive generation），并利用分离的空间与时间词表（split spatial and temporal vocabularies）结合连续运动学条件（continuous kinematic conditioning）实现建模。

Result: 在全运动学相空间（kinematic phase space）内，该方法在快速模拟、粒子识别和噪声过滤三项任务上均达到与标准几何重建（geometrical reconstruction）和先前深度学习方法相当或更优的性能，且无需修改模型架构即可直接迁移至该探测器。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了基础模型框架可作为现有任务专用模型的实用且可扩展的替代方案，为GlueX DIRC分析提供统一、高效的解决方案。

Abstract: We present a Mixture-of-Experts-based foundation model applied to the GlueX DIRC detector at Jefferson Lab, demonstrating its utility as a unified framework for fast simulation, particle identification, and hit-level noise filtering of Cherenkov photons. By leveraging a single shared transformer backbone across all tasks, the approach eliminates the fragmentation of task-specific pipelines while maintaining competitive-and in several cases superior-performance relative to established methods. The model operates directly on low-level detector inputs, performing hit-by-hit autoregressive generation over split spatial and temporal vocabularies with continuous kinematic conditioning, and supports class-conditional generation of pions and kaons through its Mixture-of-Experts architecture. We benchmark against the standard geometrical reconstruction and prior deep learning methods across the full kinematic phase space of the GlueX DIRC, demonstrating that the foundation model framework transfers effectively to this detector without architectural modification. This work positions the foundation model as a practical and scalable alternative to the suite of task-specific models currently proposed for GlueX DIRC analysis.

### [29] [Theory of Anderson localization on the hyperbolic plane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24917)
*Alexander Altland,Tobias Micklitz,Devasheesh Sharma,Maksimilian Usoltcev,Carolin Wille*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文针对二维双曲平面（ℍ²）这一尺度依赖有效维度的系统，发展了一套统一框架，通过尺度依赖曲率与电导率的双参数流，推导出一条延伸的临界线，分离金属相与绝缘相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维双曲平面（ℍ²）的维度随尺度变化——短距离表现为二维平面，大尺度下有效维度趋于无穷，这为研究量子相变（quantum phase transition）特别是安德森转变（Anderson transition）提供了独特范式。此前的研究将短距离与大尺度分开处理，缺乏统一框架。

Method: 将先前分开处理短距离与大尺度的方法推广，建立了一套统一的理论框架，在低维与高维安德森局域化（Anderson localization）原理之间进行插值，并推导出由尺度依赖曲率（scale-dependent curvature）与电导率（conductivity）张成的双参数流（two-parameter flow）。

Result: 得到了一个双参数流方程，在尺度依赖曲率（决定系统有效维度）与电导率所张成的参数平面上，存在一条延伸的临界线（extended critical line），将金属相与绝缘相分开。

Conclusion: 该统一框架成功刻画了双曲平面中因维度随尺度变化而产生的金属-绝缘体转变（metal-insulator transition），为理解变维度系统中的安德森局域化提供了新视角。

Abstract: The two-dimensional hyperbolic plane, $\mathbb{H}^2$, is an unusual system in that dimensionality changes with scale: locally two-dimensional and planar at short distances, but effectively infinite-dimensional at large scales, it provides an interesting paradigm for the study of (quantum) phase transitions, notably the disorder-driven Anderson transition. Generalizing previous work, which treated short and large distance scales separately, we develop a unified framework interpolating between the principles of low- and high-dimensional Anderson localization. As a main result, we derive a two-parameter flow in a plane spanned by scale-dependent curvature (setting the system's effective dimensionality) and conductivity, with an extended critical line separating metallic and insulating phases.

</details>


### [30] [Training cell stress patterns in 3D cellular packings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25439)
*Shabeeb Ameen,Tao Zhang,J. M. Schwarz*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过三维顶点模型（vertex model）展示了可重构细胞组织（reconfigurable cellular tissue）能够通过对比学习算法（contrastive learning algorithm）训练以实现预设的细胞应力模式（cell stress patterns），揭示了力学状态、容量与训练协议三者共同支配的可学习性（learnability）相图，并指出组织不仅可作为自适应材料，还可作为非传统AI平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统模式学习通常与在固定架构上更新参数的系统（如神经网络）相关联，通过连续优化进行学习。本文旨在探索模式学习是否也能在同时演化力学参数与网络拓扑的可重构细胞组织中涌现，从而拓展学习的物理实现形式。

Method: 采用三维顶点模型（three-dimensional vertex model）模拟细胞堆积（cellular packings），通过对比学习算法（contrastive learning algorithm）更新隐藏细胞的形状指数（hidden-cell shape indices），以实现对预设细胞应力模式的训练。

Result: 学习本质上是集体性的（collective），需要系统范围的协调参数调整；组织的刚性（rigidity）控制探索-利用权衡（exploration-exploitation tradeoff）：流体状区域通过细胞重排增强探索，刚性区域约束动力学偏向利用；重排引入不连续学习动力学，使系统可在代价函数景观的不同局部极小值间跃迁；目标细胞比例或约束负载（constraint load）增加会导致学习变慢、更异质化且更依赖稀有重排；顺序训练相比并行训练更鲁棒但通常更慢。

Conclusion: 研究提出了一个由约束负载、细胞堆积刚性和训练协议支配的学习相图（learning phase diagram）。通过实现局部内部状态的可训练性，该工作将组织定位为不仅是自适应材料，更是非传统AI平台（nonconventional AI platforms）。

Abstract: The task of learning patterns is typically associated with systems that update parameters on fixed architectures, such as neural networks, where learning proceeds through continuous optimization. Here, we demonstrate that pattern learning can also emerge in reconfigurable cellular tissue, where both mechanical parameters and network topology evolve. Using a three-dimensional vertex model, we show that cellular packings can be trained to realize prescribed cell stress patterns through a contrastive learning algorithm to update hidden-cell shape indices. We find that learning is intrinsically collective, requiring coordinated, system-wide parameter adjustments, with learnability governed by an interplay between mechanical state, capacity, and training protocol. In particular, the rigidity of the tissue controls an effective exploration-exploitation tradeoff: fluid-like regimes enhance exploration through cellular rearrangements, while rigid regimes constrain dynamics and favor exploitation of existing configurations. These rearrangements introduce discontinuous learning dynamics, enabling the system to transition between distinct local minima in the cost function landscape. As the ratio of target cells to the total number cells in the packing or constraint load increases, learning becomes slower, more heterogeneous, and increasingly dependent on rare rearrangements that allow escape from geometrically constrained states. Finally, training cells in sequence, in contrast to parallel protocols, provides an alternative route that can be more robust but generally takes longer to train for the constraint loads studied. These results suggest a learning phase diagram governed by constraint load, cell packing rigidity, and training protocol. By enabling the training of localized internal states, this work positions tissues not only as adaptive materials, but as nonconventional AI platforms.

</details>


### [31] [Excluded volume and molecular field in the Lennard-Jones fluid: a modified first-order perturbation theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25882)
*A. Trokhymchuk,V. Hordiichuk,R. Melnyk,I. Nezbeda*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过模拟方法系统评估了一种非经典一阶微扰理论（first-order perturbation theory），该理论将Lennard-Jones流体的相互作用分解为短程参考系统和长程微扰部分。结果表明，基于作用范围（range-based）的分解使微扰项在小范围超临界区域内成为近平均场（near-mean-field）量，该理论成功的关键在于参考系统的物理内容及其状态依赖性的自洽处理，而非形式上的展开截断阶数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lennard-Jones流体的状态方程（equation of state）及热力学长期以来是流体统计理论（statistical theory of fluids）的基准问题。一阶微扰理论因其Helmholtz自由能修正具有精确统计力学表达式而占有特殊地位，因此有必要系统评估并改进该理论的表现。

Method: 采用基于模拟（simulation-based）的系统评估方法，测试一种非经典一阶微扰理论。该理论将参考系统定义为整个短程相互作用部分，而微扰局限于剩余的长程尾部，通过作用范围分解将微扰贡献转化为小量、光滑、近平均场的量，并自洽保留其密度和温度导数。

Result: 该一阶微扰理论在广泛的超临界热力学区域上，微扰贡献变为小量、光滑且近平均场。当密度和温度导数被一致保留时，所得状态方程对高精度参考数据具有极佳的复现能力。

Conclusion: 一阶微扰理论的成功主要由参考系统的物理内容及其状态依赖性的自洽处理所决定，而非形式上的截断阶数（truncation order）。

Abstract: The equation of state and, more generally, the thermodynamics of the Lennard-Jones fluid have long served as a benchmark problem in the statistical theory of fluids. Among available theoretical approaches, first-order perturbation theory occupies a special position: only at this level does the correction to the Helmholtz free energy admit an exact statistical-mechanical expression. In this work, we present a systematic, simulation-based assessment of a non-classical first-order perturbation theory in which the reference system incorporates the entire short-range part of the interaction, while the perturbation is confined to the remaining long-range tail. We show that this range-based decomposition transforms the perturbation contribution into a small, smoothly varying, near-mean-field quantity over a broad supercritical thermodynamic domain. When its density and temperature derivatives are consistently retained, the resulting equation of state reproduces high-accuracy reference data with excellent fidelity. The results demonstrate that the success of first-order perturbation theory is governed primarily by the physical content of the reference system and by the consistent treatment of its state dependence, rather than by the formal truncation order of the expansion.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: PINN架构因其天然支持微分条件嵌入的特性，在微分几何问题求解中具有良好适配性。将几何泛函极小化转化为损失函数优化的策略，为几何计算提供了新的AI驱动路径。

This contribution to the Recent Progress in Computational String Geometry workshop proceedings introduces the PINN architecture defining principles, motivates how they are well suited for problems in differential geometry, and demonstrates their use via summaries of three works at this intersection.

Method: 采用残差方法（residual-based approach）构建后验误差估计子，并证明其可靠性与效率性。随后将这些估计子集成到自适应网格加密（adaptive mesh refinement）策略中。

Abstract: This paper introduces a novel a posteriori error estimation framework for the enriched Galerkin (EG) finite element method applied to linear parabolic equations. In this work, we prove reliability and efficiency using the residual-based approach. Furthermore, we integrate these error estimators into an adaptive mesh refinement strategy, demonstrating their effectiveness in achieving efficient and reliable error control through several numerical examples. The proposed approach provides a significant advancement in the mathematical foundation and practical applicability of the EG method for time-dependent problems.

### [34] [SPARSE -- Efficient High-Resolution SEM Imaging of Rare Microstructural Features Across Large Areas by Selective Rescanning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24769)
*Tom Reclik,Jan Gerlach,Maximilian A. Wollenweber,Yannis P. Korkolis,Sandra Korte-Kerzel,Ulrich Kerzel*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个开源 Python 框架，通过两阶段扫描策略（快速粗扫识别感兴趣区域 + 选择性精扫）显著降低扫描电子显微镜（SEM）中罕见微结构特征的表征时间，在 DP800 双相钢的损伤检测中验证了 99% 的检测率与约 42% 的时间节省。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在扫描电子显微镜（SEM）中表征罕见微结构特征需要大面积高分辨率成像，导致采集时间过长，成为实际应用中的瓶颈。

Method: 采用两阶段扫描策略：第一阶段快速扫描识别感兴趣区域（ROI），第二阶段对 ROI 使用适合定量分析的成像参数进行选择性重扫描；定义了通用显微镜接口（microscope interface）和模块化检测接口（modular detection interface），支持不同显微镜平台和检测方法的适配；扫描、检测与重扫描通过独立进程并行化，且仅通过队列（queue）通信，避免共享可变状态和显式同步。

Result: 在 Tescan Clara SEM 上对 DP800 双相钢的损伤检测进行验证：代表性配置下，检测率达 99% 时，采集时间约为传统方式的 58%；检测率为 95% 时，采集时间降至传统方式的 19%。这些时间节省是基于扫描像素比例估算的下界。

Conclusion: 所提出的开源框架通过并行化两阶段扫描策略，在不牺牲检测率的前提下显著降低 SEM 采集时间，具有良好的平台适应性和模块化扩展能力。

Abstract: Characterisation of rare microstructural features in scanning electron microscopy (SEM) requires imaging large areas at high resolution. This leads to prohibitively long acquisition times. We present an open-source Python framework that addresses this bottleneck through a two-stage approach: a fast scan identifies regions of interest, which are then selectively rescanned with imaging parameters suitable for quantitative analysis. The framework defines a generic microscope interface and a modular detection interface, allowing adaptation to different microscope platforms and detection methods. Scanning, detection, and rescanning are parallelized using separate processes, ensuring that computation time does not extend acquisition time. The two processes communicate exclusively through queues, avoiding shared mutable state and eliminating the need for explicit synchronization. We validate the framework on damage detection in dual-phase DP800 steel using a Tescan Clara SEM. For a representative configuration a detection rate of 99 % is achieved at approximately 58 % of the conventional acquisition time. At 95 % detection rate, acquisition time drops to 19 %. These time savings estimates represent lower bounds based on the ratio of scanned pixels. The complete implementation will be made available upon publication and upon request during peer-review.

### [35] [Hyperstatistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24783)
*Lucas Squillante,Samuel M. Soares,Constantino Tsallis,Mariano de Souza*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为超统计（hyperstatistics）的通用框架，用于处理系统中局域违反玻尔兹曼-吉布斯统计（Boltzmann-Gibbs statistics）的复杂系统。该方法保持了非可加q熵的凹性，推导出了q-广义玻尔兹曼因子的解析闭式表达式，并通过多组实验数据验证了其适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在复杂系统中，传统的玻尔兹曼-吉布斯统计（Boltzmann-Gibbs statistics）在系统的某些区域失效，因此需要建立一种更一般的统计力学框架来描述这类系统。

Method: 作者提出超统计（hyperstatistics）方法，考虑了均匀、γ、对数正态（Log-normal）、F以及q-γ五种概率分布函数，推导出q-广义玻尔兹曼因子（$q$-generalized Boltzmann factor）$B_q$的解析闭式表达式。

Result: 对于所有被研究的分布函数，$B_q$均约化为q-指数型函数（$q$-exponential-type function）。实验验证显示，该方法成功描述了电容器放电、闭环低温泵中$^4$He线的压力衰减、LHC中p-Pb碰撞的中间快度数据以及湍流系统中的加速度分布。此外，利用q-γ分布函数推导出了类幂律介电响应。

Conclusion: 超统计（hyperstatistics）为具有内在非玻尔兹曼-吉布斯统计（non-Boltzmann-Gibbsian statistics）的系统提供了一种通用的理论框架，可广泛适用于自然界中各类复杂系统。

Abstract: We propose a general approach, named by us hyperstatistics, to treat complex systems, in which Boltzmann-Gibbs statistics breaks down in domains of the system. Hyperstatistics preserves the concavity of nonadditive $q$-entropy. We obtain analytical closed-form expressions for the here proposed $q$-generalized Boltzmann factor $B_q$ considering uniform, $γ$, Log-normal, F, and the $q$-$γ$ probability distribution functions. Remarkably, for all investigated distribution functions, $B_q$ reduces to a $q$-exponential-type function. To demonstrate the applicability of hyperstatistics, we use a table top experiment of the discharge of a capacitor considering $γ$-distributed relaxation times, the pressure decay over time associated with the pumping of $^4$He lines of a closed cycle cryostat, midrapidity data for $p$-Pb collisions at the LHC, as well as data set for acceleration distribution in turbulent systems. Furthermore, we deduce the power-law-like dielectric response using the $q$-$γ$-distribution function. Our proposal is applicable to systems with inherent non-Boltzmann-Gibbsian statistics in domains of the system.

</details>


### [36] [Conductance fluctuations in random resistor networks with hyperuniform disorder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24789)
*Bikram Pal*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究具有超均匀键无序（hyperuniform bond disorder）的随机电阻网络中的电导涨落（conductance fluctuations），论证尽管超均匀无序在键密度涨落上表现出抑制效应，但电导涨落仍以 $L^{-d/2}$ 标度，并未被抑制，并给出了二维（$d=2$）数值结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超均匀无序（hyperuniform disorder）中局域键密度的涨落被显著抑制（标度为 $V^{-a}, a>1/2$），而局域电导与键密度成正比，因此自然猜想电导涨落也会被抑制。本文旨在检验这一直觉是否正确。

Method: 通过理论论证，指出在超均匀键无序的随机电阻网络（random resistor network）中，电导涨落的标度行为为 $L^{-d/2}$，与无序是否超均匀无关；并在二维（$d=2$）情况下展示数值模拟结果以支持该论点。

Result: 结果表明，尽管超均匀无序抑制了键密度的涨落，电导涨落并未被抑制，其标度形式仍为 $L^{-d/2}$，与常规无序情形一致。

Conclusion: 超均匀无序对键密度涨落的抑制效应并不会传递到电导涨落上；电导涨落保留了标准的标度行为，这修正了基于局域平均电导与键浓度成正比关系的直观预期。

Abstract: We study conductance fluctuations in random resistor networks with hyperuniform bond disorder, where the fluctuations of the number of bonds present in a test volume $V$ scale as $V^{-a}$ with $a > 1/2$. Since small changes in the concentration of bonds present in a local region give rise to a proportionate increase in the locally averaged conductance, one may expect that in hyperuniform disorder, conductance fluctuations will also show suppressed fluctuations. We argue that this is not the case: conductance fluctuations scale as $L^{-d/2}$ for a sampling size $L$. We show numerical results for $d=2$.

</details>


### [37] [Thermoinformational State Construction: Generative Energies, Entropies, and H-Theorem Consistency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24802)
*George-Rafael Domenikos,Lock Yue Chew,Victoria Leong*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 提出一种从任意数据系统的微观态测量数据出发，通过构建数据驱动的能量函数和熵函数，系统性地赋予该系统热力学结构（thermodynamic structure）的构造性框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在统计物理、机器学习等领域，数据和系统常以微观态（microstate）形式呈现，但缺乏明确的宏观热力学描述。现有方法依赖先验设定或全局约束的极大熵（maximum entropy, MaxEnt）方法，可能掩盖势垒（barrier）与共存结构（coexistence structure）等关键特征。因此需要一种普适的、从微观数据出发到热力学一致宏观描述的建构路径。

Method: 首先从经验分布出发，通过拟合玻尔兹曼（Boltzmann）类模型推断数据驱动的能量函数；然后将经验分布投影到该能量坐标上，求解一个逆极大熵问题，学习一个严格凹的迹形式熵泛函（strictly concave trace-form entropy functional），其最大化者在小约束集下复现观测的能量空间直方图。

Result: 在简谐振子（harmonic well）示例中恢复了经典平衡极限（equilibrium limit）；在双阱势（double-well）示例中，全局约束的MaxEnt代理方法遮蔽了势垒与共存结构，而本方法成功揭示了这些特征。能量和熵以耦合的、系统特异的方式定义后，内能（internal energy）、熵-能关系 S(U) 以及热信息温度（thermoinformational temperature）T^{-1}=dS/dU 沿可容许态族一致导出。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一条从微观态数据到热力学一致宏观描述符的原则性路径，其优化的熵函数与经验系统相匹配，适用于单峰与多峰等典型系统。

Abstract: We introduce a constructive framework for assigning thermodynamic structure to an arbitrary data system from its measured microstates. Starting from an empirical distribution over configurations, we first infer a data-driven energy function by fitting a Boltzmann-type model to the observed statistics, thereby defining an energy axis that is intrinsic to the system. We then push the empirical distribution onto this energy coordinate and pose an inverse maximum-entropy problem: we learn a strictly concave trace-form entropy functional whose maximizer, under a small set of constraints extracted from the data, reproduces the observed energy-space histogram. With energy and entropy defined in this coupled, system-specific manner, macroscopic variables such as internal energy, an entropy-energy relation S(U), and a thermoinformational temperature T^(-1)= dS/dU follow consistently along admissible families of states. We demonstrate the construction on canonical unimodal and multimodal examples, including a harmonic well (recovering the classical equilibrium limit up to gauge) and a bistable double-well where global-constraint MaxEnt surrogates can obscure barrier and coexistence structure. The resulting formulation provides a principled route from microstate data to thermodynamically consistent macroscopic descriptors, with an optimized entropy matched to the empirical system.

</details>


### [38] [On the Mathematics of Information-Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24948)
*Dallin Fisher,Qi-Jun Hong*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文验证了asdf方法——一个从分子构型（molecular configurations）计算热力学熵（thermodynamic entropy）的信息论框架。通过解析证明，该框架在经典理想气体和一维谐振子系统中重建了精确的热力学熵，建立了与经典统计力学（statistical mechanics）之间的一致性，并支持将热力学熵解释为一种几何上编码于微观态映射之间的信息度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的热力学熵计算方法在处理复杂凝聚相（complex condensed phases）时面临挑战，亟需一种既能从分子构型直接计算熵、又具有严格理论基础的框架。asdf方法作为一种基于信息论（information-theoretic）的熵估计框架，需要在解析可解的系统上得到验证，以确认其与经典统计力学的一致性。

Method: asdf方法将熵估计重新表述为两个去相关微观态（decorrelated microstates）之间残差映射分布（residual mapping distribution）的香农熵（Shannon entropy）。对于具有已知闭式解（closed-form Hamiltonians）的系统（经典理想气体和一维谐振子），通过残差映射对象的可压缩性（compressibility）计算熵，并与正则配分函数（canonical partition function）导出的系综熵（ensemble entropy）进行对比。

Result: 解析结果表明：在经典理想气体和一维谐振子系统中，残差映射对象的可压缩性导出的熵精确等于正则配分函数导出的热力学熵；残差映射对象关于去相关微观态的条件熵（conditional entropy）与系综熵一致。该结果建立了asdf形式体系与经典统计力学之间的一致性。

Conclusion: asdf框架与经典统计力学在解析可解系统上一致；该框架可推广至相互作用哈密顿量（interacting Hamiltonians）；研究支持将热力学熵解释为一种几何上编码于微观态映射之间的信息度量（information measure），为该框架应用于复杂凝聚相提供了理论动机。

Abstract: We present a validation of the asdf method, an information-theoretic framework for computing thermodynamic entropy from molecular configurations. The method reformulates entropy estimation as the Shannon entropy of a residual mapping distribution defined between two decorrelated microstates. We demonstrate analytically that for the closed-form Hamiltonians with known solutions, the classical ideal gas and the one-dimensional harmonic oscillator's entropy obtained from the compressibility of the residual mapping object reproduces the exact thermodynamic entropy. In each case, the conditional entropy of the residual mapping object with respect to an uncorrelated microstate is shown to coincide with the ensemble entropy derived from the canonical partition function. These results establish consistency between the asdf formalism and classical statistical mechanics for analytically solvable systems. We further discuss how the framework generalizes to interacting Hamiltonians. The analysis supports the interpretation of thermodynamic entropy as an information measure encoded geometrically in inter-microstate mappings and motivates application of the method to complex condensed phases.

</details>


### [39] [Statistical mechanics in continuous space with tensor network methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25060)
*Gunhee Park,Tomislav Begušić,Si-Jing Du,Johnnie Gray,Garnet Kin-Lic Chan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文将张量网络（tensor network）方法从统计力学中的晶格模型扩展到连续空间中的相互作用粒子系统，通过实空间离散化和基于单元的粗粒化方案构建有效晶格模型，并将其配分函数表示为张量网络进行边界收缩计算。在二维硬圆盘问题上验证了该方法相比蒙特卡罗模拟的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 张量网络方法在统计力学的晶格模型配分函数计算中已非常成熟，但传统上仅限于晶格模型（lattice models）。本文旨在将该方法的应用范围扩展至连续空间中的相互作用粒子系统（interacting particle systems in continuous space）。

Method: 通过实空间离散化（real-space discretization）结合基于单元的粗粒化方案（cell-based coarse-graining scheme），构造一个显式保持空间局域性（spatial locality）的有效晶格模型，将其配分函数表示为张量网络（tensor network, TN），并通过边界收缩（boundary contraction）计算热力学量。

Result: 将所提出的张量网络框架应用于二维硬圆盘（hard-disk）问题，验证了该方法的有效性，并展示了张量网络公式相比现有蒙特卡罗模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）的优势。

Conclusion: 张量网络方法可成功从离散晶格模型扩展至连续空间粒子系统，并在硬圆盘问题上表现出优于传统蒙特卡罗模拟的性能，为统计力学中连续系统的热力学计算提供了新工具。

Abstract: Tensor network (TN) methods are well established for computing partition functions in statistical mechanics, though this use has traditionally been limited to lattice models. We extend the scope of TN methodology to interacting particle systems in continuous space. Through a real-space discretization combined with a cell-based coarse-graining scheme, we formulate an effective lattice model that explicitly preserves spatial locality. The partition function of this model is represented as a TN, and the thermodynamic quantities are computed via boundary contraction. We apply this framework to the two-dimensional hard-disk problem and demonstrate the strengths of the TN formulation compared to existing Monte Carlo simulations.

### [40] [Markovian thermodynamics of non-Markovian Langevin equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25095)
*Andreas Dechant,Kiyoshi Kanazawa*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非马尔可夫动力学（non-Markovian dynamics）的热力学定义存在熵产生不单调等问题，亟需建立一种自洽且具有单调性保证的热力学形式体系。

Method: 将非马尔可夫广义朗之万方程（generalized Langevin equations）嵌入高维马尔可夫表示（Markovian representation），引入辅助自由度（auxiliary degrees of freedom），在记忆核满足线性及细致平衡（detailed balance）条件下给出显式构造。

Result: 嵌入方式不唯一，但所得马尔可夫系统的热力学量取值唯一；基于马尔可夫表示的熵产生严格随时间单调递增；非马尔可夫熵的表观减少可通过系统与辅助自由度之间的热量和信息交换来识别。

Conclusion: 该工作为非马尔可夫系统提供了热力学一致的熵产生定义，并揭示了非马尔可夫熵减现象背后的物理机制。

Abstract: We develop the thermodynamics of non-Markovian generalized Langevin equations by embedding them in a high-dimensional Markovian representation involving auxiliary degrees of freedom. If the memory is linear and satisfies detailed balance with the noise, we provide an explicit construction of the embedding for non-Markovian dynamics with many degrees of freedom and hydrodynamic interactions. Moreover, while the embedding is generally not unique, we show that it results in unique values of thermodynamic quantities of the Markovian system. This allows us to define the Markovian entropy production of a non-Markovian system, which, in contrast to the definition based directly on the non-Markovian dynamics, is guaranteed to increase monotonically with time. Moreover, the Markovian representation allows us to identify the apparent decrease in the non-Markovian entropy with heat and information exchange between the system and the auxiliary degrees of freedom.

### [41] [Hierarchy of entropy production and thermodynamic trade-off relations in non-Markovian systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25245)
*Ken Funo,Tan Van Vu,Keiji Saito*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过马尔可夫嵌入（Markovian embedding）方法研究非马尔可夫动力学（non-Markovian dynamics）中的熵产生层次结构，证明非马尔可夫系统的熵产率上界高于其嵌入系统，并由此推导出非马尔可夫版本的热力学不确定性关系（thermodynamic uncertainty relation）、速度极限（speed limit）和功率-效率权衡关系（power-efficiency trade-off），揭示记忆可作为热力学资源提升系统性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非马尔可夫动力学中的记忆效应如何改变不可逆性（irreversibility）以及能否被用于改善热力学性能，这一问题尚未得到充分解答。

Method: 采用广义朗之万动力学（generalized Langevin dynamics）的马尔可夫嵌入方法，将浴记忆编码为辅助模式（auxiliary modes），将不可逆耗散归入残余马尔可夫浴（residual Markovian bath），进而比较原始非马尔可夫系统与嵌入系统的熵产生。

Result: 原始非马尔可夫系统的熵产生（entropy production）上界约束嵌入系统的熵产生，建立了马尔可夫嵌入下的熵产生层次结构。基于这一层次结构，推导出非马尔可夫热力学不确定性关系、速度极限和功率-效率权衡。在欠阻尼（underdamped）广义朗之万系统中，结构充分的浴能在熵产生趋近于零时维持有限热流，而普通谱密度下有限功率的卡诺效率（Carnot efficiency）仍不可达。在过阻尼（overdamped）区域，记忆效应可同时降低熵产生和电流涨落，从而提升精度-耗散比（precision-to-dissipation ratio）。

Conclusion: 这些结果为将记忆作为热力学资源加以利用、以及在结构化环境中设计高能效协议提供了定量框架。

Abstract: Non-Markovian dynamics arise when a system is coupled to a bath with finite correlation time, giving rise to memory effects that allow the bath to temporarily store and return excitations. However, how memory modifies irreversibility and whether it can be exploited to improve thermodynamic performance is not well established. We address this question by employing a Markovian embedding of generalized Langevin dynamics, in which bath memory is encoded in auxiliary modes and irreversible dissipation in a residual Markovian bath. Here we show that the entropy production defined for the original non-Markovian system upper bounds that of the embedded system, thereby establishing a hierarchy of entropy production under Markovian embedding. Leveraging this hierarchy, we derive non-Markovian extensions of the thermodynamic uncertainty relation, speed limit, and power-efficiency trade-off. For underdamed generalized Langevin systems, sufficiently structured baths allow finite heat currents at vanishingly small entropy production, whereas Carnot efficiency at finite power remains unattainable for ordinary spectral densities. In the overdamped regime, memory effects can simultaneously reduce entropy production and current fluctuations, thereby enhancing the precision-to-dissipation ratio. We further discuss the extension of the hierarchy to generic bath models and the quantum regime. These results provide a quantitative framework for exploiting memory as a thermodynamic resource and for designing energy-efficient protocols in structured environments.

*Lakshmipriya K,Harssh Karn,Sutapa Roy*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统相分离研究多假设均匀冷却，但实际工业与自然过程中冷却源常处于运动状态，其速度与温度传播速度的耦合效应尚未被充分理解。本文旨在揭示这两种速度尺度如何共同影响相分离的模式与动力学。

Method: 采用修正的Cahn-Hilliard-Cook（卡恩-希利亚德-库克）框架，显式耦合时变温度场与浓度场，并通过数值模拟分析移动冷却源下二元混合物的相分离行为。

Abstract: We investigate phase separation dynamics in a binary mixture subjected to a moving cooling source from which cold temperature fronts propagate radially outward into the mixture. The motion of the source introduces two distinct velocity scales: $v_s$ associated with the translation of the source, and $v$ related to the propagation of the cooling thermal fronts. Competition between the two velocities determines how long a region of the fluid experiences a temperature change, which directly controls phase separation. A modified Cahn Hilliard Cook framework is employed, incorporating explicit coupling between the time-dependent temperature and concentration fields. Our numerical simulation results reveal that the evolving patterns and kinetics strongly depend on both the ratio and absolute magnitudes of these two competing velocities. Same value of $v_s/v$ yields distinctly different patterns for different $v$. The temperature profile delineating spatial regions with local temperatures above and below the demixing temperature controls the shape of the patterns formed. The rich parameter space enables one to engineer desired pattern structures by tuning the two velocities.

### [43] [Spinodal-like scaling behavior after a temperature quench across the first-order phase transition in three-dimensional $q$-state Potts models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25351)
*Andrea Pelissetto,Davide Rossini,Ettore Vicari*
