TL;DR: 本文研究了三维 q 态 Potts 模型（q≥3）在跨一级相变温度淬火时的非平衡旋节线行为，提出了基于平滑液滴成核机制的标度理论，并通过 q=6 模型的数值模拟验证了时间尺度指数发散的旋节线场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解三维 Potts 模型在跨一级相变（first-order transition, FOT）温度淬火时出现的类似旋节线（spinodal-like）的动力学行为，特别是热力学极限下动态相变中的标度规律。

Method: 采用标准淬火协议：将高温热化构型（β_i < β_fo）通过纯弛豫动力学驱动至 FOT 点 β_fo 以上的温度（β > β_fo）；基于平滑液滴（smooth droplet）成核机制推导能量密度的标度形式，并在三维 q=6 Potts 模型中进行数值分析。

Result: 当淬火深度 δ ≡ β/β_fo - 1 足够小时，时间相关能量密度按 ρ = (ln t)^(3/2) δ 标度，并在 ρ = ρ_s > 0 处出现间断；淬火时间尺度 τ 在 δ → 0⁺ 极限下呈指数发散：ln τ ≈ (ρ_s/δ)^(2/3)。三维 q=6 模型的数值结果支持上述旋节线场景。

Conclusion: 三维 Potts 模型跨一级相变淬火中存在旋节线行为，其时间尺度随淬火深度减小而指数增长，且该行为可通过平滑液滴成核机制得到解释。

Abstract: We study the out-of-equilibrium spinodal-like behavior of three-dimensional (3D) $q$-state Potts models (for $q\ge 3$), observed when the temperature is quenched across the first-order transition (FOT) point $β_{\rm fo}=T_{\rm fo}^{-1}$. We consider a standard quench protocol, in which high-temperature configurations, thermalized at $β_i<β_{\rm fo}$, are driven across the FOT by a purely relaxational dynamics at $β>β_{\rm fo}$. We focus on the emergence of spinodal-like behaviors in the thermodynamic limit, associated with the dynamic phase change. We argue that, if the nucleation of smooth droplets is the relevant mechanism of the post-quench phase change, for sufficiently small $β_{\rm fo}-β_i>0$, the time-dependent energy density should scale in terms of $ρ= (\ln t)^{3/2} δ$, where $δ= β/β_{\rm fo}-1$, with a discontinuity at a particular value $ρ=ρ_s>0$. This implies the emergence of a spinodal-like behavior, whose time scale $τ$ increases exponentially as $\ln τ\approx (ρ_s/δ)^{2/3}$ in the limit $δ\to 0^+$. We present a numerical analysis of the quench protocol in the 3D $q=6$ Potts model, which supports the above spinodal-like scenario.

Abstract: We experimentally, numerically and analytically explore the diffusive transport of active colloidal particles with sensory delay, navigating motility landscapes in which the self-propulsion speed depends on space. We obtain analytical results for the mean square displacement and the effective diffusion coefficient which accurately predict experimental measurements and numerical simulations across multiple scales. We show how, within the regime of validity of the delay-extended theory, density patterns and effective diffusion obey universal scaling forms. Our work provides minimal framework describing the transport properties of active swimmers with internal adaptation dynamics in motility landscapes.

### [45] [Hierarchical Reconstruction of Time-arrow from Multi-time Correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25749)
*Yijia Cheng,Ruicheng Bao,Zhonghuai Hou*

TL;DR: 本文提出利用多时间关联（multi-time correlations）构建熵产生率（EPR）下界的层级结构，通过定义重建操作（reconstruction operation）将观测数据中的不可逆性信息逐步编码，从而获得随关联阶数递增而趋于严格的EPR下界，并在理想条件下收敛至完整EPR。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过定义一种重建操作（reconstruction operation），将一类状态观测量的多时间关联（multi-time correlations）进行组合，从而构建出一系列EPR的下界。该方法利用不同阶数的关联来编码不同时间深度（temporal depth）上的热力学信息。

Result: 高阶关联能捕获更多热力学不可逆性，从而产生更严格的EPR下界。在理想条件下，该层级结构在有限时间窗口内观测密度趋于无穷大时收敛至完整的EPR。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个系统性的层级框架，能够基于实验可观测量的多时间关联逐步逼近EPR，为实验估计热力学不可逆性提供了理论工具。

Abstract: The entropy production rate (EPR), a key measure of thermodynamic irreversibility in stochastic thermodynamics, is difficult to determine directly in experiments, motivating lower-bound-based estimation from observations. However, a systematic framework for organizing increasing amounts of the irreversibility information in experimental state observables into progressively tighter bounds remains lacking. Here, we show that multi-time correlations of a class of state observations naturally encode this information to provide a hierarchy. By defining a reconstruction operation as a combination of correlations, we obtain a sequence of lower bounds on the EPR. Correlations of higher order capture the thermodynamic information at greater temporal depth, thereby capturing more irreversibility and yielding tighter bounds. Under ideal conditions, this hierarchy converges to the full EPR in the limit of infinitely dense observations over a finite time window.

### [46] [Finite-time transitions in optimal control and non-equilibrium relaxation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25798)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用理论分析与实验验证相结合的方法：理论构建包含位置依赖最终态能量惩罚的胶体粒子有限时间最优控制模型；实验通过操控胶体粒子通过空间非均匀环境进行验证。通过将控制代价映射为淬火（quench）后非平衡弛豫中大偏差速率函数（rate function），将控制问题与动态相变（dynamical phase transition）建立联系。

Abstract: We theoretically and experimentally study finite-time optimal control of a colloidal particle steered through a spatially inhomogeneous environment, modeled by a position-dependent energetic cost at the final state. The competition between this state-dependent penalty and path-dependent dissipation gives rise to a sharp transition in the control strategy at a critical control duration. We further show that this transition can be linked to a dynamical phase transition in nonequilibrium relaxation after a quench, where the control cost maps onto the rate function governing rare trajectories.

</details>


### [47] [Restoration of Ensemble Equivalence by Quantum Fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25837)
*Alessandro Campa,Andrea Trombettoni*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维量子自旋链在平均场和近邻相互作用及横向磁场下的热力学相图，发现横向场的量子涨落会在阈值以上消除经典Nagle-Kardar模型中存在的系综不等价性（ensemble inequivalence），并恢复系综等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在确定横向磁场引起的量子涨落对相图的影响，特别是针对系综不等价性现象的作用。

Method: 将模型称为量子Nagle-Kardar模型；利用Hubbard-Stratonovich变换处理平均场项中算符的非对易性（non-commutativity）；采用逐次逼近方法，并利用相变线的标度性质（scaling property）确定相图。

Result: 横向场存在一个阈值\(h_c\)，当\(h > h_c\)时，经典模型中存在的系综不等价性被消除，相图中仅包含二级相变（second-order phase transition）线。

Conclusion: 量子涨落足够强时（超过阈值\(h_c\)），系综等价性（ensemble equivalence）得以恢复，说明量子效应对统计力学的系综框架具有重要影响。

Abstract: We study the thermodynamic phase diagram of a one-dimensional quantum spin chain subjected to both mean-field and nearest-neighbor interactions, and to a transverse magnetic field $h$. The purpose is to determine the effect of the quantum fluctuations, due to the transverse field, on the phase diagram, in particular with respect to the occurrence of ensemble inequivalence. We denote our model as a quantum Nagle-Kardar model. To perform the calculation of the canonical partition function, we show that, due to the presence of the mean-field term, in the thermodynamic limit one can use the Hubbard-Stratonovich transformation in spite of the non-commutativity of the different operators appearing in the Hamiltonian, and we adopt a procedure of successive approximations that lead to the determination of the phase diagram thanks to a scaling property of the phase transition lines. The results show that the ensemble inequivalence, present in the classical Nagle-Kardar model, is removed above a threshold value $h_c$ for the transverse field. For $h$ larger than $h_c$ the phase diagram exhibits only second-order phase transition lines, implying therefore restoration of ensemble equivalence.

### [48] [CP violation in $Σ^+\to p\ell^+\ell^-$ within the standard model and beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24335)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析标准模型（Standard Model）中主导该过程的长程贡献（long-distance contributions）所提供的巨大吸收相位（absorptive phases），研究其与潜在新物理（new physics）贡献发生干涉时所能产生的CP破坏效应。

Result: 发现衰变率不对称性（decay rate asymmetry）目前理论上允许高达数十个百分点的量级，该信号足以被LHCb在近期实验中所探测。

Conclusion: 稀有超子衰变Σ⁺→pμ⁺μ⁻及其反粒子道可作为探测CP破坏的有效探针，相关研究还扩展至双电子衰变道Σ⁺→pe⁺e⁻和辐射衰变道Σ⁺→pγ。

Abstract: The LHCb collaboration has recently observed the rare hyperon decay $Σ^+\to pμ^+μ^-$. It can also measure the corresponding antihyperon channel with comparable precision and is thus in a position to extract information on $CP$ violation in this mode. Interestingly, the long-distance contributions that dominate it within the standard model provide large absorptive phases that could drive substantial $CP$ violation through interference with potential new-physics contributions. Here we explore this possibility, finding that the decay rate asymmetry is currently allowed to be as high as tens of percent, which can be probed by LHCb in the near future. We additionally consider the same with regard to the dielectron mode $Σ^+\to pe^+e^-$ as well as the related radiative one $Σ^+\to pγ$.

### [49] [Accidental Peccei-Quinn Symmetry from Chiral Gauge Symmetry and Mirror QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24849)
*Hajime Fukuda,Keisuke Harigaya*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过手征 U(1) 规范对称性解决强 CP 问题的新框架：该对称性衍生出偶然的 Peccei-Quinn 对称性，后者被镜像 QCD 动力学同时显式破缺和自发破缺，从而避免了无质量费米子或轻 QCD 轴子。模型中无稳定的畴壁或带色遗留物，允许足够高的再加热温度以实现轻子生成（leptogenesis）。亚稳态畴壁和一阶镜像 QCD 相变产生原初引力波随机背景，其中一个赝 Nambu-Goldstone 玻色子可作为 WIMP 暗物质候选者。手征 U(1) 规范玻色子与标准模型超电荷规范玻色子发生动力学混合，提供了连接暗物质与标准模型的矢量门户，并在暗物质现象学中发挥核心作用。带色赝 Nambu-Goldstone 玻色子可通过双喷流共振、喷流加缺失能量、含轻子多喷流事件以及偏移顶点（displaced vertices）等信号在 LHC 上被探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强 CP 问题是粒子物理标准模型的一个关键未解之谜，现有解决方案（如引入 QCD 轴子）往往伴随无质量费米子或轻轴子等概念困难。本文旨在构建一个无需这些要素的新理论框架，同时避免稳定的拓扑缺陷（畴壁）和带色遗留物，并允许宇宙重子数不对称通过轻子生成机制得到解释。

Method: 模型引入一个简单的手征 U(1) 规范对称性，其自发破缺衍生出偶然的 Peccei-Quinn 对称性；该对称性被镜像 QCD 动力学同时以显式和自发方式破缺。通过该机制，强 CP 问题得到解决而无须引入无质量费米子或轻 QCD 轴子。模型还包含手征 U(1) 规范玻色子与标准模型超电荷规范玻色子之间的动力学混合，作为连接暗物质与标准模型的矢量门户。

Result: 模型不含稳定的畴壁或带色遗留物；支持足够高的再加热温度以通过轻子生成解释宇宙重子数不对称。亚稳态畴壁和一阶镜像 QCD 相变产生原初引力波随机背景。一个赝 Nambu-Goldstone 玻色子可作为 WIMP 暗物质候选者。带色赝 Nambu-Goldstone 玻色子可在 LHC 上通过双喷流共振、喷流加缺失能量、含轻子多喷流事件和偏移顶点等信号被探测。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个解决强 CP 问题的新框架，同时囊括了暗物质候选者、引力波信号和可被对撞机检验的唯象学预言，构成了一个自洽且可实验检验的超出标准模型的新物理方案。

Abstract: We present a solution to the strong CP problem in which a simple chiral U(1) gauge symmetry gives rise to an accidental Peccei-Quinn symmetry that is both explicitly and spontaneously broken by mirror QCD dynamics, yielding a framework without massless fermions or a light QCD axion. The model contains no stable domain walls or colored relics, and it accommodates a sufficiently high reheating temperature to account for the baryon asymmetry of the Universe via leptogenesis. Metastable domain walls and first-order mirror QCD phase transition generate a stochastic background of primordial gravitational waves. Additionally, one of the pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone bosons serves as a viable WIMP dark matter candidate. The gauge boson associated with the chiral U(1) gauge symmetry, which kinetically mixes with the Standard Model hypercharge gauge boson, provides a vector portal connecting dark matter to the Standard Model and plays a central role in the dark-matter phenomenology. Colored pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone bosons can be probed at the LHC through searches for dijet resonances, jets plus missing energy, multijet events with leptons, and displaced vertices.

### [50] [The Angular Observables of $Λ_b \to Λ_c(\to Λ^0 π^+) \, τ^-(\to π^- ν_τ)\, \barν_τ$ within the Paradigm of FCCC Anomalies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24922)
*Muhammad Arslan,Ishtiaq Ahmed,Muhammad Jamil Aslam*

TL;DR: 针对B介子R(D^(*))反常（3.8σ偏离SM）进行全局分析，并扩展至重子衰变Λ_b^0 → Λ_c^+ τ^- \barν_τ，发现(C_{V_L}, C_{S_R})为最优新物理（NP）解；角可观测量分析与关联分析揭示了不同NP场景的CP性质差异，验证了重子半轻衰变作为独立探针的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: B介子味反常中的轻子味道普适性（lepton flavor universality, LFU）比率R_{τ/(μ,e)}(D^{(*)})在多个实验（BaBar、Belle、LHCb）中表现出与标准模型（Standard Model, SM）预测的3.8σ偏离，提示可能存在新物理（new physics, NP），但重子区（baryonic sector）衰变的独立检验仍不充分。

Method: 对B介子味反常进行全局分析，并扩展到重子区衰变Λ_b^0 → Λ_c^+ τ^- \barν_τ；利用最新HFLAV平均值和B_c寿命约束（B_c → τν分支比上限设为< 60%, 30%, 10%）寻找新物理（NP）解；采用晶格QCD（Lattice-QCD）形状因子（form factors）计算五重微分衰变中完整角可观测量集合，并进行关联分析。

Result: (C_{V_L}, C_{S_R}) 是全局最优NP解，受分支比约束影响最小；(C_{V_L}) 次优。角可观测量K_{1c}、K_{2ss}、K_{2cc}和K_{4s}对NP效应最敏感。(Re[C_{S_L}=4C_T], Im[C_{S_L}=4C_T]) 场景呈现K_{1c}与K_{2ss,2cc,4s}的反关联及K_{2ss}与K_{2cc,4s}的正关联，暗示可能的CP破坏相位；而(C_{S_L}, C_{S_R})场景表现为与CP守恒动力学一致的行为。

Conclusion: 重子半轻衰变（如Λ_b^0 → Λ_c^+ τ^- \barν_τ）可作为R(D^(*))反常的独立且强有力的探针；未来实验测量将为区分新物理（new physics, NP）结构（如CP破坏或CP守恒动力学）提供关键检验。

Abstract: We present a global analysis of the current $B$-meson flavor anomalies and extend it to the baryonic sector through the decay $Λ_b^0 \to Λ_c^+(\to Λ^0 π^+) τ^-(\to π^- ν_τ)\barν_τ$. The lepton flavor universality ratios $R_{τ/(μ,e)}(D^{(*)})$, measured by BaBar, Belle, and LHCb, exhibit a combined $3.8σ$ deviation from Standard Model (SM) predictions. Using the latest HFLAV averages and $B_c$-lifetime constraints, $\mathcal{B}(B_c \to τν) < 60\%, 30\%, 10\%$, found new physics (NP) solutions to the cascade decay $Λ_b^0 \to Λ_c^+(\to Λ^0 π^+) τ^-(\to π^- ν_τ)\barν_τ$. The scenario $(C_{V_L},C_{S_R})$ emerges as the most favored NP solution, largest pull from the SM and insensitive to branching-ratio constraints; followed by $C_{V_L}$ case. We study the impact of NP operators on a complete set of angular observables on the five-fold $Λ_b$ decay using Lattice-QCD form factors and find that the scenarios $(\Re[C_{S_L}=4C_T],\Im[C_{S_L}=4C_T])$ and $(C_{S_L},C_{S_R})$ generate the largest deviations from the SM predictions. In particular, the observables $\mathcal{K}_{1c}$, $\mathcal{K}_{2ss}$, $\mathcal{K}_{2cc}$, and $\mathcal{K}_{4s}$ show the highest sensitivity to NP effects. The correlation analysis reveals the $(\Re[C_{S_L}=4C_T],\Im[C_{S_L}=4C_T])$ scenario exhibits inverse correlations among $\mathcal{K}_{1c}$ and $\mathcal{K}_{2ss,2cc,4s}$ and direct correlations between $\mathcal{K}_{2ss}$ and $\mathcal{K}_{2cc,4s}$, pointing to a possible CP-violating phase, while the $(C_{S_L},C_{S_R})$ scenario displays complementary behavior consistent with CP-conserving dynamics. These results establish baryonic semileptonic decays as a powerful and independent probe of the $R_{τ/(μ,e)}(D^{(*)})$ anomalies, with future measurements providing critical tests of the underlying NP structure.

### [51] [Forward backward CP asymmetry in $τ^- \to K πν_τ$ in the Left-Right Inverse seesaw model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24924)
*David Delepine,Shaaban Khalil*

TL;DR: 本文在左-右逆跷跷板（Left-Right Inverse Seesaw, LRIS）模型框架下研究τ→Kπν_τ衰变中的CP破坏效应，发现虽然积分CP不对称性无法解释BaBar的2.8σ偏差，但微分前后向CP不对称性A_CP^FB(s)在K*(892)和K_0*(1430)共振附近具有显著信号，可作为LRIS标量区（scalar sector）的灵敏探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于LRIS模型，推导了相关的|ΔS|=1有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian），识别出由顶夸克味改变中性流箱图（top-quark flavor-changing neutral current box diagram）产生的非退耦标量算符（non-decoupling scalar operator）g_S，并计算了积分和微分CP不对称性。

Result: LRIS模型预测的积分CP不对称性过小，无法解释BaBar结果；但微分前后向CP不对称性A_CP^FB(s)在K*(892)和K_0*(1430)共振附近显著增强，该信号主要来自标量算符与SM矢量流的干涉效应（interference effect）。

Conclusion: 角分布（angular）和微分（differential）可观测量可作为LRIS标量区在Belle II等当前及未来味实验中的灵敏探针。

Abstract: Recent measurements of the integrated CP asymmetry in $τ\to Kπν_τ$ decays by the BaBar collaboration exhibit a $2.8σ$ deviation from the Standard Model (SM) prediction. In this work, we investigate CP-violating effects in $τ\to Kπν_τ$ within the model of the Left--Right Inverse Seesaw (LRIS) model. We show that, although the integrated asymmetry remains too small to account for the BaBar result, the model nevertheless predicts a pronounced signal in the \emph{differential} forward--backward CP asymmetry, $A_{\rm CP}^{\rm FB}(s)$. We derive the effective $|ΔS| = 1$ Hamiltonian relevant for these decays and identify a dominant non-decoupling scalar operator, $g_S$, generated by a top-quark flavor-changing neutral current box diagram involving heavy neutrinos and scalar exchange. Our numerical analysis demonstrates that, while this contribution largely cancels in the integrated $A_{\rm CP}$, it significantly enhances $A_{\rm CP}^{\rm FB}(s)$ through interference with the SM vector current, leading to distinctive kinematic features near the $K^*(892)$ and $K_0^*(1430)$ resonances. These angular and differential observables provide a sensitive probe of the LRIS scalar sector at current and future flavor experiments, in particular Belle~II.

### [52] [Muon $g$$-$$2$: correlation-induced uncertainties in precision data combinations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25004)
*Alexander Keshavarzi,Daisuke Nomura,Thomas Teubner,Aidan Wright*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个通用且系统的框架，用于量化数据组合中因系统相关性（systematic correlation）不完全已知所导致的不确定性。该方法在组合数据层面构建协方差矩阵（covariance matrix），实现对相关结构（correlation structure）的可控变化，从而稳健且系统地估计相关性引起的不确定性。将该方法应用于 $e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$ 截面数据，并传播至缪子 anomalous magnetic moment 中 hadronic vacuum polarization（HVP）的色散确定。结果表明，系统相关假设的不确定性总体上为次主导但不可忽略，且无法完全解释现有 $e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$ 数据组合间的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在精密测量中，数据组合常包含不完全已知的系统相关性，传统方法难以对这些相关性引起的不确定性进行可控且系统的量化。现有 $e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$ 截面数据的组合之间存在差异，其来源尚不明确，需要评估系统相关假设不确定性是否为差异的原因之一。

Method: 在组合数据的层面构建协方差矩阵，通过可控变化相关结构，直接生成组合结果上的协方差矩阵，从而稳健估计由相关性引起的不确定性。该方法是一种通用框架（framework），适用于多种精密测量中的相关数据组合问题。

Result: 将该框架应用于 $e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$ 截面数据，并将得到的协方差矩阵传播至导出观测量（derived observables），包括 $a_\mu^\mathrm{HVP}$ 的色散确定。发现系统相关假设的不确定性总体上为次主导（subdominant）但不可忽略（non-negligible），且无法完全解释现有 $e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$ 数据组合之间的差异。

Conclusion: 该框架广泛适用于精密测量中的相关数据组合，将成为即将更新的 KNTW（Keshavarzi-Nomura-Teubner-Woloshyn）数据组合在 $a_\mu^\mathrm{HVP}$ 中的一个新组成部分，有助于更系统地量化组合中的系统不确定性。

Abstract: We present a general and systematic framework to quantify uncertainties arising from imperfectly known systematic correlations in data combinations. Formulated at the level of the combined data, the method enables controlled variation of the correlation structure, leading to the construction of covariance matrices directly on the resulting combination and thus providing a robust and systematic estimate of correlation-induced uncertainties. We apply the method to $e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$ cross section data, with the resulting covariance matrices propagated to derived observables, including dispersive determinations of the hadronic vacuum polarization (HVP) contribution to the muon anomalous magnetic moment, $a_μ^\mathrm{HVP}$. We find that uncertainties from systematic correlation assumptions are generally subdominant but non-negligible, and do not fully account for differences between existing $e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$ data combinations. The framework is broadly applicable to correlated data combinations in precision measurements and constitutes a new component of the upcoming KNTW data combination for $a_μ^\mathrm{HVP}$.

</details>


### [53] [Les Houches study on inclusive jet production at NNLO+NNLL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25490)
*Terry Generet,Joey Huston,Kyle Lee,Ian Moult,Rene Poncelet,Xiaoyuan Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过NNLO QCD计算结合小喷注半径的NNLL重求和，重新评估了尺度变化方法在 inclusive jet 产生中的可靠性，发现尺度变化会严重低估高阶效应的影响，并认为不应将其作为缺失高阶不确定性的可靠估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LHC喷注产生（jet production）是检验QCD和提取部分子分布函数（parton distribution functions）及强耦合常数等参数的重要探针，但现有理论计算中由非微扰效应和缺失高阶项（missing higher orders）引起的不确定性需要被审慎评估。尺度变化（scale variation）是当前最常用的估计缺失高阶效应的方法，但其可靠性尚未在包含小喷注半径重求和（small-jet-radius resummation）的NNLO计算中得到充分检验。

Method: 在NNLO QCD精度计算的基础上，引入小喷注半径的next-to-next-to-leading-logarithmic accuracy（NNLL）重求和，对inclusive jet产生过程进行理论计算，并与基于尺度变化的不确定度估计进行系统比较。

Result: NNLL重求和对inclusive jet截面（inclusive jet cross sections）的尺度不确定性有显著影响，部分尺度选择下会导致中心截面的可观偏移；尺度变化方法在固定阶（fixed-order）和重求和（resummed）计算中均会严重低估高阶效应对常用喷注半径参数带来的影响。

Conclusion: 通过尺度变化获得的缺失高阶估计应被视为不可靠（unreliable），这一发现进一步凸显了在喷注及喷注子结构（jet substructure）计算中超越尺度变化方法的重要性。

Abstract: Jet production at the LHC is a powerful probe of QCD, making it ideal for precision tests and determinations of QCD parameters such as parton distribution functions and the strong coupling constant. To make the most of the abundant jet production data collected at the LHC, precise calculations are required. While state-of-the-art calculations reach next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO) QCD accuracy, a critical assessment of the remaining uncertainties arising from non-perturbative effects and missing higher orders remains crucial for correctly interpreting comparisons between theory and data. Scale variation is nearly always used to determine effects from missing higher orders. In this article, we reassess this method in the context of inclusive jet production by performing NNLO QCD calculations supplemented by small-jet-radius resummation through next-to-next-to-leading-logarithmic accuracy (NNLL). We find that NNLL resummation can have an appreciable impact on the scale uncertainty for inclusive jet cross sections, and, for some scale choices, can lead to sizeable shifts of the central cross section. We conclude that scale variations in fixed-order and resummed calculations can drastically underestimate the impact of higher orders for commonly used jet radius parameters, and that missing higher-order estimates obtained via scale variations should be considered unreliable. Our findings add further evidence to the importance of going beyond scale variations in jet and jet substructure calculations.

</details>


### [54] [The EDM inverse problem: Identifying the sources of CP violation and PQ breaking with electric dipole moments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25516)
*Kiwoon Choi,Sang Hui Im*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文识别了六类与低能电偶极矩（EDM）相关的CP破坏有效算子（含QCD θ项），证明不同算子类别会产生可区分的EDM模式，从而可通过实验测量反推其紫外起源，并揭示QCD轴子真空期望值的来源机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型（Standard Model）之外的新物理可能引入新的CP破坏源，从而在原子核、原子和分子中诱导出可观测的P奇和T奇永久电偶极矩（electric dipole moment, EDM）。未来若观测到非零EDM，虽可作为新物理的灵敏探针，但也构成一个非平凡的反问题（inverse problem）——如何识别其背后的紫外（ultraviolet）起源。因此需要一种能够区分不同CP破坏机制的方法。

Method: 本研究在QCD标度（QCD scale）附近识别了六类具有代表性的CP破坏有效算子（effective operator），包括QCD θ项（QCD θ-term），并系统分析了它们在不同物理系统中产生的EDM模式差异。

Result: 研究表明，这六类算子会在不同核子、原子和分子系统中产生截然不同的EDM模式，因此可以通过实验测量的EDM值来区分它们。此外，EDM测量还能揭示QCD轴子（QCD axion）真空期望值（vacuum expectation value）的起源，帮助判断该期望值是由高标度佩切伊-奎因对称性破缺效应（如量子引力相关效应）主导，还是由超出标准模型的CP破坏与QCD反常（QCD anomaly）的相互作用所致。

Conclusion: EDM测量不仅可作为新物理的探针，更能解决其反问题——通过不同系统的EDM模式区分CP破坏算子的类型；同时，EDM数据可为理解QCD轴子真空期望值的起源提供关键信息，从而区分量子引力等高标度效应与标准模型外CP破坏机制的不同贡献。

Abstract: Many extensions of the Standard Model (SM) generically introduce new sources of CP violation, which can induce observable $P$-odd and $T$-odd permanent electric dipole moments (EDMs) of nuclei, atoms, and molecules. A future observation of nonvanishing EDMs would therefore provide a sensitive probe of physics beyond the SM, while also posing a nontrivial inverse problem: identifying their underlying ultraviolet origin. In this work, we identify six representative classes of CP-violating effective operators near the QCD scale, including the QCD $θ$-term, that are particularly relevant for low-energy EDMs and can arise in a broad range of SM extensions. We show that these operator classes lead to distinct EDM patterns across different systems, thereby enabling discrimination among them through experimentally measured EDMs. We further emphasize that EDM measurements can shed light on the origin of the vacuum expectation value of the QCD axion. In particular, they may help distinguish whether a nonzero axion vacuum expectation value is predominantly induced by high-scale Peccei--Quinn symmetry-breaking effects, such as those associated with quantum gravity, or by the interplay between beyond-the-SM CP violation and the QCD anomaly.

</details>


### [55] [Determination of the $Z_c(3900)$ and the $Z_{cs}(3985)$ states from joint analysis of experimental and lattice data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25607)
*Yun-Hua Chen,Meng-Lin Du,Feng-Kun Guo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过联合分析e+e-碰撞实验数据和格子QCD（lattice QCD）模拟的有限体积能级，首次对奇特强子态Zc(3900)和Zcs(3985)进行了统一描述，表明两者是SU(3)味对称性下的八重态伙伴，并提取了它们的极点和耦合参数。成分分析（compositeness analysis）显示D\bar D^* (Ds\bar D^*+D\bar D_s^*)组分显著，但仍需其他成分才能构成这些奇特态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Zc(3900)和Zcs(3985)作为可能的奇特强子态（exotic hadron states），其内部结构和SU(3)味对称性（flavor symmetry）关系尚未明确。需要同时考虑实验数据和格子QCD（lattice QCD）模拟结果，以统一描述这两个态并检验它们是否属于同一八重态多重态（octet multiplet）。

Method: 同时拟合多个e+e-湮灭过程（包括J/ψπ+π-、J/ψK+K-、D0 D*- π+等）以及来自格子QCD模拟的有限体积能级（finite-volume energy levels）。模型中包含开放粲介子圈（open-charm meson loops）与三角奇异性（triangle singularities）、J/ψπ(J/ψ\bar K)-D\bar D^*(D\bar D_s^*)耦合道相互作用（coupled-channel interactions），以及ππ-K\bar K末态相互作用（final-state interaction）。

Result: 实验与格子数据的联合描述要求Zc(3900)和Zcs(3985)的极点贡献不可或缺。提取的Zc(3900)极点质量和半宽分别为(3879.6 ± 4.8) MeV和(32.2 ± 4.7) MeV；Zcs(3985)则为(3976.9 ± 5.1) MeV和(28.8 ± 5.9) MeV。确定了Zc(Zcs)到D\bar D^*(Ds\bar D^*+D\bar D_s^*)与J/ψπ(J/ψK)道的耦合比。成分分析表明D\bar D^*(Ds\bar D^*+D\bar D_s^*)组分虽大，但仍需额外成分。

Conclusion: Zc(3900)和Zcs(3985)被证实为共振态（resonance states），且是SU(3)味对称性下的八重态伙伴。两个奇特态具有显著的分子态（molecular state）组分，但并非纯分子态，存在其他内部结构成分。

Abstract: We present a unified analysis of the $Z_c(3900)$ and $Z_{cs}(3985)$ states considering both experimental and lattice data. The study simultaneously includes the processes $e^+e^- \rightarrow J/ψπ^+π^-, J/ψK^+ K^-, D^0 D^{\ast-} π^+, (D^{\ast 0} D_s^{-}+D^0 D_s^{\ast -}) K^+$, together with finite-volume energy levels from recent lattice QCD simulations. Open-charm meson loops with triangle singularities, the $J/ψπ(J/ψ\bar{K})$-$\bar{D}D^*(\bar{D}D^*_s)$ coupled-channel interactions, and the $ππ$-$K\bar K$ final-state interaction are all taken into account. We find that pole contributions associated with the $Z_c(3900)$ and $Z_{cs}(3985)$ are indispensable for describing the data. The successful joint description of the experimental and lattice data supports the interpretation that the $Z_c(3900)$ and $Z_{cs}(3985)$ are SU(3) flavor partners within the same octet multiplet and indicates that both are resonance states. The extracted pole masses and half-widths of the $Z_c(3900)$ and the $Z_{cs}(3985)$ are $(3879.6 \pm 4.8)$ MeV and $(32.2 \pm 4.7)$ MeV, and $(3976.9 \pm 5.1)$ MeV and $(28.8 \pm 5.9)$ MeV, respectively. The ratios of the $Z_c(Z_{cs})$ couplings to the $D\bar D^*(D_s\bar{D}^\ast+D\bar{D}_s^\ast)$ and $J/ψπ(J/ψK)$ channels are also determined. A compositeness analysis indicates that, although the $D\bar D^* (D_s\bar{D}^\ast+D\bar{D}_s^\ast)$ component in the $Z_c(3900) (Z_{cs}(3985))$ state is sizable, additional components are still needed to form these exotic states.

Abstract: Coherent hard exclusive reactions on light nuclei provide access to their quark and gluon structure and enable three-dimensional tomography of these complex systems. ### [57] [$CP$ violation in singly Cabibbo suppressed $D\to πa_0(980)$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25875)
*Yu-Kuo Hsiao,Shu-Ting Cai,Yan-Li Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过测量单卡比博压制（SCS）衰变 $D\to \pi a_0$ 的分支比，发现实验值与短距离（short-distance）预期存在显著偏离，表明长距离重散射效应（long-distance rescattering effects）的必要性，并由此在 $10^{-3}$ 量级预言了直接 $CP$ 破坏（direct $CP$ violation）信号，为 $CP$ 破坏研究开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析 $D\to K^*K\to a_0\pi$ 这一中间过程，引入长距离重散射效应，使得振幅 ${\cal M}=\lambda_d{\cal M}_d+\lambda_s{\cal M}_s$ 中的 ${\cal M}_s$ 与 ${\cal M}_d$ 量级相当，并伴随不可忽略的强相位（strong phases），从而产生直接 $CP$ 破坏（direct $CP$ violation）。

Result: 直接 $CP$ 不对称度（direct $CP$ asymmetries）自然出现在 ${\cal O}(10^{-3})$ 量级，具体结果为：${\cal A}_{CP}(D^0\to\pi^- a_0^+)=(-0.7\pm 0.1\pm 0.1\pm 0.1)\times 10^{-3}$，${\cal A}_{CP}(D^+\to\pi^0 a_0^+)=(-1.4\pm 0.1\pm 0.1\pm 0.1)\times 10^{-3}$，${\cal A}_{CP}(D^0\to\pi^+ a_0^-)=(-2.1\pm 0.9\pm 1.1\pm 0.4)\times 10^{-3}$。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了单卡比博压制（SCS）的 $D\to \pi a_0$ 衰变作为探测 $CP$ 破坏（$CP$ violation）的新途径，为相关理论和实验研究提供了新的方向。

Abstract: The singly Cabibbo suppressed (SCS) decays $D\to πa_0$, with $a_0\equiv a_0(980)$, have been measured with the branching-fraction ratios $r^{+/-}_{\rm ex}\equiv {\cal B}(D^0\toπ^- a_0^+)/{\cal B}(D^0\toπ^+ a_0^-)=7.5^{+2.5}_{-0.8}\pm 1.7$ and $r^{+/0}_{\rm ex}\equiv {\cal B}(D^+\toπ^0 a_0^+)/{\cal B}(D^+\toπ^+ a_0^0)=2.6\pm 0.6\pm 0.3$, deviating significantly from the short-distance expectations $(r^{+/-},r^{+/0})\simeq (0.07,0.2)$. This discrepancy indicates the necessity of long-distance rescattering effects. In particular, the process $D\to K^*K\to a_0π$ generates ${\cal M}_s$ comparable in magnitude to ${\cal M}_d$ in the amplitude ${\cal M}=λ_d{\cal M}_d+λ_s{\cal M}_s$, with $λ_q\equiv V_{cq}^*V_{uq}$, accompanied by nontrivial strong phases essential for $CP$ violation. Consequently, the direct $CP$ asymmetries naturally arise at the ${\cal O}(10^{-3})$ level, for example, ${\cal A}_{CP}(D^0\toπ^- a_0^+)=(-0.7\pm 0.1\pm 0.1\pm 0.1)\times 10^{-3}$, ${\cal A}_{CP}(D^+\toπ^0 a_0^+)=(-1.4\pm 0.1\pm 0.1\pm 0.1)\times 10^{-3}$, and ${\cal A}_{CP}(D^0\toπ^+ a_0^-)=(-2.1\pm 0.9\pm 1.1\pm 0.4)\times 10^{-3}$. These results establish SCS $D\to πa_0$ decays as a new avenue for probing $CP$ violation.

*Pahal D. Patel,Sanmay Ganguly*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对基于图神经网络（graph neural network）的喷注标记器（jet tagger），提出并系统比较了多种可解释性方法（GNNExplainer、GNNShap、GRADCam），在Lund平面图表示（Lund-plane graph representation）上构建了基于蒙特卡洛真值（Monte Carlo truth）的评估框架，并揭示了模型在不同横动量区间和相空间区域中对喷注亚结构物理特征的学习情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管ParticleNet和ParticleTransformer等基于图神经网络（graph neural network）和点云（point cloud）的模型在大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider, LHC）的喷注标记（jet tagging）任务上达到了当前最优性能（state-of-the-art），但它们预测背后的物理推理机制仍然不透明，因此亟需发展可解释性方法以理解模型所学到的物理内容。

Method: 作者将三类可解释性方法——基于扰动的方法（perturbation-based, GNNExplainer）、基于Shapley值的方法（Shapley-value-based, GNNShap）和基于梯度的方法（gradient-based, GRADCam）——适配到LundNet的Lund平面图表示（Lund-plane graph representation）上；利用Lund平面中每个节点对应物理上有意义的部分子分裂（parton splitting）这一特性，构建了蒙特卡洛真值解释掩码（Monte Carlo truth explanation masks），并引入了一个超越标准保真度指标（fidelity metrics）的基于物理的评估框架（physics-informed evaluation framework）。

Result: 在三个横动量区间（p_T ∈ [500,700]、[800,1000]及包含区域[500,1000] GeV）的分析表明，解释质量与关注焦点在非微扰（non-perturbative）和微扰（perturbative）区域之间发生系统性的偏移。可解释性方法赋予的节点重要性与经典喷注亚结构观测量（jet substructure observables）——包括N-subjettiness比值τ₂₁和τ₃₂以及能量关联函数（energy correlation functions）——之间存在相关性，且这种相关性在不同相空间区域呈现出预期的变化，表明训练后的神经网络确实学习到了喷注亚结构矩（jet-substructure moments）的某些方面。

Conclusion: 可解释性方法分配的重要性权重与分析观测量之间存在整体相关性，且在不同相空间区间中表现出预期偏移，这证实了训练后的神经网络确实学习到了喷注亚结构（jet substructure）的部分物理特征。论文提供的开源实现可用于对基于图的喷注标记器进行可复现的可解释性研究。

Abstract: Graph neural networks such as ParticleNet and transformer based networks on point clouds such as ParticleTransformer achieve state-of-the-art performance on jet tagging benchmarks at the Large Hadron Collider, yet the physical reasoning behind their predictions remains opaque. We present different methods, i.e. perturbation-based (GNNExplainer), Shapley-value-based (GNNShap), and gradient-based (GRADCam); adapted to operate on LundNet's Lund-plane graph representation. Leveraging the fact that each node in the Lund plane corresponds to a physically meaningful parton splitting, we construct Monte Carlo truth explanation masks and introduce a physics-informed evaluation framework that goes beyond standard fidelity metrics. We perform the analysis in three transverse-momentum bins ($\mathrm{p_T} \in [500,700]$, $[800,1000]$, and the inclusive region $[500,1000]$ GeV), revealing how explanation quality and focus shift between non-perturbative and perturbative regimes. We further quantify the correlation between explainer-assigned node importance and classical jet substructure observables -- $N$-subjettiness ratios $τ_{21}$ and $τ_{32}$ and the energy correlation functions -- establishing the degree to which the model has learned known QCD features. We find that overall the weight assigned by explainability methods has a correlation with analytic observables, with expected shift across different phase space regimes, indicating that a trained neural network indeed learns some aspects of jet-substructure moments. Our open-source implementation enables reproducible explainability studies for graph-based jet taggers.

Result: 畴壁湮灭后若产生的标量寿命足够长，其延迟衰变会驱动早期物质主导阶段，显著放大来自原初扰动的诱导引力波。随后的辐射主导转变通过熵注入稀释了畴壁的直接贡献，但保留了增强后的诱导信号，最终形成具有两个不同峰值的引力波谱。

Conclusion: 该引力波谱的双峰结构可在互补频段被探测，多波段探测能够为早期宇宙对称性破缺提供独特的观测窗口。

Abstract: Domain wall annihilation can leave a distinctive imprint on the induced gravitational wave spectrum. During annihilation, most of the domain wall energy transforms into the scalar field responsible for the initial $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry breaking that created the walls, along with any coupled species. If the produced scalar is sufficiently long-lived, its delayed decay drives an early matter-dominated phase following domain wall annihilation, significantly amplifying induced gravitational waves from primordial perturbations. The subsequent transition to radiation domination dilutes the domain wall contribution through entropy injection while preserving the enhanced induced signal. This creates a gravitational wave spectrum with two distinct peaks detectable across complementary frequency bands. We explore the observable parameter space and demonstrate how multi-band detection can probe early universe symmetry breaking.

*Claudio Corianò*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文回顾了关于规范轴子（gauged axion）宇宙学的合作研究，探讨了反常规范对称性、定向折叠有效作用（orientifold effective actions）、Stueckelberg场与暗物质之间的联系。在具有反常额外U(1)对称性的模型中，Stueckelberg赝标量通过Wess-Zumino反项参与规范不变性的恢复，并在电弱对称性破缺后可能留下一个物理的类轴子态（axion-like state）。其宇宙学历史与普通Peccei-Quinn轴子不同，物理场仅在Higgs-Stueckelberg混合后出现，经历电弱与QCD的序列错位（sequential misalignment），并且只有在Stueckelberg标度足够大时才能产生可观的暗物质遗迹丰度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纪念与合作者George Lazarides，并重新审视一项关于规范轴子宇宙学的合作工作，将其置于反常规范对称性、定向折叠有效作用、Stueckelberg场与暗物质之间更广泛的理论联系中。

Method: 分析具有反常额外U(1)对称性的模型，其中Stueckelberg赝标量通过Wess-Zumino反项恢复规范不变性；考察电弱对称性破缺后产生的物理类轴子态，并对比其与普通Peccei-Quinn轴子的宇宙学差异。

Result: 物理类轴子态仅在Higgs-Stueckelberg混合后出现，且经历电弱和QCD的序列错位机制；只有当Stueckelberg标度足够大时，该轴子态才能提供可观的暗物质遗迹丰度。

Conclusion: 轴子模型的真空结构必须与其嵌入其中的规范结构一同理解，这一视角与George Lazarides的早期洞见相一致。

Abstract: These notes are written for a memorial Session dedicated to George Lazarides. They revisit a joint work on the cosmology of a gauged axion and place it in a broader line of ideas connecting anomalous gauge symmetries, orientifold effective actions, Stueckelberg fields and dark matter. In models with an anomalous extra $U(1)$ symmetry, the Stueckelberg pseudoscalar participates in the restoration of gauge invariance through Wess-Zumino counterterms and, after electroweak symmetry breaking, may leave a physical axion-like state. Its cosmological history differs from that of an ordinary Peccei-Quinn axion: the physical field appears only after Higgs-Stueckelberg mixing, is subject to sequential electroweak and QCD misalignment, and can give an appreciable dark-matter relic abundance only when the Stueckelberg scale is sufficiently large. This perspective connects naturally with George's earlier insight that the vacuum structure of axion models must be understood together with the gauge structure in which it is embedded. I dedicate these notes to his memory, with gratitude for the collaboration and for the clarity with which he connected particle physics to the early universe.

</details>

### [62] [A density-functional perspective on force fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25215)
*Nan Sheng*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过将 Born-Oppenheimer 能量面视为核-势映射的拉回，建立了力场（force fields）与密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）之间的结构关系，并将力、核 Hessian 等量统一纳入一个导数层级框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 力场通常在核构型空间中直接表述，而密度泛函理论（DFT）则天然以外势、密度和变分对偶性为基础。两种视角之间存在根本性的形式差异，缺乏统一的结构关联。

Method: 将 Born-Oppenheimer 能量面视为核-势映射（nuclear-to-potential map）的拉回（pullback）；在 Lieb 表述下，密度是能量对外势的一阶泛函导数，密度-密度响应函数是二阶泛函导数；将这些导数对象拉回至核构型空间，得到力（force）与核 Hessian 矩阵。

Result: 力场、密度泛函理论和响应理论（response theory）被纳入同一个导数层级（derivative hierarchy）之中；核 Hessian 中包含由核生成势和核-核排斥诱导的显式项。

Conclusion: 本文的目的在于概念阐释而非算法开发，为力场与 DFT 之间提供了一种统一的微分几何视角。

Abstract: Force fields are usually formulated directly in nuclear configuration space, whereas density functional theory is naturally formulated in terms of external potentials, densities, and variational duality. In this work, we isolate the structural relation between these viewpoints. A nuclear configuration determines a nuclear-generated external potential, so the Born-Oppenheimer energy surface may be viewed as the pullback of an external-potential energy functional along the nuclear-to-potential map. In the Lieb formulation of density functional theory, the density is the first functional derivative of the energy with respect to the external potential, while the density-density response function is the second. Pulling these derivative objects back to nuclear configuration space yields the force and the nuclear Hessian, together with explicit terms induced by the nuclear-generated potential and the nuclear-nuclear repulsion. The resulting picture places force fields, density functional theory, and response theory within a single derivative hierarchy. The purpose of the present work is conceptual rather than algorithmic.

</details>


### [63] [Thermal conductivity of aligned polymers with kinks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25037)
*Igor V. Parshin,Igor V. Rubtsov,Alexander L. Burin*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过理论分析和数值计算，研究了含扭结（kinks）聚合物中的声子输运，发现热导率在长距离下呈超扩散（superdiffusive）行为，标度律为 κ ∝ L^{1/3}，并在短距离下表现出由弹道输运（ballistic transport）到安德森局域化（Anderson localization）导致的非单调变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 取向聚合物沿排列方向具有异常高的热导率，但其对分子构象（molecular conformation）高度敏感，尤其是由 gauche 扭结（gauche kinks）引起的构象变化可使热导率相差数个数量级。该工作旨在从理论上揭示扭结聚合物中声子输运的微观机制。

Method: 采用数值计算方法评估扭结聚合物中的热导率，并将结果解释为声子受随机分布扭结散射的物理图像。研究对象为强取向聚合物，限制其主链偏离线性结构的程度。

Result: 在长距离下，热输运呈现超扩散行为，热导率满足 κ ∝ L^{1/3} 的标度律。在短距离下，热导率表现出非单调行为：极短尺度下因几乎所有声子的弹道输运而上升，中等尺度下因大部分声子模式的安德森局域化而下降。

Conclusion: 理论结果与实验和分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）一致，阐明了聚合物中热输运的微观机制。

Abstract: Thermal conductivity of aligned polymer molecules can be exceptionally high along the alignment direction due to energy transport through strong covalent bonds. At the same time, it is highly sensitive to molecular conformation, varying by orders of magnitude as a result of gauche kinks. Here, we theoretically investigate phonon transport in kinked polymers by numerically evaluating thermal conductivity and interpreting the results in terms of phonon scattering from randomly distributed kinks. For strongly aligned polymers with restricted deviations from a linear backbone, we find that heat transport becomes superdiffusive at long lengths, with thermal conductivity scaling as $κ\propto L^{1/3}$. At shorter lengths, thermal conductivity exhibits non-monotonic behavior: it increases at very short scales due to ballistic transport of almost all phonons, then decreases at intermediate lengths due to the Anderson localization of most phonon modes. These results are consistent with experiments and molecular dynamics simulations, and they elucidate the microscopic mechanisms governing heat transport in polymers.

</details>


### [64] [Excitation of Low-Frequency Modes and the Effects of Protein Dynamics on Spectral Densities of Bacteriochlorophyll Molecules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25460)
*Sayan Maity,Tristan A. Mauck,Ulrich Kleinekathöfer*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文展示了基于密度泛函紧束缚近似的Born-Oppenheimer分子动力学（BOMD）方法能够准确恢复光捕集复合物中光谱密度的低频特征，其效果优于经典分子动力学（MD）模拟和简正模式分析，尤其能捕捉到色素分子自身慢速分子内振动带来的低频贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放量子系统理论中，光谱密度（spectral density）是表征系统动力学与光谱性质的关键量；在光捕集复合物中，光谱密度的低频分量对色素分子间的激子转移至关重要。然而，基于经典分子动力学（MD）模拟的常用力场难以准确刻画气相细菌叶绿素分子的慢速内部模式。

Method: 采用基于密度泛函紧束缚（density functional-based tight-binding, DFTB）近似的Born-Oppenheimer分子动力学（BOMD）方法来确定光谱密度，并将其与经典MD模拟以及简正模式分析（normal mode analysis）进行对比。

Result: BOMD方法能准确恢复光谱密度中的低频特征，而简正模式分析仅能部分捕捉；BOMD还能捕获由色素分子自身慢速分子内振动引起的低频贡献，这在经典MD方法中被忽略。该行为在B800环、B850环以及FMO复合物中均一致观察到。此外，LH2复合物B850环中色素的光谱密度不受蛋白质环境波动的影响，即基态与第一激发态之间的能隙未因环境涨落而发生显著改变。

Conclusion: BOMD方法比经典MD和简正模式分析更能准确描述光捕集复合物中光谱密度的低频区域，尤其适合处理色素分子自身的慢速分子内振动贡献。同时，B850环中色素光谱密度对环境不敏感的现象值得进一步关注。

Abstract: In the theory of open quantum systems, spectral densities are key quantities for modeling the dynamics and spectroscopic properties of the system under investigation. In the case of light-harvesting complexes, they encode the frequency-dependent coupling of electronic excitations in pigment molecules to their environment, reflecting contributions from both intrinsic vibrational modes and the protein surrounding. In particular, the low-frequency components of the spectral densities are crucial for exciton transfer between pigment molecules. Apparently, slow internal modes of bacteriocholophyll molecules in the gas phase are less well represented by common force fields based on classical molecular dynamics (MD) simulations. Here, we demonstrate that Born-Oppenheimer molecular dynamics (BOMD) based on the numerically efficient density functional-based tight-binding approach can accurately recover these low-frequency features, whereas normal mode analysis captures them only partially. In contrasting approaches for determining spectral densities, the low-frequency region of the spectral densities obtained is only associated with protein fluctuations; the usage of BOMD, however, also captures the low-frequency contributions arising from slow intramolecular vibrations of the pigment molecules themselves. Notably, this behavior is consistently observed for both the flexible B800 and the more rigid B850 rings in light-harvesting 2 (LH2) complexes of purple bacteria, as well as in the Fenna-Matthews-Olson (FMO) complex of green sulfur bacteria. Interestingly, we also find that the spectral densities of the pigments in the B850 ring of LH2 are not influenced by the environment, i.e., the gaps between ground and first excited state are not changed significantly by the fluctuations of the protein environment.

</details>

### [65] [Cosmological discrete self-similarity in primordial black hole formation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21520)
*Luis E. Padilla,Tomohiro Harada,Ethan Milligan,David Mulryne*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本论文通过广义相对论数值模拟，证明在膨胀宇宙背景下的原初黑洞（primordial black hole）形成过程中，离散自相似性（discrete self-similarity, DSS）仍然存在，并详细刻画了其质量标度关系中的对数周期振荡特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前离散自相似性（DSS）仅在渐近平直（asymptotically flat）系统中被研究，其在膨胀宇宙背景下的原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）形成中是否存续尚不清楚，而这对原初黑洞的质量谱和诱导引力波（induced gravitational waves）谱有重要影响。

Method: 在弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃克（Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker, FLRW）宇宙中，对无质量标量场（massless scalar field）的坍缩进行完全相对论性数值模拟，将临界 regime 解析到 |p−p_c|∼10^(−8) 的精度；同时分析高斯型和分段有理曲率型（piecewise rational curvature profiles）两类初始数据族。

Result: 在原初黑洞质量标度关系中发现清晰的对数周期振荡（log-periodic oscillations），其振荡结构在峰谷不对称性上比渐近平直情形更显著。两类初始数据族得到的临界指数（critical exponents）和DSS周期略有差异，但在误差范围内大体一致。

Conclusion: 离散自相似性在膨胀宇宙背景下的原初黑洞形成中依然存在，这导致原初黑洞质量谱呈现特征性的对数周期调制，进而可能影响原初黑洞丰度和诱导引力波（induced gravitational waves）谱。

Abstract: We demonstrate that discrete self-similarity (DSS), originally discovered in the collapse of a massless scalar field in an asymptotically flat system, survives in primordial black hole (PBH) formation within an expanding cosmological background. Using fully relativistic numerical simulations of massless scalar-field collapse in an Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker universe, we resolve the critical regime down to $|p-p_c|\sim 10^{-8}$, where $p$ and $p_c$ respectively are a parameter of the family of initial data and its threshold value, and find clear log-periodic oscillations in the PBH mass scaling relation. The detailed structure of these oscillations differs from that previously reported in the asymptotically flat case, exhibiting a more pronounced asymmetry between peaks and troughs. Analyzing two distinct families of initial data (Gaussian and piecewise rational curvature profiles), we find critical exponents and DSS periods that differ slightly but are broadly consistent within uncertainties. The presence of DSS implies characteristic log-periodic modulations in the PBH mass spectrum, with potential consequences for PBH abundances and the spectrum of induced gravitational waves.

### [66] [Recovering cosmological parameters from the mock gravitational wave data of the Einstein Telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25307)
*Pinaki Roy,Tomasz Bulik*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了利用第三代引力波探测器爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope, ET）探测到的双黑洞并合事件来约束宇宙学参数（哈勃常数$H_0$和物质密度参数$\Omega_{\rm m}$）的能力。通过生成模拟引力波事件目录，提出了一种基于固有啁啾质量谱（intrinsic chirp mass spectrum）的快速有效方法，并发现一年观测可将$H_0$约束至1%的不确定性，将$\Omega_{\rm m}$约束至4%的不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope, ET）作为第三代引力波探测器，灵敏度比先进LIGO（advanced LIGO）提升十倍，能够观测到红移高达10的恒星质量双黑洞并合事件，具有重要的宇宙学（cosmography）应用潜力。因此需要研究如何利用ET的观测数据有效约束宇宙学参数。

Method: 生成爱因斯坦望远镜的模拟引力波事件目录（mock gravitational wave event catalog），提出一种利用双黑洞固有啁啾质量谱（intrinsic chirp mass spectrum）来推断哈勃常数$H_0$或物质密度参数$\Omega_{\rm m}$的简单、有效且快速的技术，并在标准宇宙学模型（standard model of cosmology）下检验该方法的有效性。

Result: 若仅约束$H_0$，至少需要一年的ET观测才能达到1%的不确定性；在相同观测时长下，$\Omega_{\rm m}$可被约束至4%的不确定性。作为独立运行的仪器（standalone instrument），ET探测到的引力波频谱警笛（GW spectral sirens）可以约束哈勃常数。

Conclusion: 爱因斯坦望远镜作为独立探测器，能够通过引力波频谱警笛有效约束哈勃常数$H_0$和物质密度参数$\Omega_{\rm m}$，其中$H_0$的约束精度可达1%（一年观测），展示了ET在宇宙学参数测量中的重要潜力。

Abstract: Einstein Telescope (ET) is a third-generation gravitational wave (GW) detector with tenfold better sensitivity compared to the advanced LIGO detectors. It will be capable of observing copious stellar mass binary black hole mergers upto a redshift of 10 which will make it especially useful for cosmography. We generate a mock gravitational wave event catalog for the Einstein Telescope and show the recoverability of either the Hubble constant ($H_0$) or the matter density parameter ($Ω_{\rm m}$). We present a simple, effective and fast technique for inferring $H_0$ (or $Ω_{\rm m}$) using the intrinsic chirp mass spectrum of black hole binaries, and investigate the efficacy of the method assuming the standard model of cosmology. If only $H_0$ has to be constrained, we find that at least one year of ET's observation will be required to achieve 1% uncertainty. With the same amount of observation, $Ω_{\rm m}$ can be constrained to within 4\% uncertainty. With ET operating as a standalone instrument, we show that the GW spectral sirens detected by it can constrain the Hubble constant.

</details>


### [67] [Generalizing the CPL Parametrization through Dark Sector Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25373)
*Mikel Artola,Ruth Lazkoz,Vincenzo Salzano*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了一系列相互作用暗能量（interacting dark energy, IDE）模型，采用含常数和动力学耦合参数的背景相互作用核 $Q = 3H(δ+ ηa)ρ_\mathrm{de}$，结合DESI DR2、Pantheon+ 和 Planck+ACT 等观测数据进行了约束。对于常数耦合模型，发现与ΛCDM的偏离在2.7σ–2.9σ水平；动力学耦合下显著性降至1.3σ–1.5σ。贝叶斯模型对比显示，没有任何IDE模型在统计上优于标准ΛCDM模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准ΛCDM模型虽然在宇宙学上成功，但其暗能量成分的本质仍未得到解释。相互作用暗能量（IDE）模型通过引入暗物质与暗能量之间的非引力耦合，为理解暗能量演化提供了可能的物理机制，因此有必要系统检验这类模型是否受观测数据支持。

Method: 采用 CPL 参数化 $w_\mathrm{de} = w_0 + w_a(1-a)$ 描述暗能量状态方程，并定义背景相互作用核 $Q = 3H(δ+ ηa)ρ_\mathrm{de}$ 来刻画暗物质与暗能量之间的非引力耦合，该核允许耦合参数为常数或动力学形式。推导出暗物质与暗能量密度的闭合解析表达式，并使用 DESI DR2 重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillations）、Pantheon$+$ Ia 型超新星以及 Planck$+$ACT 压缩宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background）联合似然函数进行观测约束。

Result: 常数耦合模型显示出与ΛCDM的参量偏离，显著性为 2.7σ–2.9σ；而采用动力学耦合时，显著性下降至 1.3σ–1.5σ。贝叶斯模型比较（Bayesian model comparison）表明，所有被测试的IDE模型均未在统计上优于标准ΛCDM模型。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，在报告宇宙学关于暗能量演化和相互作用的论断时，必须同时提供贝叶斯证据（Bayesian evidence）和传统的频率论最大似然分析（frequentist maximum-likelihood analysis），以确保结论的可靠性。

Abstract: We investigate a hierarchy of interacting dark energy (IDE) models featuring a non-gravitational coupling between dark matter and dark energy. Specifically, we examine scenarios where the background interaction kernel, $Q = 3H(δ+ ηa)ρ_\mathrm{de}$, allows for both constant and dynamical coupling parameters. Adopting the CPL parametrization for the dark energy equation of state, $w_\mathrm{de} = w_0 + w_a(1-a)$, we derive closed analytical expressions for the energy densities of dark matter and dark energy. Afterwards, we obtain observational constraints using joint combinations of DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillations, Pantheon$+$ Type Ia supernovae, and Planck$+$ACT compressed cosmic microwave background likelihoods. For constant coupling models, we find parametric deviations from $Λ$ ranging from $2.7σ$ to $2.9σ$; however, for interactions with dynamical couplings, these significances are reduced to $1.3σ$--$1.5σ$. Ultimately, our Bayesian model comparison reveals that no investigated IDE scenario is statistically preferred over the concordance $Λ$CDM model. These results highlight the necessity of reporting Bayesian evidence alongside conventional frequentist maximum-likelihood analyses to ensure robust cosmological claims concerning dark energy evolution and interaction.

</details>


### [68] [Fast radio burst dispersion is an unbiased tracer of matter on large scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25828)
*Shion Andrew,Haochen Wang,Kiyoshi Masui,Josh Borrow,Calvin Leung,Ryan Raikman,Matthieu Schaller,Joop Schaye,James M. Sullivan*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文论证了快速射电暴（FRB）的色散量在宇宙大尺度结构上是物质分布的无偏示踪物，其电子偏置因子（electron bias）在百分量级内可被约束，并引入了一个与反馈物理无关的重子模拟量$B_8$。FRB色散有望成为继弱引力透镜和红移空间畸变之后，又一种大尺度物质分布的无偏探测手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 快速射电暴（fast radio bursts, FRBs）的色散（dispersion）测量的是自由电子的柱密度，可追踪包含超过90%重子（baryon）的弥散电离气体。尽管文献中长期假设FRB色散场是大尺度结构（large-scale structure）上物质分布的无偏示踪物，但这一假设直到近期才被形式化。本文旨在严格论证该假设的物理基础，量化其修正量级，并提出FRB色散在宇宙学上的新应用。

Method: 基于重子质量守恒（baryon-mass conservation）论证总重子场具有单位线性偏置（unit linear bias），FRB色散场继承该偏置，仅受恒星和中性气体组分的微小修正。利用现有的星系巡天和21厘米巡天数据将这些修正约束在百分量级，并通过FLAMINGO流体动力学模拟（hydrodynamical simulations）验证在不同反馈方案下电子偏置因子（electron bias）的变化也在百分量级。

Result: 在线性尺度上，FRB色散-星系交叉功率谱（cross-power spectrum）可直接约束$B_8 \equiv \sigma_8(\Omega_b/0.05)^{1/2}$，这是$S_8$的重子模拟（baryonic analog），且与反馈物理（feedback physics）无关。由于每个FRB色散方差中的绝大部分是宇宙学信号而非噪声，约$10^5$个局域化FRB可匹配约$10^8$个弱引力透镜（weak lensing）星系形状测量的统计能力。

Conclusion: FRB色散有望成为继弱引力透镜和红移空间畸变（redshift-space distortions）之后，又一种在大尺度上物质分布的无偏示踪物（unbiased tracer），为宇宙学探测提供新的独立途径。

Abstract: The dispersion of fast radio bursts (FRBs) measures the column density of free electrons, tracing the diffuse ionized gas that contains more than $90\%$ of all baryons. On linear scales the FRB dispersion field is an approximately unbiased tracer of the matter distribution, an idea long assumed in the FRB large-scale structure literature and recently formalized by Zhou and Zhang [arXiv:2510.11022]. This follows from baryon-mass conservation, which forces the total baryon field to have unit linear bias, with dispersion inheriting this bias up to small corrections from the stellar and neutral-gas components. We show these corrections can be bounded at the percent level using existing galaxy and 21 cm surveys, and confirm with the FLAMINGO hydrodynamical simulations that the electron bias varies at the percent level across a wide range of feedback prescriptions. The dispersion-galaxy cross-power spectrum at linear scales directly constrains $B_8 \equiv σ_8(Ω_b/0.05)^{1/2}$, a baryonic analog of $S_8$, independently of feedback physics. Because most of the per-object variance in dispersion is cosmological signal rather than noise, $\sim\!10^5$ localized FRBs can match the statistical power of $\sim\!10^8$ weak-lensing galaxy shape measurements. FRB dispersion thus joins weak lensing and redshift-space distortions as a new unbiased tracer of matter on large scales.

</details>

# astro-ph.SR [[Back]](#toc)

### [69] [The Singular Behaviour of Ambipolar Diffusion Revealed by 1D Cartesian Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25013)
*F. Moreno-Insertis,E. R. Priest,D. Nóbrega-Siverio*

Main category: astro-ph.SR

TL;DR: 该论文通过一维（1D）笛卡尔坐标系下的解析与数值方法，研究了磁场零点（null point）附近的双极扩散（ambipolar diffusion）非线性特征模，提出了可检验磁流体力学（MHD）代码中双极扩散求解器准确性的自相似解（self-similar solution）测试方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在实现三个目标：(a) 研究零点附近的一维笛卡尔双极扩散；(b) 刻画双极扩散的非线性本征模（nonlinear eigenmodes）；(c) 为MHD代码中的双极扩散求解器提供检验方法。

Method: 采用直接分析法求解双极扩散的解析解；利用相平面技术（phase-plane techniques）求解自相似解（self-similar solution）的常微分方程（ODE）以研究本征模；并求解一般含时一维问题。此外，使用Bifrost代码复现本征模行为以验证求解器准确性。

Result: (a) 发现了驻点流动（stagnation-point flow）解，磁场在外部对流区、内部双极扩散区（磁剖面B ∝ x^(1/3)）和最内侧欧姆区（B ∝ x）之间具有均匀磁通量传输率；(b) 双极扩散问题同时存在对称和反对称本征模解，在内部零点处形成尖锐电流片（current sheet），高阶级或受扰模随时间演化至最低允许本征模；(c) Bifrost代码以极高精度复现了本征模行为。

Conclusion: 存在驻点型构型，其中双极扩散在内层传输磁通量，充当外部对流与零点周围欧姆扩散核心之间的中介。自相似解可作为检验MHD代码中双极扩散求解器的强有效性测试。

Abstract: Aims. We seek to (a) study 1D Cartesian ambipolar diffusion near null points; (b) characterise the nonlinear eigenmodes for ambipolar diffusion; (c) propose tests for ambipolar diffusion solvers in MHD codes.
  Methods. (a) Direct analysis is used to find analytical solutions for ambipolar diffusion. (b) To study the eigenmodes, we solve the ODE for self-similar solutions of the 1D ambipolar diffusion equation using phase-plane techniques. We also solve the general time-dependent 1D problem for initial conditions of interest. (c) We test the Bifrost code by trying to reproduce the behaviour of the eigenmodes.
  Results. (a) A stagnation-point flow solution was found with a uniform flux transfer rate across three regions: an external advection region; an internal ambipolar diffusion region with magnetic profile B propto x**(1/3); and an innermost Ohmic region with B propto x; in the latter, flux annihilation occurs at a rate imposed by the advection. (b) Both symmetric and antisymmetric eigenmode solutions to the ambipolar diffusion problem are found with sharp current sheets at the internal nulls. The time evolution of the eigenmodes (pure or perturbed) is probed, showing how higher-order eigenmodes, or perturbed ones, evolve in time towards the lowest-order allowable eigenmodes. (c) The Bifrost code reproduces the behaviour of the eigenmodes with excellent accuracy.
  Conclusions. Stagnation-point configurations exist with ambipolar diffusion carrying magnetic flux in an inner layer and serving as an intermediary between the external advection and an Ohmic-diffusion core around the null. Our tests are compatible with the hypothesis that zero-flux higher harmonics of the self-similar equation evolve toward either the first symmetric or antisymmetric harmonic. The self-similar solutions can serve as strong tests for ambipolar diffusion solvers in general MHD codes.

</details>

### [70] [Quantitative Analyticity for Lyapunov Exponents of Random Products of Matrices with Explicit Polydiscs and Cauchy Coefficient Bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25168)
*Abdoulaye Thiam*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文通过单个Kato摄动论证，在复化马尔可夫算子（complexified Markov operator）上证明了随机矩阵乘积的最大李亚普诺夫指数（top Lyapunov exponent）关于概率权重与矩阵系数的实解析性，并给出了七条定量结论，包括显式的全纯圆盘半径、柯西界（Cauchy bounds）、以及边界衰减率，并推广至马尔可夫链驱动的上圈（cocycles）和子李亚普诺夫指数（sub-top Lyapunov exponents）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有定理（Peres定理和Bezerra-Sánchez-Tall定理）仅证明了李亚普诺夫指数关于参数的解析性，但缺乏显式的定量刻画（如收敛半径和系数的显式界）。本文旨在填补这一空白，通过一个统一的Kato摄动框架给出显式封闭形式的定量结果。

Method: 方法核心是对投影空间（projective space）上Hölder函数的复化马尔可夫算子实施Kato摄动论证（Kato perturbation argument），将解析性问题转化为算子谱（spectrum）的扰动分析，从而得到显式的全纯圆盘半径、泰勒系数（Taylor coefficients）的柯西界以及边界多项式衰减率。

Result: 获得七个主要定理：(i) 概率权重p的显式全纯圆盘；(ii) 泰勒系数的封闭形式柯西界；(iii) 权重与矩阵系数的联合解析性及显式半径；(iv) 推广至马尔可夫链驱动的上圈，半径显式依赖于链的谱间隙（spectral gap）；(v) 在谱间隙衰减假设下，边界处显式的多项式衰减率；(vi) 通过Fubini-Study度规推广至任意维度d≥2；(vii) Grassmann变体给出部分和Λ_k及每个子指数的定量解析性。圆盘半径在Kato类中达到方法最优，Bernstein型结果证明柯西增长α!·M_*/r_*^{|α|}在常数意义上是最优的。

Conclusion: 本文建立的定量解析性框架在方法论的Kato类中是最优的，且通过数值实例与姊妹篇的Hölder估计建立了联系，为随机矩阵乘积的李亚普诺夫指数分析提供了系统性的显式工具。

Abstract: The top Lyapunov exponent $λ_+(A, p)$ of a random product of matrices in $\mathrm{GL}(d, \mathbb{R})$, $d \geq 2$, with simple top spectrum, depends real-analytically on the probability weights $p$ and the matrix coefficients $A$. We establish a quantitative form of this analyticity through a single Kato perturbation argument on the complexified Markov operator on Hölder functions on projective space, yielding seven main theorems with explicit closed-form constants: (i) an explicit polydisc of holomorphy for $p \mapsto λ_+(A, p)$ in $\mathbb{C}^N$, giving the quantitative form of the Peres and Bezerra-Sánchez-Tall analyticity theorem; (ii) closed-form Cauchy bounds on its Taylor coefficients; (iii) joint analyticity in the weights $p$ and the matrix entries $A$, with explicit radii in both; (iv) an extension to Markov-chain driven cocycles, with polydisc radius explicit in the chain spectral gap; (v) explicit polynomial boundary-decay rates as $p$ approaches $\partial Δ_N$, conditional on a spectral-gap-decay hypothesis; (vi) extension to $\mathrm{GL}(d, \mathbb{R})$ for all $d \geq 2$ via the Fubini-Study metric; and (vii) a Grassmannian variant giving quantitative analyticity of the partial sums $Λ_k = λ_1 + \cdots + λ_k$ under strong $k$-irreducibility, hence of each individual sub-top Lyapunov exponent. The polydisc radius is method-optimal within the Kato class, and a Bernstein-type result shows the Cauchy growth $α! \cdot M_*/r_*^{|α|}$ is sharp up to constants. A two-matrix example with numerical values connects the bounds to the Hölder estimates of the companion paper Thiam (Nov. 2025).

</details>


### [71] [Numerical Investigations of Stable Dynamics in the Presence of Ghosts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25635)
*Jax Wysong,Samara Overvaag,Hyun Lim,Jung-Han Kimn*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究了含鬼影自由度（ghost degrees of freedom）的经典场论非线性动力学，发现在(1+1)和(2+1)维闵可夫斯基时空中，鬼影-正常系统可呈现长期动态有界演化；不稳定性由非线性谱能量传递介导，而非瞬时失控；特定势函数（如提升的φ⁶相互作用）可产生瞬态亚稳态（metastable）区域，部分抑制鬼影诱导的增长。结果揭示鬼影模式的动力学后果高度依赖于色散、非线性和相位结构，展现出比通常假设更丰富的亚稳性景观。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典场论中鬼影自由度（ghost degrees of freedom）通常被认为会导致瞬时失控性不稳定性，本文旨在系统探究此类系统在非线性动力学下的实际演化行为，检验其是否可能存在长期稳定或亚稳态（metastable）演化，从而挑战传统认知。

Method: 采用时空有限元公式化方法（spacetime finite element formulation），对(1+1)和(2+1)维闵可夫斯基时空中包含两个具有相反动能项（opposite kinetic terms）的耦合标量场（scalar fields）的系统进行系统性数值研究，覆盖广泛初始数据类别。

Result: 鬼影-正常系统可展现出长期动态有界演化，稳定性强烈受控于频谱含量（spectral content）和振幅；紫外主导（ultraviolet-dominated）和小振幅构型的稳定时间显著长于红外主导（infrared-dominated）或大振幅构型；不稳定性由非线性谱能量转移（nonlinear spectral energy transfer）介导；非线性自相互作用具有双重作用，某些势函数（如提升的φ⁶相互作用）可生成振荡子状结构（oscillon-like structures），产生瞬态亚稳态（transient metastable）区域，部分抑制鬼影诱导的增长。

Conclusion: 鬼影模式在经典场论中的动力学后果敏感地依赖于色散（dispersion）、非线性（nonlinearity）和相位结构（phase structure），展现出比通常假设更丰富的亚稳性景观（metastability landscape），表明传统关于鬼影必然导致瞬时失控的认知需要重新审视。

Abstract: We explore the nonlinear dynamics of classical field theories containing ghost degrees of freedom, focusing on two coupled scalar fields with opposite kinetic terms in (1+1) and (2+1) dimensional Minkowski spacetime. Using a spacetime finite element formulation, we perform a systematic numerical study across a broad class of initial data. We find that ghost-normal systems can exhibit long-lived, dynamically bounded evolution over extended time intervals, with stability strongly controlled by spectral content and amplitude. Ultraviolet-dominated and small-amplitude configurations remain stable significantly longer than infrared-dominated or large-amplitude data, indicating that instability is mediated by nonlinear spectral energy transfer rather than instantaneous runaway. Nonlinear self-interactions play a dual role: while they can accelerate energy exchange between sectors, certain potentials, including a lifted $φ^6$ interaction supporting oscillon-like structures, generate transient metastable regimes that partially suppress ghost-induced growth. Our results demonstrate that the dynamical consequences of ghost modes in classical field theory depend sensitively on dispersion, nonlinearity, and phase structure, revealing a richer metastability landscape than commonly assumed.

</details>

### [72] [The conformal dimension of the Brownian tree is one](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25769)
*Jason Miller,Yi Tian*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了布朗树（Brownian tree）的共形维数（conformal dimension）等于其拓扑维数（topological dimension）1，从而确定了这一重要拟对称不变量（quasisymmetric invariant）的具体数值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 布朗树作为离散随机树模型的普适标度极限（universal scaling limit），其几何性质具有基础重要性。共形维数是度量空间的关键拟对称不变量，但布朗树的共形维数此前未知，存在一个介于拓扑维数与豪斯多夫维数（Hausdorff dimension）之间的区间需要确定。

Method: 论文通过严格的数学分析，将共形维数的下界与拓扑维数进行匹配，证明布朗树的共形维数恰好等于其拓扑维数1。

Result: 布朗树的共形维数为1，与其拓扑维数相等。

Conclusion: 布朗树的共形维数达到其可能的最小值（即拓扑维数），表明在该拟对称不变量意义下，布朗树具有极值性质。

Abstract: The Brownian tree, also known as the continuum random tree, is a canonical random compact, geodesic $\mathbf R$-tree that arises as the universal scaling limit for numerous models of discrete random trees. A key quasisymmetric invariant of a metric space is its conformal dimension, defined as the infimum of the Hausdorff dimensions over all quasisymmetrically equivalent spaces. This value is always bounded below by the space's topological dimension and above by its Hausdorff dimension. In the present paper, we prove that the conformal dimension of the Brownian tree is $1$, matching its topological dimension.

</details>

### [73] [The Lieb-Liniger model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24784)
*Zoran Ristivojevic*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文综述了Lieb-Liniger模型（描述一维玻色子接触相互作用的可积模型）的Bethe ansatz精确解及其微扰结果，重点推导了物理量随相互作用参数变化的显式表达式，强调了各物理量之间的精确关系，并包含若干新结果，如强相互作用下基态能量级数的收敛性、高能激发谱以及边界能的计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该模型是一维可积多体系统的典范，但仍有若干物理量（如基态能量级数收敛性、高能激发谱、边界能）尚未被系统解析；综述旨在整合已知精确结果与微扰展开，并填补这些空白。

Method: 基于Bethe ansatz（贝特拟设）方法求解Lieb-Liniger模型的精确本征态与本征值；结合微扰理论（perturbation theory）进行强、弱相互作用展开；利用热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下的积分方程推导物理量的显式表达式。

Result: 给出了基态能量、激发谱等物理量随相互作用参数变化的显式解析形式；证明了强相互作用下基态能量级数的收敛性；计算了高能激发谱（high-energy excitation spectrum）及边界能（boundary energy）。

Conclusion: Lieb-Liniger模型作为一维可积多体系统的范例，Bethe ansatz提供了一套完备的精确框架；文中获得的新结果进一步深化了对强相互作用极限、高能动力学以及边界效应的理解，并为冷原子实验提供了定量比对的理论依据。

Abstract: The Lieb-Liniger model describes one-dimensional bosons with contact interactions. This many-body system admits an exact solution in terms of the Bethe ansatz. Some of the exact and perturbative results for this model are reviewed. Particular attention is devoted to the explicit evaluation, in terms of the interaction parameter, of physical quantities that can be formally exactly extracted from the Bethe ansatz solution. Another goal of this review is to stress exact relations between various quantities. The technical developments are explained in detail. The most relevant experimental realisations of the studied problems are eventually discussed. This review also contains several new results such as the study of convergence of the ground-state energy series at strong interactions, the excitation spectrum at high energies, and the evaluation of the boundary energy.

</details>


### [74] [Uncovering Exotic Paired States in the 2D Spin-Imbalanced Fermi Gas with Neural Wave Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24883)
*Wan Tong Lou,Gino Cassella,Andres Perez Fadon,Halvard Sutterud,David Pfau,James S. Spencer,Johannes Knolle,W. M. C. Foulkes*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本研究利用神经网络变分蒙特卡洛方法（neural network variational Monte Carlo）结合AGPs FermiNet Ansatz，绘制了二维自旋不平衡费米气体（2D spin-imbalanced Fermi gas）在零温下的相图，观测到Fulde-Ferrell-Larkin-Ovchinnikov（FFLO）相、极化超流相（polarised superfluid）、相分离以及一种由库珀对晶体（crystal of Cooper pairs）构成的奇特相位，并解释了动量空间中的空穴现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维自旋不平衡费米气体在短程吸引相互作用下的零温相图尚未被充分理解，尤其是中间相互作用强度下的新奇量子相，需要更精确的数值方法进行研究。

Method: 采用新近发展的神经网络变分蒙特卡洛方法（neural network variational Monte Carlo method），并使用AGPs FermiNet Ansatz作为变分波函数。

Result: 在弱相互作用的BCS极限（BCS limit）中观测到Fulde-Ferrell-Larkin-Ovchinnikov（FFLO）相；在强相互作用的BEC极限（BEC limit）中观测到极化超流相（polarised superfluid）。强相互作用下，少数自旋的动量密度在未被配对的多数量自旋电子占据的动量空间区域中几乎降至零。极强相互作用下发生相分离（phase separation），形成玻色子对区域和未配对的多数自旋粒子区域。中间相互作用强度下，系统出现平移对称性破缺（translational symmetry breaking），形成一种由库珀对晶体（crystal of Cooper pairs）嵌入未配对多数自旋费米流体中的奇异相。

Conclusion: 为库珀对晶体相的形成提供了可能的解释，阐明了紧束缚对（tightly bound pairs）在动量空间中产生密度空穴的起源，并讨论了该方法对未来研究方向的开辟意义。

Abstract: We study the zero-temperature phase diagram of the 2D spin-imbalanced Fermi gas with short-ranged attractive interactions using the recently developed neural network variational Monte Carlo method with the AGPs FermiNet Ansatz. The Fulde-Ferrell-Larkin-Ovchinnikov phase is observed in the weakly interacting BCS limit and a polarised superfluid is seen in the strongly interacting BEC limit. When the interactions are strong, the minority-spin momentum density is reduced almost to zero in the momentum-space region occupied by the unpaired majority-spin electrons. When the interactions are very strong, phase separation occurs, with regions containing bosonic pairs and unpaired regions occupied by the remaining majority-spin particles. In addition, we observe translational symmetry breaking at intermediate interaction strengths, where the system forms an exotic crystal of Cooper pairs in a Fermi fluid of unpaired majority-spin particles. We provide a possible explanation for the formation of the crystalline phase, explain the origins of the k-space momentum-density hole when the pairs are tightly bound, and discuss how our approach opens new directions for future work.

</details>


### [75] [Phase diagram of a dual-species Rydberg atom ladder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24889)
*Lei-Yi-Nan Liu,Shi-Rong Peng,Ze-Yuan Huang,Xing-Man Wei,Yun-Han Zou,Su Yi,Jian Cui*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用大规模密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）计算，研究了一维双物种里德伯原子梯子（dual-species Rydberg atom ladder）的基态相图，发现了无序相、多种有序相（具有 $\mathbb{Z}_2$、$\mathbb{Z}_3$、$\mathbb{Z}_4$ 对称性）以及浮游相（floating phase），并揭示了单物种系统中不存在的有序区间平滑交叉现象和多临界点（multi-critical point）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双物种里德伯原子阵列（dual-species Rydberg atom arrays）通过引入竞争性相互作用尺度和增强的量子涨落，能够产生超出均匀单物种平台的新奇量子现象。本文旨在系统研究该体系在基态相图中的新奇有序相、交叉行为（crossover）和多临界点。

Method: 采用大规模密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法，对一维双物种里德伯原子梯子模型进行基态相图的计算与分析。

Result: 研究发现无序相、具有 $\mathbb{Z}_2$、$\mathbb{Z}_3$ 和 $\mathbb{Z}_4$ 对称性的多种有序相，以及具有不可公度波矢（incommensurate wave vectors）和代数衰减关联（algebraically decaying correlations）的浮游相。观察到不同 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 有序区间存在平滑交叉（smooth crossover），并在 $\mathbb{Z}_2 \otimes \mathbb{Z}_2$ 与 $\mathbb{Z}_3 \otimes \mathbb{Z}_3$ 有序相边界处发现了一个多临界点，涉及伊辛（Ising）、手征（chiral）和一阶（first-order）相变线的交汇。

Conclusion: 双物种里德伯原子阵列是实现单物种架构中无法获得的交叉物理（crossover physics）和多临界行为（multi-critical behavior）的独特平台。

Abstract: Dual-species Rydberg atom arrays extend single-species platforms by introducing competing interaction scales and enhanced quantum fluctuations, enabling phenomena beyond homogeneous settings. In this work, we study the ground-state phase diagram of a one-dimensional dual-species Rydberg atom ladder using large-scale density-matrix renormalization group calculations. We identify disordered phases, multiple ordered phases with $\mathbb{Z}_2$, $\mathbb{Z}_3$, and $\mathbb{Z}_4$ symmetry, as well as floating phases characterized by incommensurate wave vectors and algebraically decaying correlations. Importantly, we observe a smooth crossover between distinct $\mathbb{Z}_2$-ordered regimes, reflecting a reorganization of low-energy degrees of freedom rather than a true phase transition, which is absent in single-species Rydberg arrays. We further uncover a multi-critical point at the boundary between the $\mathbb{Z}_2 \otimes \mathbb{Z}_2$ and $\mathbb{Z}_3 \otimes \mathbb{Z}_3$ ordered phases, where Ising, chiral, and first-order transition lines intersect. Our results demonstrate that dual-species Rydberg atom arrays provide a unique platform for realizing crossover physics and multi-critical behavior inaccessible in single-species architectures.

</details>


### [76] [Magnetic quantum phases of spin-orbit-coupled anisotropic dipolar bosons in square lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25694)
*Nitin Kaloya,Kuldeep Suthar*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过Gutzwiller平均场分析，研究了二维正方形晶格中各向异性偶极相互作用下的自旋-轨道耦合玻色子，揭示了有限动量超流、超固相以及多种新奇量子相，特别是在魔角附近出现的条纹-棋盘态量子相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）与各向异性偶极相互作用（anisotropic dipolar interaction）共同作用下，软核玻色子（soft-core bosons）在正方晶格中的新奇量子相行为及其相变机制。

Method: 采用位点退耦的Gutzwiller ansatz和平均场退耦理论（site-decoupled Gutzwiller ansatz and mean-field decoupling theory），计算相图并研究磁偶极子相对极化轴的倾斜效应。

Result: 发现棋盘格有限动量相在魔角倾斜角（magic tilt angle）处转变为条纹相；在较小倾斜角下出现电荷密度波相与可压缩有限动量相共存；在强自旋-轨道耦合下出现相位扭曲超固相与超流相；在较大倾斜角下发生相位扭曲态与相位条纹态之间的条纹序转变；引入位点间交叉关联后得到密度关联相、晶格诱导超固相及铁磁量子相。

Conclusion: 本工作揭示了有限动量晶体相的新奇行为，并为在量子气体实验中观测这些相提供了参数空间。

Abstract: We examine the two-dimensional spin-orbit-coupled bosons in the presence of an anisotropic dipolar interaction in square lattices. The spin-orbit coupling leads to finite-momentum superfluid and supersolid states, while the nearest-neighbour interaction induces crystalline characteristics in the quantum phases of soft-core bosons. We employ site-decoupled Gutzwiller ansatz and mean-field decoupling theory to obtain the phase diagrams and investigate the effects of the tilt of magnetic dipoles with respect to the polarization axis. Our study reveals the intriguing quantum phase transition of checkerboard finite-momentum phase-twisted and phase-stripe states into their stripe counterparts at a magic tilt angle, at which the off-site interaction along one of the directions becomes zero. At smaller tilt angles, the checkerboard charge-density-wave phase intervened by two compressible finite-momentum phases, and at strong spin-orbit coupling strengths, the phase-twisted supersolid and superfluid phases emerge. At larger tilt angles, a transition between the striped order of phase-twisted states and phase-stripe states occurs. The inclusion of off-site inter-component correlation leads to density-correlated phases, lattice-induced supersolid, and ferromagnetic quantum phases. Our study highlights novel finite-momentum crystal phases of spin-orbit-coupled dipolar bosons and provides a parameter space to observe them in quantum gas experiments.

### [77] [Bell Test of Photons from Electron-Positron Annihilation via POVM-based Compton Polarimetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25034)

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文开发了基于正算子值测度（POVM）的康普顿偏振测量框架，用于建模高能光子极化测量，证明通过多次相互作用序列可使测量逐渐收敛于理想投影测量，从而首次实现利用MeV湮灭光子的极化纠缠违反CHSH不等式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子-正电子湮灭产生的伽马射线光子之间的量子纠缠理论上应是最大的，但由于缺乏适用于高能光子的理想投影极化测量方案，MeV能级湮灭光子的极化纠缠尚未得到实验确证。

Method: 采用正算子值测度（POVM）形式论对高能光子的康普顿偏振测量进行建模，并将POVM描述扩展到重复相互作用的序列中。

Result: 随着相互作用次数增加，测量过程逐渐收敛于线性极化的理想投影测量，这种测量清晰度的渐进提升使得实验上违反CHSH不等式成为可能。

Conclusion: 本文建立的框架为高能光子极化纠缠的实验验证提供了可行路径，有望首次确证MeV湮灭光子之间的极化纠缠。

Abstract: Quantum entanglement between gamma-ray photons emitted following electron-positron annihilation is expected to be maximal and may be characterized via non-classical polarization correlations. However, this is difficult to verify experimentally because there are no established schemes that approach ideal projective-polarization measurements for high-energy photons. Hence, polarization entanglement between MeV-scale annihilation photons has not yet been conclusively demonstrated. We develop here a framework that models polarization measurements of high-energy photons via Compton polarimetry, employing the formalism of positive operator-valued measures (POVMs). We extend the POVM description to sequences of repeated interactions and show that the measurement converges toward an ideal projective measurement of linear polarization as the number of interactions increases. We demonstrate that this progressive improvement in measurement sharpness can enable the experimental violation of CHSH inequalities.

### [78] [Sector-dominant graph-local drivers for path-window barrier Hamiltonians on the Boolean hypercube](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25494)
*Takiko Sasaki,Tetsuji Tokihiro*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在布尔超立方体（Boolean hypercube）上，利用基于单调格雷码（monotone Gray-code）的扇区/路径坐标构造图局部驱动（graph-local drivers），用于有限尺寸绝热态制备（finite-size adiabatic state preparation）。实验表明，结合扇区、路径窗口和小横向场分量的混合驱动，可以显著提升中心势垒实例的基态保真度，且扇区保持骨架（sector-preserving skeleton）是主要贡献因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在布尔超立方体上利用图局部驱动进行绝热态制备时，如何通过扇区/路径坐标构建高效驱动，并检验其对不同目标哈密顿量（target Hamiltonian）的性能提升。

Method: 使用与单调格雷码代表元相关的扇区/路径坐标构造图局部驱动；对普通对角代价横向场退火（transverse-field annealing）作为基线进行测试；针对非对角目标哈密顿量，构建混合驱动（hybrid drivers）——结合扇区、路径窗口和小横向场分量；并通过重现运行、随机化及消融控制（ablation controls）分析各组件贡献。

Result: 普通横向场退火未展现鲁棒优势（negative result）。混合驱动在中心势垒实例中显著提升最终基态保真度（fidelity），代表值达0.9799（固定参数(w,α,ε)=(8,0.50,0.15)）。扇区保持骨架为保真度提升的主要贡献者，严格一位补全（strict one-bit completion）起次要细化作用。性能改进具有目标类依赖性。

Conclusion: 基于扇区/路径坐标的混合图局部驱动可在特定目标类中提升绝热态制备的基态保真度，但改进效果依赖目标哈密顿量的几何结构。研究提供了完整代码、验证证书及重现脚本，确保有限尺寸结果的可追溯性。

Abstract: We study finite-size adiabatic state preparation on Boolean hypercubes using graph-local drivers built from sector/path coordinates related to monotone Gray-code representatives. The construction is not presented as a new all-$n$ Gray-code existence theorem; rather, it provides finite representatives, explicitly checked through the cases used in the numerical experiments, for testing problem-dependent graph-local drivers. For ordinary diagonal-cost transverse-field annealing, the ordering does not yield a robust advantage, and we include this negative result as a baseline. For non-diagonal target Hamiltonians whose geometry is expressed in the same sector/path coordinates, hybrid drivers combining sector, path-window, and small transverse-field components can substantially improve the final ground-state fidelity in centered barrier instances. Reproduction runs from the accompanying code confirm a representative centered original-window barrier value of approximately \(0.9799\) for the fixed-control hybrid parameters \((w,α,ε)=(8,0.50,0.15)\), while also showing that the improvement is target-class dependent. Randomized and ablation controls indicate that the dominant contribution is the sector-preserving skeleton, with strict one-bit completion acting as a secondary refinement. We provide code, finite certificates, CSV files, validation logs, and reproduction scripts to make the finite-size claims traceable.

### [79] [Pseudo-Hermiticity of the Nakajima-Zwanzig Projected Liouvillian in the Jaynes-Cummings Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25801)
*Kejun Liu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了开放量子动力学中 Nakajima-Zwanzig 投影 Liouville 算符 QLQ 在 Jaynes-Cummings 模型下是 Mostafazadeh 意义下的赝厄米（pseudo-Hermitian）算子，存在一个正定度规 eta 使其谱为实数，从而解决了此前发现的谱实性异常。该赝厄米性在全局上由度规保护，且度规在浴截断极限下高度精确，向 Rabi 模型的连续变形还揭示了一个具有两个异常点边界的重入赝厄米相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前发现开放量子动力学（open quantum dynamics）中精确记忆核（memory kernel）的生成元 QLQ 在 Jaynes-Cummings 模型中具有纯实谱，但 QLQ 明显非厄米（non-Hermitian），这一反常现象长期缺乏结构上的解释。

Method: 通过证明 QLQ 在 Mostafazadeh 意义下是赝厄米的，即存在一个正定度规 eta 使得 (QLQ)^† eta = eta (QLQ)，从而强制谱为实数。进一步在 Delta N = 0 和 Delta N = ±2 子扇区中验证了单独的非厄米性，并展示了全局度规的保护作用。还通过向全 Rabi 模型（full Rabi model）的连续变形探索了赝厄米相的重入行为及其异常点边界。

Result: Delta N = 0 和 Delta N = ±2 子扇区分别具有非零残差（1.70 和 5.06），但全局谱仍被度规 eta 保护为实数。度规在浴截断极限（N_max = 3–20，矩阵维度高达 1764×1764）下保持小于 10^{-11} 的交缠残差。向全 Rabi 模型变形时出现一个重入赝厄米相（re-entrant pseudo-Hermitian phase），由两个异常点（exceptional points）边界界定，且度规条件数在此相中发散。

Conclusion: 该结果为典型量子光学模型中记忆核的 Hardy 空间解析性（Hardy-space analyticity）提供了结构性理由，深化了对非厄米开放量子动力学中实谱起源的理解。

Abstract: The Nakajima-Zwanzig projected Liouvillian QLQ, the generator of the exact memory kernel in open quantum dynamics, is manifestly non-Hermitian yet has been reported to possess a purely real spectrum in the Jaynes-Cummings model -- an anomaly unexplained since observation. We resolve this anomaly by showing that QLQ is pseudo-Hermitian in the Mostafazadeh sense: a positive-definite metric eta>0 exists such that (QLQ)^dag eta = eta (QLQ), forcing the spectrum to be real. The pseudo-Hermiticity is genuine: the Delta N = 0 and Delta N = +/-2 sectors are individually non-Hermitian (residuals 1.70 and 5.06, respectively), yet the global spectrum is protected by eta. The metric survives the bath-truncation limit (N_max = 3--20, matrix dimension up to 1764 x 1764) with intertwining residual <10^{-11}. A continuous deformation to the full Rabi model reveals a re-entrant pseudo-Hermitian phase with two exceptional-point boundaries, in which the metric condition number diverges. The result supplies a structural reason for Hardy-space analyticity of the memory kernel in the canonical quantum-optical model.

</details>


### [80] [Randomised measurements of a disorder-induced entanglement transition in a neutral atom quantum processor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24854)
*Apollonas S. Matsoukas-Roubeas,Oscar Scholin,Lucas Sá,Arinjoy De,Majd Hamdan,Alexei Bylinskii,Andrew J. Daley,Dorian A. Gangloff*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在可编程模拟量子模拟器上，利用一种基于局部能量调节和全局场的随机测量协议，实现了纠缠熵的测量，并展示了无序参数如何导致从混沌到局域化的纠缠动力学转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量复杂量子系统中的纠缠动力学对理解信息 scrambling、热化以及多体量子混沌到局域化的转变至关重要。然而，现有随机测量工具箱要求对各子系统实现任意幺正旋转（unitary rotations），这在缺乏通用局域控制的模拟量子模拟器中难以实现。

Method: 提出并实现了一种改进的随机测量协议（randomised measurement protocol），通过利用局部能量调节（local energy tuning）配合全局场（global field），绕过了对局域门操作（local gate control）的需求。该协议在商用的中性原子量子模拟器 QuEra's Aquila 上执行。

Result: 成功在可编程模拟量子模拟器上测量了纠缠熵（entanglement entropy），并展示了局域哈密顿量参数中的可编程无序（programmable disorder）如何驱动系统从混沌纠缠动力学向局域化纠缠动力学转变。在当前退相干时间下，清晰地分辨出了无序依赖的、随时间演化的纠缠传播行为。

Conclusion: 该工作扩展了可编程模拟量子模拟器的实用性，并为随机测量工具箱在更广泛的模拟系统中的应用开辟了新机会。

Abstract: The development and spread of entanglement in complex quantum systems is central to exploring many-body phenomena out of equilibrium. Measuring entanglement dynamics can shed light on information scrambling and thermalisation, namely on transitions from many-body quantum chaos to localisation in disordered, interacting systems. In quantum computing systems, entanglement entropy and other nonlinear functions of the density matrix have been recently measured, in particular by using the randomised measurement toolbox. However, it is difficult to implement the required arbitrary unitary rotations on specific subsystems without universal local control. Here we devise and demonstrate the measurement of entanglement entropy in a programmable analogue quantum simulator using a randomised measurement protocol that leverages local energy tuning together with a global field to bypass the need for local gate control. We implement this on a commercially available neutral-atom quantum simulator, QuEra's Aquila, and use it to show how programmable disorder in the local Hamiltonian parameters leads to a transition from chaotic to localised entanglement dynamics. Given current decoherence times, we clearly resolve disorder-specific, time-dependent entanglement spreading in small systems. Our work extends the utility of programmable analogue quantum simulators, and opens further opportunities for wider randomised measurement toolboxes in a range of other analogue systems.
