### [81] [Nonlinearity-enhanced Quantum Sensing in Discrete Time Crystal Probes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25286)
*Rozhin Yousefjani,Shaikha Al-Naimi,Saif Al-Kuwari,Abolfazl Bayat*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了非线性相互作用如何增强离散时间晶体（discrete time crystal）探针的量子传感精度，发现量子Fisher信息（quantum Fisher information）的系统尺寸标度指数随非线性指数近似线性增长，同时识别出非线性（nonlinearity）是量子增强灵敏度的资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离散时间晶体（discrete time crystals）作为一种非平衡物质相，具有鲁棒次谐波振荡和破缺的离散时间平移对称性（discrete time-translation symmetry），其长寿命相干动力学使其成为量子传感（quantum sensing）的潜在资源。已有工作实现了无无序时间晶体探针对耦合参数的量子增强估计，本文旨在将该传感机制推广至非线性相互作用（nonlinear interactions），探索非线性对传感精度的增强作用。

Method: 采用解析方法严格分离了半范数上界（seminorm upper bound）与时间晶体区域中乘积态探针（product-state probes）的物理相关标度；数值上计算了量子Fisher信息（quantum Fisher information）随Floquet周期数（Floquet cycles）的增长行为以及其系统尺寸指数（system-size exponent）随非线性指数（nonlinearity exponent）的变化关系。此外，还分析了脉冲不完美（imperfect pulses）对信息编码的影响。

Result: 量子Fisher信息随Floquet周期数保持二次增长（quadratic long-time growth），同时其系统尺寸指数随非线性指数近似线性增加。更强的非线性会缩小时间晶体的稳定窗口（stability window），使探针对共振条件的微小偏差更敏感。脉冲不完美反而可能增强而非抑制演化态中所编码的信息。

Conclusion: 非线性相互作用是提升量子传感灵敏度的有效资源。该工作还讨论了利用超导量子比特（superconducting qubits）实现非线性离散时间晶体传感协议（nonlinear DTC sensing protocol）的数字实现方案（digital implementation）。

Abstract: Discrete time crystals are non-equilibrium phases of matter in periodically driven systems, characterized by robust subharmonic oscillations and broken discrete time-translation symmetry. Their long-lived coherent dynamics and resilience to imperfections make them promising resources for quantum sensing. A disorder-free discrete-time crystal probe can provide the quantum-enhanced estimation of the coupling parameter. Here, we extend this sensing mechanism to nonlinear interactions and show that this nonlinear profile strongly enhances the sensing precision by increasing the system-size scaling exponent of the quantum Fisher information. Our analytical discussion separates a rigorous seminorm upper bound from the physically relevant scaling realized by product-state probes in the time crystal regime. Numerically, we find that the quantum Fisher information retains its quadratic long-time growth with the number of Floquet cycles, while its system-size exponent increases approximately linearly with the nonlinearity exponent, identifying nonlinearity as a resource for quantum-enhanced sensitivity. We further show that stronger nonlinearities shrink the time crystal stability window, making the probe more sensitive to small deviations from the resonant condition. We also analyze the effect of imperfect pulses and show that such imperfections can enhance, rather than suppress, the information encoded in the evolved state. Finally, we discuss a digital implementation of the nonlinear DTC sensing protocol using superconducting qubits.

</details>


### [82] [Elucidating mechanism of optical cavities in superconducting strip single photon detectors using transmission line and impedance models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25425)
*Hiroki Kutsuma,Taro Yamashita*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过传输线模型（transmission line model）和阻抗模型（impedance model）阐明了带有光学腔的超导条带单光子探测器（SSPD）的物理机制，推导了吸收率的解析公式，并通过数值模拟验证了解析结果的高度一致性。研究表明，当SSPD的输入阻抗与输入介质阻抗匹配时，吸收率达到最大。该设计概念可推广至其他超导探测器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有带有光学腔的超导条带单光子探测器（SSPD）的吸收机制尚不清晰，缺乏解析层面的理论解释。

Method: 引入传输线模型（transmission line model）推导SSPD吸收率的解析公式；引入阻抗模型（impedance model）分析最大吸收率条件；将解析结果与数值模拟结果进行对比验证。

Result: 解析公式与数值模拟结果几乎完全一致；当SSPD的输入阻抗与输入介质阻抗匹配时，光学腔SSPD达到最大吸收率。

Conclusion: 该研究所提出的设计概念可适用于其他类型的超导探测器，例如微波动力学电感探测器（microwave kinetic inductance detector）和过渡边缘传感器（transition-edge sensor）。

Abstract: We clarified the physical mechanism of superconducting strip single photon detectors (SSPDs) with optical cavities by using transmission line and impedance models. By introducing the transmission line model, we derived the analytical formulae for the absorptance of SSPDs with optical cavities. We compared the absorptance obtained from the analytical formulae for SSPDs with single-side, double-side, and dielectric multi-layer optical cavities against the results of numerical simulations. The comparison showed that the results were nearly identical. By introducing the impedance model, it was clearly shown that the SSPDs with optical cavities achieved the maximum absorptance when their input impedance of the SSPDs with optical cavities matched the impedance of the input medium. The design concepts proposed in this study are applicable to other superconducting detectors, such as microwave kinetic inductance detectors and transition-edge sensors.

### [83] [Continuous Reset-Induced Phase Transition in Measurement-Free Random Quantum Circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25640)
*Hinata Yokoyama,Kengo Anzai,Dina Syverud-Lindland,Yoshihito Kuno,Hiroaki Matsueda*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究仅含重置通道（reset channels）的随机幺正量子电路（random unitary quantum circuit），通过稳定子电路模拟发现重置诱导的纠缠相变（reset-induced entanglement phase transition）是连续的二级混合相变（second-order mixed phase transition），且其性质显著依赖于量子数维度d，与大d极限下的经典统计映射预期不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索仅含重置通道的随机幺正量子电路的多体统计物理性质，特别是重置诱导的纠缠相变，该电路对实际量子器件具有高可行性。

Method: 采用稳定子电路模拟（stabilizer circuit simulation）对d=2的情形进行高效数值计算，分析临界点附近的涨落行为并实施数据塌缩（data collapse）分析。

Result: 临界点附近观察到大幅度涨落，表明重置诱导相变为连续相变；数据塌缩结果与二级混合相变（second-order mixed phase transition）一致。相变性质显著依赖于量子数维度d，与大d极限下经典统计映射的预期不同。

Conclusion: 重置通道诱导的纠缠相变是一种连续的二级混合相变，其性质受量子数维度d的显著影响，与大d极限下的经典统计图像存在定性差异。

Abstract: We study a random unitary quantum circuit with only reset channels, which has high feasibility for real quantum devices. In particular, we investigate the many-body statistical physics properties, "reset-induced" entanglement phase transitions comparing the classical statistical picture in the large "$d$" limit of qudits. In the property of the reset-induced phase transition the parameter of qudit $d$ is essential. That is, the transition properties induced by the reset channel significantly depend on $d$. We numerically elucidate this statement employing efficient stabilizer circuit simulations for $d=2$. Specifically, large fluctuations are observed near the critical point, indicating that the reset-induced phase transition is continuous. We obtain clear data collapses, consistent with a second-order mixed phase transition. This behavior differs from expectations based on the classical statistical mapping in the large-$d$ limit.

</details>


### [84] [Quantum Error Correction Exploiting Quantum Spatial Distribution and Gauge Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25747)
*Ryo Asaka*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究量子空间分布（QSD）与规范对称性（GS）在稳定子形式（stabilizer formalism）框架内结合使用对量子纠错（quantum error correction）的贡献。利用嵌套正方形上的3+2粒子系统，编码Shor九比特码并检测错误。结果表明：GS能抵御三种噪声；QSD提供架构灵活性，支持垂直与水平堆叠纠错系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子空间分布（QSD）与规范对称性（GS）在稳定子形式（stabilizer formalism）中的协同作用，以提升量子纠错（quantum error correction）的鲁棒性与架构灵活性。

Method: 采用嵌套正方形上的3+2粒子系统，其中三个粒子编码Shor九比特码（Shor's nine-qubit code），两个粒子通过自旋态测量（spin state measurement）检测该码的错误。每个粒子通过仅作用于其自旋或位置态的量子门操作（gate operation）演化，而非量子行走（quantum walk）模型。

Result: 第一，规范对称性（GS）能抵抗作用于粒子的三种噪声：自旋态的任意退相干、位置态的任意退相干，以及两种态的联合退相位（dephasing），这些噪声会部分或完全破坏量子空间分布（QSD）。第二，QSD提供架构灵活性，允许纠错系统在垂直和水平方向堆叠，并实现了错误检测（稳定子测量）、逻辑Hadamard门、Toffoli门以及量子加法器（quantum adder），所需相互作用仅局限于最近邻和次近邻粒子之间。

Conclusion: 量子空间分布（QSD）与规范对称性（GS）在稳定子形式（stabilizer formalism）中的整合，能够有效增强量子纠错（quantum error correction）的抗噪能力，并赋予系统架构灵活性，实现仅依赖近邻相互作用的量子门操作。

Abstract: We explore what the integrated use of quantum spatial distribution (QSD), or more specifically, superposition of both spin and position states of particles, and gauge symmetry (GS) within stabilizer formalism provides for quantum error correction. The exploration employs $3+2$ particles on nested squares proposed in the companion letter (arXiv:2504.07941), where three of them encode Shor's nine-qubit code and the remaining two detect errors in this code through their spin state measurements (unlike the letter's quantum walk model, each particle evolves by gate operations acting exclusively on either its spin or position state). The first result is that the GS offers resilience against three types of noise acting on a particle: arbitrary decoherence of its spin or position state, and dephasing of both states, which partly or completely destroys its QSD. To show that, we formulate a noise model unifying the above noise and prove the correctability of this unified model under our error-correcting scheme. The second result is that QSD provides architectural flexibility allowing us to stack the error-correcting systems both vertically and horizontally. Indeed, we show implementations of the error detection (stabilizer measurement), logical Hadamard and Toffoli gates, and a quantum adder with the required interactions only between nearest-neighbor and next-nearest-neighbor particles.

</details>

### [85] [Six textbook mistakes in quantum field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24871)
*Alexandros Gezerlis*

Main category: physics.ed-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统梳理并纠正了量子场论（quantum field theory, QFT）教科书及研究文献中六类广泛存在的概念性错误，通过引用具体实例、专家共识、权威参考文献及简洁的修正方案，旨在阻止这些错误在学术文献中继续传播。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子场论教科书中普遍存在若干概念性混淆（conceptual muddledness），这些错误不仅出现在教材中，也渗入研究文献，阻碍初学者正确理解QFT，亟需系统梳理与纠正。

Method: 首先给出一个简要的QFT纲要以建立统一记号体系；随后围绕六个典型主题（六类常见错误），每类均包含：具体摘录的错误例子、专家已知但常被入门教材误处理的相关知识、正确处理该概念的权威参考文献、以及一份纠正问题的简洁修正案（concise correction）。

Result: 未在摘要中呈现具体实验结果或定量数据，但指出每类错误均配有权威参考文献出处及修正方案，以提供明确的纠正路径。

Conclusion: 本文旨在警示QFT学习者与研究者注意这些常见的概念陷阱，从而遏制错误在文献中的持续传播。

Abstract: This article discusses incorrect statements appearing in textbooks on quantum field theory (QFT); some of these mistakes also appear in the research literature. The focus is not on errors made by an individual author, but on conceptual muddledness that is widespread in introductory textbooks. We start from a bare-bones summary of QFT, meant to establish the notation. We then turn to our six paradigmatic themes, in each case quoting a specific example of the textbook mistake, a summary of material that is known to experts but is frequently mishandled in introductory works, pointers to authoritative references where the relevant concept is handled properly, as well as a concise correction that rectifies any issues. The goal of this work is to warn readers of the existence of several pitfalls and thereby stop these errors from further propagating in the literature on QFT.

</details>

### [86] [Economical and ecological impact of sector coupling applied to computing clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25540)
*P. Bechtle,O. Freyermuth,M. Geffers,M. Giffels,M. Hübner,F. Kirfel,J. Kreutz,S. Krieg,S. Matberg,M. Schnepf*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本研究通过模拟德国电力生产公开数据，分析高性能计算集群动态调度的可行性，验证其在吸收可再生能源波动性的同时降低碳排放和运营成本的效果，并评估硬件成本及未来适用条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可再生能源占比上升导致电力生产波动加剧；部门耦合（sector coupling）理念提出通过动态调度用电来吸收过剩可再生能源，但缺乏具体实践场景的验证。高性能计算集群（high-performance computing clusters）因其短期内计算结果延迟可被容忍，成为理想试验场。

Method: 利用德国电力生产的公开数据模拟计算集群的简化运行；分别确定最优利用率（optimal utilisation）及其对应的碳排放和成本降低量；考虑硬件购置成本（hardware acquisition costs）与隐含排放（embedded emissions）；在两个验证期内评估固定计算目标（fixed computing target）的稳定性；通过参数修改的额外模拟估算未来动态运行仍能实现节约的条件。

Result: 研究分别得出了最优利用率下的碳排放和成本削减效果；硬件成本与隐含排放被纳入考量；在两个验证期内确认了固定计算目标下的系统稳定性；并通过参数修改模拟推断了未来动态运行继续实现节约的潜在条件。

Conclusion: 基于动态调度的系统运行可降低总体环境影响，并可能因电价随残差负荷（residual load）变化而降低运营成本；在科学领域的高性能计算集群中实施该策略具有可行性，但需满足长期计算目标稳定的前提。

Abstract: The rising share of abundant renewable energy inevitably increases volatility in the electricity production. The concept of sector coupling means that the volatility of electricity production to a large degree can be absorbed by dispatching electricity consumption whenever excess renewable energy is available. A system that is dynamically operated based on this principle can lower its total environmental impact. In addition, operational costs might be reducible as electricity prizes strongly depend on the residual load of the energy system. High-performance computing clusters in the field of science represent an ideal testing ground for such dynamic operation. Short-term delays in computing results due to electricity production being associated with high costs or carbon emissions are often negligible, provided that an overall computing target remains constant over long time periods. This study simulates the simplified operation of computing clusters using publicly available data on electricity production in Germany. The optimal utilisation along with associated carbon emission and cost reductions are determined separately. Hardware acquisition costs and embedded emissions are taken into account. The stability of a fixed computing target given the determined utilisation optima is evaluated in two validation periods. Additional simulations with modified parameters are carried out to estimate potential conditions under which dynamic operation of a computing cluster would continue to enable savings in the future.

### [87] [Emergent Features in $U(N) \times U(\tilde{N})$ Bi-adjoint Cubic Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24830)
*Lauren Smyth*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从组合学、关联函数和CHY形式论的推广三个视角，研究了双伴随φ³理论树级散射振幅中U(N)×U(Ñ)整体对称性的作用。通过构造平面散射势，重现了Dolan与Goddard的大质量散射方程，并利用对称Ferrers图形对运动学不变量进行计数，揭示了Catalan数与Narayana数之间的关联，同时给出了简化构型下解的数量的闭式表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究U(N)×U(Ñ)整体对称性在双伴随φ³理论树级散射振幅中的角色，为理解散射方程的物理含义、运动学不变量计数以及振幅结构背后的组合学提供新的理论视角。

Method: 从组合学、关联函数（correlation functions）和大质量推广的CHY形式论（massive extension of the CHY formalism）三个角度展开分析。构造了平面散射势（planar scattering potential），其极值点重现了Dolan与Goddard的大质量散射方程；利用最大对称Ferrers图形（maximally symmetric Ferrers shapes）对运动学不变量进行计数；通过U(1)退耦恒等式（U(1) decoupling identity）推导Catalan递推关系与Catalan-Narayana数的关联。

Result: 平面散射势以共形不变交比（conformally invariant cross-ratios）表达，提供了散射方程构造的物理直观。U(1)退耦恒等式为两种不同的Catalan递推关系（Catalan recursion relations）提供了物理解释，并揭示了U(1)分裂中Catalan数与Narayana数之间的相互作用。对于固定粒子排序的关联函数，给出了解的数量的闭式表达式（closed form expression）以及离壳散射势（off-shell scattering potential）。

Conclusion: 平面散射势和对称性分析有力地揭示了双伴随φ³理论振幅结构中的组合学与物理学联系，为理解此类振幅系统的运动学不变量计数和动力学提供了新工具与新见解。

Abstract: This work investigates the role of the $U(N) \times U(\tilde{N})$ global symmetry in tree-level scattering amplitudes of the bi-adjoint $φ^3$ theory from three perspectives: combinatorics, correlation functions, and a massive extension of the CHY formalism. We derive a planar scattering potential whose extrema reproduce Dolan and Goddard's massive scattering equations, providing physical intuition of the construction. This potential enables the counting of kinematic invariants via maximally symmetric Ferrers shapes, and it is expressed in terms of conformally invariant cross-ratios. We find that the $U(1)$ decoupling identity provides a physical interpretation of two different Catalan recursion relations, and also reveals an interplay between Catalan and Narayana numbers in the $U(1)$ splitting. Finally, we construct correlation functions for a fixed particle ordering using the CHY formalism, offering new insights into the dynamics of such amplitude structures. We derive a closed form expression of the reduced number of solutions for this set-up, as well as an off-shell scattering potential.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用欧几里得路径积分方法，在AdS3超引力框架下同时分析近视界（near-horizon）与渐近区域（asymptotic region）的量子涨落，并系统纳入陈-西蒙斯场和自旋-3/2模的贡献。

Result: 明确了边界条件（boundary conditions）在AdS3中的作用，指出低温下近视界区域的引力路径积分与BTZ背景周围路径积分不等价；进一步刻画了近极端与近BPS极限之间的差异。

Conclusion: 分析强化了近区与远区动力学之间的区分，并在量子层面揭示了引力路径积分中存在的不一致性。

Abstract: Despite the archetypal status of the BTZ background in quantifying quantum aspects of black holes, several features at low temperatures remain imprecise and incomplete. Here, we systematically investigate the behaviour of the Euclidean path integral at low temperatures in the context of AdS3 supergravity, including an analysis of quantum fluctuations in both the near-horizon and asymptotic regions. We clarify and rectify aspects of the bosonic fluctuations, highlighting the role of boundary conditions in AdS3, and show in particular that the gravitational path integral in the near-horizon region is inequivalent to that around BTZ at low temperature. We further account in detail for the contributions of Chern-Simons fields and spin-3/2 modes, thereby refining the disparities between the near-extremal and near-BPS limits at low temperature. Altogether, our analysis sharpens the distinction between near- and far-region dynamics and demonstrates a disagreement in the gravitational path integral at the quantum level.

I focus on upgrading solutions of gap maximization for the spinning modular bootstrap from low to high numerical order, though the methodology is generic to a broader class of bootstrap constraints and flows. ### [90] [Optimal paths across potentials on scalar field space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24843)
*Saskia Demulder,Dieter Lust,Carmine Montella,Thomas Raml*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究利用最优传输（Optimal Transport）框架研究场空间中的距离，基于沼泽地距离猜想（Swampland Distance Conjecture），通过在无引力和有引力情形下分别构造与WKB展开和Wheeler-DeWitt方程相关的传输问题，建立了广义Wasserstein距离，并探讨了其在沼泽地纲领中的潜在应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于沼泽地距离猜想，旨在为场空间中的距离概念提供一种基于最优传输理论的新视角，从而揭示场空间几何与量子引力约束之间的深层联系。

Method: 在无动力学引力的情形下，将传输问题与薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）WKB展开中的Hamilton-Jacobi方程和连续性方程（continuity equations）联系起来；在引入动力学引力后，利用ADM形式（ADM formalism）通过Wheeler-DeWitt方程（Wheeler-DeWitt equation）建立相应的传输问题，并引入不同的代价函数（cost functions）。

Result: 该框架在完整位形空间（full configuration space）上自然地定义了距离；若要将距离解释为纯粹的标量场距离（scalar field distance），则需要额外的修正。研究还给出了若干应用与实例。

Conclusion: 该工作为沼泽地纲领内不同主题（如距离猜想与场空间几何）提供了潜在的新研究方向，表明最优传输理论可成为探索量子引力中距离概念的有效数学工具。

Abstract: Motivated by the Swampland Distance Conjecture, we study distances in field space using the framework of Optimal Transport. The associated optimisation problem naturally leads to a notion of distance in terms of a (generalised) Wasserstein distance between probability distributions over field space. In the absence of dynamical gravity, we relate the transport problem to Hamilton-Jacobi and continuity equations arising from a WKB expansion of a Schrödinger equation associated with the physical configuration. We then formulate an extension in the presence of dynamical gravity. Using the ADM formalism, we establish the corresponding transport problem through the Wheeler-DeWitt equation, giving rise to different possible choices of cost functions. The resulting notions of distances are naturally defined on the full configuration space, while an interpretation in terms of a genuine scalar field distance requires additional modifications. We further discuss several applications and examples, and indicate possible implications for different themes within the Swampland program.

### [91] [Three-Gluon Scattering Amplitude in de Sitter Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24844)
*Tomasz R. Taylor,Bin Zhu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了全局德西特时空（global de Sitter spacetime）中三胶子散射振幅，在 SO(1,4) 对称表示的角动量基下，通过三维球面上的调和一次型（harmonic one-forms）的交缠积（intertwiner integrals）在树图级别确定振幅，并推导出适用于所有螺旋度（helicity）组态的普适公式，最终将振幅表示为维格纳 3j 符号（Wigner 3j symbols）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在 SO(1,4) 对称表示的角动量基下建立散射振幅；通过三维球面上调和一次型的交缠积在树图级别确定振幅；推导涵盖所有入射和出射胶子螺旋度组态的通用公式，并将结果用维格纳 3j 符号表达。

Result: 得到了全局德西特时空中三胶子散射振幅在角动量基下的通用解析表达式，该表达式对所有螺旋度组态均有效，且用维格纳 3j 符号给出闭合形式。

Conclusion: 该工作为德西特时空非阿贝尔规范场（non-Abelian gauge field）散射振幅的角动量基描述提供了完整树图结果，并为进一步研究德西特时空量子场论及全息对偶中的高阶过程奠定了基础。

Abstract: We study three-gluon scattering amplitudes in global de Sitter spacetime, in the angular momentum basis of SO(1,4) symmetry representations. At the tree level, they are determined by the intertwiner integrals of harmonic one-forms on the three-sphere. We derive a general formula valid for all helicity configurations of incoming and outgoing gluons and express the amplitudes in terms of Wigner 3j symbols.

### [92] [On the structure of higher-dimensional integrable field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24864)
*Marco Benini,Ryan A. Cullinan,Alexander Schenkel,Benoit Vicedo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套基于d项L∞-代数（d-term L∞-algebras）的任意时空维度可积场论（integrable field theories）的通用框架，通过拓扑-全纯高维Chern-Simons理论（topological-holomorphic higher Chern-Simons theories）的构造与同调微扰理论（homological perturbation theory），实现了高维可积场论的系统化描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建一个适用于任意时空维度 $d+1$ 的通用可积场论框架，克服现有构造（如Costello-Yamazaki构造）仅适用于低维度的局限性。

Method: 引入带有适当奇异结构和边界条件的循环L∞-代数（cyclic L∞-algebras），在 $M \times \mathbb{C}P^1$ 上描述拓扑-全纯高维Chern-Simons理论，由 $\mathbb{C}P^1$ 上的亚纯1-形式（meromorphic 1-form）控制；利用同调微扰理论（homological perturbation theory）和同伦转移（homotopy transfer）构造弱等价模型，从而在 $M$ 上得到 $(d+1)$ 维场论。

Result: 该框架的可积性由从构造模型到描述高维Lax联络（higher Lax connections）的L∞-代数的自然映射保证，该映射产生与 $M$ 中高维闭链（higher-dimensional cycles）相关联的守恒荷（conserved charges）。所得理论具有自然的作用量泛函，并在2维情形下还原为Costello-Yamazaki构造。

Conclusion: 所提框架为高维可积场论提供了统一的代数化描述，以L∞-代数为核心工具建立了拓扑-全纯Chern-Simons理论与高维可积系统之间的系统联系。

Abstract: We propose a general framework for integrable field theories in arbitrary spacetime dimension $d+1$ which is based on $d$-term $L_\infty$-algebras. Specifically, we introduce cyclic $L_\infty$-algebras describing topological-holomorphic higher Chern-Simons theories on $M \times \mathbb{C}P^1$ with suitable singularity structures and boundary conditions, controlled by a meromorphic $1$-form on $\mathbb{C}P^1$. Using homological perturbation theory and homotopy transfer, we construct weakly equivalent models describing $(d+1)$-dimensional field theories on $M$. Their integrability is witnessed by a natural map to an $L_\infty$-algebra describing higher Lax connections, yielding conserved charges associated with higher-dimensional cycles in $M$. The resulting theories admit natural action functionals and recover the Costello-Yamazaki construction in $2$ dimensions.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文证明了所有自对偶理论（包括含有无质量高自旋场的理论）在Kleinian符号或复闵可夫斯基运动学下均具有非平凡树图振幅，并指出手征高自旋引力中的非平凡振幅为完成矢量化/高自旋AdS/CFT对偶的天体全息类比提供了缺失要素。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 所有SD理论在Kleinian符号或复闵可夫斯基运动学下均具有非平凡的树图振幅；其中，最大SD理论——手征高旋引力（chiral higher-spin gravity）中的非平凡振幅提供了关键缺失要素。

Following the recent [arxiv:2602.12176] we show that all SD-theories, including those with massless higher-spin fields, have nontrivial tree-level amplitudes in Kleinian signature or complex Minkowski kinematics. Within celestial holography, the nontriviality of amplitudes in chiral higher-spin gravity provides the missing ingredient needed to complete the celestial analogue of the vector-model/higher-spin AdS/CFT duality.

### [95] [Path integral for the closed superstring and the matrix model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25052)
*Yuhma Asano*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从Minkowski时空世界面路径积分出发，推导出Nambu-Goto、Schild和Polyakov三种表述在欧氏与闵氏下的等价性，证明“弦因果性”（stringy causality）在微扰弦论中可实现，并通过矩阵正则化得到一种Minkowski版本的NBI型IKKT矩阵模型，该模型具有弦因果性，为超弦理论的非微扰矩阵模型提供路径积分定义基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先推导了与Polyakov型欧氏路径积分（Euclidean path integral）等价的Nambu-Goto型Minkowski路径积分（Minkowskian path integral），建立Nambu-Goto、Schild和Polyakov三类表述在Minkowski与Euclidean两种符号差下的等效性。随后利用矩阵正则化（matrix regularisation），对微扰IIB型弦论（type IIB string theory）的路径积分进行离散化，得到具有弦因果性（stringy causality）的矩阵模型。

Result: 在微扰弦论层面证明了“弦因果性”在路径积分表述中的实现。通过矩阵正则化得到的矩阵模型是NBI型IKKT矩阵模型（NBI-type IKKT matrix model）的一种Minkowski版本，且继承弦因果性。

Conclusion: 该Minkowski版本的NBI型IKKT矩阵模型为定义超弦理论的非微扰路径积分提供了新路径，有望解决零维理论中路径积分定义的歧义性问题。

Abstract: The IKKT matrix model, which is proposed as a non-perturbative formulation of superstring theory, has an issue typical of zero-dimensional theory -- ambiguity in the definition of its path integral. To tackle this issue, we revisit the path-integral formulation of perturbative string theory. In this article, we review recent progress in the string world-sheet path-integral formulation, especially in the Minkowski signature. We first derive the Minkowskian path integral of the Nambu-Goto type equivalent to Polyakov's Euclidean path integral for critical closed string theory, showing equivalences among the Nambu-Goto-, Schild- and Polyakov-type formulations both in the Minkowskian and Euclidean signatures. We also show that ``stringy causality'' is realised in the path-integral formulation at the level of string perturbation theory. We then obtain the matrix model with a property like the stringy causality, which turns out to be a Minkowskian version of the NBI-type IKKT matrix model, by matrix regularisation of the path integral for perturbative type IIB string theory.

### [96] [Thermodynamic Phase Transitions in Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar-Gauss-Bonnet Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25100)
*Cristián Erices,Stella Kiorpelidi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量-高斯-博内理论（Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory）中曲率诱导的带电黑洞标量化（scalarization）可产生丰富的热力学相变行为，无需借助外部约束机制或扩展热力学形式体系。在正则系综（canonical ensemble）框架下，标量化黑洞与Reissner-Nordström黑洞之间可发生二级、零级等多种相变，强耦合极限下标量化分支退化为Schwarzschild-like解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 渐近平坦黑洞通常缺乏热力学相变（thermodynamic phase transitions），本文旨在探索能否在不引入外部约束机制或扩展热力学形式体系（extended thermodynamic formalism）的条件下，通过标量化（scalarization）实现黑洞的非平庸热力学行为。

Method: 采用正则系综（canonical ensemble）和欧几里得途径（Euclidean approach）研究爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量-高斯-博内理论中的带电黑洞标量化现象，分析不同耦合强度下Helmholtz自由能（Helmholtz free energy）的热力学结构。

Result: 局部稳定的标量化热态与小Reissner-Nordström热态共存，促使自由能交叉成为平衡相之间的真正相变。弱耦合时二级相变（second-order phase transition）发生在第二个分岔点（bifurcation point），标量化分支自发脱落标量毛（scalar hair）。耦合增强后该相变变为零级（zeroth order），标量化分支收缩，Helmholtz自由能出现鱼形结构（fish-like structure），局部稳定态部分变为亚稳态，最多出现三个相变。强耦合极限下标量化分支退化为Schwarzschild-like解，Reissner-Nordström相成为唯一热力学首选构型。

Conclusion: 曲率诱导的标量化为渐近平坦带电黑洞提供了无需外部机制的自然热力学相变途径，展示了黑洞标量化与热力学复杂性之间的内在联系。

Abstract: Although asymptotically flat black holes generically lack thermodynamic phase transitions, we show that curvature-induced scalarization of electrically charged black holes in Einstein-Maxwell- Scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory provides a natural setting for nontrivial thermodynamic behavior, without invoking external confining mechanisms or an extended thermodynamic formalism. Working within the canonical ensemble and employing the Euclidean approach, we identify the coexistence of locally stable scalarized and small Reissner-Nordström thermal states, which promotes free-energy crossings to bona fide phase transitions between equilibrium phases. For weak coupling, a second-order phase transition coincides with the second bifurcation point, at which the scalarized branch reconnects with the Reissner-Nordström branch and scalar hair is spontaneously shed. As the coupling strength increases, this transition becomes zeroth order, the scalarized branch shrinks, and a fish-like structure develops in its Helmholtz free energy, rendering locally stable thermal states partially metastable, and yielding up to three phase transitions. In the strong-coupling limit, the scalarized branch reduces to a Schwarzschild-like solution, and the Reissner-Nordström phase ultimately emerges as the sole thermodynamically preferred configuration

</details>

### [100] [Integrand Analysis, Leading Singularities and Canonical Bases beyond Polylogarithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25270)
*Felix Forner,Cesare Carlo Mella,Christoph Nega,Lorenzo Tancredi,Fabian J. Wagner*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文探讨了超越多对数函数的费曼积分（Feynman integrals）中主导奇点（leading singularities）与规范基（canonical bases）之间的联系。通过将主导奇点概念从黎曼球面推广到更复杂的几何结构，并利用维度正规化（dimensional regularization）框架，展示了选择具有单位主导奇点的费曼积分如何必然引入与底层几何周期相关的新超越函数（transcendental functions）。这些积分满足ε-因子化微分方程，新超越函数直接对应其高斯-曼宁联络（Gauss-Manin connection）中出现的新微分形式。该构造在数学上等价于将周期矩阵分裂为半单部分（semi-simple）与单幂部分（unipotent）并附加清理步骤，并通过多个几何结构相互作用的复杂度递增示例加以验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在维度正规化框架下，将主导奇点的定义从黎曼球面推广到更一般的几何结构；利用该推广选择具有单位主导奇点的费曼积分，分析其满足的ε-因子化微分方程；将构造与周期矩阵的数学分裂（半单部分与单幂部分）建立等价对应。

Result: 具有广义单位主导奇点的费曼积分满足ε-因子化微分方程，其中新超越函数直接对应于高斯-曼宁联络中的新微分形式。该构造在数学上等价于周期矩阵分裂为半单与单幂部分并附加清理步骤。

Conclusion: 本文建立了超越多对数函数的费曼积分中主导奇点与规范基之间的系统联系，为涉及多种几何结构相互作用的复杂积分计算提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In this paper, we elaborate on the connection between leading singularities and canonical bases of Feynman integrals beyond polylogarithms. We start by discussing a notion of leading singularities in dimensional regularization, which can be generalized from the Riemann sphere to more complex geometries, and use it to demonstrate how selecting Feynman integrals with unit leading singularities necessitates introducing new transcendental functions related to the periods of the underlying geometries. Integrals with unit leading singularities in this generalized sense, satisfy $ε$-factorized differential equations, and the new transcendental functions are in direct correspondence to the new differential forms appearing in their Gauss-Manin connection. We argue that this construction is mathematically equivalent to the splitting of the period matrix into semi-simple and unipotent parts plus a clean-up step, and demonstrate its use with examples of increasing complexity that require the interplay of multiple geometries.

TL;DR: 本文研究谱网络（spectral networks）在量子刘维尔理论（quantum Liouville theory）中的作用，特别是Fenchel-Nielsen型谱网络。第一部分通过q-非阿贝尔化构造了Fenchel-Nielsen网络的q-平行输运（q-parallel transport），并与Moore-Seiberg形式论比较，提出了NRS提议的量子版本。第二部分通过自由场形式论（free-field formalism）与Fenchel-Nielsen型积分轮廓再现了刘维尔共形块（Liouville conformal blocks），但发现该方法在墙穿越（wall-crossing）下不完备。为此，将自由场形式论推广到光滑谱覆盖（smooth spectral coverings），其中Maulik-Okounkov R-矩阵起核心作用。猜想该新形式论能生成刘维尔共形块的完整谱，并为Goncharov-Shen共形块提供第一性原理定义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自由场形式论在墙穿越（wall-crossing）下无法完整生成刘维尔共形块（Liouville conformal blocks），需要发展更完备的理论框架以覆盖全部谱。

Method: 第一部分：通过q-非阿贝尔化（q-nonabelianisation）构造Fenchel-Nielsen型谱网络的q-平行输运（q-parallel transport），并与Moore-Seiberg形式论比较；第二部分：将标准自由场形式论（free-field formalism）推广到光滑谱覆盖（smooth spectral coverings），引入Maulik-Okounkov R-矩阵作为核心元件。

Result: 标准自由场形式论在墙穿越（wall-crossing）下不完备；新形式论在光滑谱覆盖上给出更完整的构造。

Conclusion: 所提出的新形式论有望生成刘维尔共形块（Liouville conformal blocks）的完整谱，并为Goncharov-Shen共形块提供第一性原理（first-principle）定义。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the role of spectral networks in quantum Liouville theory, with particular emphasis on spectral networks of Fenchel-Nielsen-type. In the first part, we construct q-parallel transport for Fenchel-Nielsen networks through q-nonabelianisation, and compare with quantum parallel transport computed using the Moore-Seiberg formalism. This motivates a proposal for a quantum version of the NRS proposal. In the second part, we reproduce Liouville conformal blocks through the standard free-field formalism with Fenchel-Nielsen-type integration contours. However, we observe that this approach is not complete with respect to wall-crossing. We therefore develop an extension of the free-field formalism to smooth spectral coverings, with the Maulik-Okounkov R-matrix playing a central role. We conjecture that this new formalism generates the full spectrum of Liouville conformal blocks, and provides a first-principle definition for Goncharov-Shen conformal blocks.

### [102] [Phase Transitions and Chaos Bound in Horava Lifshitz Black Holes using Lyapunov Exponents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25495)
*Mozib Bin Awal,Prabwal Phukon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过Lyapunov指数分析，研究了四维Hořava-Lifshitz黑洞的热力学相结构，发现Lyapunov指数可作为一阶相变的有效序参量，其临界指数δ=1/2符合平均场普适类，并观察到混沌界（chaos bound）在热力学稳定相内的普遍违反现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探索替代引力理论中黑洞热力学与混沌动力学之间的深层关联，验证Lyapunov指数作为探针（probe）在Hořava-Lifshitz黑洞相变研究中的普适性与鲁棒性。

Method: 对无质量与有质量试验粒子计算Hořava-Lifshitz黑洞背景下测地线运动的Lyapunov指数，分析该指数随温度的变化关系，并考察其在相变点处的临界行为。

Result: 在一阶相变区域，Lyapunov指数随温度呈现多值依赖，对应小、中、大黑洞三个分支，该多值性在临界点消失；Lyapunov指数的不连续性可作为序参量，临界指数δ=1/2；混沌界在小于某一阈值视界半径时被违反，且违反发生在热力学稳定相内，即使无相变也存在。

Conclusion: Lyapunov指数在替代引力理论的黑洞热力学中具有普适且鲁棒的探针功能，能够有效刻画相变特征并揭示混沌界违反等非平凡动力学行为。

Abstract: We probe the thermodynamic phase structure of four dimensional Horava Lifshitz black holes by Lyapunov exponent analysis. For both massless and massive test particles, the Lyapunov exponent exhibits a multivalued dependence on temperature in regimes with a first-order phase transition, with distinct branches corresponding to small, intermediate, and large black hole phases, and this behaviour disappears at the critical point. The discontinuity in the Lyapunov exponent acts as an effective order parameter with critical exponent $δ=1/2$, consistent with mean-field universality. We also find that the chaos bound is generically violated below a threshold horizon radius, with the violation occurring within the thermodynamically stable phase and persisting even in the absence of a phase transition. These results establish the robustness and universality of Lyapunov exponents as probes of black hole thermodynamics in alternative theories of gravity.

### [103] [Criticality of ISCOs and AdS/CFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25518)
*Chandrasekhar Bhamidipati,Parashar Chatterjee,Sudipta Mukherji,Yogesh Kumar Srivastava*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 基于球对称黑洞（spherically symmetric black holes）中质点轨道（trajectories of massive particles）的拓扑分类（topological classification），发现固定点（fixed points）的普适特征：中心固定点（center）要么始终存在（如全局AdS时空），要么在角动量低于临界值时消失并伴随鞍点（saddle point）出现；中心与鞍点合并处对应极限稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbits, ISCOs），其守恒量呈现类范德瓦尔斯平均场标度（van der Waals-like mean-field scaling），且通过AdS/CFT对偶计算了双扭算符（double-twist operators）的反常维度（anomalous dimensions），发现了非解析行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高维球对称黑洞中质点轨道运动的普适规律，基于固定点拓扑分类方法，揭示不同时空背景下轨道结构的共性特征。

Method: 采用固定点拓扑分类方法分析轨道；通过AdS/CFT对偶及重-重-轻-轻四点关联函数（heavy-heavy-light-light four point correlators）计算双扭算符的反常维度。

Result: 中心固定点要么始终存在（全局AdS时空），要么在角动量低于临界值时消失并伴随鞍点出现。中心与鞍点合并时对应ISCO；该临界点处守恒量呈现类范德瓦尔斯平均场标度（二级相变特征）。通过AdS/CFT得到中心与鞍点对应的反常维度分别为负值和正值，并在ISCO处出现非解析行为；还获得了中心的亚领头修正项。

Conclusion: 球对称黑洞的质点轨道具有拓扑根源的普适行为，ISCO对应参数空间中的特殊临界点，其临界现象与二级相变类似，并可通过全息对偶在CFT中得到验证。

Abstract: We study the trajectories of massive particles in spherically symmetric black holes in arbitrary dimensions, and find certain universal features based on the topological classification of the fixed points. If the system admits a center, we find two possible outcomes: regardless of the value of the angular momentum, the center always survives, which is realized in global AdS spacetimes or, the center disappears below a critical value of angular momentum, which happens for various spherically symmetric black holes. For the latter case, we find that irrespective of the details of the black hole, there must always be a saddle point. Topological arguments show that there exists a certain critical value of energy, angular momentum and the angular velocity, where the center and the saddle coalesce. This happens at a special point in the parameter space where the trajectories are the limiting innermost stable circular orbits (ISCOs). At the critical point, conserved quantities show universal, van der Waals-like mean-field scaling typical of a second-order phase transition. The anomalous dimensions $γ$ of the double-twist operators in the CFT are found, both using AdS/CFT and through the the heavy-heavy-light-light four point correlators, giving negative and positive values for the center and saddle, respectively, including the emergence of certain non-analytic behaviour at the ISCO. For the center, we also find subleading corrections in $\frac{1}{Δ_H}$ to $γ$ in the dual CFT, and dsicuss the implications of our results.

</details>

Abstract: We investigate a pre-inflationary dynamical compactification scenario in which a higher-dimensional expanding universe evolves into an effectively four-dimensional one through curvature-assisted modulus trapping. We show that negative curvature can sustain tracker-like radion evolution, allowing the radion to be trapped in a compactified vacuum before a subsequent four-dimensional inflationary phase dilutes the curvature remnant. While our analysis is performed in a 5D toy model, it illustrates a broader mechanism by which dynamical compactification can arise in a pre-inflationary higher-dimensional cosmology.

Conclusion: 本文为图形函数这一未纳入标准教科书的领域提供了一个连贯的入门综述，涵盖了其理论基础、最新进展以及与动量空间、对偶性之间的联系，旨在为后续深入学习提供指引。

Abstract: Graphical functions have emerged as a powerful framework for evaluating multi-loop Feynman integrals in perturbative quantum field theory. Defined as massless three-point position-space integrals, they reveal rich analytic structures and have enabled major advances, including the highest-loop results currently known in several quantum field theories. Their role extends to conformal field theory, and recent algorithmic developments now allow many graphical functions to be computed automatically. This review, based on graduate-level lectures held by O.S. in 2025/26 at the University of Hamburg, introduces the central ideas behind graphical functions, covering periods, Feynman residues, and the treatment of regular and singular cases in both integer and non-integer dimensions. It also discusses connections to momentum space and self-duality, and provides guidance for further study, offering a coherent entry point into a topic not addressed in standard textbooks.

Abstract: Different gaugings of the global symmetry of a quantum field theory are closely related to its various phases. In this work, we study candidate gaugeable symmetries by analyzing candidate Lagrangian algebra data in the Drinfeld center of a symmetry category $\mathscr{C}^k(G)$ associated to a QFT with continuous global $G$-symmetry and possible 't Hooft anomaly labeled by an integer $k$. TL;DR: 本文提出与具有't Hooft反常的连续群G相关的二维量子场论的对称性范畴为扭曲可测希尔伯特空间场范畴Hilb^k(G)，等价于由乘性丛群胚标记的卷积代数的酉表示范畴；并计算了其Drinfeld中心、3D SymTFT中的编织结构，适用于一大类李群。

Abstract: We propose that the symmetry category associated to a 2D quantum field theory with 0-form $G$-symmetry with 't Hooft anomaly $k\in H^4(BG,\mathbb{Z})$ for a large class of Lie groups $G$ is the category of twisted measurable fields of Hilbert spaces over $G$ denoted by $\mathrm{Hilb}^k(G)$, which is equivalent to the category of unitary representations of $C_0(G)$ with convolution product twisted by a multiplicative bundle gerbe labeled by $k$ denoted by $\textbf{Rep}^k(C_0(G))$. To the full generality, our framework applies to a Lie group $G$ that is a direct product of a compact connected Lie group and a number of $\mathbb{R}$ or $GL(1,\mathbb{C})$ factors. We compute the braiding of anyon lines in the bulk 3D SymTFT from this formalism. ### [109] [(Super-)renormalizable hairy meronic black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25844)
*Luis Avilés,Borja Diez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在四维爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-杨-米尔斯理论（Einstein-Maxwell-Yang-Mills theory）中，构建了一个带共形标量场（conformally coupled scalar field）的解析黑洞解，推广了带自引力非阿贝尔规范场（non-Abelian gauge fields）情形下的带电MTZ黑洞，并进一步得到带所有（超）可重整化标量场贡献的新meronic时空解，同时展示了非诺特（non-Noetherian）共形标量场扩展下静态黑洞解可加载杨-米尔斯场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有带电MTZ黑洞（charged Martínez-Troncoso-Zanelli black hole）尚未包含自引力非阿贝尔规范场的完整推广，且对共形标量场在非诺特框架下的黑洞解结构缺乏系统研究。

Method: 通过在四维含共形标量场的爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-杨-米尔斯理论中构造解析黑洞解，利用共形种子（conformal seed）方法生成新meronic时空，并引入非诺特共形标量场扩展以保持二阶共形不变标量方程。

Result: 内禀规范群由视界曲率决定：正曲率情形为SU(N)，负曲率情形为SU(N-1,1)。所得解推广了带非阿贝尔规范场的AC解（Anabalón-Cisterna solution）。非诺特扩展下仍存在可加载杨-米尔斯场的静态黑洞解。

Conclusion: 该工作为研究含非阿贝尔规范场与共形标量场的黑洞物理提供了新的解析框架，并揭示了规范群结构与视界几何之间的内在联系。

Abstract: We construct an analytical black hole solution in the Einstein-Maxwell-Yang-Mills theory with a conformally coupled scalar field in four dimensions, which generalizes the charged Martínez-Troncoso-Zanelli (MTZ) black hole in the presence of self-gravitating non-Abelian gauge fields. The internal gauge group is determined by the horizon curvature, becoming $SU(N)$ in the case of positive curvature and $SU(N-1,1)$ when the curvature is negative. Moreover, this solution is employed as a conformal seed to obtain new meronic spacetimes dressed with all (super-)renormalizable contributions of the scalar field, which provides the generalization of the Anabalón-Cisterna (AC) solution when self-gravitating non-Abelian gauge fields are included. Finally, we consider the non-Noetherian extension of the conformal scalar fields, which still yields a second-order conformally invariant scalar equation, even though the action is not. In that case, we show that static black hole solutions can also be charged with Yang-Mills fields.

</details>


### [110] [Nonlocal-in-time tail effects in gravitational scattering to fifth Post-Minkowskian and tenth self-force orders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25916)
*Christoph Dlapa,Gregor Kälin,Zhengwen Liu,Rafael A. Porto*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用世界线有效场论（worldline effective field theory）形式，推导了引力散射中由尾部效应（tail effects）产生的非定域保守贡献，达到了第五后闵可夫斯基阶（5PM）和第十自力阶（10SF），计算中采用了包括新型分部积分算法 SpideR 在内的前沿积分技术，结果与通过第六后牛顿阶（6PN）的所有现有文献完全一致，为隔离5PM阶保守两体动力学中的定域分量提供了关键要素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在引力两体散射问题中，尾部效应（tail effects）对保守动力学的非定域贡献需要被精确解析计算，尤其在高阶后闵可夫斯基（Post-Minkowskian）阶数下，当前理论尚缺乏完整的非定域贡献表达式，这限制了隔离定域（local-in-time）分量并完整描述双星旋进（binary inspiral）保守动力学的进展。

Method: 采用世界线有效场论（worldline effective field theory）形式进行场论推导；计算过程依赖于多种函数的多对数（multiple polylogarithms），最高权重为三；运用前沿积分技术，特别包括一种新颖的分部积分（integration-by-parts, IBP）算法——稀疏积分归约器（Sparse Integral Reducer, SpideR）。

Result: 推导出由尾部效应（tail effects）产生的非定域保守贡献，达到第五后闵可夫斯基阶（5PM）和第十自力阶（10SF）；结果含有最高权重为三的多对数（multiple polylogarithms）；与通过第六后牛顿阶（6PN）的现有文献在所有重叠区间内完全一致。

Conclusion: 本文结果为隔离第五后闵可夫斯基阶（5PM）双星旋进（binary inspiral）保守两体动力学中的定域分量（local-in-time component）提供了关键要素。

Abstract: Using the worldline effective field theory formalism, we derive the nonlocal-in-time conservative contributions arising from tail effects in gravitational scattering to fifth Post-Minkowskian (5PM) and tenth self-force (10SF) orders. The result features multiple polylogarithms of up to weight three. This challenging computation relies on state-of-the-art integration techniques, including a novel integration-by-parts algorithm: the Sparse Integral Reducer (SpideR). We find perfect agreement in the overlap with all existing literature through sixth post-Newtonian order. The results presented here provide a key ingredient for isolating the local-in-time component of the conservative two-body dynamics of binary inspirals at 5PM order.

</details>


### [111] [de Sitter in String Theory vs. Gibbons & Hawking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25918)
*Yoav Zigdon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文论证了微扰弦理论（perturbative string theory）在 $α'$ 和 $g_s$ 展开的所有阶上，都不允许以德西特时空（de Sitter）乘以闭流形（closed manifold）作为时空度规的解；其依据是欧几里得量子引力球面配分函数（sphere partition function）的鞍点近似中，存在一个与 $1/G_N$ 成正比的非零贡献，这一假设与 Gibbons-Hawking 关于静态宇宙学视界熵为 $A/(4G_N)$ 的提议相关。多个独立方法得到的弦论有效作用量均一致表明，对于闭欧几里得靶空间解（closed Euclidean target-space solutions），树级作用量（tree-level action）为零。这一结论的一个可能含义是，宇宙的状态将偏离渐近德西特时空。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在验证一个论断：微扰弦理论（perturbative string theory）不存在以德西特（de Sitter）时空乘以闭流形（closed manifold）为度规的解，且该论断在 $α'$ 和 $g_s$ 展开的所有阶上均成立。该工作延续并检验了 Gibbons-Hawking 关于宇宙学视界熵的提议，试图为弦理论中德西特时空的缺失提供严格的理论依据。

Method: 论文假设欧几里得量子引力球面配分函数（sphere partition function）的鞍点近似（saddle-point approximation）中包含一个正比于 $1/G_N$ 的非零贡献。基于此假设，研究者通过多个独立途径考察弦论的有效作用量（effective action），并比较所有方法在闭欧几里得靶空间解（closed Euclidean target-space solutions）下树级作用量（tree-level action）的行为。

Result: 所有独立考虑的有效作用量方法均一致得出：对于闭欧几里得靶空间解，弦论的树级作用量（tree-level action）为零。这一结果表明，微扰弦理论在 $α'$ 和 $g_s$ 展开的所有阶上，均不允许德西特时空乘以闭流形的解存在。

Conclusion: 论文所得结论的一个可能含义是，宇宙的状态将偏离渐近德西特（asymptotically de Sitter）时空。这意味着，若弦理论成立，现实的宇宙学演化可能无法长期保持近似德西特膨胀（如暴胀或暗能量主导阶段）。

Abstract: This paper corroborates a statement that perturbative string theory does not admit a solution whose spacetime metric is de Sitter times a closed manifold, to all orders in the $α'$ and $g_s$ expansions, under the assumption that the logarithm of the sphere partition function of Euclidean quantum gravity receives a nonzero contribution proportional to $\frac{1}{G_N}$ in a saddle-point approximation. This assumption is related to the Gibbons-Hawking proposal that the entropy of the cosmological horizon of the static patch is $\frac{A}{4G_N}$. Evidence for the statement comes from independent approaches to the effective action of string theory, all of which agree that the tree-level action vanishes for closed Euclidean target-space solutions. One possible implication is that the state of the Universe will depart from an asymptotically de Sitter spacetime.

</details>

### [112] [The Legacy of Enrico Fermi to Varenna](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24829)
*Vladislav Gavryusev,Massimo Inguscio*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本文追溯了恩里科·费米（Enrico Fermi）1954年在瓦伦纳学院（Varenna school）的讲座如何影响现代原子、分子与光学物理，从高能物理延伸到激光光谱、精密计量、超冷原子控制，最终导向量子模拟与量子计算，并强调了费米早期“建造而非购买计算机”的主张对当今量子科技的预示意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示费米科学遗产在现代原子、分子与光学（atomic, molecular, and optical physics, AMO）物理中的持续影响，并梳理从高能物理到量子信息科学的历史脉络。

Method: 采用历史追溯与学术遗产分析（historical tracing and legacy analysis）的方法，以费米1954年瓦伦纳学院讲座为起点，梳理关键里程碑事件的发展线索。

Result: 识别出无多普勒光谱（Doppler-free spectroscopy）、光频梳（optical frequency combs）、玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensation）和简并费米气体（degenerate Fermi gases）等转折点，这些进展最终导向量子模拟（quantum simulation）与量子计算（quantum computation）。

Conclusion: 费米的科学遗产，包括其早期关于计算机应“建造而非购买”（building a computer, rather than buying it）的主张，持续影响着当前量子物质（quantum matter）与信息科学的研究方向。

Abstract: The Varenna school is a hub where generations of physicists, including numerous Nobel laureates, have shaped the field, often through collaborative exchanges across political and cultural boundaries. We examine the scientific legacy of Enrico Fermi and its influence on modern atomic, molecular, and optical physics. Beginning with Fermi's 1954 lectures at the Varenna school, key developments are traced from high-energy physics to laser spectroscopy, precision metrology, and the control of ultracold atoms. Milestones such as Doppler-free spectroscopy, optical frequency combs, Bose-Einstein condensation, and degenerate Fermi gases are highlighted as turning points leading to quantum simulation and quantum computation. Fermi's early advocacy for building a computer, rather than buying it, can be viewed as a precursor to today's efforts in quantum science and technologies. This historical trajectory and legacy continues to inform current research in quantum matter and information science.

</details>

### [113] [Control of relaxation properties of a macroscopic nuclear spin ensemble](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25548)
*János Ádám,Andrew J. Winter,Deniz Aybas,Dmitry Budker,Derek F. Jackson Kimball,Arne Wickenbrock,Alexander O. Sushkov*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本研究展示了通过405 nm激光在含铅铁电晶体PbTiO₃和PMN-PT中诱导顺磁中心，实现了对²⁰⁷Pb核自旋系综T₁弛豫时间的光学调控，在4.6 MHz和40 MHz下分别将T₁缩短约一倍。研究还表征了光诱导Pb³⁺和Ti³⁺顺磁中心的自旋密度与弛豫动力学，并建立了核弛豫率与光诱导顺磁中心密度之间的关系模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固态中的宏观自旋系综（macroscopic spin ensembles）是量子传感和精密测量的重要平台，但低温下因声子冻结（phonon freeze-out）导致核自旋系综的纵向弛豫时间T₁过长，成为关键障碍。本研究旨在开发一种光学手段来主动控制核自旋弛豫，以加速热极化和动态核极化过程。

Method: 采用X波段电子顺磁共振（electron paramagnetic resonance, EPR）光谱学和饱和恢复核磁共振（saturation-recovery nuclear magnetic resonance）技术，在10 K下研究405 nm激光对PbTiO₃和PMN-πT晶体中²⁰⁷Pb核自旋T₁的影响。通过功率依赖的EPR测量提取自旋弛豫时间，并建立核弛豫率与光诱导顺磁中心密度之间的理论模型。

Result: 在PbTiO₃中观测到顺磁Pb³⁺中心及其与附近核自旋的超精细相互作用（hyperfine interaction）。在PMN-PT中识别出各向同性Pb³⁺中心和各向异性占据d轨道的Ti³⁺中心，自旋数密度分别为(2.5±1.0)×10¹⁷ cm⁻³和(4.1±1.7)×10¹⁷ cm⁻³。激光照射使²⁰⁷Pb核T₁在4.6 MHz下从(17±2) s降至(7±1) s，在40 MHz下从(1550±40) s降至(850±70) s，即缩短约一倍。

Conclusion: 实现了基于光照的核自旋弛豫光学控制，为固态核磁共振（solid-state NMR）精密测量中的加速热极化和动态核极化（dynamic nuclear polarization）提供了新途径，可应用于轴子类暗物质（axion-like dark matter）搜索等前沿方向。

Abstract: Macroscopic spin ensembles in solids are powerful platforms for quantum sensing and precision metrology. A key challenge is controlling the nuclear spin population relaxation time $T_1$, which can become prohibitively long at cryogenic temperatures due to phonon freeze-out. We demonstrate optical control of the $T_1$ relaxation time of the $^{207}$Pb nuclear spin ensemble in lead-containing ferroelectric crystals PbTiO$_3$ (PT) and (PbMg$_{1/3}$Nb$_{2/3}$O$_3$)$_{2/3}$-(PbTiO$_3$)$_{1/3}$ (PMN-PT). Using X-band electron paramagnetic resonance (EPR) spectroscopy at 10 K, we characterize light-induced paramagnetic centers created by 405 nm laser illumination. In PT, we observe paramagnetic Pb$^{3+}$ centers and their hyperfine interaction with nearby nuclear spins. In PMN-PT, we identify two populations: isotropic Pb$^{3+}$ centers and anisotropic Ti$^{3+}$ centers occupying $d$-orbitals, with spin number densities of $(2.5 \pm 1.0) \times 10^{17}$ cm$^{-3}$ and $(4.1 \pm 1.7) \times 10^{17}$ cm$^{-3}$, respectively. Power-dependent EPR measurements enable extraction of spin relaxation times. We investigate the ionization and recombination dynamics of these transient paramagnetic centers. Using saturation-recovery nuclear magnetic resonance, we demonstrate that laser illumination reduces the $^{207}$Pb nuclear $T_1$ by approximately a factor of two, from $(17 \pm 2)$ s to $(7 \pm 1)$ s at 4.6 MHz, and from $(1550 \pm 40)$ s to $(850 \pm 70)$ s at 40 MHz. We develop a model relating the nuclear relaxation rate to the density of photoinduced paramagnetic centers. This optical control of nuclear spin relaxation provides a pathway toward accelerated thermal polarization and dynamic nuclear polarization in solid-state NMR-based precision measurements, including searches for axion-like dark matter.

</details>


### [114] [Microscopic Theory of Chiral-Phonon-Induced Orbital Selectivity in Helical Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25328)
*Tomomi Tateishi,Akihito Kato,Alexander S. Ovchinnikov,Jun-ichiro Kishine*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文提出了螺旋晶体中手性诱导轨道选择性（CIOS）的微观理论，指出真正的手性声子通过晶体角动量守恒选择性地将角动量传递给电子轨道自由度，并在三折螺旋晶体中基于微扰理论揭示了轨道响应在布里渊区不同位置的增强与抑制特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究尚未从微观层面阐明手性声子如何将角动量选择性传递至电子轨道自由度，缺乏对晶体角动量（CAM）守恒下轨道转移机制的定量理解。

Method: 基于具有线群对称性$L3_1$的三折螺旋晶体，推导出声子诱导的局域旋转所产生的旋转型电子-声子相互作用（rotational electron-phonon interaction），其形式正比于$\hat{L}^{\pm}$；通过微扰论（perturbation theory）计算$\langle\hat{L}^{z}\rangle$至主导阶。

Result: 轨道响应在$\Gamma$点附近和布里渊区（BZ）边界处受到抑制，而在中间波矢区域得到增强；该特征与声子带的简并结构（degeneracy structure）密切相关。

Conclusion: 手性声子通过晶体角动量守恒实现轨道转移$m_{\ell}\to m_{\ell}-m_{s}$，其中$m_{s}=\pm 1$为声子旋转模式的本征值；轨道选择性在波矢空间的非均匀分布由声子带简并结构决定。

Abstract: We present a microscopic theory of chirality-induced orbital selectivity (CIOS) in helical crystals, in which truly chiral phonons selectively transfer angular momentum to electronic orbital degrees of freedom. For a threefold helical crystal with line-group symmetry $L3_1$, we show that phonon-induced local rotations generate a rotational electron--phonon interaction proportional to $\hat{L}^{\pm}$, which drives the orbital transfer $m_{\ell}\to m_{\ell}-m_{s}$ in accordance with crystal angular momentum (CAM) conservation, where $m_{s}=\pm 1$ denotes the eigenvalue of the phonon rotational mode. Evaluating $\langle\hat{L}^{z}\rangle$ to leading order in perturbation theory, we find that the orbital response is suppressed near the $Γ$ point and the BZ boundary, and enhanced at intermediate wave vectors -- a feature intimately tied to the degeneracy structure of the phonon bands.

</details>

### [115] [A radon emanation measurement system at the Carleton Noble Liquid Detector Laboratory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25609)
*P. Adhikari,M. G. Boulay,R. Crampton,D. Gallacher,M. Perry*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一种在卡尔顿低温液体探测器实验室（COLD Lab）开发的氡检测系统，用于测量材料在真空条件下的氡析出率，并评估氮气及过滤器中的氡水平，以支持DEAP-3600等稀有事件探测实验的辐射本底控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氡（radon）是稀有事件探测实验（如暗物质和中微子搜索）中最重要的本底源之一，因其来自天然铀的不可避产生。在低本底实验中，探测器材料和组件的氡析出（radon emanation）是污染的主要来源，因此需要开发检测系统进行定量研究。

Method: 该系统由不锈钢析出室、低本底ZnS(Ag)闪烁室以及氡转移与收集装置组成，用于在真空条件下测量材料氡析出率。此外，还构建了装有活性炭的冷阱（charcoal trap）并配备流量计，用于研究氮气中的氡水平及DEAP-3600处理系统气体过滤器中的残余氡。基于这些测量数据，进一步计算了关键探测器组件安装手套箱中的氡浓度。

Result: 该氡检测系统已完成校准并投入使用，成为了COLD Lab中降低稀有事件探测实验本底的重要诊断工具。

Conclusion: COLD Lab开发的氡析出计数器已校准并运行，可作为未来稀有事件探测实验中降低本底的关键诊断工具。

Abstract: Radon is one of the most important sources of background in rare event search experiments, such as those searching for Dark Matter and neutrinos, due to its unavoidable production from natural uranium. In low-background experiments, radon emanation from detector materials and components accounts for a major portion of contamination. To investigate this, a radon detection system was developed at the Carleton nOble Liquid Detector Laboratory (COLD Lab). The setup consists of a stainless steel emanation chamber, a low-background ZnS(Ag) cell, and an assembly for radon transfer and collection. This setup was used to study radon emanation from materials under vacuum conditions. Additionally, a charcoal trap made of activated charcoal and equipped with a flow meter was constructed to study radon levels in nitrogen gas and the residual radon in the gas filter used in the DEAP-3600 processing system. The radon concentration in the glove box, where critical DEAP-3600 internal detector components were completed, was also calculated based on these measurements. Now calibrated and in-use, the COLD lab radon emanation counter is an essential diagnostic tool for reducing backgrounds in future rate-event search experiments.

### [116] [NTL-amplified cryogenic light detectors with optically transparent electrodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25730)
*Matteo Biassoni,Andrea Nava,Oscar Azzolini,Mattia Beretta,Tommaso Bradanini,Chiara Brofferio,Paolo Carniti,Simone Copello,Mourad El Idrissi,Marco Faverzani,Elena Ferri,Massimo Girola,Luca Gironi,Claudio Gotti,Léonard Imbert,Giorgio Keppel,Nicola Manenti,Ilaria Molinari,Irene Nutini,Maura Pavan,Daniele Peracchi,Gianluigi Pessina,Sonja Schneidewind,Davide Trotta*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于透明氧化铟锡（ITO）电极的硅光探测器技术，在毫开尔文温度下利用Neganov-Trofimov-Luke（NTL）效应实现信号放大，同时利用ITO电极兼具抗反射涂层功能，简化了器件制备流程。研究完成了首批探测器的室温与低温表征，并建立了适用于电离粒子和光学光子的NTL增益解析模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低温探测器实验利用Neganov-Trofimov-Luke（NTL）效应提升光敏器件的灵敏度至单光子水平。现有技术中，实现NTL放大所需的结构（如电极与抗反射层）通常分离设计，导致制备工艺复杂、成本较高。本文旨在通过引入透明氧化铟锡（ITO）电极，将电场施加与抗反射功能集成于同一元件，从而简化工艺、提升器件鲁棒性与经济性。

Method: 采用透明的氧化铟锡（ITO）电极在毫开尔文温度下实现NTL放大。ITO电极可产生垂直于晶片表面的电场，抑制表面电荷复合，并凭借其光学特性同时充当抗反射涂层。研究对首批探测器进行了室温下的结构性与光学特性表征，并在毫开尔文温度下将其中两个器件作为低温量热器（cryogenic calorimeter）运行。此外，开发了一个一致的解析模型，描述电离粒子和光学光子的NTL增益，显式考虑器件表面的部分电极覆盖率对增益偏压依赖性的影响。

Result: 室温表征验证了所沉积ITO电极的结构与光学特性符合预期。在毫开尔文温度下成功运行了两个器件作为低温量热器。所建立的NTL增益解析模型能够准确描述增益随NTL偏压的变化关系，并成功解释了部分电极覆盖率对增益行为的影响。

Conclusion: 证明基于ITO电极的硅光探测器技术可在毫开尔文温度下有效实现NTL放大，且通过电极与抗反射涂层的功能集成，简化了器件制备。该技术路线有望为需要单光子灵敏度的低温探测实验提供更稳健、成本更低的器件方案。

Abstract: The Neganov-Trofimov-Luke (NTL) effect is used by experiments based on cryogenic detectors to boost the sensitivity of light-sensitive devices down to a few optical photons. In this work we introduce a silicon light-detector technology that implements NTL amplification at millikelvin temperatures using transparent indium-tin-oxide (ITO) electrodes. The ITO electrodes enable an electric field perpendicular to the wafer surface, mitigating surface charge recombination, and thanks to their optical properties, simultaneously serve as an anti-reflective coating. By combining these two functions in a single element, the fabrication process is simplified, yielding more robust and cost-effective devices. We report on the production and characterization of the first batch of these detectors. We performed a room-temperature characterization of the ITO electrodes, verifying the structural and optical characteristics of the deposited electrodes. We then operated 2 of these devices as cryogenic calorimeters at millikelvin temperatures. Finally, we develop a consistent analytical model for the NTL gain for both ionizing particles and optical photons, successfully describing the gain dependence on the NTL bias and explicitly accounting for the partial electrode coverage of the device surface.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计并开发了专用于SPMT系统的水下前端电子学，包含128个PMT通道的读出链（readout chain），支持数字化采集、同步时间戳（time-stamping）、电荷测量、事件打包（event packaging）和带宽管理（bandwidth management），并进行了机械、热学集成及系统级验证。

Result: 该电子学系统达到0.04光电子的噪声水平，串扰（crosstalk）低于0.4%，带宽达57 MB/s，确保在高计数率条件下可靠实现单光电子检测。系统已完全集成并安装于JUNO探测器。

Conclusion: 综合验证结果表明该水下电子学系统已准备就绪，能够满足JUNO严格的物理目标需求。系统的调试运行和物理性能将在后续论文中报告。

Abstract: The Jiangmen Underground Neutrino Observatory (JUNO) is a 20-kton liquid scintillator-based, low-radioactivity, multi-purpose neutrino detector located 693 meters (1800 m.w.e.) underground in the Guangdong province, China. To detect scintillation light produced in the target, the detector is equipped with 17,612 20-inch photomultipliers (PMTs), forming the Large PMT system (LPMT). In addition, 25,600 3-inch photomultipliers (the Small Photomultiplier System or SPMT) are deployed in the gaps between the LPMTs.
  This paper presents the design and performance of the underwater front-end electronics developed for the SPMT system. It details the individual electronics boards and their key components, the inter-board interfaces, the system-level design, and the firmware architecture that supports data acquisition and control. It also outlines mechanical and thermal integration, board validation procedures, and system performance metrics. The readout chain includes digitization of 128 PMT channels per unit, synchronized time-stamping, charge measurement, event packaging, and bandwidth management. Comprehensive validation confirms the system's readiness to meet JUNO's stringent physics goals. The underwater electronics achieve noise levels as low as 0.04 photoelectrons with minimal crosstalk (below 0.4%) and a bandwidth of 57 MB/s, ensuring reliable single photo-electron detection and operation under high-rate conditions. The SPMT system has now been fully integrated and installed in JUNO. Its commissioning and physics performance will be reported in a future publication.

### [118] [Nonlocal Cooper pairs in finite topological superconductors and their relation to Majorana nonlocality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25169)
*Hiroto Mizoguchi,Yutaro Nagae,Yasuhiro Asano,Satoshi Ikegaya*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文发现有限一维拓扑超导体中Gor'kov格林函数的两个基本性质：低频下正常格林函数和反常格林函数除了相位因子外完全相同，且两者表现出显著的非局域性——系统两端之间的关联随长度指数增长，而局域关联在零频极限下消失。这些特征标志着由杂化马约拉纳端模组成的非局域费米子模所对应的非常规非局域库珀对的出现，并与费米子宇称和非局域输运性质直接相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深入理解有限一维拓扑超导体中马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes）的非局域性，这是拓扑量子计算（topological quantum computation）中的关键概念，但此前缺乏从配对关联（pair correlations）角度对马约拉纳非局域性的系统性分析。

Method: 基于Gor'kov格林函数（Gor'kov Green's function）框架，理论分析有限一维拓扑超导体在低频（低能）区间的正常格林函数（单粒子关联）和反常格林函数（库珀对关联）的性质，考察其频率依赖性和空间非局域性。

Result: (1) 低频下正常格林函数与反常格林函数除了一个相位因子外完全相同；(2) 系统末端之间（非局域）的关联随系统长度呈指数增长，而末端处（局域）的关联在零频极限下趋于零。

Conclusion: 上述结果揭示了由杂化马约拉纳端模（hybridized Majorana end modes）组成的非局域费米子模所对应的非常规非局域库珀对（unconventional nonlocal Cooper pairs），这些非局域库珀对与费米子宇称（fermion parity）和有限拓扑超导体的非局域输运性质直接关联，从而在配对关联层面增进了对马约拉纳非局域性这一拓扑量子计算核心概念的理解。

Abstract: We identify two fundamental properties of the Gor'kov Green's function of finite one-dimensional topological superconductors. In the low-frequency (low-energy) regime, the normal and anomalous Green's functions, which describe single-particle and Cooper-pair correlations, respectively, become identical up to a phase factor. Moreover, they exhibit pronounced nonlocality: correlations between the two ends of the system grow exponentially with system length, whereas local correlations at either end vanish in the zero-frequency limit. These striking features signify the emergence of unconventional nonlocal Cooper pairs associated with a nonlocal fermionic mode composed of hybridized Majorana end modes. The nonlocal Cooper pairs are directly linked to fermion parity and to the nonlocal transport properties of finite topological superconductors. By focusing on pair correlations, our analysis advances the understanding of Majorana nonlocality, a key concept in topological quantum computation.

</details>


### [119] [High-field magneto-optical imaging of superconducting critical states beyond 10 T using a paramagnetic garnet sensor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25274)
*Yuto Kinoshita,Masayuki Toyoda,Yoshiaki Kobayashi,Masayuki Itoh,Masashi Tokunaga*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种在高达13T稳态磁场下的磁光成像（magneto-optical imaging, MOI）技术，能够对超导体的临界态进行空间分辨表征。利用该技术，研究者直接成像了铁基超导体Ba(Fe1-xCox)2As2单晶的磁通分布，并定量重构了临界电流密度（critical current density）Jc的空间分布，同时实现了电流流动的矢量映射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高磁场下超导体临界电流密度Jc的空间分辨表征对基础研究和实际应用均至关重要，但传统技术主要提供体平均（bulk-averaged）值，难以解析Jc的局域变化，尤其是在高磁场条件下。

Method: 采用顺磁Nd-garnet指示剂结合偏振显微镜（polarizing microscope）系统，开发了可在高达13T稳态磁场下工作的磁光成像（MOI）技术。利用该方法对铁基超导体Ba(Fe1-xCox)2As2 (x=0.075)块体单晶在12K和20K温度下进行全样品区域（约1mm）的磁通分布成像，并从测量的磁场分布中定量重构临界电流密度Jc的空间分布。

Result: 提取的Jc磁场依赖性与传统磁化测量（magnetization measurements）结果高度一致。进一步通过将磁场分布转换为局域电流密度分布，实现了样品内电流流动的矢量映射（vector mapping）。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了高场MOI作为一种强大的空间分辨评估超导体临界态的方法，为在高磁场下研究超导体中不均匀的电流输运（inhomogeneous current transport）提供了新途径。

Abstract: Spatially resolved characterization of the critical current density Jc in superconductors under high magnetic fields is crucial for both fundamental understanding and practical applications. However, conventional techniques primarily provide bulk-averaged values, making it difficult to resolve local variations of Jc, especially in high magnetic fields. In this work, we develop a magneto-optical imaging (MOI) technique that enables visualization of superconducting critical states in steady magnetic fields up to 13 T. This is achieved by employing a paramagnetic Nd-garnet indicator combined with a polarizing microscope system. Using this method, we directly image the magnetic flux distribution in a bulk single crystal of an iron-based superconductor Ba(Fe1-xCox)2As2 (x = 0.075) at 12 K and 20 K across the entire sample area (approximately 1 mm). From the measured magnetic field distributions, we quantitatively reconstruct the spatial distribution of the critical current density. The extracted field dependence of Jc is in good agreement with that obtained from conventional magnetization measurements. Furthermore, we demonstrate vector mapping of current flow within the sample by converting the magnetic field distribution into local current-density distributions. Our results establish high-field MOI as a powerful approach for spatially resolved evaluation of superconducting critical states and provide a new pathway for investigating inhomogeneous current transport in superconductors under high magnetic fields.

</details>


### [120] [Differentiation of electron doping and oxygen reduction in electron-doped cuprates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25450)
*M. Miyamoto,M. Horio,K. Moriya,A. Takahashi,K. Tanaka,Y. Koike,T. Adachi,I. Matsuda*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过结合碱金属蒸镀与角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy），在不改变氧含量的条件下向电子掺杂铜氧化物表面注入额外电子，发现长程反铁磁序导致的费米面重构被抑制，而与短程自旋/电荷关联相关的赝能隙（pseudogap）依然存在，表明杂质氧原子对赝能隙的形成有重要贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子掺杂铜氧化物（electron-doped cuprates）的超导性不仅需要化学替代的电子掺杂，还需后生长还原退火处理，但还原退火同时改变电子浓度和氧非化学计量比（oxygen non-stoichiometry），导致难以区分两者各自的贡献。本研究旨在解耦电子浓度与氧含量变化对电子结构的影响。

Method: 将碱金属蒸镀（alkali-metal dosing）与角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）结合，在不改变氧含量的情况下向电子掺杂铜氧化物表面注入额外电子，并监测其电子结构变化。

Result: 碱金属沉积抑制了由长程反铁磁序（long-range antiferromagnetic order）导致的费米面重构（Fermi surface reconstruction），而与短程自旋/电荷关联（short-range spin/charge correlations）相关的赝能隙（pseudogap）并未被抑制，仍然存在。

Conclusion: 杂质氧原子（impurity oxygen atoms）对电子掺杂铜氧化物中赝能隙的形成具有显著贡献，这说明仅靠电子浓度变化无法完全解释赝能隙的行为，氧非化学计量比是关键因素。

Abstract: Electron-doped cuprates require not only electron doping by chemical substitution but also post-growth reduction annealing for realizing superconductivity. However, electron concentration can also be varied by reduction annealing, making it challenging to disentangle the respective influences of electron concentration and oxygen non-stoichiometry. Here, by combining alkali-metal dosing and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, we monitored changes in the electronic structure of an electron-doped cuprate while supplying additional electrons to its surface without modifying oxygen content. Whereas a Fermi surface reconstruction due to long-range antiferromagnetic order was suppressed by alkali-metal deposition, the pseudogap -- which is associated with short-range spin/charge correlations and can be suppressed by efficient reduction annealing -- was found to persist. The results highlight significant contribution of impurity oxygen atoms to pseudogap formation in electron-doped cuprates.

</details>


### [121] [Critical Role of Hydrogen in Unconventional Superconductors: The Case of Hydrogenated FeSe Layers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25500)
*Lan-Lin Du,Yang Yang,Shiqi Hu,Sheng Meng*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究以氢化FeSe为原型，揭示了在强电子关联（strong electronic correlations）存在下，氢如何通过关联诱导的轨道重整化（orbital renormalization）将谱权重从高能区移至费米面（Fermi surface, FS），显著增强电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling, EPC），并预测出超导转变温度（Tc）超过40 K的稳定FeSeH相，从而为铁基超导提供了一种关联增强EPC的微观机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢化作用已被证实可调控多种材料的超导电性，但在铜氧化物（cuprates）和铁基超导体（iron-based superconductors）等强关联体系中，氢的微观作用机制仍不清楚，甚至其基本结构基元（structural motifs）也尚未明确。

Method: 以氢化FeSe为原型体系，采用第一性原理电子-声子耦合（EPC）计算结合动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean field theory, DMFT）的方法，并辅以全各向异性Eliashberg理论（fully anisotropic Eliashberg theory）分析超导能隙结构。

Result: 预测了一个结构稳定的FeSeH相：氢的引入重塑了费米面拓扑（FS topology）并增加了电子-声子散射通道，同时引入高频声子（high-frequency phonons）强化配对；EPC计算结合DMFT得出Tc超过40 K；全各向异性Eliashberg理论揭示了一个两能隙超导态（two-gap superconducting state），与掺杂FeSe中实验观测到的能隙结构一致。

Conclusion: 关联增强的EPC是铁基超导电性的一种可行的微观机制，为强关联体系中的配对问题提供了新视角；同时，氢化FeSe被确立为构建二维超导体和超导量子器件的有前景的平台。

Abstract: Hydrogenation is known to tune superconductivity in a wide range of materials. While its microscopic role has been clarified in phonon-mediated superconductors such as hydrogenated MgB2, LaH10, and H3S, much less is known for hydrogenated cuprates and iron-based superconductors, where even the underlying structural motifs remain elusive. Using hydrogenated FeSe as a prototypical example, we reveal how hydrogen affects superconductivity in the presence of strong electronic correlations: correlation-induced orbital renormalization shifts hydrogen-derived spectral weight from the high-energy region toward the Fermi surface (FS), remarkably enhancing the electron-phonon coupling (EPC). We predict a structurally stable FeSeH phase where, compared to bare FeSe, hydrogen incorporation reshapes the FS topology and increases the number of channels for electron-phonon scattering, while simultaneously introducing high-frequency phonons that strengthen pairing. First-principles EPC calculations combined with dynamical mean field theory (DMFT) yield a superconducting transition temperature (Tc) exceeding 40 K. Fully anisotropic Eliashberg theory reveals a two-gap superconducting state, consistent with the gap structure experimentally observed in doped FeSe. Our findings identify correlation-enhanced EPC as a plausible microscopic mechanism for iron-based superconductivity and offer a new perspective on pairing in strongly correlated systems. In addition, this work establishes hydrogenated FeSe as a promising platform for engineering two-dimensional superconductors and superconducting quantum devices.

</details>


### [122] [Geometric Rashba Control of Polar Pairing at LaAlO$_3$/KTaO$_3$ Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25805)
*Yi Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于埃利亚什伯格（Eliashberg）理论的最小有效框架，将LaAlO₃/KTaO₃界面超导转变温度（T_c）的准线性晶向依赖归因于过阻尼极性纳米区域（PNRs）涨落提供的配对胶，并通过几何拉什巴耦合（Rashba coupling）调控其角度依赖性，同时解释了KTaO₃相较于SrTiO₃界面具有更强取向依赖和更高T_c的原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解LaAlO₃/KTaO₃界面超导转变温度（T_c）随晶向近似线性变化、并与可开关极性纳米区域（PNRs）共存的物理机制。

Method: 构建最小有效埃利亚什伯格（Eliashberg）框架，将过阻尼PNR涨落作为配对胶，并由几何拉什巴耦合（Rashba coupling）控制角度依赖；在简化各向同性螺旋度带（helicity-band）描述下，动力学拉什巴顶点（Rashba vertex）按sin(θ)标度，配对强度λ(θ)=λ₀+C sin²(θ)；采用精确的马祖巴拉–埃利亚什伯格（Matsubara-Eliashberg）数值求解。

Result: 非线性映射在简化模型内自然重现了相同的准线性T_c(θ)依赖关系。基于Ta 5d轨道大原子自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）对拉什巴激活极性通道的放大作用，该框架也解释了KTaO₃界面相较于SrTiO₃界面具有更强取向依赖和更高T_c尺度的原因。

Conclusion: 所提出的埃利亚什伯格（Eliashberg）框架成功统一描述了晶向依赖的超导电性与极性纳米区域（PNRs）共存现象，并为KTaO₃界面超导的增强机制提供了自洽解释。

Abstract: At LaAlO$_3$/KTaO$_3$ interfaces, the superconducting $T_c$ exhibits a striking quasi-linear dependence on crystallographic orientation, coexisting with switchable polar nanoregions (PNRs). We propose an effective minimal Eliashberg framework in which overdamped PNR fluctuations provide the pairing glue, while geometric Rashba coupling controls its angular dependence. Within a reduced isotropic helicity-band description, the dynamic Rashba vertex scales as $\sin(θ)$, yielding a pairing strength $λ(θ)=λ_0+C\sin^2(θ)$. Exact Matsubara-Eliashberg numerical solutions show that this non-linear mapping naturally yields the same qualitative quasi-linear $T_c(θ)$ dependence within the reduced model. Because the Rashba-activated polar channel is amplified by the large atomic spin-orbit coupling of Ta $5d$ orbitals, the same framework also rationalizes why KTaO$_3$ interfaces exhibit both a much stronger orientational dependence and a substantially higher $T_c$ scale than their SrTiO$_3$ counterparts.

</details>


### [123] [Bragg-Williams order competes with superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25843)
*Xu Liu,Xu Chen,Chuizhen Chen,Boqin Song,Jing Chen,Xijing Dai,Qinghua Zhang,Feng Jin,Xingya Wang,Weiwei Dong,Dongliang Yang,Gefei Li,Pengju Zhang,Jiangping Hu,Jian-gang Guo,Tianping Ying,Xiaolong Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文通过In₂/₃PSe₃体系，发现布拉格-威廉斯序（BWO）作为独立序参量可直接与超导电性竞争：无序相在压力下呈现11 K的超导转变温度（Tc），显著高于有序相的7 K，并通过Ginzburg-Landau分析与BCS-McMillan描述结合实验证据，揭示了BWO通过电子-声子相互作用机制抑制超导的物理图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，电荷序和自旋序与非常规超导电性的关联已被广泛研究，但布拉格-威廉斯序（BWO）——一种描述合金中位点占据的经典结构序参量——对超导行为的影响尚不清楚。其作用难以被分离，主要因为BWO总是与电荷掺杂或竞争性电子不稳定性共存。本研究旨在建立可靠的实验平台以孤立地考察BWO对超导电性的影响。

Method: 选取In₂/₃PSe₃作为平台，其中铟空位可通过热处理在有序态与无序态之间可逆调控。对有序相和无序相分别施加压力，测量其超导转变温度（Tc）；结合Ginzburg-Landau唯象分析与BCS-McMillan微观描述进行理论建模，并利用超低波数拉曼散射（ultra-low-wavenumber Raman）测量提供实验支持。

Result: 无序相在压力诱导下发生超导转变，Tc为11 K，显著高于有序相的7 K。这是纯BWO变化驱动Tc发生大幅移动的罕见实例。超低波数拉曼测量支持BWO通过电子-声子相互作用（electron-phonon interactions）抑制超导的机制。

Conclusion: BWO是一个独立于传统电子有序和磁有序的序参量，能够直接与超导电性竞争，从而将竞争序（competing orders）的概念从常规的电子和磁自由度拓展至结构自由度。

Abstract: Orderings in charge and spin have been extensively studied to unravel their correlation to emergent superconductivity over the past decades. Bragg-Williams order (BWO), a classical structural order parameter describing site occupancy in alloys, has long been speculated to influence superconducting behavior. Yet, its role still remains ambiguous, largely due to the difficulty of isolating BWO from concomitant charge doping or competing electronic instabilities. Here, we establish In2/3PSe3 as a platform wherein indium vacancies are reversibly configurable between ordered and disordered states via thermal treatment. We show that the disordered phase undergoes a pressure-induced superconducting transition with a Tc of 11 K, significantly higher than the 7 K observed in its ordered counterpart. This constitutes a rare instance in which pure BWO variation drives a substantial shift in Tc. By combining a Ginzburg-Landau phenomenological analysis with a BCS-McMillan microscopic description, we demonstrate that BWO naturally suppresses superconductivity through electron-phonon interactions, a mechanism supported by ultra-low-wavenumber Raman measurements. Our findings support BWO as an independent order parameter that competes directly with superconductivity, extending the concept of competing orders beyond conventional electronic and magnetic degrees of freedom.

</details>


### [124] [Thermodynamic Identification of the Internal Superconducting Phase Boundary in UTe$_2$ for $H \parallel b$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25896)
*Michal Vališka,Tetiana Haidamak,Andrej Cabala,Petr Proschek,Andreas Hausprug,Sergei Zherlitsyn,Vladimír Sechovský*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文利用超声测量在超净UTe₂单晶中沿硬b轴方向磁场下，首次提供了约14–15 T处内部边界的体热力学证据，确认其为相边界并揭示其与晶格应变的对称选择性耦合，最终在H–T相图中定位到一个四临界点，支持UTe₂中磁场诱导的多组分超导电性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: UTe₂在磁场沿硬b轴方向的H–T相图中，约14–15 T附近存在一个先前由交流磁化率（ac susceptibility）和输运实验推测但缺乏热力学证据的内部边界，本研究旨在通过超声测量提供该边界的热力学确认。

Method: 对一块超净（ultraclean）UTe₂单晶（T_c > 2 K）在H ∥ b方向、0.33 K至18 T范围内，测量了多种弹性模量的超声响应。

Result: 纵向C₃₃模出现显著异常，C₄₄模响应较弱，C₅₅模无可分辨异常，表明该特征为体热力学相边界（bulk thermodynamic phase boundary）并具有对称选择性耦合（symmetry-selective coupling）到晶格应变。该相界线在约14 T附近近乎恒定，终止于约13.5 T和1.25 K处的四临界点（tetracritical point）。

Conclusion: 该结果为H–T相图提供了第四条相边界的热力学证据，约束了高磁场相的有序参量结构（order-parameter structure），并支持UTe₂中磁场诱导的多组分超导电性（field-induced multicomponent superconductivity）。

Abstract: The $H$--$T$ phase diagram of UTe$_2$ for magnetic field along the hard $b$ axis contains an unresolved internal boundary near $μ_0H \sim 14$--15~T, previously inferred from ac susceptibility and transport experiments but lacking thermodynamic evidence. We report ultrasound results for several elastic modes in an ultraclean UTe$_2$ single crystal with $T_c>2$~K for $H \parallel b$ down to 0.33~K and up to 18~T. A pronounced anomaly in the longitudinal $C_{33}$ mode, with a weaker response in $C_{44}$ and no resolvable anomaly in $C_{55}$, establishes this feature as a bulk thermodynamic phase boundary and reveals a symmetry-selective coupling to lattice strain. The phase line remains nearly constant in field near 14~T and terminates near 13.5~T and 1.25~K at a tetracritical point, providing the thermodynamic evidence for the fourth phase boundary in the $H$--$T$ phase diagram. The results constrain the order-parameter structure of the high-field phase and support field-induced multicomponent superconductivity in UTe$_2$.

### [125] [The Classification of Pauli Stabilizer Codes: A Lattice and Continuum Treatise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24847)
*Bowen Yang,Matthew Yu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于代数L-理论（algebraic L-theory）框架，对移动泡利稳定子码（mobile Pauli stabilizer codes）在有隙界面（gapped interfaces）和粗粒化（coarse-graining）意义下进行分类，并与有框拓扑量子场论（framed TQFTs）的分类进行结构比较，建立了一个适用于晶格理论的体-边界对应（bulk-boundary correspondence）关系，并引入了稳定子码的普适目标范畴（universal target category）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有的连续统理论（如TQFT）分类框架难以直接适用于晶格（lattice）上的泡利稳定子码，二者之间的分类关系尚未被系统揭示。本文旨在建立一个能统一处理晶格理论与连续统理论的分类方案，并明确二者之间的结构异同。

Method: 利用代数L-理论框架，在劳伦多项式环（Laurent polynomial ring）$R = \mathbb{Z}/p[x_1^{\pm 1}, \ldots, x_n^{\pm 1}]$上的完美链复形（perfect chain complexes）范畴中，配备二次函子（quadratic functor），将泡利稳定子码的拓扑算符（topological operators）集合作为该范畴中的对象进行处理。进一步引入稳定子码的普适目标范畴——一种具有存在性和普适性质的范畴谱（categorical spectrum）。

Result: 建立了晶格理论的体-边界对应：泡利稳定子码在有隙界面意义下的等价类可由高一维的克利福德量子元胞自动机（Clifford QCA）描述。同时指出，泡利稳定子码的分类与TQFT分类之间存在细微差异，导致了晶格理论与连续统理论的定性区别。

Conclusion: 通过代数L-理论构建的分类框架，揭示了泡利稳定子码与有框TQFT之间的紧密结构关系，但二者并不完全等价。这一工作为理解晶格理论与连续统理论之间的异同提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We classify mobile Pauli stabilizer codes up to gapped interfaces and coarse-graining using the framework of algebraic $\mathrm{L}$-theory. We compare this classification with that of framed TQFTs, theories that arise naturally in the continuum, highlighting a close structural relationship between the two. Our approach is formulated in the category of perfect chain complexes equipped with quadratic functor over the Laurent polynomial ring $R = \mathbb{Z}/p[x_1^{\pm 1}, \ldots, x_n^{\pm 1}]$, within which the collection of topological operators of Pauli stabilizer codes arise naturally as objects. In particular, we establish a bulk-boundary correspondence for lattice theories: the equivalence class of a Pauli stabilizer code up to gapped interface is described by a Clifford QCA in one dimension higher. This is done using the universal target category for stabilizer codes, which is the categorical spectrum whose existence and universal properties are introduced in this work. We conclude by highlighting subtle differences between the classification of Pauli stabilizer codes and TQFTs, leading to qualitative distinctions between lattice and continuum theories.

### [126] [Prefactorization algebras of superselection sectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24865)
*Marco Benini,Victor Carmona,Alexander Schenkel*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文从预因子化代数（prefactorization algebras）的现代视角重新审视代数量子场论（algebraic quantum field theory, AQFT）中的超选择扇区（superselection sectors）理论。在Haag对偶性（Haag duality）和局部忠实真空表示（locally faithful vacuum representation）的标准假设下，证明了每个定义在满足一定几何假设的过滤正交时空区域范畴上的AQFT，都有一个相伴的局部常值$C^\ast$-范畴预因子化代数。对于$(n\geq 2)$维闵可夫斯基时空中的双锥体情形，该方法通过Dunn-Lurie可加性（additivity）$\mathbb{E}_n\simeq \mathbb{E}_1\otimes \mathbb{E}_{n-1}$，将来自Haag对偶性的$\mathbb{E}_1$-幺半结构（monoidal structure）与来自洛伦兹几何（Lorentzian geometry）的$\mathbb{E}_{n-1}$-幺半结构相结合，为超选择扇区的$C^\ast$-范畴上著名的$\mathbb{E}_n$-幺半结构提供了概念性解释。文章还将结果推广到离散群$G$下的等变（equivariant）语境中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从预因子化代数的现代视角重新理解和统一代数量子场论中的超选择扇区理论，并为超选择扇区范畴上已知的$\mathbb{E}_n$-幺半结构提供概念性解释。

Method: 基于预因子化代数（prefactorization algebras）的框架，在Haag对偶性和局部忠实真空表示的假设下，对定义在过滤正交范畴上的AQFT构造其相伴的局部常值$C^\ast$-范畴预因子化代数；利用Dunn-Lurie可加性$\mathbb{E}_n\simeq \mathbb{E}_1\otimes \mathbb{E}_{n-1}$分解$\mathbb{E}_n$-幺半结构。

Result: 每个满足适当几何假设的AQFT都有一个相伴的局部常值$C^\ast$-范畴预因子化代数；超选择扇区的$\mathbb{E}_n$-幺半结构可分解为来自Haag对偶性的$\mathbb{E}_1$部分和来自洛伦兹几何的$\mathbb{E}_{n-1}$部分；结果可推广到离散群$G$下的等变语境。

Conclusion: 预因子化代数视角能够为AQFT中超选择扇区的代数结构提供统一且概念清晰的理论框架，并自然地兼容等变推广。

Abstract: This paper revisits the theory of superselection sectors in algebraic quantum field theory from the modern perspective of prefactorization algebras. Under the standard assumptions of Haag duality and a locally faithful vacuum representation, it is shown that every AQFT defined over a filtered orthogonal category of spacetime regions, satisfying some mild additional geometric hypotheses, has an associated locally constant $C^\ast$-categorical prefactorization algebra of superselection sectors over the same orthogonal category. In the case of double cones in the $(n\geq 2)$-dimensional Minkowski spacetime, our approach provides a conceptual explanation for the well-known $\mathbb{E}_n$-monoidal structure on the $C^\ast$-category of superselection sectors as the combination, through Dunn-Lurie additivity $\mathbb{E}_n\simeq \mathbb{E}_1\otimes \mathbb{E}_{n-1}$, of the familiar $\mathbb{E}_1$-monoidal structure from Haag duality and an $\mathbb{E}_{n-1}$-monoidal structure from Lorentzian geometry. A refinement of our results to equivariant contexts under a discrete group $G$ is also provided.

### [127] [Invariant Measures in Hamiltonian Systems: The Analytical Foundations of Statistical Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25066)
*Luis A. Cedeño-Pérez,Alexis E. López-Velázquez*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在哈密顿函数水平集上构造了一种短时不变、长时流保持的测度，从而为固定能量状态空间中的哈密顿系统提供了概率论研究框架。该测度生成了物理学中的微正则配分函数（microcanonical partition function），并在渐近极限下可转化为正则配分函数（canonical partition function），从而复现经典统计物理（classical statistical physics）。此外，这一方法还为西蒙第二问题（Simon's second problem）提供了替代性解答。
