  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为哈密顿系统（Hamiltonian system）在固定能量状态空间中建立一种严格概率论框架，并弥合微正则系综（microcanonical ensemble）与正则系综（canonical ensemble）之间的数学联系。

Method: 在哈密顿函数水平集（level set）上构造一种在短时哈密顿流（Hamiltonian flow）下不变、在任意长时间下保持流不变性的测度（measure）。

Result: 该测度生成了物理上使用的微正则配分函数，并在渐近极限下可转换为正则配分函数，从而复现经典统计物理的全部内容。同时，该方法给出了西蒙第二问题的一个替代解答。

Conclusion: 构造的测度为固定能量哈密顿系统的概率论研究提供了严格基础，在渐近意义上统一了微正则与正则系综，并解决了西蒙第二问题。

Abstract: We construct a measure in the hamiltonian function level sets that is invariant under the hamiltonian flow for short times and flow preserving for arbitrarily long times. This allows a probabilistic approach to the study of hamiltonian systems, in the space of states with fixed energy. We prove that this measure generates the microcanonical partition function employed in physics and show that it can be transformed into the canonical partition function in an asymptotic limit, hence reproducing classical Statistical Physics. We also argue that this gives an alternative solution to Simon's second problem.

### [128] [Gegenbauer polynomials and fluctuation properties of the one-dimensional Riesz gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25078)
*Peter J. Forrester*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用Beenakker泛函导数方法，计算了一维Riesz气体在无穷密度极限下光滑线性统计量的协方差，给出了基于盖根鲍尔多项式（Gegenbauer polynomial）展开的泛化公式，并将幂和统计量的结果简化为伽马函数（gamma function）乘积形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的一维Riesz气体（Riesz gas）在s=0（对数势）情形下的线性统计量协方差已有已知的余弦展开形式，本文旨在将该结果推广到更一般的指数s ∈ (-1,1)、s ≠ 0的情形。

Method: 采用Beenakker提出的泛函导数方法（functional derivative method），在粒子支撑集为区间[-1,1]的无穷密度极限下，计算两个光滑线性统计量（smooth linear statistics）的协方差。将结果展开为关于盖根鲍尔多项式（Gegenbauer polynomial）{C_n^{(s/2)}(x)}基的傅里叶分量（Fourier component）求和形式。

Result: 得到了Riesz气体在s ∈ (-1,1)、s ≠ 0情形下光滑线性统计量协方差的通用公式，该公式以盖根鲍尔多项式展开的傅里叶分量之和表示。对于幂和（power sum）线性统计量，通用公式可简化为伽马函数（gamma function）的乘积形式。

Conclusion: 该结果将已知的s=0（对数势）情形下的余弦展开公式推广到了更广泛的s ∈ (-1,1)区间，并与近期文献中幂和统计量的精确结果一致。

Abstract: The Riesz gas in one-dimension consists of particles interacting via a pair potential, ${\rm sgn}(s) |x - x'|^{-s}$, $s \ne 0$ and $-\log | x - x'|$ for $s=0$. In the infinite density limit, with the particle support the interval $[-1,1]$, we apply a functional derivative method due to Beenakker to compute the covariance of two smooth linear statistics for the Riesz gas with exponent $s \in (-1,1)$, $s \ne 0$. This we give in terms of a sum over Fourier components of the linear statistics with respect to a Gegenbauer polynomial $\{C_n^{(s/2)}(x) \}$ basis, which generalises a known form in the case $s=0$ involving a cosine expansion. For the power sum linear statistic, our general formula can be reduced to a product of gamma function form, and compared against recent exact results in the literature for this case.

</details>


### [129] [Lie symmetry classification and invariant solutions of time-fractional telegraph systems with variable coefficients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25079)
*Sodbaatar Adiya,Khongorzul Dorjgotov,Bayarmagnai Gombodorj,Bayarpurev Mongol,Uuganbayar Zunderiya*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用李对称分析（Lie symmetry analysis）和Riemann-Liouville分数阶导数，对一类具有空间变化系数的时间分数阶电报方程（time-fractional telegraph equations）进行了完整的李群分类（Lie group classification），推导出三种对称类及其最优系统，得到了以Mittag-Leffler函数、广义Wright函数和Fox H-函数表示的精确不变解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间分数阶电报方程是描述具有记忆效应（memory effects）和非局域性（nonlocal effects）的输运过程的基础数学模型，广泛应用于热传导、粘弹性介质波动和半导体器件电荷输运等工业与物理系统中，但空间变系数情形下的对称结构与精确解尚待系统研究。

Method: 采用李对称分析结合Riemann-Liouville分数阶导数（Riemann-Liouville fractional derivative），对具有空间变化系数的时间分数阶电报系统进行分类；构建一维李子代数（Lie subalgebras）的最优系统（optimal systems），将分数阶偏微分方程约化为分数阶常微分方程。

Result: 建立了系数函数在充分可微条件下的完整李群分类，确定了三类对称结构，其分类依赖于输运系数与势函数之间的关系；获得了以Mittag-Leffler函数（Mittag-Leffler functions）、广义Wright函数（generalized Wright functions）和Fox H-函数（Fox H-functions）表示的闭式精确不变解。

Conclusion: 所得解析解为分数阶电报型输运现象提供了重要理论洞见，并可作为工业输运建模与分数阶演化系统数值方法验证的关键基准。

Abstract: Time-fractional telegraph equations provide fundamental mathematical models for transport processes that exhibit memory and nonlocal effects in industrial and physical systems. These models arise naturally in heat transport in materials with thermal memory, wave propagation in viscoelastic media, and charge transport in spatially heterogeneous semiconductor devices. In this study, we investigate a class of time-fractional telegraph systems with spatially varying coefficients using Lie symmetry analysis and the Riemann--Liouville fractional derivative. We establish a complete Lie group classification for sufficiently differentiable coefficient functions and determine all functional forms that admit such symmetry extensions. The symmetry structure is shown to depend fundamentally on the relationship between the transport coefficient and the potential function, resulting in three distinct symmetry classes. For each case, optimal systems of one-dimensional Lie subalgebras are constructed, and the governing fractional partial differential equations are systematically reduced to fractional ordinary differential equations. Exact invariant solutions are obtained in closed form and expressed in terms of Mittag--Leffler functions, generalized Wright functions, and Fox $H$-functions. These analytical solutions provide valuable insights into fractional telegraph-type transport phenomena and serve as important benchmarks for validating numerical methods in industrial transport modeling and fractional evolution systems.

</details>


### [130] [The SK model with a sparse variance profile: free energy and AMP algorithm for TAP equations at high temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25535)
*Walid Hachem*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文对Sherrington-Kirkpatrick（SK）自旋玻璃模型进行了推广，考虑了具有任意方差剖面（variance profile）且可能稀疏的相互作用矩阵。第一部分在足够高温下推导了自由能（free energy）的渐近等价形式；第二部分利用基于Thouless-Anderson-Palmer（TAP）方程的近似消息传递算法（Approximate Message Passing, AMP）估计Gibbs测度下的自旋向量均值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典SK模型假设相互作用矩阵具有全连接且方差均匀的结构，而真实系统中相互作用往往具有异质性（heterogeneity）和稀疏性（sparsity）。本文旨在推广SK模型至更一般的方差剖面，并研究其在高温度区间的统计力学性质。

Method: 第一部分采用解析方法推导自由能的渐近等价形式，不依赖于方差剖面矩阵的符号特征（signature）。第二部分将Adhikari等人（J. Stat. Phys., 2021）针对经典SK模型发展的动力学方法（dynamical approach）加以改编，结合TAP方程构建AMP算法，用于估计Gibbs测度下的自旋向量均值。

Result: 在足够高的温度下，无论方差剖面矩阵的符号特征如何，均可获得自由能的渐近等价表达式。同时，基于TAP方程的AMP算法能够有效估计Gibbs测度下的自旋均值。

Conclusion: 本文所推广的SK模型在高温区域具有良好的可解性，且所提出的动力学方法适用于具有一般方差剖面的自旋玻璃系统，为处理异质性和稀疏性相互作用提供了理论工具。

Abstract: A generalization of the Sherrington-Kirkpatrick (SK) model for spin glasses is considered, in which the interaction matrix is endowed with a variance profile that has no particular structure an may be sparse. In the first part of this paper, an asymptotic equivalent of the free energy is derived at sufficiently high temperatures, regardless of the signature of the variance profile matrix. In the second part, the mean of the spin vector under the Gibbs measure is estimated using an Approximate Message Passing algorithm based on the Thouless-Anderson-Palmer equations. The dynamical approach of Adhikari et.al. (J. Stat. Phys., 2021), originally developed for the classical SK model, is adapted to the present setting to obtain these results.

</details>


### [131] [Geometry of Logarithmic Topological Recursion: Dilaton Equations, Free Energies and Variational Formulas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25622)
*Alexander Hock,Olivier Marchal,Nicolas Orantin*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在拓扑递归（topological recursion）的对数推广——即对数拓扑递归（logarithmic topological recursion）框架下，推导了胀子方程（dilaton equations）与变分公式（variational formulas），并给出了在标准拓扑递归失效情形下自由能（free energies）的定义。该新定义可直接复现4d $\mathcal{N}=2$纯超对称规范理论的Nekrasov–Shatashvili配分函数（partition function）的完整微扰部分，以及条带几何（strip geometries）镜像曲线（mirror curves）的全亏格自由能，其中包括拓扑顶点（topological vertex）与解链锥形（resolved conifold）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑递归在谱曲线（spectral curves）的函数$(x,y)$出现对数奇点（logarithmic singularities）时具有重要应用，例如Seiberg–Witten曲线与计算环面卡拉比–丘三折叠（toric Calabi–Yau threefolds）的Gromov–Witten不变量的镜像曲线。标准拓扑递归在此类曲线下存在局限性，因此需要发展对数拓扑递归及其相关方程与自由能定义。

Method: 本文在对数拓扑递归框架下，推导了胀子方程与变分公式，并给出了自由能在标准拓扑递归失效情况下的新定义。

Result: 新定义的自由能可直接复现4d $\mathcal{N}=2$纯超对称规范理论的Nekrasov–Shatashvili配分函数的完整微扰部分，以及条带几何镜像曲线的全亏格自由能，包括拓扑顶点与解链锥形。

Conclusion: 对数拓扑递归及其新自由能定义为处理具有对数奇点的谱曲线提供了有效工具，可覆盖标准拓扑递归无法处理的场景，并在多个物理与几何模型中取得直接验证。

Abstract: One of the most important applications of topological recursion concerns spectral curves for which the functions $(x,y)$ defining the spectral curve are allowed to have logarithmic singularities. This occurs for instance for Seiberg-Witten curves and mirror curves computing Gromov--Witten invariants of toric Calabi--Yau threefolds. A recently introduced extension of topological recursion, the so-called logarithmic topological recursion, exhibits the correct behavior under certain limits of those spectral curves.
  In this article, we derive the dilaton equations in the setting of logarithmic topological recursion, as well as variational formulas, and provide a definition of the free energies in situations where standard topological recursion was known to fail. We present examples in which the new definition of the free energies \textit{directly} (without any computation) reproduces the full perturbative part of the Nekrasov--Shatashvili partition function of 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ pure supersymmetric gauge theory, as well as the all-genus free energies of mirror curves of strip geometries, including in particular the topological vertex and the resolved conifold.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用有限差分算子（finite difference operators）作为构造工具，分别在连续傅里叶变换（continuous Fourier transform）和离散傅里叶变换（discrete Fourier transform）的多维情形下，系统构造相位恢复的非唯一性反例。

Result: 得到了包含稀疏性条件在内的一大类非唯一性例子；构造了大量非平凡的Pauli对（即两个不同的函数在配置域和傅里叶域中具有相同的强度分布）；解决了傅里叶全息等领域中关于背景信息的相位恢复的一个长期开放问题。

Conclusion: 有限差分算子为多维相位恢复的非唯一性构造提供了一种统一且有效的方法，其成果不仅推广了已有的连续情形结果，还对离散信号处理、稀疏恢复以及全息成像等应用领域具有重要理论意义。

Abstract: We continue studies on phase retrieval for continuous and discrete Fourier transforms in multidimensions. Using finite difference operators, we give a large class of unexpected examples of non-uniqueness for this problem, including examples with the sparsity condition. A prototype of this construction in the continuous case is given in the work Novikov, Xu (JFAA, 2026), using linear differential operators. The construction of the present work also yields a large class of non-trivial Pauli partners, i.e., different functions with the same intensities in both configuration and Fourier domains. Besides, our construction yields examples that solve an old open question in phase retrieval with background information arising in many areas including Fourier holography.

### [133] [Co-rotating Vortices on Surfaces of Variable Negative Curvature: Hamiltonian Structure and Drift Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25682)
*Gaurang Mangesh Joshi,Rickmoy Samanta*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究在悬链面（catenoid）——一种具有可变负高斯曲率（Gaussian curvature）的最小曲面——上的哈密顿涡旋运动（Hamiltonian vortex motion），推导了显式运动方程、守恒量及共转涡旋对的约化理论，发现运动由曲率梯度而非曲率本身主导，对称态线性不稳定，并揭示了弯曲面上的集体涡旋漂移机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流体和超流体中的涡旋（vortices）广泛存在于玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensate）、超流体薄膜、中子星及水动力微转子等现象中，曲面几何可强烈影响涡旋运动，且曲率（curvature）可诱发无平面类比（planar analogue）的运动模式。本文旨在系统研究负曲率最小曲面上的涡旋动力学。

Method: 采用哈密顿形式（Hamiltonian formalism）推导悬链面上的涡旋运动方程；利用守恒量（哈密顿量和旋转动量）将非线性动力学约化为单求积（single quadrature）；对相同强度涡旋对进行解析求解和线性稳定性分析；通过数值模拟验证约化理论和曲率诱导的输运机制。

Result: 推导了显式运动方程与守恒量；发现两相同涡旋的对跖解（antipodal solution），涡旋对在固定纬度刚性旋转，角速度由高斯曲率的梯度而非曲率本身决定：$Ω=(Γ/16π)\,K'(V)/\sqrt{-K(V)}$；该对称态线性不稳定，增长率 $λ=\sqrt{3}|Ω|$；一般等强度涡旋对呈现有界相对振荡及长期方位漂移（secular azimuthal drift）；数值模拟验证了约化理论，并发现同样的曲率诱导输运机制在局域多涡旋团簇中依然成立。

Conclusion: 负曲率最小曲面上的涡旋运动由曲率梯度主导，对称涡旋对存在不稳定性，守恒量约化有效描述了非线性动力学。曲率诱导的集体漂移机制在多个涡旋系统中普遍存在，为建立弯曲面上集体涡旋漂移（collective vortex drift）的更广泛理论提供了基础。

Abstract: Vortices in fluids and superfluids underpin phenomena ranging from Bose--Einstein condensates and superfluid films to neutron stars and hydrodynamic micro-rotors, where geometry can strongly influence their motion. Curvature can induce vortex motion with no planar analogue. We study Hamiltonian vortex motion on a catenoid, a minimal surface of variable negative curvature, and derive explicit equations of motion, conserved quantities, and reductions for co-rotating vortex pairs. For two identical vortices we find an exact antipodal solution in which the pair rotates rigidly at fixed latitude, with angular velocity $Ω=(Γ/16π)\,K'(V)/\sqrt{-K(V)}$, where $K(V)$ is the Gaussian curvature. Thus the motion is governed by the curvature gradient rather than the curvature itself. The symmetric state is linearly unstable, with growth rate $λ=\sqrt{3}|Ω|$, in agreement with numerical simulations. For generic equal-strength pairs, conservation of the Hamiltonian and rotational momentum reduces the nonlinear dynamics to a single quadrature, yielding bounded relative oscillations together with a secular azimuthal drift. Simulations of the full equations confirm the reduced theory and reveal the same curvature-induced transport mechanism in a localized many-vortex cluster, motivating a broader theory of collective vortex drift on curved surfaces.

### [134] [Griffiths inequalities and Gibbs-Bogoliubov inequality for general gauge glasses with Gaussian disorder on Nishimori line](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25697)
*Manaka Okuyama,Masayuki Ohzeki*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了一类沿西森线（Nishimori line）的高斯无序规范玻璃模型（gauge glass models）满足第一、第二Griffiths不等式，并建立了类似Gibbs–Bogoliubov不等式的结论，从而表明复制对称平均场近似（replica-symmetric mean-field approximation）给出的淬火自由能（quenched free energy）总是高于真实值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前关于西森线上高斯无序伊辛自旋玻璃（Ising spin glass）的Griffiths不等式和自由能变分性质已得到证明，但尚未推广到更广泛的规范玻璃模型类。本文旨在建立这些不等式在更一般模型类中的成立性，以深化对无序系统中西森线性质的理解。

Method: 通过理论分析与数学证明，作者考察了包含伊辛自旋玻璃、XY规范玻璃、Z_q规范玻璃以及规范不变波茨模型（gauge-invariant Potts model）在内的模型类。在任意晶格结构上，严格证明了第一、第二Griffiths不等式成立，并推导出Gibbs–Bogoliubov不等式在该类模型中的类似形式。

Result: 沿西森线，压力（pressure）和相关函数（correlation functions）关于逆温度（inverse temperature）单调递增；此外，采用复制对称平均场近似的复制方法（replica method）得到的近似淬火自由能总是大于真实的淬火自由能。

Conclusion: 本文结果是对伊辛自旋玻璃在西森线上已知结论的广泛推广，为理解规范玻璃类模型的统计力学性质提供了更普适的基础。

Abstract: We consider a class of gauge glass models with Gaussian disorder on the Nishimori line, including the Ising spin glass, the $XY$ gauge glass, the $Z_q$ gauge glass, and the gauge-invariant Potts model. We prove that the first and second Griffiths inequalities hold for these models on arbitrary lattice structures. As a consequence, both the pressure and the correlation functions are monotonically increasing with respect to the inverse temperature along the Nishimori line. Furthermore, we establish an analogue of the Gibbs--Bogoliubov inequality for this class of models. This result implies that, on the Nishimori line, the approximate quenched free energy obtained via the replica method with a replica-symmetric mean-field approximation is always greater than the true quenched free energy. Our results provide a broad generalization of previous results established for the Ising spin glass with Gaussian disorder on the Nishimori line.

### [135] [Long-time asymptotics of the Newell equation on the line](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25703)
*Deng-Shan Wang,Yingmin Yang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用Riemann-Hilbert（黎曼-希尔伯特）方法，结合Deift-Zhou（德夫特-周）非线性最速下降法，首次获得了Newell方程（Newell equation）在Schwartz初值条件下的长时间渐近行为（long-time asymptotics）的严格表达式，并通过数值模拟验证了其可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Newell方程（Newell equation）由A. C. Newell于1978年提出，用于模拟长波与短波之间的显著相互作用机制，然而其长时间渐近行为（long-time asymptotics）自提出以来近五十年间始终未有结果报道，成为一个长期悬而未决的问题。

Method: 采用Riemann-Hilbert（黎曼-希尔伯特）方法框架：通过正散射（direct scattering）与逆散射分析（inverse scattering analysis）构造对应的Riemann-Hilbert问题，并利用消失引理（vanishing lemma）证明其解的存在唯一性；随后运用Deift-Zhou（德夫特-周）非线性最速下降法（nonlinear steepest descent method）在色散波区域（dispersive wave region）获得渐近表达式。

Result: 首次获得了Newell方程在Schwartz初值条件下、色散波区域中解的长时间渐近表达式；严格证明了Newell论文第4节中的相关结果，并给出了显式形式；直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulations）与理论结果的对比验证了渐近表达式的可靠性。

Conclusion: 该工作填补了Newell方程长时间渐近行为研究的空白，为长波与短波相互作用模型的渐近分析提供了严格的理论框架；其方法与结果可推广至同类可积系统（integrable systems）的长时间行为研究。

Abstract: In 1978, A. C. Newell [SIAM J. Appl. Math. 35(4) (1978) 650-664] proposed an exactly solvable model called Newell equation, which simulates the investigation of significant interaction mechanism between long and short waves. Nearly fifty years have passed, yet the long-time asymptotics of the Newell equation remains an open problem to date, with no results reported. In this work, the long-time asymptotic behaviors of the solutions to this model under Schwartz class initial conditions are studied by using the Riemann-Hilbert formulation. Through direct and inverse scattering analysis, the corresponding Riemann-Hilbert problem is formulated, and its relationship with the solution to the initial-value problem of the Newell equation is established. The existence and uniqueness of the solution to the Riemann-Hilbert problem is proved by vanishing lemma. Subsequently, the asymptotic expressions of the solution to the initial-value problem in the dispersive wave region are obtained by using the Deift-Zhou nonlinear steepest descent method. This work extends Newell's original results, providing a rigorous proof for the findings presented in Section 4 of his paper, along with explicit expressions. Furthermore, the comparison between direct numerical simulations and the theoretical results obtained in this paper demonstrates the reliability of the asymptotic expressions.

*Hiromu Nakano*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用精化Frobenius同态（Frobenius homomorphism）的技术路径，在$\mathcal{W}_{p_+,p_-}$上显式构造导子，并验证Adamovi\'c-Milas导子性质在该构造下的保持性。随后将该构造推广至三重W-超代数（triplet W-superalgebra）$\mathcal{SW}(m)$，并计算其全自同构群（full automorphism group）。

Result: 构造的导子自然赋予了$\mathcal{W}_{p_+,p_-}$一个$\mathfrak{sl}_2$-对称性（$\mathfrak{sl}_2$-symmetry）。对于$\mathcal{SW}(m)$，该方法同样有效，并确定了其全自同构群为$PSL_2(\mathbb{C})\times \mathbb{Z}_2$。

Conclusion: Frobenius同态的精化是一种统一且可推广的导子构造方案，它连接了三重W-代数与W-超代数的对称性结构，并为计算相关代数的自同构群提供了有效工具。

Abstract: We construct derivations on the triplet $W$-algebras $\mathcal{W}_{p_+,p_-}$ by refining the Frobenius homomorphisms of Tsuchiya-Wood and show that the property of the Adamović-Milas derivation for $\mathcal{W}_{2,p}$ extends to our derivations. As an application, we show that the $\mathfrak{sl}_2$-symmetry of $\mathcal{W}_{p_+,p_-}$ arises naturally from our construction. We further show that our method applies to the triplet $W$-superalgebra $\mathcal{SW}(m)$ and that the full automorphism group ${\rm Aut}(\mathcal{SW}(m))$ is $PSL_2(\mathbb{C})\times \mathbb{Z}_2$.

### [137] [Level Crossing in Random Matrices. III. Analogs of Girko's circular and Wigner's semicircle laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25785)
*B. Shapiro*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了随机矩阵束（random matrix pencils）A_n+λB_n中水平穿越（level crossings）的渐近分布，推导了归一化对数判别式（normalized log-discriminant）的表示，并在多种系综（包括复/实i.i.d.和Gauss/Hermitian设定）中证明了经验测度收敛到显式确定性极限。在复Gauss情形下验证了相关假设，在一般i.i.d.设定中结果依赖于普适性理论（universality theory）的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解随机矩阵束中水平穿越的渐近行为，并将其与对数能量（logarithmic energy）和普适性理论建立联系，以刻画谱退化（spectral degeneracies）的统计规律。

Method: 将归一化对数判别式表示为成对特征值相互作用（pairwise eigenvalue interactions）的形式，并建立其极限由确定性势（deterministic potential）控制的条件。利用均匀圆律（uniform circular law）、对数尾部控制（logarithmic tail control）和小间距排斥估计（small-spacing repulsion estimates）证明经验测度的收敛性。

Result: 在复Gauss系综中，上述假设（除均匀性步骤外）得到验证，证明了水平穿越经验测度收敛到显式确定性极限；在实i.i.d.系综中，证明了在适当假设下任何极限测度不会集中（concentrate）于实射影直线（real projective line）；讨论了椭圆/Hermitian系综中的类似现象。

Conclusion: 对数能量和普适性理论在调控随机矩阵束的谱退化中起关键作用；结果揭示了水平穿越渐近分布的结构，并指出了普适性假设在一般i.i.d.设定中的必要性。

Abstract: We study the asymptotic distribution of level crossings for random matrix pencils A_n+λB_n in several ensembles, including complex and real i.i.d. matrices and Gaussian/Hermitian settings. We derive a representation of the normalized log-discriminant in terms of pairwise eigenvalue interactions and formulate conditions under which its limit is governed by a deterministic potential.
  Under assumptions combining a uniform circular law, logarithmic tail control, and small-spacing (repulsion) estimates, we prove convergence of the empirical measure of level crossings to an explicit deterministic limit. In the complex Gaussian case these assumptions are verified (modulo a uniformity step), while in the general i.i.d. setting the results are conditional and motivated by universality theory.
  We further analyze the real case, showing that any limiting measure does not concentrate on the real projective line under suitable hypotheses, and discuss analogous phenomena for elliptic/Hermitian ensembles. Our results highlight the role of logarithmic energy and universality in governing spectral degeneracies of random matrix pencils.

### [138] [Entropic Trapping of Hard Spheres in Spherical Confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24967)
*Praveen K. Bommineni,Junwei Wang,Nicolas Vogel,Michael Engel*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过硬球模拟，发现添加少量大颗粒作为缺陷时，会被熵力驱动至二十面体团簇的顶点，形成完美二十面体框架；伞形采样自由能计算表明，迁移和顶点俘获均由自由能最小化驱动，且该过程具有系统鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验观察到单分散球形胶体颗粒在乳液液滴中可结晶形成二十面体团簇（icosahedral clusters），且少量大颗粒会优先迁移至团簇顶点。为理解这一结构形成现象背后的物理机制，作者进行了模拟研究。

Method: 采用硬球受限自组装（confined self-assembly）模拟，在存在少量大颗粒的条件下研究体系行为；通过伞形采样（umbrella sampling）进行自由能计算，定量分析大颗粒的迁移与俘获过程。

Result: 大球受到结晶转变附近小球同心壳层的显著影响；熵力（entropic forces）驱动大球迁移至团簇表面，并稳定在二十面体顶点的自由能极小值处；添加十二个大球可形成完美二十面体框架；顶点俘获强度达多个$k_\text{B}T$；结晶路径和动力学在不同系统中表现一致。

Conclusion: 大球迁移至表面并俘获于顶点的过程源于自由能最小化（free energy minimization），且该熵俘获（entropic trapping）机制在多种系统中具有鲁棒性（robustness）。

Abstract: Monodisperse spherical colloidal particles confined within emulsion droplets can crystallize into icosahedral clusters. Experimentally it was observed that a few large colloidal particles added as defects preferentially migrate to the vertices of the icoshedral clusters. To understand this structure formation phenomenon, we simulate the confined self-assembly of hard spheres in the presence of a small number of larger particles. The results demonstrate that large spheres are significantly influenced by concentric shells of small spheres near the crystallization transition. Entropic forces drive the large spheres to the cluster surface, where they settle into free energy minima at the icosahedron vertices. Notably, the addition of twelve large spheres results in the formation of a perfect icosahedral frame. Free energy calculations via umbrella sampling are used to quantify this process and show that both the migration to the cluster surface and the trapping at the vertices with trapping strength of multiple $k_\text{B}T$ results from free energy minimization. Moreover, our study reveals that the crystallization pathway and dynamics of large spheres are consistent across different systems, suggesting robustness of entropic trapping.

</details>


### [139] [Electrohydrodynamic lubrication theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25350)
*Anirban Chatterjee,Yacine Amarouchene,Thomas Salez*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文针对带电胶体在离子溶液中靠近带电边界壁面运动的现象，构建了一个电水动力学润滑理论框架，推导并数值与渐近分析了圆柱体的法向、纵向和旋转运动耦合方程，揭示了超越现有渐近电粘升力表达式的复杂行为，并扩展了经典的Faxen-Brenner迁移率矩阵以包含表面电荷与溶解离子的效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 带电胶体在离子溶液中靠近带电边界壁面的自由运动广泛存在于自然、生物和工业场景中，但现有理论对其描述尚不完善，特别是缺乏耦合电水动力学效应的系统框架。

Method: 结合流体动力学润滑理论（hydrodynamic lubrication theory）、Debye–Hückel静电学（Debye–Hückel electrostatics）和Nernst–Planck电动力学（Nernst–Planck electrokinetics），推导了无限长刚性圆柱体在刚性壁面附近法向、纵向和旋转三个自由度的耦合运动方程，并采用数值方法和渐近分析（asymptotic analysis）进行求解。

Result: 数值与渐近分析结果揭示了超越现有渐近电粘升力（electroviscous-lift）表达式的复杂行为；在引入表面电荷和溶解离子时，扩展了经典的Faxen–Brenner类迁移率矩阵（Faxen–Brenner-like mobility matrix）。

Conclusion: 构建的电水动力学润滑理论框架能够有效描述带电胶体在带电壁面附近的耦合运动行为，为后续研究和应用提供了更全面的理论工具。

Abstract: The free motion of charged colloids within ionic solutions and in the vicinity of charged boundaries, is a phenomenon that occurs in various natural, biological and industrial settings. Here, we develop an electrohydrodynamic lubrication theoretical framework, in order to characterize such a motion in the case of an infinite rigid cylinder near a rigid wall. Combining hydrodynamic lubrication theory, Debye-H\''uckel electrostatics, and Nernst-Planck electrokinetics, we derive the three coupled equations of motion for the normal, longitudinal and rotational degrees of freedom of the cylinder, which are then investigated numerically and through asymptotic analysis. Our results reveal complex behaviours, beyond existing asymptotic electroviscous-lift expressions, and extend the classical Faxen-Brenner-like mobility matrix when surface charges and dissolved ions are incorporated.

</details>


### [140] [Fundamental picture of the conduction mechanism in solid-state polymer electrolytes revealed by terahertz spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25497)
*Johanna Weidelt,Jijeesh Ravi Nair,Diddo Diddens,Wentao Zhang,Felix Pfeiffer,Tiago de Oliveira Schneider,Markus Meinert,Tomoki Hiraoka,Linda Nesterov,Masoud Baghernejad,Dmitry Turchinovich,Hassan A. Hafez*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究利用太赫兹时域光谱（THz-TDS）作为非接触式无损技术，探测交联聚环氧乙烷（PEO）基固态聚合物电解质（SPEs）的导电特性，通过洛伦兹模型和密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，揭示了聚合物基体共振振动对锂离子跳跃传输的促进作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交联聚环氧乙烷（PEO）基固态聚合物电解质（SPEs）在固态锂金属电池中具有重要应用前景，但其导电机制尚不清晰，亟需一种非侵入式手段来探测其离子传导特性及其对锂盐和温度的依赖性。

Method: 采用太赫兹时域光谱（THz-TDS）获取交联SPEs的导电谱；利用洛伦兹模型（Lorentz model）对导电谱进行拟合分析，定量评估聚合物振动模式；结合密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，探究共振振动的微观机理。

Result: THz导电谱主要由太赫兹吸收带主导，归因于聚合物基体中的共振振动；通过洛伦兹模型成功解析了相关振动模式；DFT计算为这些共振振动的微观机制提供了理论支持。

Conclusion: 该研究阐明了聚合物基体振动对锂离子跳跃传输（hopping transport）的重要性，进而揭示了固态聚合物基电解质中技术相关的离子传导机制。

Abstract: Solid polymer electrolytes (SPEs) based on cross-linked poly(ethylene oxide) (PEO) encompassing lithium salts have gained significant attention as separators in solid-state lithium metal batteries. Here, we employ terahertz time-domain spectroscopy (THz-TDS), as a noninvasive contact-free technique, to investigate the conduction properties of these cross-linked SPEs and unravel their dependencies on the added lithium salt and the sample temperature. The obtained THz conductivity spectra are dominated by THz absorption bands, which we attribute to resonant vibrations within the polymer matrix of the electrolyte. By careful application of Lorentz model, the conductivity spectra have been analyzed, and the relevant polymer vibration modes have been quantitatively assessed. Calculations based on the density functional theory (DFT) were performed to elucidate the possible microscopic mechanisms of these resonant vibrations. This study sheds light on the relevance of polymer matrix vibrations validating the hopping transport of lithium ions in SPEs which ultimately leads to the technologically relevant ionic conduction in the solid-state polymer-based electrolytes.

</details>


### [141] [Universal material basis for biocompatible printed electrolytes in Organic Electrochemical Transistors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25830)
*Moritz Flemming,Paul Zechel,Rakesh R. Nair,Emil Mahnke,Markus Löffler,Alyna Ong,Bernd Rellinghaus,Lukas M. Eng,Karl Leo,Hans Kleemann*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于有机电化学晶体管（OECT）的新型生物相容性电解质材料基础，该材料可与离子液体结合，兼具流变可调性（适用于喷墨和丝网印刷）和UV固化特性，使全印刷晶体管能在环境空气中稳定工作超过30天，并最终在叶片基底上实现了完全由生物相容材料组成的全丝网印刷晶体管。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有OECT集成电路中的多数电解质缺乏生物相容性（biocompatibility），并且存在与流变性（rheology）相关的印刷工艺难题，限制了其在实际生物应用中的推广。

Method: 提出一种新型材料基础，与离子液体（ionic liquid）结合制备电解质；通过流变调整使其同时适用于喷墨印刷（inkjet printing）和丝网印刷（screen printing）；采用UV固化（UV-curable）技术使电解质在印刷后转变为固态结构。

Result: 延长了丝网印刷结构的墨水与器件寿命，制备的先进OECT可在环境空气中稳定运行超过30天；最终在叶片基底上展示了完全由生物相容材料制成的全丝网印刷晶体管。

Conclusion: 该生物相容性电解质方案解决了OECT集成工艺中的生物安全性与可印刷性两大关键挑战，为低成本、高通量制备柔性生物电子系统提供了可行的材料路径。

Abstract: Organic Electrochemical Transistors (OECTs) stand out for their interplay between ionic and electronic conduction, making them ideal analogues to biological synapses for neuromorphic computing and biosensing applications. Furthermore, they can be printed into integrated circuits on flexible substrates, enabling low-cost and high-throughput fabrication of complete electronic systems. However, most OECT electrolytes for integrated circuits still lack biocompatibility and suffer from rheology-related printing challenges. This paper presents a novel material basis that can be combined with an ionic liquid to fabricate an electrolyte for OECTs that only contains biocompatible materials. It allows rheological adjustments to enable the use of electrolyte in both inkjet and screen printing. Furthermore, the electrolyte is UV-curable, enabling it to transition into solid-state structures after printing. Extended ink and device lifetimes for screen-printed structures enable the fabrication of advanced OECTs that can operate in ambient air for over 30 days after fabrication. Ultimately, a fully screen-printed transistor using only biocompatible materials on a leaf substrate is shown

</details>

### [142] [Measurement of muon (anti-)neutrino charged-current quasielastic-like cross section using off-axis NuMI beam at ICARUS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24925)

Pietropaolo,F. Poppi,M. Pozzato,M. L. Pumo,G. Putnam,X. Qian,A. Rappoldi,G. L. Raselli,S. Repetto,F. Resnati,A. M. Ricci,M. Rosenberg,M. Rossella,N. Rowe,P. Roy,C. Rubbia,A. Ruggeri,S. Saha,G. Salmoria,S. Samanta,A. Scaramelli,D. Schmitz,A. Schukraft,D. Senadheera,S-H. Seo,F. Sergiampietri,G. Sirri,J. S. Smedley,J. Smith,M. Sotgia,L. Stanco,J. Stewart,H. A. Tanaka,M. Tenti,K. Terao,F. Terranova,V. Togo,D. Torretta,M. Torti,R. Triozzi,Y. -T. Tsai,K. V. Tsang,T. Usher,F. Varanini,N. Vardy,S. Ventura,M. Vicenzi,C. Vignoli,F. A. Wieler,Z. Williams,R. J. Wilson,P. Wilson,J. Wolfs,T. Wongjirad,A. Wood,E. Worcester,M. Worcester,S. Yadav,H. Yu,J. Yu,A. Zani,J. Zennamo,J. Zettlemoyer,S. Zucchelli*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于ICARUS探测器在费米实验室NuMI束流中收集的数据，首次测量了不含π末态（即类准弹性散射主导）的中微子通量平均微分截面，并比较了多种事件生成器的预测结果。整体上预测与数据一致，但当前不确定度尚不足以区分各模型优劣。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核效应（nuclear effects）是中微子振荡测量系统不确定度的主要来源，而ICARUS探测器尚未进行过中微子截面测量。本文旨在利用NuMI束流数据提供首个截面测量，以促进对核效应的理解并检验事件生成器的预测能力。

Method: 利用ICARUS探测器在两次束流运行期间（对应2.5×10^20质子打靶，中微子束流模式）采集的NuMI数据。信号定义为末态无π介子产生的事件（即类准弹性散射（CCQE-like）主导拓扑），测量通量平均微分截面（flux-averaged differential cross sections），涉及四个运动学变量：出射轻子角、轻子与领头质子之间的张角、以及垂直于入射中微子平面内μ子与质子之间的运动学不平衡量。将结果与多种中微子事件生成器预测进行比较，并计算p值。

Result: 报告了四个运动学变量上的通量平均微分截面。多种事件生成器的预测与实验数据整体一致；但当前不确定度预算（uncertainty budget）尚不足以提供足够的区分能力以偏向某一特定模型。

Conclusion: ICARUS探测器成功实现了首批中微子截面测量，为理解核效应提供了新数据。然而，现有不确定度水平限制了模型区分的统计能力，未来需要更高统计量或降低系统误差以甄别不同生成器的预测差异。

Abstract: This paper presents the first neutrino cross-section measurement from the ICARUS detector at Fermilab, using NuMI (Neutrinos at the Main Injector) beam data collected from two beam operation periods corresponding to $2.5\times10^{20}$ protons-on-target in neutrino beam mode. The signal is defined by events with no pions produced in the final state, a topology dominated by charged-current quasi-elastic-like (CCQE-like) signatures. The measurement is reported as flux-averaged differential cross sections as functions of kinematic variables that provide sensitivity to the complex nuclear effects which often dominate the systematic uncertainty budgets of neutrino oscillation measurements. Specifically, this work reports cross sections in two angular variables -- the angle of the outgoing lepton and the opening angle between the lepton and leading proton -- and two variables characterizing the kinematic imbalance between the muon and proton in the plane transverse to the incoming neutrino. These results are compared against predictions from a variety of neutrino event generators, with $p$-values calculated between the extracted cross sections and each prediction. Overall, the predictions agree with the data; however, the current budget of uncertainties does not yet provide sufficient discriminating power to favor a specific model.

### [143] [Simultaneous measurements of $N$-subjettiness observables in jets from gluons and light-flavour quarks, and in decays of boosted W bosons and top quarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25538)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于CMS实验138 fb^{-1}的质子-质子对撞数据，对具有高横向动量的大半径喷注中的25个亚结构观测量（substructure observables）进行了同时测量，覆盖双喷注事件和富含洛伦兹增强W玻色子与顶夸克的t\bar{t}事件。测量结果解卷绕至稳定粒子层级，并提供了观测量之间的粒子级相关性估计，可用于系统性检验和改进喷注中辐射的模型描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 喷注亚结构（jet substructure）是检验量子色动力学（QCD）辐射模型和提升新物理搜索灵敏度的关键工具，但此前缺乏对多个亚结构观测量之间关联的系统性实验约束。本文旨在通过同时测量大量亚结构观测量并揭示其相关性，为理论模型的精细化提供全面的实验基准。

Method: 利用CMS探测器在质心能量13 TeV的质子-质子对撞中收集的138 fb^{-1}数据，选取大半径喷注样本（包含双喷注事件以及洛伦兹增强的W玻色子和顶夸克强子衰变事件）。采用基于N-subjettiness观测量的6体基（6-body basis）对喷注中已分辨辐射的相空间进行过完备约束，同时测量25个亚结构观测量，并将结果通过解卷绕（unfolding）处理至稳定粒子层级。

Result: 首次实现了25个喷注亚结构观测量的同时测量，覆盖了对应胶子或轻味夸克（单叉）、两个夸克（双叉）和三个夸克（三叉）的三种数据样本。提供了粒子层级上观测量之间相关性的估计，给出了过完备约束下对喷注内部已分辨辐射相空间的详细刻画。

Conclusion: 该测量结果为喷注中辐射过程的建模提供了系统性的实验约束和相关性信息，可用于系统评估和精细化改进QCD辐射模型，有助于提升未来对撞机分析中对喷注亚结构的理论描述精度。

Abstract: A simultaneous measurement of 25 substructure observables is presented using large-radius jets with high transverse momentum from proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV. The measurement is carried out on dijet events and $\mathrm{t\bar{t}}$ events enriched in Lorentz-boosted W bosons and top quarks decaying hadronically. The three data samples consist of jets with one, two, or three prongs from the showering and hadronization of a gluon or light-flavour quark, two quarks, or three quarks, respectively. The data correspond to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$, recorded by the CMS experiment in 2016$-$2018. A detailed characterization of the jet substructure is provided using a 6-body basis of $N$-subjettiness observables that overconstrains the phase space of the resolved emissions in the jet. The measurements are unfolded to the level of stable particles, and an estimate of the particle-level correlations between observables is provided, ensuring that the results can be used to systematically assess and refine the modelling of radiation in jets.

</details>


### [144] [Search for electroweakinos in compressed-spectrum scenarios with low-momentum isolated tracks in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25604)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 使用低动量孤立径迹和大横动量缺失事件，针对质量近简并的higgsino型chargino和neutralino搜索超对称电弱微子。基于138 fb⁻¹的13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据，采用参数化神经网络区分信号与背景，未观察到超出标准模型预期的显著信号，在95%置信水平下排除了一定质量区间的higgsino模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验自然超对称（natural supersymmetry）理论场景中的电弱微子（electroweakino），尤其是质量近简并的higgsino型带电微子（chargino）和最轻中性微子（lightest neutralino）信号，填补低质量分裂区间的探测空白。

Method: 选取低动量（soft）孤立径迹与大横动量缺失（missing transverse momentum）事件；针对质量分裂0.3–1 GeV下chargino衰变为最轻neutralino和低动量π介子的过程，利用参数化神经网络（parameterized neural network）结合运动学（kinematic）与撞击参数（impact parameter）信息区分信号与背景。

Result: 未观察到超出标准模型（Standard Model）预期的显著信号；在95%置信水平下，higgsino模型在质量分裂0.28–1.15 GeV区间、chargino质量最高至185 GeV范围内被排除。

Conclusion: 该结果对自然超对称场景施加了严格约束，表明在上述质量区间内higgsino型电弱微子存在的可能性受到显著限制。

Abstract: A search for supersymmetric electroweakinos is performed using events with a low-momentum (soft) isolated track and large missing transverse momentum, targeting nearly mass-degenerate higgsino-like charginos and neutralinos. For mass splittings of 0.3$-$1 GeV, the chargino decays to the lightest neutralino and a low-momentum pion, which can produce a soft, potentially displaced track. A parameterized neural network separates signal from background using kinematic and impact parameter information. The analysis uses 138 fb$^{-1}$ of proton$-$proton collision data at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV recorded with the CMS detector. No significant excess above the standard model expectation is observed. At 95% confidence level, the considered higgsino model is excluded for mass splittings in the range 0.28$-$1.15 GeV and for chargino masses up to 185 GeV, setting stringent constraints on natural supersymmetry scenarios.

</details>


### [145] [Measurement of the Z $\to$ $μ^+μ^-$ angular coefficients in pp collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV as functions of transverse momentum and rapidity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25678)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于LHC上CMS探测器采集的质子-质子（proton-proton, pp）对撞数据（质心系能量$\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV，积分亮度140 fb$^{-1}$），在双缪子Drell–Yan产生过程中测量了八个角极化系数$A_0$至$A_7$，并在双微分运动学区间（横向动量和快度）内呈现结果，与微扰量子色动力学（perturbative quantum chromodynamics）的次次领头阶（next-to-next-to-leading order, NNLO）理论预言进行了比较，为理解部分子动力学和Z玻色子产生机制提供了关键信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 角极化系数反映了Drell–Yan过程中轻子对的角分布，是检验微扰量子色动力学（perturbative QCD）预言和探究部分子（parton）级动力学机制的重要观测量。在$\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV的高能量下对这些系数进行精确测量，有助于深入理解Z玻色子的产生机制和相关的非微扰效应。

Method: 基于CMS探测器在LHC上收集的质子-质子（proton-proton）对撞数据，质心系能量$\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV，积分亮度140 fb$^{-1}$。将八个角极化系数$A_0$至$A_7$按缪子对（$\mu^+\mu^-$）的横向动量（transverse momentum）和快度（rapidity）划分为八个横向动量区间和两个快度区间进行双微分（double differential）测定，缪子对不变质量限定在81–101 GeV范围内。

Result: 获得了八个角极化系数$A_0$至$A_7$在双微分运动学区间上的测量结果，并与次次领头阶（NNLO）微扰量子色动力学（perturbative QCD）的理论预言进行了比较。

Conclusion: 该测量为理解Drell–Yan过程中的部分子动力学（partonic dynamics）和Z玻色子产生机制提供了重要信息，实验数据与NNLO理论预言的比较可用于检验和进一步约束标准模型量子色动力学部分的理论计算。

Abstract: A measurement of the eight angular polarization coefficients, $A_0$ to $A_7$, in the cross section for the Drell$-$Yan production of two muons is presented. The analysis is based on proton-proton (pp) collision data recorded with the CMS detector at the LHC at a center-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 140 fb$^{-1}$. The coefficients are determined double differentially in eight intervals of transverse momentum and two intervals of rapidity of the muon pair $μ^+μ^-$. The results are presented for the $μ^+μ^-$ invariant mass range 81$-$101 GeV and are compared with theoretical predictions calculated at next-to-next-to-leading order in perturbative quantum chromodynamics. The measurement provides relevant information about the underlying partonic dynamics and the Z boson production mechanisms.

*E. Sánchez García,Y. Shi,N. Ackermann,H. Bonet,C. Buck,J. Hakenmüller,G. Heusser,M. Lindner,W. Maneschg,M. Meier,S. Mertens,D. Piani,T. Rink,H. Strecker*

Abstract: The CONUS+ experiment has recently reported the first detection of coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering (CEvNS) of reactor antineutrinos on germanium nuclei and is now entering a precision phase. The dominant uncertainty in the first measurement was the energy scale, which contributed 14% to the uncertainty of the prediction of the combined signal. We present a dedicated neutron activation campaign in which one of the new 2.4 kg CONUS+ germanium detectors was irradiated with a strong 241AmBe source, demonstrating that a contribution below 4% to the uncertainty of signal prediction is achievable. For the first time, the 71Ge M-shell X-ray line was clearly resolved at (158.7+-1.4) eVee, validating the CONUS+ energy reconstruction down to the detection threshold. This validation includes the understanding of the energy scale, the energy resolution, the trigger efficiency, and the correct separation of physical from noise events. These results establish the foundation for a future activation campaign at the Kernkraftwerk Leibstadt reactor site, strengthening the CONUS+ energy calibration and extending its sensitivity to precision CEvNS and beyond Standard Model physics measurements.

### [147] [Seismic background mitigation with the Lunar Gravitational-wave Antenna](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24866)
*Han Yan,Jan Harms*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文针对月球引力波探测器（Lunar Gravitational-wave Antenna, LGWA）面临的地震背景噪声问题，首次定量评估了双台站配置对地震噪声的抑制能力。研究表明，台站间距相对于地震相关长度（seismic-correlation length）是决定降噪效果的关键因素；在最优布设下，0.3 Hz处的等效地震噪声幅度谱密度（ASD）可比单台站降低约2.3倍，且噪声谱呈现由贝塞尔函数（Bessel function）结构导致的振荡与抑制特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 月球引力波探测器（LGWA）易受地震背景噪声干扰，该噪声可能构成基本灵敏度极限。虽然LGWA最初设想通过加速度计阵列处理数据来区分引力波信号与地震背景，但此前缺乏对地震背景抑制效果的定量评估。

Method: 在各向同性、随机、高斯地震场（isotropic, random, Gaussian seismic field）假设下，推导了双台站配置下最优平方信噪比（optimal squared signal-to-noise ratio）的解析表达式，并进行了数值分析。

Result: 双台站间距相对于地震相关长度是抑制能力的关键参数。最优布设下，0.3 Hz处等效地震噪声幅度谱密度（ASD）相比单台站可降低约2.3倍；噪声等效ASD呈现由噪声相关性的贝塞尔函数结构导致的独特振荡与抑制特征。

Conclusion: 双台站最优布设能显著降低地震噪声对月球引力波探测器的影响，为LGWA的台阵设计提供了定量依据。

Abstract: Lunar gravitational-wave (GW) detectors relying on the measurement of the response of the Moon to GWs are susceptible to a seismic background, which might pose a fundamental sensitivity limitation. The Lunar Gravitational-wave Antenna (LGWA) was conceived as an array of accelerometers with the idea that data can be processed to distinguish between a GW signal and the seismic background. As a result, the seismic noise of the GW measurement would be mitigated. However, so far, no quantitative assessment of the mitigation of the seismic background has been provided. In this article, we derive the analytical expressions for the optimal squared signal-to-noise ratio considering two seismic stations in an isotropic, random, Gaussian seismic field. Our numerical analysis reveals that the capacity to mitigate the seismic noise critically depends on the distance between the two stations relative to the seismic-correlation length. We demonstrate that optimal placement of the two stations can yield significant improvements in the equivalent seismic noise amplitude spectrum density (ASD), approximately a factor of 2.3 at 0.3 Hz, compared to the measurement with a single station. The equivalent ASD of the seismic noise also exhibits distinct oscillatory and mitigation features arising from the Bessel-function structure of the noise correlation.

Furthermore, to suppress spurious numerical artifacts that originate from large Lorentz boosts due to the Lorentz symmetry of the model, we nonperturbatively fix the Lorentz symmetry using the Faddeev--Popov procedure. Conclusion: M<0的Szekeres度规因ρ始终为负，不具备作为宇宙学模型的资格；从M<0推导出ρ<0在Friedmann极限中直接成立，在一般Szekeres度规中需要更复杂的推理。

Abstract: The evolution equation of the Szekeres metrics allows solutions with the mass function $M < 0$. They exist in both classes of the Szekeres metrics, have no Big Bang singularity and no origin. In both classes, the conditions for no shell crossings ensure that the mass density $ρ$ of the dust source in the Einstein equations is negative at all times. Thus, these metrics do not qualify as cosmological models. In the Friedmann limit, the implication $M < 0 \Longrightarrow ρ< 0$ is immediate. In the general Szekeres metrics it follows through a rather intricate reasoning.

### [151] [Renormalization-group improved Schwarzschild black hole: shadow, ringdown, and strong cosmic censorship](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24798)
*Ahmad Al-Badawi,Faizuddin Ahmed,İzzet Sakallı*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于重整化群改进的类史瓦西黑洞模型，系统研究了其视界结构、光子球与阴影半径、标量场/电磁场/狄拉克场的拟正则模、强宇宙监督审查（SCC）的满足情况、热力学相变与几何、霍金辐射稀疏性，并与多个正则黑洞模型进行了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索重整化群（renormalization group, RG）改进的史瓦西黑洞在无电荷和无旋转条件下能否生成内视界（inner Cauchy horizon），以及该视界能否通过强宇宙监督审查（Strong Cosmic Censorship, SCC）的检验，同时刻画这一改进模型的全部观测与热力学特征。

Method: 采用含截断尺度ξ和插值参数γ的重整化群修正度规，统一处理标量、电磁和狄拉克场的Regge-Wheeler-Zerilli问题；通过六阶WKB方法计算基频和泛音拟正则模（quasinormal modes），并与时域ringdown结果交叉验证；在热力学部分使用Davies相变分析和Weinhold-Ruppeiner几何方法。

Conclusion: 重整化群改进的史瓦西黑洞在无电荷条件下生成了内柯西视界，该视界对强宇宙监督审查的满足情况与多极矩弱相关；其热力学行为由参数(ξ,γ)通过一个与外表面积引力相关的辅助函数干净地调控；在阴影成像层面与Hayward和Bonanno-Reuter模型以1%水平简并。

Abstract: We study a renormalization-group (RG) improved Schwarzschild-like black hole (BH) whose lapse interpolates between a classical Schwarzschild exterior and a quantum-smoothed interior governed by a cutoff scale $ξ$ and an interpolation parameter $γ$. We work out the horizon structure together with the photon sphere and shadow radius $R_{\mathrm{sh}}$, set up the scalar, electromagnetic, and Dirac Regge-Wheeler-Zerilli problems in a unified treatment, and compute fundamental and overtone quasinormal modes via sixth-order WKB cross-checked against time-domain ringdown. We examine Strong Cosmic Censorship (SCC) at the inner Cauchy horizon -- a horizon the improved geometry generates without charge or rotation -- and find the ratio $β=|\mathrm{Im}\,ω|/κ_-$ to be multipole-independent at the $6\%$ level, following $β\simeqλ_{L}/κ_{-}$. A thermodynamic analysis uncovers a Davies-type phase transition of the outer horizon and a nontrivial Weinhold-Ruppeiner geometry on the $(S,γ)$ slice; the Schwarzschild $T_{H}\propto 1/r_{+}$ decay is replaced by a bell-curve profile peaking at $T_{H}^{\max}\simeq 0.062$. A scan of the $(ξ,γ)$ plane summarizes the joint behavior of the shadow, the scalar barrier, the SCC ratio, and $T_H$, and exhibits a thin crescent adjacent to the extremal boundary where Christodoulou-SCC marginally fails. A comparison against Bardeen, Hayward, and Bonanno-Reuter BHs places the improved Schwarzschild BH as the most Schwarzschild-like of the regular-BH family at matched perturbation scale, with shadow-degenerate imaging against Hayward and Bonanno-Reuter at the $1\%$ level. We close with the sparsity of the Hawking flux and the energy-emission rate, both depending cleanly on $(ξ,γ)$ through a single auxiliary function tied to the outer-horizon surface gravity.

### [152] [Link-based causal set propagators in $1+1$ dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24812)
*Haye Hinrichsen,Arsim Kastrati*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了因果集（causal sets）上的延迟标量传播子（retarded scalar propagator）是否可以用链接矩阵（link matrix）$\mathbf{L}$ 表示。通过在$1+1$维闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）中的泊松撒点（Poisson sprinklings），作者利用渐近分析和数值模拟证明，平均后的无质量延迟传播子自然地与归一化指数函数$\exp(\mathbf{L})$相关联。随后通过质量散射级数（mass-scattering series）将构造推广至有质量情形，平均后与连续传播子吻合良好。最后讨论了逆核$\exp(-\mathbf{L})$作为离散达朗贝尔算子（discrete d'Alembertian）的候选可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索因果集（causal set）这一离散时空背景下的量子场论（quantum field theory）构造，具体尝试将延迟标量传播子（retarded scalar propagator）用基础的链接矩阵（link matrix）$\mathbf{L}$表达，以建立离散与连续理论之间的联系。

Method: 采用渐近分析（asymptotic analysis）和数值模拟（numerical simulations）方法，针对$1+1$维闵可夫斯基时空中的泊松撒点（Poisson sprinklings），研究平均后的因果集传播子与链接矩阵指数函数$\exp(\mathbf{L})$的关系，并通过质量散射级数（mass-scattering series）推广至有质量情形。

Result: 平均后的无质量延迟传播子（massless retarded propagator）自然地与归一化的$\exp(\mathbf{L})$相关联；有质量情形下，基于质量散射级数的构造在平均后与连续传播子达到良好一致。

Conclusion: 链接矩阵的指数函数$\exp(\mathbf{L})$可有效构造因果集上的传播子，其逆核$\exp(-\mathbf{L})$则可能是离散达朗贝尔算子（discrete d'Alembertian）的一个候选方案。

Abstract: We investigate whether retarded scalar propagators on causal sets can be expressed in terms of the link matrix $\mathbf{L}$. For Poisson sprinklings into $1+1$ dimensional Minkowski spacetime, we show by asymptotic analysis and supporting numerical simulations that the averaged massless retarded propagator is naturally associated with a normalized exponential exp$(\mathbf{L})$. We then extend the construction to the massive case via the usual mass-scattering series and obtain good agreement with the continuum propagator after averaging. Finally, we discuss the inverse kernel exp$(-\mathbf{L})$ as a possible candidate for a discrete d'Alembertian.

### [153] [Quasinormal Modes, Greybody Factors and Rigorous Bounds for Quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder Black Hole with Quintessential Dark Energy and a String Clouds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24813)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子修正背景下，研究黑洞的似正规模和灰体因子有助于理解黑洞的稳定性及量子引力效应；引入精质暗能量和弦云等外部场，可更真实地描述黑洞所处的宇宙学环境。

Method: 采用六阶Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin（WKB）近似方法，分别计算标量场（scalar field）和矢量场（vector field）扰动下的有效势（effective potentials）及似正规模频率（quasinormal mode frequencies），并考察精质参数（quintessence parameters）和弦云参数（string cloud parameters）的影响。

Abstract: We obtained quasinormal modes and greybody factors of the quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder (QOS) black hole with quintessential dark energy and string clouds. We observe the quasinormal frequencies by analyzing both the quintessence parameters and the string cloud parameters. It is found that GFs are significantly influenced by the parameters of $\tilde{a}_{e}$, $\tildeσ_{e}$, and $\tilde{h}_{e}$. The resulting Born-Infeld-type gravity is a ghost-free $f(R,{\cal G})$ theory which reduces to Einstein gravity in the low energy limit. In this work we focus on bouncing cosmological solutions of such a theory, which require positive spatial curvature. Method: 将近视界 S 矩阵方法（near-horizon S-matrix method）从纯声学区域推广至超光速色散区域；针对一类偶、凸且多项式有界的色散关系，计算 Bogoliubov 系数（Bogoliubov coefficients）；并在低能及绝热极限下将其与近似射线隧穿结果进行对比。

Abstract: We investigate Hawking-like particle production in analogue gravity systems with superluminal modified dispersion relations. For a broad class of even, convex, and polynomially bounded dispersion relations, we show that the relevant outgoing modes are governed by an effective horizon induced by dispersive propagation. Extending the near-horizon S-matrix method beyond the purely sonic regime, we compute the Bogoliubov coefficients and demonstrate that, in the low-energy and adiabatic limits, they agree with the tunneling result obtained from the approximant ray. In both cases, the emission spectrum is controlled by an effective surface gravity associated to the effective horizon, leading to controlled deviations from exact thermality. Our results establish an analytical connection between the Bogoliubov and tunneling descriptions in dispersive settings and clarify the conditions under which Hawking radiation remains robust against ultraviolet modifications, with implications extending beyond analogue gravity.

  <summary>Details</summary>

There exists a phenomenological description of this result based on Landau theory, but the underlying mechanisms which determine the coefficients of the Landau expansion were unknown. In this study we calculate these coefficients starting from first principles. To this end, we start with an energy functional that describes the nonlinear behavior of the theory, and reduce it to an energy function. This allows us to explain the previously observed, but not well-understood, features of the scalarization phase transition, and enables us to predict which phase transition order will be present for which coupling function or in which regime of the parameter space. The details of the phase transition determine certain astrophysical observables such as signals sourced by transitions from metastable states in first-order scalarization. Thus, predicting these details is an important part of understanding scalarization itself.

Abstract: We study the analytic properties and three equivalent representations of the Toller matrices $T^{(\pm)}$ which appear in the causal formulation of spinfoam transition amplitudes for 4d Lorentzian quantum gravity. We show that, equivalently, they can be represented as an integral over eigenvalues of the boost operator, which results in a sum over residues. ### [161] [Peculiar velocities in the $Λ$CDM universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24974)

TL;DR: 本文在广义相对论（general relativity）框架内，统一分析了复合（recombination）后无压物质分布中本动速度扰动（peculiar-velocity perturbations）的线性演化，涵盖了早期爱因斯坦-德西特（Einstein-de Sitter）时期与随后的宇宙学常数主导（Λ-dominated）时期。研究发现，线性本动速度在爱因斯坦-德西特时期正比于时间增长，而在宇宙学常数贡献增大的阶段，其增长先被抑制后转为衰减，但早期增长的部分延续至今，导致中等红移处的整体流速度（bulk-flow velocities）高于 ΛCDM 模型预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从非相互作用、非共动（non-comoving）的辐射与尘埃混合物出发，推导出控制速度扰动演化的广义微分方程组，并在完整广义相对论框架下进行分析。

Result: 线性本动速度在爱因斯坦-德西特时期以 v∝t 形式增长；在 Ω_Λ 贡献增大的后期，增长先被抑制后转为衰减；但早期增长的部分保留至今。因此，中等红移处的整体流速度高于 ΛCDM 模型的预测值，而在较低红移处则出现下降。

Conclusion: 此类本动速度剖面（peculiar-velocity profiles）已在文献中有所报道，暗示现有观测可能与本文的理论预测相符。

Abstract: We present a unified analysis of the linear evolution of peculiar-velocity perturbations in the distribution of pressureless matter after recombination. Our study is carried out within the framework of full general relativity and encompasses both the earlier Einstein-de Sitter epoch and the subsequent $Λ$-dominated phase. Starting from a non-interacting, non-comoving mixture of radiation and dust, we derive the generalized differential equations governing the evolution of these velocity perturbations. We confirm that linear peculiar velocities ($v$) grow as $v\propto t$ throughout the Einstein-de Sitter era. In contrast, during a later phase of increasing $Ω_Λ$-contribution, we find that the growth of the peculiar-velocity field is progressively suppressed, before reversing to decay. Nevertheless, part of the earlier velocity growth persists to the present. Hence, bulk-flow velocities at intermediate redshifts are expected to exceed those predicted by the $Λ$CDM model, followed by a decline in their value at lower redshifts. Interestingly, such peculiar-velocity profiles have already been reported in the literature.

*James Kennington,Joshua Black,Zach Yarbrough,Yun-Jing Huang,Chad Hanna,Leo Tsukada,Amanda Baylor,Olivia Godwin,Prathamesh Joshi,Cody Messick,Surabhi Sachdev,Ron Tapia*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在数值和操作层面验证了一种基于规范理论（gauge theory）的因果最小相位白化滤波框架，该框架通过功率谱流形上的平行移动（parallel transport）严格保持最小相位特性并精确守恒匹配滤波信噪比（matched-filter SNR）。在LIGO-Virgo O3数据上的注入实验及生产级sgnl管线中，该方法将白化延迟降低1.0秒（33%），且不损失探测灵敏度与定位精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有低延迟引力波搜索管线使用非因果线性相位（acausal linear-phase）滤波器，需要前瞻缓冲区（look-ahead buffer），引入数秒算法延迟。消除这一延迟需改用因果最小相位（causal minimum-phase）白化滤波器，但在非平稳噪声下维持其性能面临三大挑战：跟踪漂移的功率谱密度（power spectral density）、保持滤波器的最小相位条件、补偿相位响应变化以维持天区定位（sky-localization）精度。本文旨在数值与操作层面验证Paper I提出的规范理论框架的有效性。

Method: 采用规范理论信号处理框架，在功率谱流形上定义最小相位联络（minimum-phase connection），通过平行移动实现因果滤波器的几何精确更新规则。通过数值方法验证该联络的平坦性（flatness），证明最优滤波器是瞬时噪声的路径无关状态函数。在LIGO-Virgo O3数据上进行15,347个双黑洞（binary black hole）信号的注入实验，并在生产级sgnl管线中部署该框架，对比线性相位基线方法的探测灵敏度和时间相位精度。

Result: 数值验证确认该联络的平坦性，平行移动严格保持最小相位属性并精确守恒匹配滤波信噪比。注入实验表明，该架构在探测灵敏度、探测器间定时与相位精度方面与线性相位基线一致。在生产级sgnl管线中，以4秒噪声估计节律（cadence）实现白化延迟降低1.0秒（33%）。节律缩减实验表明，在亚秒级管线节律下最多可消除91%的基线触发延迟（trigger latency）。

Conclusion: 基于规范理论的因果最小相位白化滤波框架在数值和操作层面均得到验证，能够在非平稳噪声条件下精确保持最小相位特性和匹配滤波信噪比，同时显著降低引力波搜索管线的算法延迟。该方案为低延迟多信使（multimessenger）天文预警提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: Low-latency gravitational-wave search pipelines provide early-warning alerts for multimessenger astrophysical transients. Current pipelines whiten the data stream using acausal, linear-phase filters, which require a look-ahead buffer that introduces several seconds of algorithmic latency. Eliminating this latency requires causal, minimum-phase whitening filters using only past data. However, operating causal filters under non-stationary noise is non-trivial: the drifting power spectral density must be tracked without degrading the matched-filter signal-to-noise ratio (SNR), filter updates must preserve the minimum-phase condition, and the altered phase response must be compensated to maintain sky-localization accuracy. In Paper I we introduced a gauge theoretic signal processing framework and showed that the minimum-phase connection on the manifold of power spectra provides a geometrically exact update rule for causal filters. Here we validate that framework numerically and operationally, demonstrating that parallel transport along this connection strictly preserves the minimum-phase property while exactly conserving the matched-filter SNR. We numerically certify the flatness of this connection, showing that the optimal filter is a path-independent state function of the instantaneous noise. Through an injection campaign on O3 data with 15,347 binary black hole signals across the LIGO-Virgo network, we confirm that this architecture preserves the detection sensitivity and inter-detector timing and phase accuracy of the linear-phase baseline. Implementing the framework in the production sgnl pipeline reduces whitening latency by 1.0 s (33%) at a 4-second noise estimation cadence, confirmed in controlled tests and on live O3 replay data at production scale. Stride reduction experiments show that up to 91% of baseline trigger latency can be eliminated with sub-second pipeline cadence.

</details>


### [163] [Covariant quantization of the Einstein-Hilbert theory in first-order form](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25117)
*S. Martins-Filho*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文采用路径积分（path integral）和BV形式论（BV formalism）对爱因斯坦-希尔伯特理论的一阶形式进行了协变量子化，证明了其规范代数是闭合且不可约的，并揭示了辅助场（连接场）与经典值之间的结构恒等式。此外，通过一种技巧推导出森雅诺维奇测度（Senjanović measure）的显式协变形式，并证明当辅助场在壳（on-shell）时一阶与二阶形式在有效作用量层面等价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对爱因斯坦-希尔伯特理论的一阶形式进行协变量子化，并澄清一阶与二阶形式之间的量子等价关系。

Method: 采用路径积分（path integral）和BV形式论（BV formalism）作为量子化框架，将度规（metric）$g^{μν}$和联络（connection）$Γ^λ_{μν}$视为独立变量，后者作为辅助场（auxiliary field）。通过一种技巧推导出森雅诺维奇测度（Senjanović measure）的显式协变形式。

Result: 规范代数是闭合且不可约的；存在一种新的平凡局域对称性（trivial local symmetry），由此导出辅助场的格林函数（Green's function）与其经典值之间的结构恒等式；推导出了森雅诺维奇测度的显式协变形式。

Conclusion: 当辅助场在壳（on-shell）时，爱因斯坦-希尔伯特理论的一阶与二阶形式在有效作用量层面是等价的。

Abstract: We present a covariant quantization of the first-order formulation of the Einstein-Hilbert theory using the path integral and BV formalisms. In this approach, the metric $g^{μν}$ and the connection $Γ^λ_{μν}$ are treated as independent, with the connection playing the role of an auxiliary field. We show that the gauge algebra is closed and irreducible. A novel trivial local symmetry arises, leading to structural identities that relate the Green's functions of the auxiliary field to its classical value. We revisit the quantum equivalence between the first- and second-order formulations of the Einstein-Hilbert theory. By employing a suitable trick, a manifestly covariant form of the Senjanović measure is derived. We also show that the two formulations are equivalent at the level of the effective action when the auxiliary field is on-shell.

### [164] [Early-Time Nonlinear Growth in an Unstable Q-Ball Hairy Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25223)
*Lang Cheng,Guangzhou Guo,Peng Wang,Haitang Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 在Einstein-Maxwell理论中，非线性系统远离不稳定平衡的早期演化可能并非由线性不稳定性主导：对于Q-ball毛黑洞，标量场中响应较弱的组分在早期增长阶段由二阶准正则模（second-order QNM）主导，而非线性不稳定模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验非线性系统中远离不稳定平衡的早期演化是否始终由线性不稳定性（linear instability）主导这一常见预期。

Method: 将完全非线性演化（full nonlinear evolution）与一阶和二阶准正则模（quasinormal mode, QNM）计算相结合，分析Einstein-Maxwell理论中具有带电自相互作用标量场的Q-ball毛黑洞的不稳定增长阶段。

Result: 线性不稳定QNM在标量场的一个组分中振幅远大于另一组分；响应较强的组分遵循该线性模演化，而响应较弱的组分的早期增长由线性不稳定模源激发的二阶QNM主导。这一现象发生在演化仍处于微扰（perturbative）阶段时。

Conclusion: 非线性系统中单个组分的早期增长不一定由其线性响应（linear response）所支配，二阶QNM可能在早期阶段起主导作用。

Abstract: Early-time evolution away from an unstable equilibrium in a nonlinear system is often expected to be governed by the associated linear instability. Combining full nonlinear evolution with first- and second-order quasinormal mode (QNM) calculations, we show that this expectation can fail during the unstable growth stage of a Q-ball hairy black hole in Einstein-Maxwell theory with a charged self-interacting scalar field. The linear unstable QNM has a much larger amplitude in one component of the scalar field than in the other: the more strongly responding component follows that mode, whereas the early growth of the more weakly responding component is dominated by a second-order QNM sourced by the linear unstable mode. This occurs while the evolution remains perturbative. Our results thus show that the early growth of an individual component need not be governed by its linear response.

### [165] [The properties and predictions of quasi-periodic oscillations around a black hole in nonlocal gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25254)
*Tao-Tao Sui,Chen Long,Ye zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了非局域引力（nonlocal gravity）中静态黑洞周围有质量测试粒子的动力学，分析了非局域参数α对高频准周期振荡（HF QPOs）的影响，并将α限制为α/M ≤ 0.452。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非局域引力框架下探讨静态黑洞周围有质量测试粒子的动力学行为，并利用高频准周期振荡（HF QPOs）作为观测探针来约束非局域参数α。

Method: 通过分析非局域引力中的有效势（effective potential），求解圆形轨道的能量E和角动量L，进而推导内稳定圆形轨道（ISCO）半径、辐射效率、开普勒频率Ω_φ、垂直外旋频率Ω_θ以及径向外旋频率Ω_r等物理量；结合双峰HF QPO模型，施加2ν_U = 3ν_L共振条件分析共振半径、上QPO频率及黑洞质量限制。

Result: 非局域参数α增强有效势V_eff，系统性地降低圆形轨道的能量E和角动量L；ISCO半径及其对应的能量和角动量随α单调减小，辐射效率最高达约8.9%；开普勒频率与垂直外旋频率重合且受α抑制，而径向外旋频率被增强；上QPO频率范围ν_U ~ (673/M - 4360/M) Hz，在TOV极限下ν_U ≲ 1450 Hz；结合观测要求ν_U ≥ 100 Hz，黑洞质量M ≲ 43.6M_⊙；引力时间延迟小于约1.3 ms。

Conclusion: 非局域参数α显著影响黑洞周围粒子的轨道动力学和QPO频率特性，通过观测约束可将α限制在α/M ≤ 0.452，且引力时间延迟效应在当前观测能力下可忽略。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of massive test particles around a static black hole in nonlocal gravity and examine the corresponding properties of HF QPOs, constraining the nonlocal parameter to $α/M \leq 0.452$. The nonlocal parameter $α$ enhances the effective potential $V_{eff}$ and leads to a systematic reduction in the energy E and angular momentum L of circular orbits. Consequently, the ISCO radius, along with the associated energy and angular momentum, decreases monotonically with $α$, while the radiative efficiency increases, reaching a maximum of approximately $8.9\%$. Due to the spherical symmetry of the spacetime, the Keplerian frequency $Ω_φ$ and the vertical epicyclic frequency $Ω_θ$ coincide and are suppressed by $α$, whereas the radial epicyclic frequency $Ω_{r}$ is enhanced. The impact of $α$ on several twin-peak HF QPO models is examined, revealing that $α$ increases both the lower and upper bounds of the predicted QPO frequency ranges. By imposing the $2ν_U = 3ν_L$ resonance condition, we analyze the resonant radius, upper QPO frequency, maximum allowed black hole mass, and the time delay between the shadow and QPO signals. We find that the resonant radius decreases with $α$, while the upper QPO frequency increases, spanning the range $ν_U \sim(673/M-4360/M)$Hz. When the TOV imit is imposed, the upper frequency is further constrained to $ν_U \lesssim 1450$Hz. Combining astronomical observations for the classification of QPOs, where $ν_U \geq 100$Hz, the black hole mass in the nonlocal gravity should satisfy $M \lesssim 43.6M_\odot$. Although the radial separation between the resonant radius and the photon sphere decreases with $α$, the associated gravitational time delay increases, remaining below $\sim 1.3$ms and thus negligible for current observational capabilities.

### [166] [Dynamical analysis of the covariant $f(Q)$ gravity models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25412)
*S. A. Narawade,S. A. Kadam*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在协变 $f(Q)$ 引力框架下，通过构建与哈勃参数成比例的耦合函数（包括幂律模型和对数模型），利用自治动力系统分析临界点及其稳定性，证明两种模型均能重现从辐射、物质到暗能量主导的宇宙演化序列，并有效解释晚期宇宙加速膨胀。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在协变 $f(Q)$ 引力理论中引入一个随哈勃参数动态演化的耦合函数，探索该框架是否能够一致地描述宇宙的完整演化历史，特别是解释宇宙晚期加速膨胀现象。

Method: 将宇宙学场方程重写为自治动力系统（autonomous dynamical system），确定并分类临界点（critical points），利用中心流形理论（center manifold theory）分析非双曲临界点的稳定性，并绘制相空间轨迹（phase space trajectories）及宇宙学量演化图。

Result: 幂律模型和对数模型均能重现辐射、物质和暗能量主导时期的宇宙演化序列及其转变过程。通过总状态方程参数（EoS parameter）、密度参数（density parameters）和减速参数（deceleration parameter）等关键宇宙学量描述了各临界点的物理性质，并展示了相空间轨迹和稳定性行为。

Conclusion: 在协变形式下所考虑的 $f(Q)$ 模型能够为宇宙演化提供一致描述，为解释宇宙晚期加速膨胀提供了一种有前景的理论路径。

Abstract: In this study, we explore the cosmological evolution of the Universe in the framework of covariant $f(Q)$ gravity, with a coupling function that evolves dynamically in proportion to the Hubble parameter. Two specific forms of the function are examined: a power-law model and a logarithmic model. By rewriting the cosmological field equations as an autonomous dynamical system, we determine and classify the corresponding critical points and analyze their stability. Our results show that both models are able to reproduce the sequence of cosmic evolution, including radiation, matter, and dark energy-dominated eras, along with the transitions between them. The physical properties at each critical point are described using key cosmological quantities such as the total EoS parameter, density parameters, and the deceleration parameter. The stability of the non-hyperbolic critical point is analyzed through center manifold theory. In addition, we present phase space trajectories along with the stability behavior of each critical point. The evolution plots for the density parameters of radiation, matter, and dark energy, along with the EoS parameter for the total, are illustrated for further analysis. Overall, the analysis suggests that the $f(Q)$ models considered here, within the context of covariant formulation, provide a consistent description of cosmic evolution and offer a promising approach to explaining the late-time acceleration of the Universe.

### [167] [Massive scalar quasinormal modes of an asymptotically flat regular black hole supported by a phantom Dirac--Born--Infeld field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25471)
*Milena Skvortsova*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用高阶WKB近似结合Padé求和与时间域积分方法，系统计算了phantom DBI标量场支持的渐近平坦规则黑洞中大规模试探标量场的拟正态频谱，揭示了场质量和正则性参数对频谱的调控效应，并发现了准共振行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验大规模标量场在phantom Dirac–Born–Infeld (DBI)标量场支持的精确渐近平坦规则黑洞（regular black hole）几何中的拟正态谱（quasinormal spectrum），探索该规则几何的可观测印记。

Method: 采用经Padé求和（Padé resummation）改进的高阶WKB近似（WKB approximation），并结合特征时域积分（time-domain integration）与Prony提取法（Prony extraction），计算了基模和前两个泛音（overtones）。

Result: 增大场质量会提高振荡频率（oscillation frequency）并降低阻尼率（damping rate）；增大正则性尺度（regularity scale）通常使振铃更柔和、寿命更长。当场质量足够大时，阻尼趋于零，暗示准共振行为（quasiresonant behavior）的 onset，但时域中这些模式最终会被振荡晚期尾部掩盖。时域剖面与WKB–Padé结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 大规模标量振铃（massive scalar ringing）可作为该DBI支持的正则几何的灵敏探针（sensitive probe）。

Abstract: We study the quasinormal spectrum of a massive test scalar field in the exact asymptotically flat regular black-hole geometry supported by a phantom Dirac--Born--Infeld scalar. Using high-order WKB approximation improved by Padé resummation, together with characteristic time-domain integration and Prony extraction, we compute the fundamental mode and the first two overtones for representative values of the regularity parameter and the field mass. We show that increasing the field mass raises the oscillation frequency and reduces the damping rate, while increasing the regularity scale generally makes the ringing softer and longer lived. The time-domain profiles are in very good agreement with the WKB--Padé results and confirm the robustness of the spectrum. For sufficiently large field mass, the damping tends to zero, indicating the onset of quasiresonant behavior, although in the time domain these modes are eventually masked by oscillatory late-time tails. Our results show that massive scalar ringing provides a sensitive probe of this DBI-supported regular geometry.

TL;DR: 本文发展了用于计算高偏心率（eccentricity）后牛顿（post-Newtonian）双星系统引力波傅里叶模式（Fourier modes）的解析渐近方法，并构造了一种端点约束解析近似（endpoint-constrained analytic approximation），将计算加速且误差控制在$10^{-3}$以内，适用于$p\le200$的傅里叶模式。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用了后牛顿框架下的准开普勒参数化（quasi-Keplerian parametrization），发展了解析渐近方法计算高偏心率下的引力波傅里叶模式；推导了尾贡献（tail contributions）中偏心率增强函数（eccentricity enhancement function）的大偏心率渐近展开；并基于这些结果构造了端点约束解析近似。

Conclusion: 该方法为高偏心率双星系统的频域引力波建模提供了解析构建模块，有望提升极端质量比旋近（extreme mass ratio inspiral）等场景下的波形计算效率。

Abstract: In this work, we developed analytic asymptotic methods for computing the Fourier modes of gravitational waves from post-Newtonian binary systems in the quasi-Keplerian parametrization in the high eccentricity regime. We have also derived the large-eccentricity asymptotic expansion of the eccentricity enhancement function appearing in the tail contributions to the radiation. Furthermore, based on these results, we constructed an endpoint-constrained analytic approximation that significantly accelerate the computation of the Fourier modes at large eccentricity.The overall error of this analytic approximation is controlled within $10^{-3}$, and it remains valid for Fourier modes with $p\le200$. This approach provides an analytic building blocks for modeling frequency-domain gravitational wave from highly eccentric binaries.

### [169] [Lessons from binary dynamics of inspiralling equal-mass boson-star mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25582)
*Tamara Evstafyeva,Antonia Seifert,Ulrich Sperhake,Christopher J. Moore,Tamanna Jain*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值相对论模拟，研究了等质量旋进致密双星中的玻色子星双星系统与黑洞双星系统在引力波波形上的差异，发现前者在晚期旋进与并合阶段偏差最大，且部分玻色子星双星可激发次主导奇数次m-多极矩；尽管部分信号与现有波形模板存在简并性，但旋进-并合-振铃一致性测试可突破这一局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索玻色子星双星（boson-star binary）作为引力波源与黑洞双星（black-hole binary）之间的波形差异，从而识别可能区分两种致密天体（compact objects）的观测特征。

Method: 采用数值相对论（numerical relativity）模拟等质量旋进玻色子星双星系统；在早期旋进阶段将波形匹配至后牛顿（post-Newtonian）表达式，在晚期振铃阶段提取残余天体的准正则模（quasi-normal mode）频率。

Result: 玻色子星双星在晚期旋进与并合阶段显示出与可比黑洞双星系统最大的波形偏差；部分具有特定标量场相位偏移的等质量玻色子星双星系统激发了引力波辐射中次主导的奇数次m-多极矩（subdominant odd m-multipoles），而等质量无自旋黑洞双星中无此现象；部分玻色子星信号注入探测器噪声后与现有波形模板存在简并性（degeneracy）。

Conclusion: 旋进-并合-振铃一致性测试（inspiral-merger-ringdown consistency tests）能够克服玻色子星双星与黑洞双星信号之间的简并性，从而提供区分两类天体的有效途径。

Abstract: We explore the gravitational-wave phenomenology of equal-mass inspiralling boson-star binaries using numerical relativity simulations. In particular, we characterise the waveform differences between binary boson-star and black-hole systems across (i) the early inspiral, by matching our waveforms to post-Newtonian expressions, (ii) merger, and (iii) late ringdown, by extracting the quasi-normal mode frequencies of the remnants. We find that boson-star binaries exhibit the largest deviations from comparable binary black-hole systems during the late inspiral and merger phases. Remarkably, for a subset of these equal-mass boson-star binaries (with certain phase offsets in the scalar-field profiles) we identify the excitation of subdominant odd $m$-multipoles in the gravitational-wave emission, absent in equal-mass nonspinning black-hole binaries. Despite differences in the phenomenology of binary boson-star and black-hole signals, injections of some boson-star signals into detector noise exhibit degeneracy with current waveform approximants. Building on these results, we demonstrate how inspiral-merger-ringdown consistency tests can overcome these degeneracies.

</details>

Method: 采用扩展相空间形式（extended phase-space formalism），推导热力学量，验证修正后的第一定律（first law）和斯马尔关系（Smarr relation）；通过状态方程和临界行为分析探究相变；利用几何光学近似（geometric-optics）计算光子球（photon sphere）和黑洞阴影及发射率。

Result: 欧拉-海森堡耦合与环绕物质场显著改变了温度分布、稳定性结构和临界点位置；同时影响了霍金辐射的稀疏性、光子球半径和黑洞阴影的大小及几何光学发射率。

Conclusion: 非线性电动力学效应和周围物质环境对AdS黑洞的热力学稳定性、临界现象和可观测特征（如辐射与阴影）有不可忽略的修正作用。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamics, criticality, and selected radiative and optical properties of an Euler-Heisenberg AdS black hole surrounded by quintessence, perfect fluid dark matter, and a cloud of strings. Within the extended phase-space formalism, we derive the thermodynamic quantities, verify the modified first law and Smarr relation, and analyze the corresponding equation of state and critical behavior. We show that the Euler--Heisenberg coupling and the surrounding matter fields substantially modify the temperature profile, the stability structure, and the location of the critical point. We also examine the sparsity of Hawking radiation, together with the photon sphere, black hole shadow, and the associated geometric-optics emission rate.

### [171] [Mean first passage time and the Kramers escape rate of phase transitions for the Bardeen-AdS-class black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25791)
*Chen Ma,Bin Wu,Zhen-Ming Xu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用广义自由能、平均首通时间（Mean First-Passage Time）以及随机动力学中的Kramers逃逸速率，系统刻画了Bardeen-AdS类黑洞的相变景观。研究发现，这类黑洞存在两类解：第一类（Type I）具有规则黑洞解，其小黑洞与大黑洞之间的相变可经历稳定、亚稳态或不稳定规则黑洞作为中间态；第二类（Type II）仅包含真空态解，其相变仅在真空态与小黑洞之间发生，且不涉及任何规则黑洞中间态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对Bardeen-AdS类黑洞的相变机制尚未充分揭示，尤其是不同类型黑洞（规则黑洞解 vs. 真空态解）在相变过程中所扮演的角色尚不明确。本文旨在通过随机动力学视角，系统分析该类黑洞的相变路径与中间态结构。

Method: 构建广义自由能（generalized free energy），并结合平均首通时间（Mean First-Passage Time）和Kramers逃逸速率（Kramers escape rate）等随机动力学工具，对Bardeen-AdS类黑洞的相变过程进行定量刻画与分类。

Result: Bardeen-AdS类黑洞存在两类解：Type I（规则黑洞解）和Type II（真空态解）。对于Type I，小黑洞与大白洞之间的相变可能以稳定、亚稳态或不稳定规则黑洞作为中间态；对于Type II，相变仅在真空态与小黑洞之间进行，且不涉及任何规则黑洞中间态。

Conclusion: 本文的相变景观分析揭示了Bardeen-AdS类黑洞中两类解在相变路径上的本质差异：Type I存在丰富的中间态结构（包括稳定、亚稳态与不稳定规则黑洞），而Type II的相变路径更为简单、直接。该结果有助于深入理解黑洞热力学中不同拓扑类型解的相变行为。

Abstract: In this study, by utilizing the constructed generalized free energy alongside the Mean First-Passage Time and the Kramers escape rate from stochastic dynamics, we have obtained a comprehensive landscape of the phase transitions for the Bardeen-AdS-class black hole. This black hole model admits two distinct categories of solutions. Type I black holes feature a regular black hole solution, and Type II black holes possess a vacuum state solution. In the phase transition between the small black hole and the large black hole for Type I, the process may pass through a stable, metastable, or unstable regular black hole as an intermediate state. In contrast, for Type II black holes, the phase transition occurs exclusively between the vacuum state and the small black hole, and the transition process does not involve any regular black hole intermediate states.

</details>


### [172] [The Equivalence Principle and Kinematical Structure in the ADM Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25793)
*L. G. Pereira*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用阿尔诺维特-德瑟-米斯纳（ADM）形式体系，将均匀加速实验室与引力场中支撑的实验室统一纳入一个共同的度规描述框架，并通过ADM位移矢量（shift vector）的物理解释，阐明了二者在动力学上的等价结构，进而为引力时间膨胀与观测者依赖视界提供了关系性说明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 等效原理（Equivalence Principle）在局域层面建立了均匀加速与引力支撑之间的联系，但其在动力学层面的精确内容尚不明确。本文旨在发展一种统一的度规描述，以厘清这两种构型之间超越局域考虑的动力学关系。

Method: 采用广义相对论（General Relativity）中的标准ADM形式体系，将时空分解为空间超曲面及其时间演化；将ADM位移矢量解释为编码所选叶状结构（foliation）中空间切片与时间嵌入之间动力学关系的物理量。

Result: 具有相同固有加速度（proper acceleration）的均匀加速实验室与引力支撑实验室共享等价的局域位移结构。该形式揭示了加速运动的空间位移与能量代价与其在引力支撑观测者现象学描述中看似缺失之间的不对称性。该解释还导出了引力时间膨胀（gravitational time dilation）的关系性说明以及观测者依赖视界（observer-dependent horizons）的出现。

Conclusion: 该ADM位移矢量解释在保持与标准广义相对论场方程和约束完全等价的前提下，使得通常隐含在几何描述中的动力学特征得以显式呈现。

Abstract: The relation between uniformly accelerated laboratories and laboratories supported in a gravitational field lies at the conceptual core of the Equivalence Principle, yet its precise kinematical content beyond strictly local considerations remains subtle. In this work we develop a unified metric description of these configurations using the standard Arnowitt-Deser-Misner (ADM) formulation of General Relativity, which provides an explicit decomposition of spacetime into spatial hypersurfaces and their temporal evolution. In this setting the ADM shift vector is interpreted as a physical quantity encoding the kinematical relation between spatial slices and their temporal embedding associated with a chosen foliation. This interpretation allows uniformly accelerated laboratories and laboratories supported in a gravitational field to be described within a common structural framework, showing that configurations experiencing identical proper acceleration share an equivalent local shift structure. This viewpoint clarifies the apparent asymmetry between the spatial displacement and energetic cost associated with accelerated motion and their apparent absence in phenomenological descriptions of observers supported in a gravitational field. The formulation remains fully equivalent to standard General Relativity at the level of the field equations and constraints while making explicit kinematical features that are usually implicit in its geometric description. Consequences of this interpretation include a relational account of gravitational time dilation and the emergence of observer-dependent horizons.

</details>
