### [173] [Quantum Rotors on the Fuzzy Sphere and the Cubic CFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24840)
*Andreas Stergiou*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用模糊球正则化（fuzzy sphere regularisation）方法，通过引入立方不变两体相互作用，非微扰地研究了具有立方各向异性的海森堡磁体中的三维立方共形场论（cubic CFT），成功分离了与O(3)模型数值上非常接近的临界点，并计算了关键算子的标度维度（scaling dimensions）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维立方共形场论（cubic CFT）描述了具有立方各向异性的海森堡磁体的临界行为，但其可观测量的数值与更高对称性的O(3)模型极为接近，导致非微扰研究十分困难。因此，需要一种能够明确区分这两个相近普适类（universality classes）的新方法。

Method: 采用模糊球正则化（fuzzy sphere regularisation）方法，在用于O(3)模型的量子转子哈密顿量（quantum rotor Hamiltonian）中添加立方不变两体相互作用（cubic-invariant two-body interaction），从而显式破缺连续旋转对称性，孤立出立方临界点。利用精确对角化（exact diagonalisation）和密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalisation group, DMRG）进行计算。

Result: 计算了多个关键算子的标度维度（scaling dimensions），包括领头标量单态（leading scalar singlets），并解析了O(3)秩二无迹对称张量（rank-two traceless symmetric tensor）在立方群（cubic group）的$E_g$和$T_{2g}$表示下的分裂情况。结果与已有的蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）、共形微扰论（conformal perturbation theory）和$\varepsilon$展开（$\varepsilon$ expansion）基准一致。

Conclusion: 研究结果验证了模糊球方法在分辨数值上相近的普适类（universality classes）方面的强大能力，为研究难以通过常规方法区分的临界理论提供了有效工具。

Abstract: The three-dimensional cubic conformal field theory governs the critical behaviour of Heisenberg magnets with cubic anisotropy. Studying this theory non-perturbatively is challenging, because its most easily accessible observables are numerically very close to those of the more symmetric $O(3)$ model. In this work, we overcome this difficulty using the fuzzy sphere regularisation method. By adding a cubic-invariant two-body interaction to the quantum rotor Hamiltonian used for the $O(3)$ model, we break the continuous rotational symmetry by construction and unambiguously isolate the cubic critical point. Using exact diagonalisation and the density matrix renormalisation group, we calculate the scaling dimensions of several key operators, including the leading scalar singlets, and resolve the splitting of the $O(3)$ rank-two traceless symmetric tensor into the $E_g$ and $T_{2g}$ representations of the cubic group. Our results are consistent with existing Monte Carlo, conformal perturbation theory, and $\varepsilon$ expansion benchmarks, demonstrating the power of the fuzzy sphere in resolving closely spaced universality classes.

</details>


### [174] [Magnetic phases of the anisotropic triangular Hubbard model from the ghost-Gutzwiller approximation in the rotating spin-frame](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24848)
*Azin Kazemi-Moridani,Samuele Giuli,Tsung-Han Lee,A. -M. S. Tremblay,Michel Côté,Nicola Lanatà,Olivier Gingras*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用Gutzwiller近似（GA）及其鬼影推广（ghost-GA）研究了各向异性三角晶格上半填充哈伯德模型的磁相图。通过将旋转自旋框架与高分辨率动量网格相结合，直接最小化总能量确定磁基态。与动力学平均场理论（DMFT）和双费米子结果对比发现，标准GA虽能捕捉相图定性结构，但高估了磁有序稳定性；而引入少量辅助“鬼影”轨道即可恢复大部分动力学效应，显著改善与DMFT的定量一致性。鬼影GA被证明是一种高效、可系统改进的框架，可在极低计算成本下达到接近DMFT的精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 各向异性三角晶格上的哈伯德模型是研究强关联和几何阻挫（geometric frustration）系统中磁性的重要模型。然而，传统解析方法难以同时兼顾计算效率与精度，现有方法（如标准GA缺乏动力学涨落，DMFT计算成本高昂）均存在局限。因此，需要发展一种高效且可系统改进的框架来准确描述该体系中的磁性。

Method: 采用Gutzwiller近似（GA）及其鬼影推广（ghost-GA）方法，结合旋转自旋框架（rotating spin-frame formulation）与高分辨率动量网格，通过对序参量波矢（ordering wavevector）进行直接总能量最小化（total-energy minimization）来确定磁基态。同时，以动力学平均场理论（DMFT）和双费米子（dual-fermion）结果作为基准进行对比验证。

Result: 标准GA能定性正确描述相图结构，但系统性地高估了磁有序的稳定性。引入少量鬼影轨道即可恢复大部分动力学效应，使鬼影GA的定量结果与DMFT高度一致。在全布里渊区（full Brillouin zone）扫描中，获得了包含顺磁相和多种磁相的完整相图。与梯子双费米子（ladder dual-fermion）磁化率预测不同，一维反铁磁相（one-dimensional antiferromagnetic phase）从未稳定存在，尽管其在某些区域是主导不稳定性。

Conclusion: 鬼影GA是一种高效且可系统改进的计算框架，能在极低计算成本下达到接近DMFT的精度，适用于研究阻挫体系（frustrated systems）中的磁性。标准GA虽在定量上有偏差，但在定性捕捉一般相图方面表现良好，可用于探索更复杂体系中非公度磁有序（incommensurate magnetic orders）。

Abstract: We investigate the magnetic phase diagram of the half-filled Hubbard model on the anisotropic triangular lattice using the Gutzwiller approximation (GA) and its ghost generalization (ghost-GA). By combining a rotating spin-frame formulation with high-resolution momentum grids, we determine magnetic ground states through direct total-energy minimization over the ordering wavevector. We benchmark standard GA and ghost-GA against dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT) and dual-fermion results. We show that GA already captures the qualitative structure of the phase diagram, but systematically overestimates the stability of magnetic order due to the absence of dynamical fluctuations. We find that introducing a small number of auxiliary ''ghost'' orbitals is sufficient to recover most dynamical effects and significantly improves quantitative agreement with DMFT. Exploring the full Brillouin zone, we obtain a phase diagram comprising paramagnetic and various magnetic phases. In contrast to ladder dual-fermion susceptibility-based predictions, we find that the one-dimensional antiferromagnetic phase is never stabilized, despite being the leading instability in certain regimes. Our results establish ghost-GA as an efficient and systematically improvable framework for studying magnetism in frustrated systems, capable of achieving near-DMFT accuracy at a fraction of the computational cost. They also highlight that standard GA performs qualitatively well for capturing the general phase diagram, enabling the investigation of incommensurate magnetic orders in more complex systems.

</details>


### [175] [Universal Topological Power Transfer with Arbitrarily Large Chern Number in Driven Quantum Spin Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24851)
*Anshuman Tripathi,Mircea Trif,Thore Posske*

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维XXZ海森堡自旋-1/2链中的拓扑频率转换效应，发现通过改变链长和交换各向异性可以系统调控陈数，从而实现任意大且量子化的转换比，为拓扑频率转换器提供了新的物理机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的少自旋系统拓扑频率转换器（topological frequency converter）虽然已在理论上得到验证，但其转换因子通常被限制在较小的整数值上。本文旨在探索能否在相互作用的自旋链（spin chain）系统中实现任意大的量子化转换比。

Method: 研究考虑了一个相互作用的XXZ海森堡自旋-1/2链（Heisenberg spin-1/2 chain），该系统受到两个频率不可公度（incommensurate frequencies）的磁驱动场的绝热驱动。通过分析由绝热轨迹包围的简并点（degeneracy points）所决定的陈数（Chern number），并研究其随链长和交换各向异性（exchange anisotropy）的变化规律。

Result: 陈数随链长增加而系统性地增大，并且可以通过交换各向异性进行调控，从而直接控制拓扑泵浦强度（topological pumping strength）。研究还揭示了量子临界点（quantum critical points）的各向异性和磁场强度对奇偶链长的普适依赖关系。

Conclusion: 该机制能够在相互作用的量子自旋链中实现具有任意大且量子化转换比的拓扑频率转换器，且该机制在驱动场的任意耦合区域（arbitrary coupling regions）中均保持不变。

Abstract: Topological frequency converters exploit a quantized transfer of power between two driving fields in a quantum system, a phenomenon topologically protected by the Chern number of the associated fiber bundle. While realizations with few-spin systems have theoretically demonstrated this effect, the conversion factors have typically been restricted to small integer values. Here, we investigate an interacting $XXZ$ Heisenberg spin-$1/2$ chain driven adiabatically by two magnetic drives with incommensurate frequencies. The Chern number, determined by the degeneracy points enclosed by the adiabatic trajectory, increases systematically with the chain length and can be tuned through the exchange anisotropy, providing direct control of the topological pumping strength. We reveal a universal dependency of the anisotropy and magnetic field strength for odd and even chain lengths of the quantum critical points. This provides a mechanism for a topological frequency converter with an arbitrarily large, quantized conversion ratio in interacting quantum spin chains. The mechanism remains the same for arbitrary coupling regions of the drives.

### [176] [Dynamical dimer structure factor of the triangular $S=1/2$ Heisenberg antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24868)
*Markus Drescher,Laurens Vanderstraeten,Roderich Moessner,Frank Pollmann,Johannes Knolle*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用大规模GPU加速的矩阵乘积态（matrix-product-state, MPS）模拟方法，对三角晶格上的扩展自旋-1/2反铁磁海森堡模型（extended spin-1/2 antiferromagnetic Heisenberg model）进行数值计算，提取动力学二聚体响应。

Result: 在有序相（120°共面序、共线条纹序和四面体自旋序）中，发现了双磁子连续谱（two-magnon continuum）起始能量以下的低能模，体现了避免的准粒子衰变（avoided quasiparticle decay）。在候选的无隙U(1)狄拉克QSL中，观察到布里渊区角一半（X ≡ K/2）动量点处的绝对色散极小值，与场论预言一致。

Conclusion: 高分辨率的动力学二聚体响应为U(1)狄拉克量子自旋液体（U(1) Dirac QSL）的存在提供了支持，该态具有自旋单态单极子激发（singlet monopole excitations）。

Abstract: The dynamical dimer structure factor is an observable probing spin-singlet excitations of quantum magnets distinct from those commonly studied by the spin structure factor. We report the dimer response for the extended spin-$1/2$ antiferromagnetic Heisenberg model on the triangular lattice using large-scale GPU-accelerated matrix-product-state simulations. We investigate the ordered phases with $120^\circ$ coplanar, collinear stripe, and tetrahedral spin order, as well as candidate quantum spin-liquid (QSL) regimes, comprising an expected gapless $U(1)$ Dirac QSL and a chiral QSL at finite spin-scalar-chirality coupling. In the ordered phases, we find low-energy modes below the onset of the two-magnon continuum illustrating avoided quasiparticle decay. Within the candidate gapless QSL, we observe absolute dispersion minima at momenta of half the Brillouin zone corners, $X\equiv K/2$, in agreement with field-theory predictions that singlet monopole excitations of the $U(1)$ Dirac spin liquid become gapless at these points. Thus, the high-resolution dynamical dimer response provides support for a $U(1)$ Dirac QSL with singlet monopole excitations.

### [177] [Anomaly and symmetry-charge flow in mixed states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24872)
*Ze-Min Huang,Sebastian Diehl*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过对称性与通量插入算子（flux-insertion operator）之间的代数关系，将$(1+1)$维手征反常（chiral anomaly）从零温纯态推广到混合态（mixed states），提出“对称荷流（symmetry-charge flow）”作为谱流（spectral flow）的混合态推广，恢复了手征反常的普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统$(1+1)$维手征反常理论仅适用于零温纯态，在混合态中谱流机制失效，朴素的推广导致模型依赖的反常系数（anomaly coefficients），使得手征反常的普适性受到质疑。本文旨在解决这一问题。

Method: 从对称性与其通量插入算子之间的代数关系出发推导反常，从而获得“对称荷流”——一种谱流的混合态推广。在外加场作用下，统计权重在对称荷分辨的电荷扇区（symmetry-resolved charge sectors）之间重新分布。

Result: 该方法仅由对称性固定，恢复了反常的普适性，同时适用于费米子体系和玻色子体系中的纯态与混合态。在具有连续对称性的紧束缚费米子模型（tight-binding fermionic models）和具有离散对称性的自旋模型（spin models）中验证了上述结果。

Conclusion: 手征反常的混合态推广通过纯代数途径实现，其普适性不依赖于具体模型细节，为量子场论中反常现象在有限温度和开放系统中的应用奠定了基础。

Abstract: The $(1+1)$-dimensional chiral anomaly is a paradigmatic exact result in quantum field theory, traditionally formulated for zero-temperature pure states where it arises from spectral flow induced by external gauge fields and captures universal ground-state properties. In mixed states, however, the participation of many states and charge exchange with the environment invalidate this mechanism. Naive extensions yield model-dependent anomaly coefficients, calling its universality into question. Here, we resolve this problem for Abelian symmetries by deriving the anomaly from an algebraic relation between the symmetry and its flux-insertion operator. We obtain symmetry-charge flow, a mixed-state generalization of spectral flow, in which an applied field redistributes statistical weight across symmetry-resolved charge sectors. Fixed solely by symmetry, the anomaly restores universality and applies to both pure and mixed states in fermionic and bosonic systems. We substantiate these results in tight-binding fermionic models with continuous symmetry and in spin models with discrete symmetries.

</details>

Abstract: We map the phase diagram of the triangular-lattice Majorana-Hubbard model on a four-leg ladder using DMRG and variational uniform matrix product states, revealing a richer variety of phases than previously known. Analysis of entanglement-spectrum degeneracies and adiabatic connections identifies multiple symmetry-protected topological (SPT) phases. These phases could be realized in arrays of vortex-bound Majorana modes on the surface of a topological superconductor.

### [179] [Dielectric signatures of crystal-field and low-temperature correlated dynamics in NdMgAl11O19](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24937)
*Sonu Kumar,Gaël Bastien,Maxim Savinov,Małgorzata Śliwińska-Bartkowiak,Ross H. Colman,Stanislav Kamba*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在局域化 \ce{Nd^{3+}} 磁矩与可极化 \ce{AlO5} 双锥网络共存的中心对称阻挫磁铅石体系中，能否通过介电谱区分激发态 CEF 能级与基态 Kramers 二重态（Kramers doublet）的介电响应，从而为相关材料提供参考体系。

Method: 对单晶 \ce{NdMgAl11O19} 沿晶轴 $c$ 方向测量复介电常数实部 $\varepsilon'_c(T)$，温度范围为 275~K 至更低温度（低于 2~K），频率范围为 4~Hz 至 50~kHz，并辅以等温磁场依赖测量 $\varepsilon_c'(H)$。

Result: 高温区（275~K 至 30~K）$\varepsilon'_c(T)$ 随降温增大且无频率依赖；低温区出现频率依赖的介电常数下降，并在 2~K 以下再次回升。高频数据可用 Barrett 公式加有效二能级贡献拟合，得到能隙 $Δ= 25.85 \pm 0.32$~K，与最低 \ce{Nd^{3+}} CEF 劈裂一致。低于 ~30~K 时介电响应呈现强频率和磁场依赖；等温 $\varepsilon_c'(H)$ 在 $μ_0H_c \simeq 0.85$~T 附近观察到低场交叉，归因于反铁磁关联与基态 Kramers 二重态塞曼分裂的竞争。

Conclusion: \ce{NdMgAl11O19} 可作为 Kramers 参考体系，在其中能够区分激发态 CEF 能级与场调控、关联主导的基态二重态在中心对称阻挫磁铅石宿主中的不同介电特征。

Abstract: We report dielectric spectroscopy of single-crystalline \ce{NdMgAl11O19}, a magnetoplumbite hexaaluminate in which localized \ce{Nd^{3+}} moments coexist with a polarizable \ce{AlO5} bipyramidal network. The real part of the permittivity, $\varepsilon'_{c}(T)$, measured along the crystallographic $c$ axis, increases as the temperature is lowered from 275~K to 30~K and is frequency-independent between 4~Hz and 50~kHz. At lower temperatures, a frequency-dependent decrease in permittivity is observed, followed by a further upturn below 2~K. The high-frequency $\varepsilon'_{c}(T)$ is described by a Barrett formula supplemented by an effective two-level contribution, yielding a robust gap of $Δ= 25.85 \pm 0.32$~K consistent with the lowest \ce{Nd^{3+}} crystal-electric-field (CEF) splitting. Below $\sim 30$~K, the dielectric response becomes strongly frequency and magnetic-field dependent. Isothermal $\varepsilon_c'(H)$ measurements reveal a reproducible low-field crossover near $μ_0H_c \simeq 0.85$~T, which we attribute to the competition between antiferromagnetic correlations and Zeeman splitting of the ground-state Kramers doublet. \ce{NdMgAl11O19} thus provides a Kramers reference system in which dielectric signatures of the excited-state CEF manifold can be distinguished from those of the field-tuned, correlation-dominated ground-state doublet sector in a centrosymmetric frustrated magnetoplumbite host

Method: 理论分析局域晶场对称性对Kramers二重态内矩阵元的约束；实验采用热力学测量（thermodynamic measurements）和弹性能中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering, INS）进行验证。

Result: 对称性强制⟨ψ₊|J±|ψ₋⟩=0，消除最低阶横向通道；零场下出现两个异常信号；在场下热力学响应分裂为相边界（phase boundary）和宽交叉线（crossover line）；有序温度以上INS未发现低能色散磁模式。

Abstract: We show that the local crystal-field symmetry of ErBr$_3$ enforces $\langle ψ_\pm | J^{\pm} | ψ_\mp \rangle = 0$ within the ground-state Kramers doublet, thereby removing the lowest-order transverse channel from the low-energy sector. Thermodynamic measurements reveal two zero-field anomalies. Under an in-plane magnetic field, the thermodynamic response separates into a phase boundary and a broader crossover line. Consistently, inelastic neutron scattering measurements above the ordering temperature reveal no well-defined low-energy dispersive magnetic modes. These results show that the crystal-field ground-state symmetry strongly constrains the low-energy dynamics and provides a natural framework for understanding the field-dependent thermodynamic response of ErBr$_3$.

### [181] [Tunable thermal conductivity through dual spin-phonon coupling in van der Waals ferromagnetic insulator Cr2Ge2Te6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25115)
*Zhongbin Wang,Wenlong Tang,Simin Pang,Hongxing Zhu,Renkang Fan,Baohai Jia,Junxue Li,Ben Xu,Jun Zhang,Lin Xie,Jiaqing He*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在铁磁绝缘体Cr2Ge2Te6中实验证实了自旋-声子耦合（spin-phonon coupling）对声子输运的调控作用，通过磁场强度和方向实现了对热导率的可调控制，为动态声子工程（phonon engineering）提供了统一框架和可行的材料平台。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合热输运测量、布里渊光散射（Brillouin light scattering）和铁磁共振（ferromagnetic resonance）技术，系统研究铁磁绝缘体Cr2Ge2Te6在磁场调控下的声子输运行为及其微观机制。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了自旋-声子耦合影响声子输运的实验证据，展示了SPC在统一系统中的双重作用，拓宽了对准粒子相互作用（quasiparticle interactions）的基本理解，并在二维磁性材料等类似平台上展示了实现场可调声子输运的潜力。

Abstract: The active manipulation of phonon transport remains a central challenge in phononics and spin caloritronics due to the charge-neutral nature of heat carriers. Spin-phonon coupling (SPC) offers a promising route for the dynamic control of heat carriers, yet its progress has been limited due to the lack of a unified framework and suitable material platforms. Here, we report on the magnetic field-tunable phonon transport behavior in the ferromagnetic insulator Cr2Ge2Te6. We observed two distinct anomalous regimes at both the high and low fields that were governed by isotropic magnon-phonon hybridization and an anisotropic magnon softening process, respectively. By integrating detailed transport behavior with Brillouin light scattering and ferromagnetic resonance, we uncovered the microscopic origins of these anomalous regimes and demonstrated that both the field magnitude and orientation could act as versatile tuning knobs to manipulate the thermal conductivity. Our findings provide experimental evidence of the SPC effect on phonon transport, demonstrating the dual impact of SPC within a unified system. This work will not only broaden the fundamental understanding of quasiparticle interactions but also establish a viable framework for dynamic phonon engineering. Furthermore, the characteristics of this system highlight the potential for achieving field-tunable phonon transport in similar platforms such as two-dimensional (2D) magnetic materials.

### [182] [Identifying strong correlation using only the Kohn-Sham density of one-electron states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25125)
*Daniel D. Rivera,Gustavo M. Dalpian,John P. Perdew*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: No AI summary available.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: No AI summary available.

Method: No AI summary available.

Result: No AI summary available.

Conclusion: No AI summary available.

Abstract: Strongly correlated systems have long been a central and highly non-trivial topic in condensed matter physics. At the non-interacting level, strong correlation can be associated with powerful (near) degeneracies between occupied and unoccupied states, which leads to a high density of states near the Fermi level in metallic configurations. Such regimes are commonly treated with beyond-density functional theory (DFT) approaches, such as DFT+U or DFT+DMFT while maintaining symmetric configurations. Here, we explore the hypothesis that symmetry breaking in the Kohn-Sham (KS) non-interacting system can qualitatively account for the energetic effects of strong correlation in the corresponding interacting system within standard DFT. By lifting near-degeneracies around the Fermi level, symmetry breaking diminishes the potential correlation effects, reducing the need for an explicit treatment of electron correlation, transforming an otherwise strongly correlated symmetric configuration into a normally correlated one, thus avoiding the need for interacting methods beyond DFT. This naturally connects nonmagnetic to magnetic states. We apply this idea to both strongly and normally correlated metals and observe that spin symmetry breaking leads to a pronounced reduction of the density of states at the Fermi level and a significant lowering of the total energy in strongly correlated cases. To describe the degree of correlation that the interacting system would have relative to the KS state, we introduce a correlation parameter ($Γ$), defined as the ratio between the Kohn-Sham density of one-electron states at the Fermi level and that of a corresponding uniform electron gas. This parameter distinguishes strongly correlated systems, which would require explicit treatment, from normally correlated ones, which do not.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对TbPt6Al3单晶样品施加单轴应力（uniaxial stress）σ，通过磁化测量（magnetization measurements）研究磁场沿三角a轴方向时的磁化响应，分析压磁效应的线性与非线性行为，并提取压磁系数Q11及其温度依赖的临界指数β。

Conclusion: TbPt6Al3中巨大的压磁系数Q11以及达到单畴态所需的大极化场（10000 Oe），归因于Tb³⁺离子4f电子的强相对论性自旋-轨道耦合（relativistic spin-orbit coupling）。

Abstract: We have investigated the piezomagnetic (PZM) effect of the rare-earth-based g-wave altermagnet TbPt6Al3 by magnetization measurements of single-crystalline samples under uniaxial stress sigma. The magnetization in magnetic field along the trigonal a axis increases linearly with sigma for T < TN, indicating the emergence of PZM effect, while the theoretically predicted nonlinear PZM effect was not observed. PZM coefficient of Q11 at 2 K is obtained as 9.1 times 10^-3 mu_B/(f.u. MPa), which is larger by more than two orders of magnitude than those for other altermagnets and noncollinear antiferromagnets. Temperature dependence of Q11 below TN yielded the critical component beta as 0.28, whose value is close to that of the magnetic moment estimated by the neutron powder diffraction. We propose that the large Q11 and the large poling field of 10000 Oe to achieve the single-domain state in TbPt6Al3 are due to the strong relativistic spin-orbit coupling of the 4f electrons in the Tb3+ ions.

Abstract: We report the growth of high-quality single crystals of the magnetic topological semimetal EuAuBi using a Pb flux method, which effectively suppresses the formation of secondary Au2Bi impurity phases that were prevalent in the previously reported Bi flux grown crystals. This growth optimization enables reliable investigation of the intrinsic physical properties of EuAuBi. Importantly, Pb flux growth stablilizes c axis oriented single crystals, enabling Hall measurements in a previously unexplored geometry. In this configuration (I parallel to c, B perpendicular to c), a finite residual Hall contribution, known as topological Hall signal emerges below the antiferromagnetic ordering temperature and within a narrow magnetic field range. This Hall contribution coincides with the metamagnetic transitions, anomalies in magnetoresistance, and an additional feature in field-dependent specific heat, indicating strong coupling between the electronic transport and field induced magnetic reconstructions. Consequently, these findings underscore the significance of crystal orientation in uncovering topological transport signatures in magnetic semimetals such as EuAuBi.

Method: 本文基于最近邻反铁磁XXZ哈密顿量，在多种准周期与周期二分晶格上，通过自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit interaction）诱导的间接电偶极耦合机制，计算并比较一阶（单磁子）非弹性光散射谱。

Unlike second-order (two-magnon) Raman scatterings based on an exchange interaction between neighboring spins, the present observations involve an indirect electric-dipole coupling which proceeds through a spin-orbit interaction. We discuss the nearest-neighbor antiferromagnetic XXZ Hamiltonian on various quasiperiodic and periodic bipartite lattices. The first-order spectra, of our present interest, consist only of rotation-invariant and mirror-symmetric magnons, while the second-order ones cannot select any particular magnon. With the exchange anisotropy moving away from the Ising limit toward the Heisenberg isotropic point, every initial delta-function peak bifurcates or divides into more in each individual manner on quasiperiodic lattices, while it remains singly peaked all the way on periodic lattices. ### [187] [Highly fluctuating double-$q$ magnetic order in the van der Waals metal CeTe$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25436)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CeTe₃具有简单的准二维电子结构和可解理性，是探索低维关联磁性（correlated magnetism）的理想平台；然而其低温磁态的性质尚不明确，需要澄清。

Method: 采用单晶中子衍射（single-crystal neutron diffraction）技术测量至0.3 K，并辅以扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）进行表征。

Result: 在约1.5 K附近观察到磁相变，出现非公度布拉格峰（incommensurate Bragg peaks），位置在q₊∼(±0.17, 0, 0.31)，对应双-q（double-q）磁有序，磁矩主要沿c轴排列。有序磁矩显著减小，传播矢量偏离简单嵌套（nesting）条件。

Conclusion: CeTe₃在范德瓦尔斯极限下存在关联磁基态，其中自旋与巡游电荷自由度紧密耦合，磁矩减小与c-f杂化（c-f hybridization）增强的量子涨落一致，传播矢量的偏离则与准一维Te能带的残余电荷密度波（charge-density-wave, CDW）不稳定性有关。

Abstract: CeTe$_3$ is a van der Waals antiferromagnet composed of magnetic [CeTe]$^+$ layers coupled to highly conducting Te$^{0.5-}$ square nets. Its simple quasi-two-dimensional electronic structure and cleavable nature make it an appealing platform for exploring correlated magnetism in reduced dimensions. To clarify the nature of its low-temperature state, we performed single-crystal neutron diffraction down to 0.3 K, complemented by scanning tunneling microscopy. A magnetic transition near 1.5 K gives rise to incommensurate Bragg peaks at $q_{\pm}\sim(\pm0.17,0,0.31)$, consistent with a double-$q$ magnetic order whose moments are predominantly aligned along the $c$ axis. The strongly reduced ordered moment is consistent with enhanced quantum fluctuations driven by $c$-$f$ hybridization, while the deviation of the propagation vectors from simple nesting suggests a coupling to residual charge-density-wave instabilities of the quasi-one-dimensional Te-derived bands. These results indicate that CeTe$_3$ hosts a correlated magnetic ground state where spin and itinerant charge degrees of freedom are intimately linked in the van der Waals limit.

Method: 采用互补探测深度的光电子能谱（photoemission spectroscopy）与磁化率（magnetic susceptibility）测量相结合的方法，对Cr掺杂V2O3纳米晶体进行分析。

Abstract: We investigated the size dependence of the metal-insulator transition (MIT) in Cr-doped V2O3 nanocrystals by photoemission spectroscopy using complementary probing depths, together with magnetic susceptibility measurements. Photoemission spectra show that MIT signatures persist down to an average particle size of 5.6 nm, and magnetic susceptibility measurements exhibit a nearly size-invariant transition onset. The contrast between surface-sensitive and deeper-probing photoemission spectra reveals that the transition survives in the nanocrystal interior. At the same time, the spectra indicate a systematic suppression of coherent quasiparticle weight with decreasing size, pointing to the growth of an insulating surface dead layer. These results demonstrate that nanoscaling does not intrinsically eliminate the MIT itself, but progressively enhances the influence of surface-driven insulating behavior, thereby providing insight into the practical limits of miniaturizing Mott-based devices.

Using large-scale density matrix renormalization group simulations, we uncover a rich phase diagram comprising five gapped phases and, remarkably, two critical floating phases. These incommensurate Luttinger liquid phases emerge from the proliferation of non-magnetic domains - 0-states and dimers - within a trimerized background and are confined to the zero magnetization sector, while magnetic excitations remain gapped. We show that the transition between the topological Haldane phase and the floating phases are governed by a composite critical line with central charge c=2, consistent with a coexistence of magnetic and non-magnetic critical modes. ### [190] [The odd-parity ALM induced reconstruction of the Chern-insulating phase in Haldane-Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25537)

Abstract: Odd-parity altermagnetism(ALM) extends compensated collinear magnetism beyond the even-parity spin splitting of conventional altermagnets, but its role in correlated topological phases remains largely unexplored. Using the cluster slave-spin method, we show that the odd-parity ALM appearing in the ALM Chern-insulating phase of Haldane-Hubbard model significantly reconstructs the local topology in the conventional Chern-insulating phase, while the total Chern number remains unchanged compared to the Chern-insulating phase. The Berry curvature becomes spin and valley selective; zigzag ribbons develop chiral-symmetry-breaking edge states; while armchair ribbons remain inversion symmetric. The optical response mirrors this separation between the local reconstruction and the global topology: low-energy spectra are governed by quasiparticles near the gap, whereas the low-frequency Hall conductivity stays quantized, $σ_{\rm T\uparrow}(Ω\to 0)=σ_{\rm T\downarrow}(Ω\to 0)=e^2/h$. These results establish the Haldane-Hubbard model as a minimal correlated platform for odd-parity altermagnetic topology.

### [191] [Topochemical Fluorination of La$_2$NiO$_{4+δ}$ Single Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25575)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Topochemical fluorination offers a low--temperature route for modifying the anion chemistry and electronic ground states of layered transition-metal oxides, providing access to metastable phases and functionalities that are not able to be achieved through conventional solid--state synthesis. Despite extensive work on polycrystalline samples and thin films, topochemical fluorination of bulk single crystals has not been studied, limiting insights into intrinsic structure property relationships. Here, we investigate the topochemical fluorination of optical float zone grown (OFZ) La$_2$NiO$_{4+δ}$ single crystals using polymer-based PTFE, PVDF and inorganic CuF$_{2}$ fluorination agents and compare it to our topochemical pathways of reduction of LaNiO$_{3-x}$. This even induces a clear superstructure, which was not reported before and extends the understanding of anion insertion reactions beyond what is known on stage ordering in nickelates. Energy-dispersive X--ray spectroscopy confirms strong fluorine incorporation on the surface and reduced homogeneity in the bulk. These results identify THC as a reliable route to lower-cost sc$GW$ and sc$GWΓ$ calculations

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管摩尔折叠能带（folded band structures）理论上可孕育狄拉克态，但直接通过动量分辨（momentum-resolved）方式观测无带隙的摩尔狄拉克准粒子（moiré-Dirac quasiparticles）极具挑战，此前尚未实现。

Method: 在外延表面摩尔结构（epitaxial surface-moiré structure）上进行角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）测量，直接获得动量分辨的能带信息。

Result: 观测到一维超晶格势（superlattice potential）驱动下各向异性（anisotropic）但沿约束方向具有弱无质量狄拉克色散（massless Dirac dispersion）的电子态；能带交叉（band crossings）属于拓扑节线（topological nodal lines），锁定在迷你布里渊区（mini-Brillouin zone）边界，受非点式对称性（non-symmorphic symmetry）保护；通过调节摩尔周期可近乎连续地控制拓扑激发（topological excitations）。

Conclusion: 研究为摩尔异质结构（moiré heterostructures）作为创建与调控拓扑摩尔狄拉克态（topological moiré-Dirac states）的平台提供了直接实验证据。

Abstract: Moiré heterostructures provide a powerful framework for tailoring electronic band structures via controlled long-range periodic superlattice potentials. Beyond widely studied moiré-tailored flat bands, folded band structures can host emergent Dirac states, which have recently attracted considerable interest. Direct momentum-resolved observation of gapless moiré-Dirac quasiparticles, however, is challenging and has so far remained elusive. By performing angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy measurements on an epitaxial surface-moiré structure, we here provide direct spectroscopic evidence of moiré-dressed Dirac states with topological character. Driven by the one-dimensional superlattice potential, electrons propagate anisotropically with a weak but massless Dirac dispersion along the confinement direction. The observed band crossings belong to topological nodal lines pinned to the mini-Brillouin zone boundaries. As such, they are enforced and robustly protected by the non-symmorphic symmetry of the superlattice. Finally, we demonstrate that the topological excitations can be almost continuously controlled by tuning the moiré lattice periodicity, directly unveiling moiré heterostructures as a promising platform for creating and controlling topological moiré-Dirac states.

</details>


### [194] [Collective and separate metal-insulator transitions in correlated vanadium dioxide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25638)
*Xuanchi Zhou,Xiaohui Yao,Wentian Lu,Chunwei Yao,Xiaomei Qiao*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过在VO2体系中人工设计氧缺陷、插入TiO2中间层以及引入可移动氢离子，实现了对关联电子系统中集体性与分离性金属-绝缘体相变（MIT）的可逆调控，将集体长度尺度从被动阈值转变为动态设计参数，为自适应关联电子器件提供了工程化手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 关联电子系统中一阶金属-绝缘体相变（first-order metal-insulator transition, MIT）由集体行为与分离行为之间复杂的相互作用所支配，二者之间的临界平衡定义了一个关键的集体长度尺度（collective length scale，通常小于5 nm），该尺度决定了新兴量子有序的涌现，然而对此二分法的主动调控一直难以实现。

Method: 在关联VO2体系中人工设计氧缺陷构建VO2/VO2-x同质结，以集体长度尺度扩展的方式促进集体性MIT；引入TiO2中间层，通过解耦电子序参量（electronic order parameter）驱动从集体性MIT到两步分离性MIT的交叉；进一步在VO2/TiO2/VO2-x三层膜中嵌入可移动氢离子，实现电子相调制（electronic phase modulations）的可逆控制，使两步MIT向一步MIT或集体性电子局域化（collective electron localization）转变。

Result: 通过氢离子对VO2电子能带结构（electronic band structure）的离子控制，可以灵活触发多态MIT（multi-state MIT），该过程受氢相关能带填充（hydrogen-related band filling）所支配。

Conclusion: 本文发现将集体长度尺度从被动的阈值转化为动态的设计参数，为工程化调控集体性与分离性MIT、构建自适应关联电子器件（adaptive correlated electronics）提供了可行手段。

Abstract: Deciphering the complicated interplay between collective and separate behaviors lies at the heart of first-order metal-insulator transition (MIT) in correlated electron systems, enabling the rational design of exotic electronic states and functionalities. The critical balance between collective and separate behaviors defines a fundamental collective length scale, typically shorter than 5 nm, that governs emergent quantum orders, yet active control over this dichotomy remains elusive. Here, we realize on-demand manipulation of the collective and separate MIT within the correlated VO2 system in a reversible fashion. Artificially designing the oxygen deficiency in VO2/VO2-x homojunction fosters a collective MIT with an extended collective length scale, whereas the introduction of a TiO2 interlayer drives a crossover from this collective to a two-step separate MIT via decoupling of the electronic order parameter. Incorporating mobile hydrogens into the VO2/TiO2/VO2-x trilayer enables reversible control over electronic phase modulations, transitioning a two-step MIT towards either a one-step MIT or collective electron localization. This ionic control over the electronic band structure of VO2 flexibly triggers multi-state MIT, a process governed by hydrogen-related band filling. Our findings transform the collective length scale from a passive threshold into a dynamic design parameter, establishing a viable handle for engineering collective and separate MIT for adaptive correlated electronics.

</details>


### [195] [Validity of DFT+U band gaps in all its known functional forms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25706)
*Andrew C. Burgess,David D. O'Regan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文从理论上证明了DFT+U方法的本征能隙与其总能量差定义的基本能隙等价，系统梳理了所有已发表的DFT+U类泛函，并通过Mott-Hubbard极限下的氢晶格案例验证了分析结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管DFT+U方法被广泛应用于过渡金属和镧系元素晶体的模拟，但其本征能隙与基本能隙之间的概念有效性一直存在争议，有必要从理论上澄清这一关联的有效性条件。

Method: 基于近年来关于局域和半局域泛函的研究进展，针对完整周期性体系、缺陷体系和孤立体系，在赝势、PAW势、杂化泛函及不同子空间投影水平下，建立了统一的符号体系来检验各类DFT+U类泛函的本征能隙与基本能隙的等价性。

Result: 证明在k点采样收敛的完整周期性体系中，DFT+U本征能隙与总能量差计算的基本能隙匹配；这一结论在赝势、PAW势、杂化泛函及不同DFT+U(+J)投影水平下均成立，但对于缺陷体系或孤立体系不成立；同时对所有已发表的DFT+U类泛函进行了统一符号化梳理和分析验证。

Conclusion: DFT+U本征能隙在完整周期性固体中具有概念有效性，可用于表征基本能隙，但该有效性不适用于缺陷体系或孤立体系，这一澄清为DFT+U方法在能隙计算中的合理应用提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The Density Functional Theory plus Hubbard $U$ (DFT+$U$) technique is one of the most widely used tools by condensed matter physicists and solid state chemists for the simulation of transition-metal and lanthanide bearing crystals, and increasingly of much more diverse chemistries. Although often synonymous with the corrective functionals of Dudarev et al. and Liechtenstein et al., there exists a wide variety of DFT+$U$-type functionals ready to be utilized, and no doubt yet to be developed. Since the earliest days, the gap in the DFT+$U$ single-particle eigenspectrum has been associated with the fundamental band gap, and the method has typically found more success for spectra than for total-energy derived properties. There has been some doubt, however, as to the conceptual validity of this association. Here, extending findings from recent years regarding local and semi-local functionals, we prove that the DFT+$U$ eigenspectrum gap is indeed valid, in the sense that it matches its own fundamental gap calculated using total-energy differences. This is true for pristine periodic systems with converged $k$-point sampling but not, however, for defective ones or isolated systems. We show that bandgap validity for solids holds in the presence of pseudopotentials and PAW potentials, when using hybrid functionals, and in DFT+$U$(+$J$) irrespective of the level of subspace projection onto the band-edge states. We survey every DFT+$U$-type functional known to have been published to date, within a unified notation. We verify analytically under which conditions the eigenvalue gap equals its fundamental gap for each functional, and analyze its effect on total energies and gaps for the hydrogen lattice in the Mott-Hubbard limit.

</details>


### [196] [Exact results for the Hubbard model on bipartite lattices in spatial dimensions $d>1$: Seven theorems from the full [SU(2)$\times$SU(2)$\times$U(1)]/$\mathbb{Z}_2^2$ symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25712)
*J. M. P. Carmelo*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于空间维度 d>1 的二部晶格上的哈伯德模型，精确结果极为稀少。然而该模型是描述许多凝聚态系统中电子关联的最简单玩具模型（toy model），具有重要的物理意义，迫切需要建立新的精确框架来深入理解其物理。

Method: 论文在具有 N_a 个格点的二部晶格（包括正方、蜂窝、立方、体心立方、面心立方和金刚石晶格）上，建立了基于物理自旋和物理 η-自旋的精确框架，并在此基础上推导出七个精确定理。

Result: 建立了七个关于哈伯德模型的精确定理，这些定理为该模型提供了新的物理洞察（physical insight）。

Conclusion: 该精确框架为哈伯德模型以及由其描述的凝聚态材料（如铜氧化物超导体、石墨烯及其衍生体系等）的未来研究提供了坚实且鲁棒的基础。

Abstract: There are few exact results for the Hubbard model on bipartite lattices of spatial dimension $d>1$. Nevertheless, the Hubbard model with transfer integral $t$ and onsite repulsion $U$ on bipartite lattices with $N_a$ sites, such as the square, honeycomb, cubic, body-centered cubic, face-centered cubic, and diamond lattices, provides the simplest toy model for describing electronic correlations in many condensed-matter systems and is therefore a quantum problem of considerable physical interest. Seven exact theorems that provide new physical insight into the model are established. Overall, the exact framework based on physical spins and physical $η$-spins for the Hubbard model on bipartite lattices of spatial dimension $d>1$ introduced in this paper offers a robust foundation for future studies of the model, as well as of the condensed-matter materials, such as cuprate superconductors, graphene and graphene-derived systems, and other quantum systems, that it describes.

</details>


### [197] [Pareto Frontier of Neural Quantum States: Scalable, Affordable, and Accurate Convolutional Backflow for Strongly Correlated Lattice Fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25775)
*Yuntian Gu,Zeyao Han,Wenrui Li,Zhiyu Xiao,Tao Xiang,Mingpu Qin,Liwei Wang,Dingshun Lv*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出两种互补的神经量子态（Neural Quantum States, NQS）架构——SCALE（高效型）和ACE（高精度型），在强关联晶格费米子模拟中实现了新的帕累托前沿（Pareto frontier），其中SCALE通过低秩行列式更新将计算复杂度从O(N⁴)降至O(N³)并实现超过40倍的实际加速，ACE则通过深度卷积堆叠在大系统上达到前所未有的精度；在Hubbard和t-J模型上的基准测试表明，两种架构分别在效率和精度上达到领先水平，并应用于此前无法访问的1/8掺杂纯Hubbard模型中，未发现水平与垂直填充条纹态之间存在显著能量差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经量子态（NQS）虽已成为研究强关联多费米子系统的最精确方法之一，但计算资源消耗极大，现有方法难以在大系统上兼顾效率与精度。本文旨在通过设计互补的NQS架构，突破这一效率和精度的瓶颈。

Method: 引入两个基于反流（backflow）相关架构的卷积神经量子态：Sparse Convolutional Ansatz for Lattice Electrons (SCALE)，采用定制化卷积设计并通过低秩行列式更新实现高效局部更新；Accurate Convolutional ansatz for lattice Electrons (ACE)，使用深度卷积堆叠以最大化表达能力。

Result: SCALE将反流方法的计算复杂度从O(N⁴)降至O(N³)，实际测试中实现超过40倍的加速，同时保持高变分精度；ACE在大型系统上达到前所未有的精度，在16×4系统中仅用1/6的运行时间超越了近期成果。在32×32的1/8掺杂纯Hubbard模型中，未发现水平与垂直填充条纹态之间存在显著能量差异。

Conclusion: SCALE和ACE两种NQS架构分别在效率和精度上定义了新的帕累托前沿，为探索强关联费米子物理（如非常规超导的微观机制）提供了可扩展、低成本和精确的计算工具。

Abstract: Neural Quantum States (NQS) are now among the most accurate methods for studying strongly correlated many-fermion systems, outperforming existing many-body approaches for large systems. However, NQS calculations remain extremely resource-intensive. Here, we introduce a new Pareto frontier of efficiency and accuracy for NQS in simulating strongly correlated lattice fermions, defined by two complementary backflow-related architectures: the Sparse Convolutional Ansatz for Lattice Electrons (SCALE) (state-of-the-art efficiency) and the Accurate Convolutional ansatz for lattice Electrons (ACE) (state-of-the-art accuracy), benchmarked on the iconic Hubbard and $t-J$ models for large lattices. SCALE uses a tailored convolutional design enabling efficient local updates via low-rank determinant updates, reducing computational scaling from $O(N^4)$ to $O(N^3)$ in backflow methods and yielding a >40$\times$ practical speed-up in tests while maintaining high variational accuracy. As an application, we study the previously inaccessible 1/8-doped pure Hubbard model up to $32 \times 32$, finding no significant energy difference between horizontal and vertical filled stripe states - contrasting with half-filled stripe states when next-nearest-neighbor hoppings are included. ACE employs a deep convolutional stack to maximize expressive power, achieving unprecedented accuracy on large systems. Extensive benchmarks on Hubbard and $t-J$ models show SCALE delivers variational energies competitive with leading methods at a fraction of the cost, while ACE sets a new accuracy benchmark, surpassing recent results with only 1/6 the runtime for $16 \times 4$ systems. These new NQS approaches provide scalable, affordable, and accurate tools for exploring strongly correlated fermionic physics, such as the microscopic mechanism of unconventional superconductivity.

</details>

### [198] [Absence of Quasi-Majorana False Positives in Full-Shell Hybrid Nanowires](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24858)
*Carlos Payá,César Robles,Pablo San-Jose,Elsa Prada*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文指出，在传统部分壳层混合纳米线中，由于平滑边界限制等原因会产生准马约拉纳零模（quasi-MZMs），导致隧穿谱无法可靠检测真实马约拉纳零模（MZMs）；而在全壳层混合纳米线设计中，平滑边界产生的拓扑平庸表皮（trivial skin）能抑制准MZMs的干扰，从而恢复隧穿谱作为检测MZMs的可靠工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决传统部分壳层混合纳米线（partial-shell hybrid nanowires）中隧穿谱（tunneling spectroscopy）无法明确检测马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes, MZMs）的问题，即准马约拉纳零模（quasi-MZMs）会模仿真实MZMs的局域信号，造成检测歧义。

Method: 对比分析两种纳米线设计：部分壳层纳米线（仅有部分超导壳层包围半导体核心）与全壳层纳米线（超导壳层完全包围半导体核心）；在全壳层纳米线中，通过超导壳层形成人工涡旋（synthetic vortex），宿主卡洛利-德热纳-马特里康类比态（Caroli-de Gennes-Matricon analog states），并研究平滑边界限制下这些态的拓扑性质及其对隧穿谱检测的影响。

Result: 在全壳层混合纳米线中，平滑边界限制会导致卡洛利-德热纳-马特里康类比态在纳米线末端形成拓扑平庸表皮（topologically trivial skin），阻止局域探针探测到准MZMs；而当真实MZMs在边缘形成时，该平庸表皮消失。

Conclusion: 全壳层混合纳米线（full-shell hybrid nanowires）设计能够克服传统部分壳层纳米线中MZM检测的歧义性问题，使隧穿谱成为一种在存在平滑无序（smooth disorder）条件下可靠的MZM检测技术。

Abstract: Tunneling spectroscopy cannot be used as an unambiguous detection tool for Majorana zero modes (MZMs) in conventional partial-shell nanowires. The presence of smooth confinement at the end of the hybrid wire (among other sources of disorder) can create exponentially pinned zero-energy states, called quasi-MZMs, that mimic all local signatures of MZMs but lack topological protection. We find that this ambiguity in MZM detection does not occur in full-shell hybrid nanowires, an alternative nanowire design where a superconducting shell fully surrounds the semiconductor core. Acting as a synthetic vortex, a full-shell hybrid nanowire hosts Caroli-de Gennes-Matricon analog states. In the presence of smooth confinement, these states create a topologically trivial skin at the wire's end that prevents the local probe from detecting quasi-MZMs. Conversely, the trivial skin disappears when true MZMs form at the edge. This renders tunneling spectroscopy a reliable MZM detection technique for full-shell hybrid nanowires in the presence of smooth disorder.

</details>


### [199] [Dispersion of Anyon Bloch Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24859)
*Kishore Iyer,Andreas Feuerpfeil,Valentin Crépel,Nicolas Regnault,Christophe Mora*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从刘维林（Laughlin）波函数出发，解析构造了理想能带中分数量子陈绝缘体（FCI）的单任意子布洛赫态（Bloch state），揭示了任意子谱的m重简并性及其与量子几何非均匀性的关系，发现任意子色散带宽由量子几何非均匀性控制，并可被高阶谐波显著抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分数量子陈绝缘体（FCI）是零磁场下的分数量子霍尔态类似物，但其任意子激发（anyonic excitations）由于多体贝里相位（many-body Berry phase）的有限磁通会经历动量色散。理解任意子的色散性质对于揭示FCI的拓扑物态及其量子几何机制至关重要，但目前缺乏解析可控的分析方法。

Method: 基于填充因子为1/m的刘维林（Laughlin）波函数，在理想能带中解析构造了单任意子布洛赫态（Bloch state），并以此为基高效计算任意子色散。通过分析量子几何（quantum geometry）的非均匀性以及其各阶谐波对色散带宽的影响，研究了磁平移对称性（magnetic translation symmetry）的作用。

Result: 任意子谱在缩小的磁布里渊区（magnetic Brillouin zone, BZ）中表现出m重简并，源于FCI的拓扑简并性。任意子色散带宽由量子几何非均匀性控制，在弱调制下线性增长，强调制下趋于饱和。高阶谐波单独作用可显著抑制色散，这一现象归因于涌现的磁平移对称性。第二阶谐波的符号决定系统主导的调制类型，从而降低或增强带宽。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种解析可控的方法来评估理想能带FCI中的任意子谱，揭示了非均匀量子几何与涌现对称性如何共同塑造任意子的色散行为。

Abstract: Fractional Chern insulators (FCIs) are zero magnetic field analogs of fractional quantum Hall states. While the electrons forming an FCI are not subject to an external magnetic field, their anyonic excitations experience a magnetic field with finite-flux due to a many-body Berry phase, whose lattice periodicity generically induces some dispersion. From Laughlin wavefunctions at filling 1/m, we analytically construct single-anyon Bloch states in an ideal band, providing a basis to efficiently compute the dispersion. The anyon spectrum exhibits an $m$-fold degeneracy in the reduced magnetic Brillouin zone (BZ), which originates from the topological degeneracy of the FCI. From our wavefunctions, we derive the m^2-fold degeneracy seen in previous works, showing it to be a splicing of anyon momenta into the electronic BZ. Finally, we find that the anyon dispersion bandwidth is controlled by quantum geometry non-uniformity, growing linearly at weak modulation and saturating at strong modulation. Remarkably, higher harmonics of the quantum geometry alone strongly suppress the dispersion, which we attribute to emergent magnetic translation symmetries. When combined with the first harmonic, a positive (negative) second harmonic drives the system toward a second- (first-) harmonic-dominated regime, thereby reducing (enhancing) the bandwidth. Our results offer an analytically controlled method for evaluating anyon spectra in ideal band FCI, shedding light on how non-uniform quantum geometry and emergent symmetries shape the dispersion of anyons.

</details>


### [200] [Probing Spin Dynamics Across Magnetic Phase Transitions in CrCl3 Nanoflakes Using Nitrogen-Vacancy Microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25002)
*Ben Hammons,Jitender Kumar,Sehrish Iqbal,Prem Karki,Karishma Prasad,Tianlin Li,Aram Pirali,Ayodimeji E. Aregbesola,Rupak Timalsina,Xia Hong,Jian Wang,Kapildeb Ambal,Ilja Fescenko,Abdelghani Laraoui*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用低温金刚石量子传感显微镜，通过氮空位（NV）色心的光学探测磁共振、拉比振荡和自旋-晶格弛豫时间测量，研究了层状范德华磁体CrCl₃纳米片在磁性相变过程中的自旋动力学。实验发现铁磁区NV自旋共振对比度显著下降、拉比振荡崩溃、弛豫率增强两个数量级，表明千兆赫兹范围内自旋涨落加剧；结合宽频铁磁共振谱与唯象模型，揭示了磁噪声在铁磁区最强并在整个相图中显著演变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CrCl₃是一种层状范德华（van der Waals, vdW）磁体，具有面内磁各向异性和堆叠增强的层间耦合，是研究磁子流体动力学和类梅伦拓扑自旋缺陷等奇异纳米磁现象的理想平台。理解CrCl₃在其磁性相变处的自旋动力学对于其在磁子学（magnonics）中的应用至关重要。

Method: 使用低温金刚石量子传感显微镜（cryogenic diamond quantum sensing microscopy），基于浅层氮空位（nitrogen vacancy, NV）色心的光学探测磁共振（optically detected magnetic resonance）、拉比振荡（Rabi oscillations）和自旋-晶格弛豫时间（spin-lattice relaxation time, T₁）测量；并结合CrCl₃微晶的宽频铁磁共振（broadband ferromagnetic resonance）光谱学以及磁噪声诱导NV弛豫的唯象模型。

Result: 在铁磁区观察到NV自旋共振对比度显著降低、拉比振荡崩溃、弛豫率G₁=1/T₁增强两个数量级，表明千兆赫兹（GHz）范围自旋涨落加剧；宽频铁磁共振测得共振频率4-15 GHz、线宽约24 mT，支持NV测量结果；唯象模型将反铁磁、铁磁和顺磁涨落通道结合，成功再现G₁的温度依赖性，表明磁噪声在铁磁区最强并在整个相图中显著演变。

Conclusion: 这些结果对于将CrCl₃应用于二维磁子学（2D magnonics）和混合量子-磁子系统（hybrid quantum-magnon systems）具有重要意义。

Abstract: CrCl3, a layered van der Waals (vdW) magnet, exhibits in-plane magnetic anisotropy and enhanced interlayer coupling upon stacking, making it an ideal platform to host exotic nanoscale magnetic phenomena such as magnon hydrodynamics and meron-like topological spin defects. When interfaced with other vdW materials, its antiferromagnetic-to-ferromagnetic and ferromagnetic-to-paramagnetic phase transitions and magnetic anisotropy can be tuned by voltage, strain, and layer stacking. Understanding the spin dynamics of CrCl3 at its magnetic phase transitions is crucial to its applications in magnonics. Here, we investigate the spin dynamics of CrCl3 nanoflakes using cryogenic diamond quantum sensing microscopy, based on measuring optically detected magnetic resonance, Rabi oscillations, and spin-lattice relaxation time (T1) of shallow nitrogen vacancy (NV) centers in diamond. In the ferromagnetic regime, we observe a pronounced reduction in the NV spin resonance contrast, a collapse of the Rabi oscillations, and a strong enhancement by two orders of magnitude of the relaxation rate, G1 = 1/T1. These observations indicate intensified spin fluctuations in the gigahertz range. Broadband ferromagnetic resonance spectroscopy on CrCl3 microcrystals reveals resonance frequencies in the 4-15 GHz range together with a linewidth of ~24 mT, further supporting the NV measurements. A phenomenological model of magnetic-noise-induced NV relaxation reproduces the temperature dependence of G1 by combining antiferromagnetic, ferromagnetic, and paramagnetic fluctuation channels, indicating that magnetic noise is strongest in the ferromagnetic regime and evolves markedly across the phase diagram. These results are crucial for using CrCl3 in 2D magnonics and hybrid quantum-magnon systems.

### [201] [Femtosecond tunneling spectroscopy of ultrafast band bending dynamics at the atomic limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25146)

Method: 采用光波驱动的太赫兹扫描隧道显微镜（THz-STM）探测共振带间激发后局部电子结构的超快演化；结合太赫兹时域光谱（terahertz time-domain spectroscopy）在针尖近场中分离太赫兹驱动场的相干亚周期动力学与本征样品响应。

Conclusion: 建立了一种超快隧穿光谱学（ultrafast tunneling spectroscopy）新机制，能够以前所未有的时空分辨率捕获瞬态电子结构和动态能带对齐，对理解载流子输运、缺陷介导过程以及基于动态可调材料的光电子技术发展具有重要意义。

Abstract: Atomic-scale disorder shapes the potential energy landscape traversed by photoexcited charge carriers, while the carriers themselves also dynamically reshape this landscape. However, resolving ultrafast photocarrier motion at atomic length scales has remained a central challenge in materials science. Here, we demonstrate that lightwave-driven terahertz scanning tunneling microscopy (THz-STM) provides access to these dynamics by probing the ultrafast evolution of local electronic structure following resonant interband excitation. Applying this approach to the photoexcited GaAs(110) surface, we image the resulting femtosecond carrier dynamics by tracking the transient photocurrents produced by ultrafast shifts in the energy alignment of surface and bulk electronic states near individual surface defects. Supported by modeling, we experimentally resolve the time-dependent band bending produced by photoinduced charge carriers across the atomic-scale landscape of the sample surface. Crucially, we employ terahertz time-domain spectroscopy in the tip near-field to disentangle the coherent sub-cycle dynamics induced by the terahertz driving field from the intrinsic sample response. We establish a new regime of ultrafast tunneling spectroscopy that captures transient electronic structure and dynamic band alignment with unprecedented spatio-temporal resolution, which has significant implications for understanding carrier transport, defect-mediated processes, and the development of optoelectronic technologies based on dynamically tunable materials.

### [202] [Anomalous Mixed-State Floquet Topology in One-Dimensional Open Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25248)
*Görkem D. Dinc,Alexander Schnell,Andy M. Martin*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对开放量子系统中的Floquet拓扑理解有限，缺乏从微观耦合模型出发的系统分析。本文旨在探索周期性驱动和耗散共存时非平衡拓扑的存续条件与分类结构。

Method: 采用Floquet-Born-Markov理论微观描述系统与热库的耦合；利用系综几何相位（EGP）推广Zak相位到开放量子系统；通过纯化谱（purity spectrum）建立混合态（mixed states）的能带拓扑对应。

Result: 辨识出一对拓扑不变量$(φ^{0}_{\mathrm{EGP}}, Δφ^π_{\mathrm{EGP}})$，揭示其与孤立Floquet SSH系统的$\mathbb{Z}\times\mathbb{Z}$分类一致；证明在稳态结构定义良好的参数区域内，该分类可拓展至耗散、有限温度场景。

Conclusion: 周期性驱动可在耗散稳态中诱导非平凡缠绕（winding）和准能谱（quasienergy spectrum）中的$0$与$π$带隙，每个带隙中存在受保护的边缘模（edge modes）。Floquet拓扑是超越孤立零温系统的鲁棒概念，所发展的形式为具有线性库耦合的二次费米子系统提供了普适框架。

Abstract: We investigate the non-equilibrium topology of a periodically driven, dissipative Su-Schrieffer-Heeger chain using the ensemble geometric phase (EGP) $φ_{\mathrm{EGP}}$-a generalisation of the Zak phase to open quantum systems. In contrast to earlier work, we use Floquet-Born-Markov theory to describe the coupling to thermal reservoirs microscopically. We show that the steady state can be characterised by a Hermitian purity spectrum, providing a direct analogue of band topology for mixed states. The periodic drive induces nontrivial winding and a quasienergy spectrum with distinct $0$ and $π$ band gaps, with protected edge modes in each gap. We identify a pair of topological invariants $(φ^{0}_{\mathrm{EGP}}, Δφ^π_{\mathrm{EGP}})$, revealing a structure consistent with a $\mathbb{Z}\times\mathbb{Z}$ classification known from isolated Floquet SSH systems, and show how it extends to a dissipative, finite-temperature setting in regimes where the steady-state structure remains well defined. Our results demonstrate when and how known Floquet topology survives in a driven-dissipative Gaussian steady state and establish Floquet topology as a robust concept beyond isolated zero-temperature systems. The underlying formalism provides a general framework for quadratic fermionic systems with linear bath couplings.

Conclusion: 该工作为理解倾斜能谱（tilted spectrum）与结构形变（structural deformation）如何共同影响量子输运提供了统一的理论框架，并指出在应变工程（strain-engineered）系统中存在明确的实验可观测输运特征。

Abstract: We investigate the transport signatures of pseudo-Landau levels (PLLs) in two-dimensional anisotropic Dirac systems with tilted cones, whose effective bandstructure results from strain-induced pseudogauge fields. In contrast to conventional Landau quantisation, the PLLs exhibit explicit momentum-dependence by being dispersive, leading to finite longitudinal group-velocities. We analyse the transport properties within the semiclassical Boltzmann framework by computing the electrical, thermoelectric, and thermal response in the linear regime, which acquire nonzero longitudinal components. We also check the validity of the Mott relation and Wiedemann-Franz law in our system. Our results provide a unified framework for understanding the interplay between tilted spectrum and structural deformation in affecting quantum transport, and suggest unambiguous experimental signatures in strain-engineered systems.

Beyond their fundamental interest, these materials hold potential for future technological applications through the emergence of novel concepts and functionalities. Synthetic materials have been engineered using a wide range of physical platforms, including both natural atoms and fabricated artificial atoms in the solid-state. A particularly intriguing approach relies on photons. When confined in optical cavities and strongly coupled to matter excitations, photons acquire an effective mass and can experience interactions, giving rise to hybrid light-matter quasiparticles known as polaritons. By arranging polaritons in periodic structures, one can engineer synthetic photonic materials with tailored band structures and controllable interactions, offering a promising route toward exploring strongly correlated photonic phases. This chapter focuses on a solid-state realization of such systems: exciton polaritons confined in semiconductor microcavities. Following a general introduction, we describe how photon mass and photonic band structures emerge from cavity confinement, and how interactions arise via strong coupling to excitons in quantum wells. We finally review how these ingredients can be used to explore rich physics from the mean-field to the quantum regime.

### [205] [Temporal hopping dynamics in exciton-polariton condensation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25519)
*Elena Rozas,Wojciech Bukalski,Yannik Brune,Adbhut Gupta,Kirk Baldwin,Loren N. Pfeiffer,Hassan Alnatah,Jonathan Beaumariage,David W. Snoke,Paolo Comaron,Marzena H. Szymanska,Marc Aßmann*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用光学捕获（optical trapping）与零差探测（homodyne detection）直接测量凝聚体的光子统计（photon statistics）与二阶关联函数g^(2)(0)；数值模拟基于驱动-耗散极化激元场的随机截断维格纳描述（stochastic Truncated Wigner description）。

Conclusion: 观测到的时间跳跃（temporal hopping）是极化激元凝聚的内在特征，为冷凝相变提供了超越静态描述的动力学视角。

Abstract: Polariton condensates provide a versatile platform for exploring non-equilibrium phase transitions and collective phenomena in open quantum systems. Near the condensation threshold, these systems are particularly sensitive to fluctuations and instabilities, which can strongly influence the condensate formation. Using optical trapping and homodyne detection, we directly access the photon statistics and second-order correlation function $g^{(2)}(0)$ of the condensate. We show that polariton condensation near the threshold is not a purely static transition, but instead undergoes a dynamical regime characterized by stochastic hopping between condensed and non-condensed states. These intermittent dynamics are accompanied by a gradual reduction of $g^{(2)}(0)$ towards unity, revealing the progressive build-up of coherence even in the presence of strong temporal fluctuations. Numerical simulations, based on a stochastic Truncated Wigner description of the driven-dissipative polariton field, reproduce these dynamics and capture the essential role of noise and reservoir interactions. This work demonstrates that the observed temporal hopping is an intrinsic feature of polariton condensation, providing a dynamical perspective that goes beyond static descriptions of the condensation phase transition.

### [207] [Magnomechanical Coupling in Suspended 2D van der Waals Ferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25588)

Conclusion: 悬浮的范德瓦耳斯磁体膜为磁机械学（magnomechanics）提供了一个稳健且高度可调谐的平台。

Abstract: Magnomechanical systems provide a promising route for exploring coherent hybrid magnon-phonon interactions and hybrid information processing, but their realization has so far been limited by weak magnon-phonon coupling in conventional bulk platforms. We show that a suspended membrane of a two-dimensional van der Waals ferromagnet with in-plane magnetization and out-of-plane mechanical oscillations exhibits large magnomechanical coupling dominated by magnetoelastic interactions. The parametric single magnon-phonon coupling rate scales linearly with pre-strain and can reach hundreds of Hertz to low kiloHertz in suspended membranes of van der Waals ferromagnets such as CrGeTe_3 under experimentally realistic conditions. This rate exceeds typical values reported for YIG spheres by more than three orders of magnitude. Our results demonstrate that suspended membranes of van der Waals magnets provide a robust and highly tunable platform for magnomechanics.

</details>


### [208] [Binary topological logic gates in Kane-Mele nanostructures via local control of edge-state transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25633)
*K. Zberecki*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在Kane-Mele纳米结构中，通过在局域控制区域施加静电、交换类及Rashba型微扰，在Landauer-Büttiker框架下实现了NOT和AND逻辑门。其工作机制依赖于边缘电流的受控重路由而非精细调谐干涉，并展示了稳定的工作窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑边缘态（topological edge states）有望用于后CMOS器件，但将其转化为基本逻辑单元仍需要结构简单且物理机制清晰的方案。

Method: 在Kane-Mele纳米结构中设置空间局域控制区，通过静电场、交换类及Rashba型自旋-轨道耦合（Rashba-type spin-orbit coupling）微扰编码逻辑输入；输出通过终端透射（terminal transmission）在相干Landauer-Büttiker框架（Landauer-Büttiker framework）中读取。

Result: 在多端蜂窝状几何结构中实现了NOT门和AND门；电流图（current maps）表明其运作受控于边缘电流的受控重路由（controlled rerouting）而非精细调谐干涉；NOT门在测试参数范围内具有稳定工作窗口，AND门窗口略窄但仍可靠。

Conclusion: Kane-Mele纳米结构可作为实现原始拓扑二进制逻辑（topological binary logic）的透明平台。

Abstract: Topological edge states are an attractive starting point for post-CMOS device concepts, but turning them into elementary logic still requires simple architectures with a clear physical mechanism. Here we investigate binary logic in Kane-Mele nanostructures with spatially localized control regions. Logical inputs are encoded through local electrostatic, exchange-like, and Rashba-type perturbations, while the output is read out from terminal transmission within a coherent Landauer-Büttiker framework. We demonstrate working NOT and AND gates in multiterminal honeycomb geometries and show, with the help of current maps, that their operation is governed by controlled rerouting of edge currents rather than by fine-tuned interference. Robustness tests further indicate a stable operating window within the tested parameter range for the NOT gate and a somewhat narrower but still reliable one for the AND gate. These results identify Kane-Mele nanostructures as a transparent platform for primitive topological binary logic.

</details>


### [209] [Magnetoplasma excitations in interacting GaAs disks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25736)
*S. A. Andreeva,A. A. Gavrilov,K. R. Dzhikirba,A. S. Astrakhantseva,A. V. Shchepetilnikov,O. V. Orlov,V. V. Solovyev,I. V. Kukushkin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 通过太赫兹光谱实验研究二维电子气圆盘阵列中圆盘间耦合对磁等离子体激元色散的调控作用，发现随晶格周期减小、耦合增强，集体激发模式从独立圆盘磁等离子体模式演变为色散发生显著修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究二维电子系统（2DES）圆盘阵列中圆盘间耦合对磁等离子体激元（magnetoplasmon）色散关系的影响，以理解周期性结构中集体模式的耦合行为。

Method: 采用磁光太赫兹（terahertz, THz）光谱技术，通过系统减小圆盘晶格周期来增强耦合强度，进而追踪集体激发模式的演化过程。

Result: 在大间距条件下，系统呈现对应于单个圆盘独立激发的磁等离子体模式；当圆盘间距减小时，磁等离子体色散关系发生明显修正。

Conclusion: 圆盘间耦合强度是调控二维电子系统阵列中磁等离子体激元色散的关键参数，耦合的增强可显著改变集体激发模式的行为。

Abstract: We investigate the effect of inter-disk coupling on the magnetoplasmon dispersion in a square lattice of two-dimensional electron system (2DES) disks etched from a GaAs quantum well. Using magneto-optical terahertz (THz) spectroscopy, we track the evolution of the collective modes as disk lattice period is systematically reduced, thereby increasing the coupling strength. At large distances, the system exhibits magnetoplasma modes corresponding to individual excitations in disks. As the inter-disk distance decreases, we observe a modification to magnetoplasma dispersion.

</details>


### [210] [3D integration of a hybrid quantum dot circuit-QED device for fast gate dispersive charge readout and coherent spin-photon coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25871)
*Sebastien Granel,Frederic Gustavo,Jean-Luc Thomassin,Heimanu Niebojewski,Benoit Bertrand,Frederic Berger,Alain Gueugnot,Chafik Mhamdi,Etienne Dumur,Romain Maurand,Simon Zihlmann*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于铟凸点互连与氮化铌超导薄膜的三维集成工艺，解决了混合电路量子电动力学（cQED）中异质材料堆叠导致微波损耗过高的问题。该工艺在半工业级硅MOS自旋量子比特中实现了高质量因子超导谐振腔、高灵敏度电荷色散读出，以及强自旋-光子耦合（gs/2π = 75 MHz），验证了三维集成在量子点自旋cQED中的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合电路量子电动力学（hybrid circuit quantum electrodynamics, cQED）旨在将门定义量子点中的自旋和电荷自由度、声子、磁振子等多种量子自由度与超导微波腔中的量子化电磁场耦合，以探索基础物理问题并用于量子计算与模拟。然而，低微波损耗是许多混合cQED实验的关键，但由于这些量子自由度所需的材料堆叠（如半导体、铁磁体或压电材料）往往具有特殊性与复杂性，实现低损耗极具挑战。

Method: 提出一种三维集成（3D-integration）工艺，基于间距为10 μm的密集铟凸点（indium bump）互连与氮化铌（Niobium Nitride, NbN）超导薄膜。首先测试直流与射频互连特性，验证了高电流互连良率以及单光子区NbN谐振腔在单个铟凸点互连中断后仍高于10⁵的内腔品质因子（internal quality factor）。随后制备了一个基于半工业级MOS空穴双量子点与高阻抗NbN谐振腔的三维集成混合cQED器件。

Result: 三维集成混合cQED器件的腔体内腔品质因子超过10000。基于栅极的电荷自由度色散读出实现创纪录灵敏度，在300 ns内信噪比（SNR）达到100。自旋-光子耦合强度（spin-photon coupling）为 gs/2π = 75 MHz，属于强耦合区域。

Conclusion: 该工作验证了三维集成工艺在量子点混合自旋电路量子电动力学中的可行性，为实现高保真度自旋读出以及基于微波光子的远程自旋量子比特纠缠开辟了路径。

Abstract: Hybrid circuit quantum electrodynamics (cQED) aims at coupling various quantum degrees of freedom, among which are spin and charge degrees of freedom in gate defined quantum dots, phonons or magnons... with quantized electromagnetic fields in superconducting microwave cavities to investigate fundamental physics questions or for quantum computation and simulation. However, low microwave losses, key for many hybrid cQED experiments, are challenging to achieve given the often exotic and/or complex material stacks (e.g. semiconducting material, ferromagnets, or piezoelectric materials) required to host the various quantum degrees of freedom. In this work, we present a 3D-integration process to overcome this challenge for semi-industrial silicon MOS spin qubits. The process is based on dense indium bump interconnects at a pitch of 10 μm and superconducting thin films of Niobium Nitride (NbN). First, we report on DC and RF interconnect properties that demonstrate a high galvanic interconnection yield and internal quality factors above 105 in the single photon regime for NbN resonators interrupted by a single indium bump interconnect. Eventually, we fabricated a 3D-integrated hybrid circuit quantum electrodynamics (cQED) device based on a semi-industrial MOS hole double quantum dot and a high impedance NbN resonator. For this device, we report a cavity internal quality factor above 10000 and demonstrate record sensitivity for gate-based dispersive readout of the charge degree of freedom with an SNR of 100 in 300 ns. Finally, we demonstrate strong spin-photon coupling of gs/{2π} = 75 MHz, which highlights the viability of 3D-integration for quantum dot based hybrid spin circuit quantum electrodynamics and opens to high-fidelity spin readout and microwave photon-based remote spin qubit entanglement.

</details>

### [211] [Measurement of jet photoproduction in ultra-peripheral Pb+Pb collisions without nuclear breakup at $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}} = 5.02$ TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24435)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于ATLAS探测器在LHC上记录的1.72 nb⁻¹ Pb+Pb超外围碰撞数据（√s_NN = 5.02 TeV），首次测量了核碰撞中光子-坡密子过程（γ+IP→jets）的截面，并通过模板拟合法统计分离了光子-坡密子、光子-光子和外围光核过程，同时发现无前向中子发射的γ+A→jets事件对应更外围的碰撞类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验已测量了超外围Pb+Pb碰撞中单侧前向中子发射的γ+A→jets过程，本研究旨在扩展该测量至双侧均无中子发射（0n0n）的情形，并首次在LHC核碰撞中分离并测量光子-坡密子（γ+IP→jets）过程，以更深入理解不同光子诱发过程的贡献与碰撞几何的关联。

Method: 利用ATLAS在2018年采集的5.02 TeV Pb+Pb超外围碰撞数据（积分亮度1.72 nb⁻¹），选取双侧均无核碎裂的0n0n事件；通过最小快度间隙（minimum rapidity gap）分布的模板拟合（template fit），统计分离光子-坡密子（γ+IP→jets）、光子-光子（γ+γ→jets）和外围光核（γ+A→jets）三种过程；硬过程运动学由基于anti-k_t算法、锥参数R=0.4的重建喷注（jets）确定。

Result: 首次在LHC核碰撞中测量了γ+IP→jets过程的截面；测量了0n0n事件中γ+A→jets过程电磁离解（electromagnetic dissociation）率，并与单侧中子发射结果进行了对比。

Conclusion: 比较结果支持如下假设：无前向中子发射的γ+A→jets事件对应更外围的一类γ+A碰撞，表明前向中子发射可作为碰撞中心度（centrality）的敏感探针。

Abstract: In ultra-relativistic heavy ion collisions at the LHC, each nucleus acts as a source of high-energy quasi-real photons that can participate in scattering processes without causing either participating nucleus to break up and emit forward neutrons. This paper extends recent measurements of $γ+A\rightarrow\mathrm{jets}$ production in ultra-peripheral Pb+Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}} = 5.02$ TeV with forward neutron emission on exactly one side of the event. The data presented here was recorded by the ATLAS collaboration at the LHC in 2018, corresponding to a luminosity of $1.72$ nb$^{-1}$. These results examines $5.02$ TeV Pb+Pb collisions where neither nucleus breaks up ($0n0n$), providing a mixture of photon--pomeron ($γ+I\!\!P\rightarrow\mathrm{jets}$), photon--photon ($γ+γ\rightarrow\mathrm{jets}$), and peripheral photonuclear ($γ+A\rightarrow\mathrm{jets}$) events. The different processes are statistically separated via a template fit of the minimum rapidity gap distribution. The kinematics of the hard processes are determined from $R = 0.4$ jets reconstructed using the anti-$k_t$ algorithm. The statistical separation of the different processes then allows for the first measurement of $γ+I\!\!P\rightarrow\mathrm{jets}$ cross-sections in nuclear collisions at the LHC. The rate for electromagnetic dissociation of $0n0n$ $γ+A\rightarrow\mathrm{jets}$ events is also measured and compared to the analogous result from collisions with single-sided neutron emission. These comparisons support the hypothesis that $γ+A\rightarrow\mathrm{jets}$ events without forward neutron emission select a more peripheral class of $γ+A$ collisions.

</details>
